Þæt Geāned Cynerīce hæfþ twa and hundnigontige scīra. Ēac hātaþ þisse scīra
eardfæstan scīra oððe gamola scīra.

Þisse scīra nabbað ane gerecþegnung, æfter mdccclxxxviiij, oððæt ðe to
mdcccclxxviiij stōwlicu āstyrung bād gestaðolod on hieran gierdum.

In Uladstire, stowlica ræden edniwung in mdcccclcciij arærde twa-endebyrdnes
stowlica ræden æt regio and læppa had; eall Uladstir wearþ seo regio.

On Engla and Norþ-wealum, þæt Local Government Act 1972 arærde scira for þæm
gesetnesa forþsetennesse utweard Grietran Lundene and Sylliege. Þa gerecþegnung
scira on Wealum wæron endedon in mdcccclxxxxvj.

In Englalande wæron mænigefealde læppan gesundrede fram hierum scirum æfter
mdcccclxxxx. Ælc "anfeald eard" (buton þa fram Bearrucscire) is scir be selfe
for þære gesetnesa, mid ānan læppan geond hierum halum earda, and hiere geþinge
is sēo geþinge þære scīre oððe sēo geþinge þæs læppan.

Scotland and Norþwealas habbaþ an-endebyrdnes "geþingedomas" and "fyrmestan
earde", þa on Wealum sume hetaþ "scīra" and sume "scīr-burgscipas".

Þæt Grietra Lunden eard (seo ne hatan næfre "scīr") wæs gearæred in mdcccclxv.
Þæt Grietra Lunden Gerec (Se Lundene Burgeald and Lundene Samnung) wæs in mm
gearæred.

On 1 Ēastermōnaþ 2009 (mmuiiii) weard þā Scīrgeþingas for Cornweallum,
Dunholmscīre, Norþhymbralande, Scrobbesbyrigscīre and Wiltunscīre ælc ānfeald
scīr. Beadanfordscīre and Ceasterscīre Scīregeþingas wæron beendedon.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sc%C4%ABr

In Bretene ƿǣron þa forman scīra ȝefundenon on Ƿestseaxum. Hīe ƿǣron dālas þæs
rīċes for lēodƿearde and for dōme, ǣlċ under ānum ealdormenn and in æfterȝēarum
ānum scirȝerefan. Þā fram þǣm lande ādrifon Ƿestseaxna cyningas þa Dene þā
ƿyrhtede hie scīra in eallum Englarīċe. Ēac in þǣm ȝēarum ārærde Mælcolm II
Cyning scīra on Scottum æfter þǣre Engliscan bisene and æftercyning David I
āsprēadede þis endebyrd.

Ƿillelm I cyning and his Frencisc hired brōhtedon to Englarīce þæt ƿord counte
oþþe in Nīƿum Englisce county sƿā sƿā hīe namedon eorlas count.

In Irlande and on Ƿealum ƿǣron scīra ȝeūpāræred be Engliscum ȝesetnese, oþþæt þe
oft folgedon hie ieldre eardum.

Mǣst þāra Bryttiscan scīrena nimaþ hiere naman æfter hierum hēafodburgum: sƿā
ȝebisnunga Eoferƿīcscīr æfter Eoferƿīce, Oxnafordscīr after Oxnaforde, ac sume
scīra nimaþ hiere naman fram ieldrum stedum, sƿā ȝebisnunga Defenascir, Cent and
Fif þā ƿǣron rīċu in ȝēardagum.

Ēac ofersǣ land þæs Bryttiscan Cyneƿises and þā Ȝeānlǣht Rīcu American habbaþ
scīra æfter þara Bryttiscan bisene.

Þa ēastern riciu Australie, and dælas Westernes Australie and Sūþaustralie sind
bedæleden in scirum (under þæm naman counties).

Þa scira sind underbedæled in tunscipum in Niwum Suþum Wealum, Uictorie,
Tasmanie and Cwenalande oððe hundredum in Suþaustralie. Þa counties nabbaþ ne
gerecbrūnung and hie sind ungecnawen on mæst þæm Australiacynn.

Scira for stowelican gerecþegnunga in Australie sind under þæm naman shires, ēac
mid municipalities.

In Ontarioe and Niwum Scotlande sind þas scira stowelicu gerecþegnung earda, ac
in Nīwum Brunswice, Quebece and Eadweard Æþeling Iega sind hie nu landgemet.

Mæst scira habbað þærin municipalities, ac sume sind ane miclu ceaster. In
norþerne Ontarioe and norþerne Quebece, sind þas landdālas boldgetalu
(districts) ne scira. In landum mid manigum burgum in suþerne middle Ontarioe
sind nīwe regional municipalities for stowelicre gerecþegnunga, ne scira.

For stowlicre gerecþegnunga hæfþ þæt Cynerice mænigfealde sōcna mid missenlicum
namum. Stowlice gerecþegnung scira in Englalande sindon ceasterniscan scira and
unceasterniscan scira, and on Norþwealum sind "scira" and "scirburgscipas".
(Beforan 1975 wæron administrative counties (gerecþegnung scira) and
scirburgscipu þa wæron gearærde in 1889.) Būton in Bearrucscire, ælcu
unceasterniscu scira on Englum hæfþ scirgeþinge. Þa mæra scira and eall
ceasterniscan scira sind gedæled in boldgetalum, ælc boldgetæl mid his agan
geþinge.

In Norþerne Irlande wæron þa siexe scirgeþingu and scirburgescipgeþingu geended
in 1973 and in hiere stedum sind 26 stowlicu gerecþegnung boldgetalu. Þa siexe
eardfæstan scira abidað in gemænelicum nytte for mænigefealdum wisum.

Irland Īege is bedæled in 32 scīra, hwærof 26 sind Irland-cynewise and 6 sind
Norðerne Īrland.

Þas scira sind be ealdgesegene gesamned in feower underriciu - Leinster (tweolf
scīra), Munster (siexe scīra) Connaught (fif scīra) and Uladstir (þrie scīr, ac
siexe Uladstires scīra sind Norðern Irland). Ælce scīr hæfþ "scīr geþinge". Þa
underrīciu nabbað ne onweald.

Þæt getæl and þa mæru þara gerec scirena þære Iriscan Cynewise wæron onwended
fram 1990. Difelinscīr wæs gebrocen in þrim: Dun Laoghaire-Rathdown, Fingal, and
Suþ Difelin - Difelin-ceaster wæs geo scirburgscipe. Ēac sōþlic is
gerec-"Tipperary Scīr" gedælede in twæm gerecþegnungum scirum, þa hatað Norþ
Tipperary and Suþ Tipperary. Þa miclu ceasterniscan stedas, Corc, Galwæg,
Limerice, and Weðerford sind scīrburgscipas, bedæled fram hierum scīrum. Forþæm
hæfþ seo Cynewise feower and þeortig scīrhad geþingu.

Naþylæs, þa siexe and tweontig scīra and hiere landgemæro wuniað be æwe [1]. Þas
scīra and underrīciu abidað in gemænige bryce, and scīrfæstnes is
geforþgestranged be stōwlice holdscipe and gamen.

Man broceð þæt word "scir" to awendenne þæt Cinisc word xiàn. In þære Folclican
Cynewīsum Cīnum, scira sind þæt stowlic gerecþgnung þing under þæm
ealdormanndome, se is under þæm underrice.

In þara landum þara Hanwara (oþþe "ealdum Cinan") sind 2,000 scira, þas habbaþ
abiden siððan þa Han Caserecynn (206 BC - AD 220). Seo scir is an þara ieldestan
onwealda in Cinan; þa underriciu wæron be þæm Yuan Caserecynn (1279 - 1368)
uparæred. Seo scir wæs hēahþegnung in caserelicum Cinan forþæm wæs hit se
stowlicosta onweald þæs caserelican wealdes, under an scirgerefan.

Þa scīra sind in 48 þara 50 rīce þāra Geāneda Rīca American landsceap oþþe
tōþegnung dālas fæst under þǣm rīce, and ofer þǣm burgscipe oþþe tunscipe.

Louisiana hæfþ þing gelic scīra ac hiere nama is parish (tūnsocn). Alaska is
bedæled in burgscipum.

Apskritis is þæt Liþuanisc word for scir. Siþþan 1994 hæfþ Liþuania 10 scira
(beforan 1950 wæron 20). Þære scire ānglide þegnung is scirgerefscipe. Se
scirgerefa is weard æ and gereces in þæm scire.

Sweoland hæfþ to cynn dæla; þæt landskap and þæt län. In þæm Niwan Engliscan
gereorde is hit geþeawe to awendienne landskap (se is on Englisce "landsceap")
swa province and län" swa county (se is scir) oððæt ðe län" is neor "híernes"
oððe "scipfylleþ". Finnland wæs dæl Sweorices oððæt 1815 and hæfþ þa ilcan
landmet, ac from 1634 to 1997

Þa landskap sindon eardfæst. Sweoland hæfþ 25 landskap. Hie nabbaþ ne
gerecþegnung bruc. Þa landskap sind in gemænige bryce, and sind þa landsceap
hwærto Sweonas habbaþ stowlicum holdscipe.

Þa län wæron uparæsed in 1634 in Sweolande and Finnlande. Sweoland hæfþ nu 21
län, ælc mid ealdormann and geþinge. In Finnlande wæron 12 lääni ac siððan 1997.
6 lääni (and siððan þæm geare Finnas awendað lään oððe län on Niwe Englisce swa
"region", se is "regio").



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/S%C5%AB%C3%BEsudan

Sūþsudan is a landfæst rīce on Ēasternum Affrice. His hēafodstōl is Juba. In
Sūþsudanes landum is þæt micel fenn Sudd be naman, þæt weorcþ sē Hwīta Nīl. Hē
is nīw rīce in Affrican, þe hiera selfdōm nōm fram Sudane on 9 Mǣdmōnþe, 2011.

Þis land hæfþ landgemæras wiþ Sudanwarum be norþen, Sigelhwarum be ēasten;
Cenie, Ugandan, and Congolande be sūðen and Middelaffrica be westen.

Ǣr was þis land dæl þæs landrīces Sudan þærofen wealdod Bretþeod and Ǣgyptware
ætgædre. Sudan þæt land weard his agan rīce in 1956, ac blōdig ingewinn folgode
Æfter þone Forma Sudaniscum Ingewinne, in 1972 wæs gestaðoled Sūþern Sudan
Selfwealdend Landrīce oð 1983. Oðer Sudanisc Ingewinn eftsōn begann and endede
in þæm Eallymbgyrdende Friþ Ānnes of 2005. In þæm ilcan geare Sūþern Sudanes
Leodweard staðold man. In leodceasnesse in þæm Æfterran Gēolan 2011, 99% þæs
landes manna ceas bedælunge of Sudanes lāfe. Sūþsudan weard frēorīce on 9
Mǣdmōnþe 2011.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/One_World_Trade_Center

One World Trade Center (ēac Freedom Tower oþþe 1 WTC gehāten) biþ nama þæs
hēafodboldes þæs nīwan World Trade Center-es be Nīweoforwīce þe be stede standeþ
þǣr twintorras þæs forman World Trade Center-es stōdon fore þǣm 11. Hāligmōnþes
þæs 2001. torngemōte. Se torr biþ gemearcod of hēahbytlere Daniel Libeskind.

Se torr wearþ gebylded be norþwesternum bȳge þǣre 16 æcera grēatan World Trade
Center stōwe. Torr hæfþ gehāle hīehþu ymbe þām 1776 fōta (ymbe 541 metera), þæt
swā tācn standeþ 1776. gēares þanne Geānedu Rīcu American hīe seolfa
unofhengelīcnesse nǣmon. Hīehþu be þæce biþ 417 meteras tō dragenne forþon þȳ
sēo gelīc biþ þǣre þæs forman World Trade Center-es. Be 27 Ēastermōnaðe 2006
wearþ þæt One World Trade Center ambihtlīce ongunnen mid fundrum þāra underdǣla
torres. Be Wēodmōnaðe 2012 wearþ timbor þæs torres geendod, and openungdæg sceal
stede findan be 1 Blōtmōnaðe 2013.

Wiþ þone torr cumað þǣr fīf ōþra torras: 7 World Trade Center (bē 2006 geendod),
200 Greenwich Street (2 torr), 175 Greenwich Street (3 torr), 150 Greenwich
Street (4 torr) and World Trade Center 5 Torr.

Wiþ One World Trade Center hine ēac findeþ Gemyndigunge Twintorra. Gemyndigung
biþ ‘Reflecting Absence’ gehāten and wæs ūtworpen of Michael Arad. Þæt bestendeþ
ūt sumum ‘pōle’ be undergrundlīcum flōrum þǣr mann ymbe 9/11 āþencenne binnan
mæg cuman. Þā pōl bā standað gerihte þǣr þā twēgen Twintorras stōdon. Be stede
þæs National September 11 Memorial & Museum-es hine ēac findeþ museum mid
belīfdǣlum þāra Twintorra (þǣrunder twā þāra dragendena þrītēþ-timborgeweorca
and geþing þe hwīlum gerȳmunge of Ground Zero wurdon gefunden).

Tō onginn sceolde torr Freedom Tower (Frēodōmtorr) gehāten. In Hæglmōnaðe 2009
gewǣre gesceōd Hæfenweald Nīweoforwīca and Nīwe Cēsarēa āgend þæt þone naman One
World Trade Center bet se torr meahte dragan mid þȳ þe hē mā geldberende biþ.
Þēos gesceādnes hæfþ fela geanword undergangen.

Þǣræfter þā twintorras fēollon þǣm grunde uppan be 11 Hāligmōnaþ 2001
torngemōtum wurdon fela gesprec ymbe tōweardnesse þǣre stōwe. Forestealla þā
ǣresta cwōmon, and be 2002. gēares geopenode Lower Manhattan Development
Corporation sum wiþstrīþ tō gesceādenne þȳ se stede gebrocen weorþe.

Folcgetācnung þæs ǣrestan ūtweorp-getemesedes (þæt “Primarly Design Concept”)
lǣdde tō sumum ōþran getemesede be Ǣrran-Gēolan þæs 2002. gēares (þæt
“Innovative Design Concept”). Þǣrūt wearþ sum ūtweorp of Daniel Libeskind
ūtcoren. Beforan þæt ūtweorp tō gode gecoren wurde, wearþ hit fela sīþ gesawen
forþon of mænigum unānignessum mid Larry Silverstein, āgend tō þǣm forman World
Trade Center-e.

Be 28 Ǣrran-Līðan þæs 2002. gēares wearþ sum ambihtlica geþynge gecoren æt þǣm
nīwan torre. Swāþæt se torr fulle geborgen weorþe swāswā āscode New York City
Police Department, wearþ be Ēastermōnaðe ān 57-meteras hēah betōnen fōt tō
geþynge gefēged. Swā andwyrde tō þām þe þōhton þæt se torr swā “betōnen buncer”
bewlātian meahte, biþ betōnen fōt þæs boldes mid glæse geclǣþed.

Þā ūtweorpendas þæs boldes bescrīfaþ 1 WTC swā “monoliþisc glæsen getimbor […]
geþeaht suma biliþhēawenena wanda.” Geāscod ymbe ende þǣra getimbra sægde L.
Silverstein: “Be 2012. gēares willað wē sumne fulle gebȳedan torr habban, hīera
and wundorfullra þanne hit ǣg wæs."

Torr wearþ be Wēodmōnaðe þæs 2012. gēares tō þæce geendod and be Þrīmilcemōnaðe
þæs 2013. gēares wæs wand fullbȳed.

Be 26 Ēastermōnaðe þæs 2006. gēares stealde Port Authority of New York and New
Jersey sum oncnāwlīca gefēg, þǣrmid se torr his geweorc ongunnen cūþe weorþan.
Sum ambihtlīce ānrǣdnes wearþ be þǣm folgiendan dæge geseted, and þā wæs 75an
gebyrddæg þæs Empire State Building his openungdæges.

Be 30 Ēastermōnaðe þæs 2012. gēares wearþ se torr hīehst bold be Nīweoforwīce,
ofergangende þæt Empire State Building be fēowum meterum, þēah næs se hīehst
torr be Norþamerican forþȳ þæt Willis Tower be Chicago (442 meteras hēah) giet
hīerra wæs. Þēos hīehþu is be Wīnmōnaðe þæs 2012. gēares oferscriðen geworden,
þǣrmid One World Trade Center hīehst gebolde be Norþamerican ēacswā is geworden.
Þā þā weorcere tōbecwōmon ongann þæt geweorc mid ambihtlīcum gescrife. Se torr
is gebiden be 2014. gēares gebrūcbǣr tō weorþenne.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kescwisc_spr%C7%A3ccynn

Þæt Kescwisce sprǣccynne (on Nīwum Englisce hāteþ Quechua, on Spēonisce quechua,
and on Kescwisce qheshwa oþþe runa simi, þe tācnaþ "sēo sprǣc þæs folces") is
sprǣccynn þætte mann spriceþ on Sūðamerican, on þǣm Andes. Hit hæfþ hūhwēga tīen
þūsenda þūsenda sprecenda, þēah þe hit is swīðe earfoþ tō witenne gewisslīce hū
fela sprecenda þǣr sind; and sind þǣr manige ānlīce on Bolifie, Perwe, and
Ecuadore, ac ēac on Argentinan, Cilan, Brasile, and Colombie.

Hit is þæt gesprecenoste sprǣccynn þāra inlendiscena Wīnlandes. Sōþlīce is hit
betere tō hātenne hit "sprǣccynn" þonne "sprǣc" for þȳ þe hit is swīðe missenlīc
betweox þǣm undersprǣcum. Oft ne cann mann þe spriceþ āne undersprǣce his
forstandan ōðerne mann þe spriceþ ōðre undersprǣce his. Þǣr sind þrēo
hēafodundersprǣccynn his: Norþkescwisc sprǣc, Midkescwisc sprǣc, and Sūþkescwish
sprǣc, þe hæfþ þæt mǣste rīm sprecenda eallra þāra undersprǣca. Þis sprǣccynn is
gecūþ tō "þǣre sprǣce þāra Incena", for þȳ þe hit heora hēafodsprǣc wæs.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fenberge

Fenbergan sind hlōþ þāra æfregrēna dweorga plantra oþþe wīn þæs cnōsles
Vaccinium undercnōsl Oxycoccus, oþþe hwīlum, in þǣm scēadum cnōsle Oxycoccus.
Man findeþ him in fennum þurh þā cōlan dǣlas þæs Norðernan Healftrydles.

Fenbergan sind unhēah, snīcende plantu oþþe wīn oþ 2m lang and 5 oþ 20cm hēah,
mid smælum stelum, and lȳtlum æfregrēnum lēafum. Þā blōsmas sind deorc rose, mid
swīðum scēadum bæcbēgendum blōsmalēafum, gecyðend þā dǣlas and ordend him
forþweard. Hāmlicu hunigbēo berendiaþ hīe. Sēo berge is falsu berge þe is miclor
þonne þā lēaf þǣre plante; hēo is ǣrest hwīt, ac wierþ dēop rēad hwonne ful
rīpe. Hēo is mete, mid sūrre byrgunge þe āhwylfeþ þā swētenesse mæg.

Fenbergan sind weorþlica cīepisca wyrte in sumum US and Canadianiscum
underrīcum. Man wyrcþ mǣste fenbergan intō warum swelce wōs, wōssop, and swēta
dryga fenbergan, mid þǣm oferēacum cīepende fræsce tō bygerum. Fenbergesop is
fæst mete Americanisces and Canadisces Þancasgiefendes, and Ēoropisc
winterfrēolstīde.

Siþþan þǣm ǣr 21 gēarhundrede innan þǣm woruldiscum brūcungefōdacēape, hit cȳðde
man ymbe fenberga nutrient innan and antioxidant sundorgecynd, giefende hīe
cēapisce byrdnesse æs "oferblōstm".



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fenber%C8%9De

Vaccinium undercnōsl Oxycoccus, oþþe hwīlum, in þǣm scēadum cnōsle Oxycoccus.

https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Campw%C4%ABg_be_Tannebeorge

Se Campwīg be Tannebeorge', oðre naman se Forma Campwīg be Tannebeorge wæs miclu
beadu gefeahten on 15 Mǣdmōnaþ in 1410, hwīlum se Polisc–Liþuanisc–Þēodisc
Gewinn in Prēosslande. Þone wælfeld agnede the alliance betwuh Polaland se
Cynerīce and Liþuanie se Hēahbregorīce, þara bregas wæron Władysław Jagiełło
Cyning and Witold Hēah Þēoden, and mid fultum of Bæmum, be Jan Sokol of Lamberk
and Jan Žižka, and hie decisively defeated þā Þēodiscan Cnihtas, þara here weas
gelæd be Ulrich von Jungingen þæm Hēam Dryhtne. Se mæsta dæl þæs Þēodiscan
Cnihta hēafodmanna wæron geslegen oððe genumen.

Æfter þære garmittinge fōr se sigefæsta here to Marienbyrig and seo burg
besettede. Hēr wiþstōden þa Þēodiscan Cnihtas þisse siege of their burgstealle
in and hie þoleden lytel loss of hierum landrīce æt þæm Þorn Friþ (1411).
Territorial disputes continued oð Melno Friþ in 1422. Næfre þæræfter eft gained
þā cnihtas hiera former power, and the financial burden of war reparations
caused internal conflicts and an economic downturn in their lands. Se campwīg
shifted the balance of power in Ēasternum Europan and betacnede þæs
Polisca–Liþuaniscan Gædes astignes þe he hæbbe dryhtscipe be wealde and here in
Europan norþēastdæle.

On Germanie is þes bilgesliht folces scamu and gemynd wiþ þā ēastlandena menn.
In 1914 þæn Germanie here gewonn sige ofer Russum on Ēastprēosslande, nemnede
Bismarck þone fēoht 'Campwīg be Tannebeorge' þe be þissum nīwan sige meaht man
eald scame adrifan.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C4%92adgar_%C3%86%C3%B0eling

Ēadgar Æþeling oþþe Ēadgar Cild wæs se endemesta wer þæs Westseaxna Cerdicinga
cynecynn. Þa Witan him tō cyninge geceoren, ac næfe fōn hē þæt cynehelm.

On Ungerlande wæs Ēadgar geboren. Hē wæs Ēadweardes Eardwreccaes ana sunu, ierfa
þæs Engla cynedōm, and wæs Ēadmundes II Cyninges ("Irensides") sunsunu.

Æt his fæder deaþ in 1057 wæs Ēadgar genamod ierfa be his fæderan Ēadweard
Cyning. Æt þæs cyninges dēaðe in Æfterran Gēolan 1066 wæs Ēadgar giet ofergeong
tō werienne þæt rīce, forþǣm þe him wæs gecyðd þæt Wyllelm bastard eorle of
Normandige wolde hider 7 þis land gewinnen. Þy Witenagemot cēos Harold
Godwinson, Ēadweardes Cyninges āðum, swa Harold II. Æfter Haroldes dēaðe æt
Hæstinga Bēadwe on Sæternesdæge 14 Winterfylleþes 1066 wæs Ēadgar tō cyninge
gecoren be Witenagemot in Lundene. Næfre wæs hē tō cyninge gehalod, and be niede
cwōm hē tō Willelme and swēor him aðas æt feowertiene oþþe fiftiene wintra
ielde.

Æfter his scortum cynedōme lifde Ēadgar Æþeling lang and full līf. Hē fōhtede in
þrim wiþfeohtum wiþ Frenciscum cyningum of Englalande. Hē þegnede for þǣm Casere
of Constantinopolis in þǣm Wæringa Weard æt Constantinopolis and wæs campealdor
þæs Caseres þrēates in þǣm Firstum Fare. Man sægþ þe hē forþfērde on 1126 on
Scottum.

Ēadgares fæder wæs Ēadweard Eardwrecca, ierfa þæs Engliscan cynedōm, and his
mōdor wæs Agatha. Ēadgares ieldrafæder wæs Ēadmund II þone hēt man Ēadmund
Irensīd. Ēadweard and Ēadgar Æþelingas cwōmon on Englas of Ungerlande in 1057,
ac in þǣm ilcan geare forþfērde Ēadweard. Ēadgar wæs afēded in Ēdweardes
Cyninges hired, mid his sweostrum, Margareta (seo wearþ Scotta Cwēn) and
Christina.

Willelm bastard gehiersomode eall Englalande on 1066. Willelm heold Ēadgar in
his griþe and brōhtede hine on his hired in Normandig. Nāþȳlǣs, þā Ēadwine and
Morkere Eorlas wigon wiþ Willelme in 1068, āfēgede Ēadgar hie and þa Willelm
sige hæfde fliemede Ēadgar on Mælcolmes III Scotta Cyninges gryþ. Þæt niehste
gēar married Ēadgares Melcolm sweoster Margaret, and geaf Ēadgare fulltum tō
sēcenne þone Engliscan cynedōm.

Ēadgar geþingode mid Swegne Dena Cyning (Cnutes Cyninges nefa (sē gelīefde þe hē
wæs Engla riht cyning). Ēadgares and Swegnes þrēatas inswēogon Englaland in 1069
and āfōn Eoferwic. Willelm cwōm on þone norþan, and āwēstede þæt land. Hē gieald
þa Dene tō āfeorsienne and Ēadgar flīemede eft on Scottas. Þa bād hē on wræcce
oþ 1072 þa Mælcolme Cyning be niede geþingode mid Willelme, and þǣrin sweor
Ēadgar Æþeling tō forewriītenne of Scotlande. Ēadgar macode tīmlīce his friþ mid
Willelme in 1074.

Æfter Willelmes I dēaðe in 1087 geaf Ēadgar fulltum tō Willelmes ieldsta sune
Rodbeart wiþ his ōðrum sune Willelm II (Willelm Rufus) in 1091 and eft be niede
flīemede on Scottas. On Scottum geaf hē fultum his swēostorsunan, Ēadgar, þe
meahte þone Scyttiscan cynedōm niman and þæs giengra Ēadgares fadera, Dyfenal
III Scotta Cyning, oferweorpan in 1097.

Stǣrwritere Sir Steven Runciman secgþ þe Ēadgar wæs on wræcce in
Constantinopolis siþþan 1098 and perhaps hē þegnede in þǣm Wæringa Weard under
Alexius I Constantinopolis Casere, þæt wæs in þissum ielde gefylled mid
Engliscum hūscarlum. In 1098 geaf Alexius I Casere him flēot tō bringenne
fulltume þǣm Forman Fare. Ēadgar brōhte fultum and heregeatu þǣm Casere æt
Antiochie on 4 Hrēþmōnaþ 1098.

Ēadgar cwōm on Europan mid Rodbeart Eorl and fōhtede mid Rodbeart æt Tenercebrai
in 1106 wiþ Heanrig I Engla Cyning. Ēadgar æþeling þe litle ær fram þǣm cynge tō
þǣm eorle wæs gefaren þǣr wæs ēac gefangen. Þǣræfter abēag hē tō his tūne on
Heortfordscire. Ēadgares sweostorbearn Ēadgyþ Mahalde wæs Heanriges Cyninges
cwēn.

Man ālīefþ þe Ēadgar fōr tō Scotlande late in his līfe (forþǣm þe hē wæs giet
cwic on Scottum in 1125 þa wæs Dauid I Scotta Cyning), ac hē forþfērde eftsōn þa
wæs hē æfter seofentieþ wintre.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/S%C3%BA%C3%BE_America

Sūðamerica (on Nīwenglisce: South America) is sē sūþerne worulddǣl American,
ligende fullicum in þæm Westerneum Healftrendele and mǣstlicum in þæm Sūþernum
Healftrendele, mid smælum dǣlum in Norþe. Hit is ymbhammen on west Sericus
Garsecge and on norþ and ēast Atlantiscan Garsecge; Norðamerica and sēo
Caribbean Sǣ ligeaþ tō norþwestum.

Sūðamerica habbaþ 17,840,000 km² lande, oþþe ælmǣst 3.5% of Eorðan fulne. Swā
fram 2005, his landware wæs telleþ æt māra þanne 371 millgeon. Sūðamerica is
fēorþa mid grīete (æfter Asia, Affrica, and Norðamerica) and fīfta mid landware
(æfter Asia, Affrica, Europe, and Norðamerica).

Sūðamerica is wel missenlic mid līfe of Eorðan worulddǣlum. Sūðamerica is hām
manigum ungelīcum dēorum swā llama, anaconda, piranha, jaguar, vicuna, and
tapir. Sē Amazon Regnweald hæfeþ micelne missenlicne mid līfe, mid micelum of
Eorðan cyndum. Rīcu in Sūðamerica ymbhabbaþ Andean Rīcu, Guianas, Sūþerne Cone,
and Brasil þæt is grēatest mid grīete and landware. * Fruma



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rutherford_B._Hayes

Rutherford B. Hayes (geboren þæs 4. Winterfylleðes þæs 1822. gēares; cwæl þæs
17. þæs Æfterran Iūlan þæs 1893. gēares) wæs se nigontēoða Foresittend þāra
Geāndena Rīca Wīnlandes, fram þǣm 1877. gēare ōþ þæt 1881. gēar. Þǣr hē
foresittend wæs bewiste hē þā Edstaðolunge þāra Geāndena Rīca onginn þǣre Ōðerre
Searucræfta Brǣdunge.

Hē wæs geboren on Delaware on Ohigwe, and hē worhte tō lāhwitan on Niðeran
Sanduscige. Hē alēt spēdigne stēormǣllicne weorcryne tō þēodenne hine wiþ þōne
Ānnesse Here. Hē wæs fīf mǣla gewundon, and þæs earnode hē naman bealdnesse of
campe; hē wæs gesett tō ealdorheretogan. Æfter þǣm campe þegnode hē on þǣm
Geānedrīciscan Gemōte fram þǣm 1865. gēare oþ þæt 1867. gēar tō Cynewīsiscum. Hē
afōr fram þǣm Gemōte tō sēcenne þæt ambeht þæs gȳmendes Ohigwes, and hē þæt dyde
twegen nēa tīman, fram þǣm 1868. gēare oþ þæt 1872. gēar. Siþþan his ōðer tīma
wæs geendod, ongann hē eft tō lāhwitan wyrcan, ac hē ongann eft stēormǣl tō
weorðenne gȳmend þriddan mǣles on þǣm 1876. gēare.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Merem%C3%A6gden

Meremægden is gelēaflic wæterwiht mid menniscum hēafde and bodige, and þǣm tægle
wæterdēores, swylce fisc. Þæt ƿord meremægden wearþ mermaid on Nīwum Englisce
gecweden. Se werlic efengemæcca is merewer, þēah man brȳceþ ēac þone wordcwide
meremægden for werlicum wihtum. Mænig land þǣre worulde gelīca wihta habbaþ,
gemǣne būtan clāðas.

Micel gelīc sirena, meremægdnu sungon tō lēodum and godum, and hīe besungon,
tōstregdende hīe fram hiera weorc, āfylaþ hīe of hiera scipum, oþþe hiera scipu
on grunde stīeran. In ōþrum lārum, hīe þringaþ sencende menn hwīlum fandiaþ hīe
tō sparienne. Man gelīefeþ ēac þæt meremægdnu bringaþ menn tō hiera
undermererīcum. In Hans Christian Andersenes Lȳtlum Meremægdne, man þynceþ hit
þæt meremægdnu forgietaþ þe menn underwæter āblāwan ne magon, hwīlum ōþra menn
gelīefaþ þæt meremægdnu menn āsencaþ forþǣm hiera wræðe.

Man þynceþ Grēcisc hǣðenscipes sirena hwīlum bēoþ in laterum folclāre
meremægdenlic; sum sprǣca brūcaþ þæt ælce word for begen bridd and fiscwihta,
swylce þæt Maltesisc word 'sirena.' Ōðer sibbcynna gelēaflicra wihta sind
wæterylfe and selkies, dēor þe fram sǣcūm intō mannum weorðaþ.

In Bryttiscum folclāre, man þenceþ hit þæt meremægdnu unspēdlica hwata wǣron -
begen forebodende misgelimp, and hīe wiðeriende. Mænig cynn þæs cwidegieddes Sir
Patrick Spens hæfþ meremægden mid þǣm dēaþwyrdodum scipum sprecende; in sumum,
hēo sægeþ þæt næfre sēoþ hīe land ongēan, and in ōþrum, hēo sægeþ þæt hīe nēah
stæþ bēoþ, ac hīe sind wīs genōg tō witenne þæt begen ælce bēoþ. Hīe magon ēac
tācn unwederes bēoþ.

Meremægdn magon ēac up īe swimman, tō færscwæterum lagum. On ānum dæge, in læge
nēah his hūs, Lornties Hlāford wīfmann sēah, and fandode hīe tō sparienne; his
þegn warnode þæt hēo meremægden wæs, and þæt meremægden begeal þe hēo hine
cwellan, gif ne forþǣm his þegn.

Meremægdnu magon ēac mā helpfulle bēon, sellende mannum gescēad hǣle. Sum tala
āsciaþ þā frignunge gif meremægdnu þurhlīfende sāwla hæfden. Man þynceþ hit ēac
þæt mereweras wildera and mā unfæger bēoþ þonne meremægdnu, ac ne reccaþ menn.

Þæt meremægden, oþþe syrenka, is Warsawes tācn. Man brēac meremægdenbiliðas on
Warsawes tācnscielde swā hiera tācn siþþan middlunge þæs 14ª gēarhundredes.
Mæniga gesegena tōefnaþ gelēaflic Triton mid þǣre byrig, þe mæg se fruma bēon
þæs meremægdnes geþēodes mid þǣre byrig.

Oninnan þǣm Nīwum Taíno þēodum þāra Caribbean īega, þæt meremægden Aycayia
hātte. Hire mearcunga sind gelīc þā gydenne Jagua, and þā hibiscus blōstm þæs
majaguabēam Hibiscus tiliaceus. Bisena ōðra sidaþinga beinniaþ þā Mami Wata of
Westum and Middlum Affrica, þā Jengu of Cameroon, sēo Merrow of Scotlande and
Īrlande, þā Rusalkas of Russlande and Ucrægne, þā Iara fram Brazil and þā
Grēcisc Oceanids, Nereids, and Naiads. Ān fræscwæter meremægdenlic wiht
Ēoropisces folclāre is Melusine, þe twegen fisctæglas hæfþ, ac ōðer fadunga
habbaþ hīe mid þǣm nǣdres niðerhealfe. Man þynceþ hit þæt in Iapane, etenne þone
ningyes flǣscmete unealdiende undēadlicnesse seleþ. In sumum Ēoropiscum
gesegenum meremægdnu bēoþ unspēdlic.

Meremægdnu sind cūþ for hiera rence, ac ēac for hiera unsceaþfulnesse. Hīe oft
lufiaþ menn, and swīðe willaþ hiera lufe for werum sōðian (sēo meremægdendeorf).
Mislimplīce, gewisse mid geongum meremægdnum, hīe oft forgīetaþ þe menn ne magon
underwæter āblāwan. Mereweras seldbeþencaþ ymbe mennisc gelimpas, ac in
Finniscum hǣðenscipe merefolc magon wysca bēodan, sēocnessa hǣlan, wyrgþa
forniman, wyrtdrincas brēowan and ēac mattuc beran. Meremægdnu ēac habbaþ sumra
þissa mearcunga.

Gerǣswoda gesihþa ymbe dēad oþþe līfende meremægdnu cwōm of stedum swylce swā
Java and Bryttiscum Columbian. Þǣr sind twā Canadisca cȳþþa of Vancouver and
Victorian, sum fram betweonan 1870 and 1890, and sēo ōþran fram 1967.

In Wēodmōnaðe 2009, Qiryat Yam þorp in Israele bēad $1,000,000 lēan for ǣnige þe
meremægdnu sōðian in hiera rimum, æfter mænigra twelfa lēode cūðdon meremægden
sēonende, hlēapende ūt þǣm wætere gelīc delfin and fremmende lyftsealta fore tō
þǣm dēopum eftgānde.

Of Dorothy Dinnersteines bēc Þæt Meremægden and se Werbula, mennisc-dēorisc
dōcas swylce þā werbula and meremægden bēoþ ealdmanna understandnes þæt menn and
dēor begen syndrig and ælce sind, and manna "mearcunga sind inweardlic unefen,
þe ūre þurhstandnes mid, and ūre sundornes fram, eorðan ōþrum dēordum tō mannum
rūnisc and dēop bēoþ; and of þissum þurhstandnessum, and þissum sundornessum,
habbaþ begen on eorðe fremdnes and mihtelicne þēaw tō þencenne hēr æt hām."

John William Waterhouse macode getæse biliþ fram 1895 oþ 1905, hātte Meremægden
(sēo þæt hēafod þisses gewrites). Late Bryttisc Academyes cynstweorcmōd, man
onwrāh þās mētinge mid gōdum dōme (þe him earnode þone Cynelices Academyes
geþēodscipe), ac intō sundorhorde tōfōr and ne oþ þā 1970a ne eftcwōm. Hit is nū
in Andrew Lloyd-Webberes sundorhorde.

Þæt mǣste welcūðe weorc nīwlic gēarhundredes is Hans Christian Andersenes
folcatalu Þæt Lȳtle Meremægden (1836), þe man ontō mænigum sprǣcum āwendode.
Andersenes tācnung, þe man fæst macode mid bræsene hēahgræfte in
Cēapmannahæfnhȳðe, wearþ sēo Westerne rihtbisen siþþan hēo wrīten wæs. Þæt
meremægden, swā Andersen gewrāt, mæg efne þurhstandende sāwle begīetan bȳ
beweddiende mann.

Þæt mǣste welcūðe glīwweorc ymbe meremægdnu sind þās of Felix Mendelssohn in his
Fair Melusina glīwsange and þā þrēo "Rīnisc dohtor" Richard Wagneres Der Ring
des Nibelungen. Lorelei, se nama ān þāra Rīnisc meremægda, wearþ tācnung
sirenes. Mā nīwlicu tācnung glīwes is Taiwanisc glīwwyrhta Fan-Long Ko's Þæt
Wēpende Meremægden.

Sue Monk Kidd gewrāt bōc gehāten Se Meremægdenstōl. Se nama cymþ of meremægdne
þe unwǣre sanctas wearþ.

Film ymbe meremægdnu beinnaþ 1984 lustfilm Splash, mid Daryl Hannah. Scēawung
1963 feorrsīenendebyrdnesse Route 66, Sēo Wælhrēoƿoste Sǣ hātte, wæs ymbe wǣre
meremægden þe in Weeki Wachee wæterperroce swanc. Man hæfde ēac meremægdnu in
þǣre gelēaflicum feorrsīenendebyrdnesse Charmed, and þonne þǣre
dohtorendebyrdnesse Mermaid. Tācniscu film beinniaþ Disneyes glīwisce fadunge
Andersenes tale, and Hayao Miyazakies Ponyo.

In herewealdscipe, þæt biliþ meremægdnes gemǣne camb and scēawere hæfþ, and cūþ
swā 'meremægden in hire īdelnesse' is. Man brēac Merefolc tō tācnienne
cræftignesse and fægernesse in sprǣce.

Scield- and sweordwieldende meremægden (Syrenka) is on þǣm wǣrum Warsawes
herewealdscield, sēo hēafodburg Polalandes. Sēo burg Norþfolc, Virginia ēac
brȳceþ meremægden swā hiera tācn, and byrgisc cynstweorc mid missenlicum
gefægrodum meremægdengræfte bēoþ geond þǣm burhstede. Sēo hēafodburh Hamilton,
Bermuda hæfþ þæt meremægden on hire herewealdscielde, þe man mæg geond þǣre
byrig gesēon.

Michaëlle Jeanes sundorherewealdscield, Canada's Governor General, hæfþ twegen
Simbi, meremægdenlicu wihta fram Haitisc Fūdū, swā bearwan.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indisc_r%C4%ABce

Indealandes grundgesetnes is secgeþ þe þæt rīce is rica gæd. Hit hæfþ eahta and
tweontig rīciu and seofon Gædes Landscipas. Þā rīciu and landscipas sind ælc
bedǣled on læppaum and swa forþ.

Dǣlas on Jammu and Cascmiere sind bīsæcu land forþæm Indea, Pacistan and Cīna
bespricaþ him and ælc land hæfþ weald ofer dǣl þæs ealdan Cascmier-rīces

Todæges Indie toþegnung dālas begunnon in þære Bryttiscum anwealde of Indie.
Bryttisc Indea heald ælmæst eall þæs landes on todæges Indeum, Pacistane, and
Bangladesce and hæfde seofontīene underrīciu, ūtan Afghanistane þæt gefriþode
rīce and Burman sēo landbūnes. Būtan Bryttiscum anweald ac in þæm Indiscum
Casererīce wæron forþgelangu rīciu under stōwlicum æþelingum. Mæst þissum dālas
abādon æfter selfdōm in 1947, ac Punjab and Bengal þā underrīciu twæmedon Indea
and Pacistan.

Æfter selfdōm unfriþ betwēonum mægþum arās and þȳ in 1956 wræsnede sē Indisce
Witangemōt þæt land be mægþa eardum.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez

Hugo Rafael Chávez Frías (man mihte on Englisce Hugo Ceafes secgan) (wæs geboren
þæs 28. dæges þæs Ǣrran Līðan þæs 1954. gēares; cwæl þæs 5. dæges Hlȳdan þæs
2013. gēares) wæs Foresitten Feneswelan fram þǣm 1999. gēare oþ his dēaþ on þǣm
5. dæge Hlȳdan þæs 2013. gēares. Hē wæs efnungrǣdlīc and worhte fela
efnungrǣdlīcra wendinga on his lande tō dǣle þæs efnungrǣdlīcan weorces þæs
Bolifariscan Ahebbunge, ēac þǣre wyrcunge nīwes staðolwrites, dǣlnimendlīcum
folcwealdgemōtum, þǣre rīcāgnunge missenlīcra hefigra tilunga, and ēacnunge þæs
gewealdes feohfultumes hǣlobegȳmunge, æfter þæs gewealdes getalum.

Þæs 30. dæges þæs Ǣrran Līðan þæs 2011. gēares sægde Chávez þe hē wolde drēogan
lǣcesnīðunge tō animenne bītes geswelles. Hē þurfte ōðerre lǣcesnīðunge þæs
Ǣrran Gēolan þæs 2012. gēares. Hē wolde dōn þæs foresittendes āðas on þǣm 10.
dæges þæs Æfterran Iūlan þæs 2013. gēares, ac þæt Rīcisce Gemōt Feneswelan
geþafode þe þā āðas bēon geildede tō lǣtenne hine getrumian and cyrran fram
þriddan lǣcecræftlīcre fōre tō Cuban. Hē cwæl þæs 5. dæges Hlȳdan þæs 2013.
gēares, 58 gēara ealdum.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/H%C4%93afodburg

On stēormǣle is hēafodstōl (ēac hēafodburg and hēafodburh hātte) sēo hēafodlice
burg oþþe tūn gesibb hire wealde. Hēo is nēan ā sēo burg þe līchāmlīce befēhþ
þæt setlærn and þæt gemōtærn þæs setles wealdes and is geseted be lage.

Þā setlu wealdes on mægenum underrīciscum dōmum sind gewunelīce hēafodstōlas
gehāten, ac æfter læssum wealdendum underdǣlum, word swelce fylces tūn, fylces
setl, oþþe byrig setl sind ēac gebrocen.

Þǣr sind maniga gelimpunga þǣr rīcu oþþe ōðre ānstandendas habbaþ manige
hēafodstōlas. On Sūþaffrican, tō bȳsne, se wealdenda hēafodstōl is Pretoria, se
lagsettenda hēafodstōl is Næsstūn, and se dēmenda hēafodstōl is Blōtsmanwelle,
þe is þæt gelimp þæs gesēmes þætte gesciepede þæt Sūþaffrican Gæd on 1910.

On swelcum gelimpungum is sēo burg þe hielt þone wealdenda hēafodstō gewunelīc
understanden wesan se "rīcisca hēafodstō" ongemang elemanna. Tō bȳsne, Santiago
is understanden wesan se hēafodstōl of Cilan þēah hire Gemōt is in Falparegse.

Tō hēafodlicum stede wealdes þæs landscipes oþþe rīces, se hēafodstōl
gecyndelīce atihteþ þā stēormǣllīce geānmētedum and him þāra cræftas sind
þorftene tō welwyrcendum wealde swelce ǣswutolas, tīdingwrīteras, and folclices
rǣdes cneordlǣcendas. Ieldre hēafodstōlas habbaþ ēac oft grōwen on fornytte
stēormǣllice, līfwīsisce, oþþe andgietfule stōlas. Swelc is hūru sēo gelimpung
Parises on Franclande and Buenos Airese Argentinan ongemang rīciscra
hēafodstōla, and Irkutskes oþþe Saltlagburge on Utā on heora landscipum.
Nāþȳslæs swelc hālgung mæg wesan wiðerwinnende. Sēo settung of Brasilie in
Brasiles inlande wæs gedōn be dǣl tō ēowienne þæs gewealdes gesundrodnesse fram
þǣm crodenan and gewemedan ealdan hēafodstōle Rio de Janeiro. Þæt geweald
Sūþcorēan gehēt on 2004 þæt hit wege his hēafodstōl fram Seoule tō
Geongi-Gongtscu — þēah þe þæt word "Seoul" self mǣnþ "hēafodstōl" in þǣre
Corēiscan sprǣce.

Sēo gæderung wealdlices and feohhweorfunglices oþþe līfweglices dōmes nis nānum
wīsum woruldwīde. Þēawlice hēafodstōlas magon feohhweorfunglīce aþēostrian fram
bifylclicum ofersteallum, swā swā hit gelamp mid Thēbane, þe aþēostrode fram
Alexandrie, Nantscing fram Scanghai, oþþe Edinburg fram Glasgowe. Þæt geafeall
cynecynnes oþþe līfweges cūðe ēacswā wyrcean þone dēaþ his hēafodstōles, swā swā
hit gelamp be Bablōnie and Cahocie. Ēac wǣron manige nīwlice hēafodstōlas,
swelce Abuja and Ottawa, rǣdlīce geseted onweg fram feohhweorfunglicum stōwum
and nabbaþ gīet weaxen grēate tō nīwum feohhweorfunglicum burgum.

Andefen þǣra ēacnunge nīwlicra cāserrīca and geþēodrīca, hēafodstōlas habbaþ
worden tācn for heora rīcum heora gewealdu,, and gesetede be gewealdlicum
andgiete. Ungelīce midealdum ceastrum, þe wǣron geset ǣghwǣr wealda hēold his
gemōt, is sēo cēosung, edsettung, staðoling, oþþe se onfeng nīwlices
hēafodstōkes carful gelimpung. Tō bȳsne:



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ge%C4%81nl%C7%A3hte_Cyner%C4%ABce

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce Grēatre Brytene and Norþīrlandes is cȳnerīce ofer norþenam
Europan. Man nemneþ hit sceortlīce Geānede Cynerīce oþþe UK (of Nīwum Englisce:
United Kingdom).

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce līþ on garsecges īeglandum be westnorðan Europan. His mǣste
īeg is Bryten (Nīwenglisc: Great Britain) and his oþru Īrland hwǣron licgaþ
siexe scīra þæs rīces. Eall ymbe þissum sǣrīman sind manigfealdum īege and
īegoþe.

Cynerīce is þæt Geānede Cynerīce, þærof is Elisabeþ II Cwēn. His hēafodstōl is
Westmynster (oþþe Lunden þærof is Westmynster nū dǣl). Sēo Cwēn hæfþ hiere stōl
hēr and hiere hām æt Windlesōran.

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce wearþ gescapen æfter syndrigum "Acts of Union", þæt habbaþ
þā sweotolan rīċu Englaland, Wēalas, Scotland, and Īrland geānlǣht under ān
rǣdena in Lundene. Mǣst þæs landes Īrlandes tōsyndrode of þǣm Geānlǣhtan
Cynerīce in 1922, and tōdæg is Īrland Cynewīse, ac se northēasterna dǣl þæs
īeglandes, Norðerne Īrland gehāten, gewunaþ in þǣm Geānedan Cynerīce.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Teutoburg_Weald_Beadu

Teutoburg Weald Beadu was fēoht þæs Rēmiscan Here wið Germaniscan mægþum under
Hermanne Cyninge. Hermann hæfde sige and seo fēoht endede þæs Rōmāniscan Rīces
willnunge to gehiersumenne Germanie.

In þæm geare 9 æfter Cristes cyme, sende Agustus Quintillus þone consul on
Germanie mid þrim legian. Ac hiora wearþ ælc ofslagon būton þæm consule ānum.
For þære dæde wearþ Agustus swa sarig þæt he oft unwitende slog mid his heafde
on þone wag, þonne he on his setle sæt, and þone consul he het ofslean.

In þæm geare 9 ærre Criste fōron Agustes Caseres legian ofer Rīne of Gallie and
gehiersumodon ealla mægþa betwuh Rīne and Ælfe. Rōmware wolde eall þæt land
weorþian nīw Rōmānisc underrīce Germania Magna.

Hermann (Lǣden: Arminius) wæs æþeling on þære mægþ sēo is on Lædene Cherusci ac
hwæs nama on hiera aganspræc ne wit man. He þeowede swa Rōmānisc fēða beforan þa
fōr he eft on Germanie.

In þæm gēare 9 brōhtede Uarus his þrie legian andlang weg dēop in wealde.
Hermann mid þæm Cherusci abrācon of þæm wude and hie onsæccedon.

In þæm geare 14 fōr Germanius Rēmisc æþeling on Germanie mid his legian and þā
lice afund. Þā Rēmiscan fēðan byrgedon þā licas þā legon hie.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nica_%C5%AAphebbung

Seo Nica Uphebbung (Crēacisc: Στάσις τοῦ Νίκα) wæs wuculang unfriþ in
Constantinopolis in þæm geare 532. Gram wǣron þæm dagas; seo gramste friþleasnes
þa hæfþ seo micle ceaster geseon and ælmæst healf þære byrig wæs be fyre oððe
sæcce adiglode and manige þūsanda menn wǣron geslēan. Þes ingerec blitt todæg ān
on Europan stære wierrstena.

Seo uphebbing hæfde his onginnung æt þære Hippodroman þǣr wǣron rǣs scridwægna
teamum. Þæt Rīce hæfde ealda scridwægnframscipas be namum Þa Reada, Þa Hwita, Þa
Grena and Þa Bleowa and mid ealcum framscipe wǣron his lufiendas. Þa Reada and
Þa Hwita næron folcmǣre ac folgendas Þara Grēnena and Þara Bleowena fylledon
eall Constantinipolis. Iustinianus I Casere wæs Þara Bleowan folgiend.

Iustinianus geaf him hira hēafdas and bad scridrǣs on 13 Æfter Gēol, ac Bleowena
and Grēnena lufiendas crafedon þe þa menn hæbben heale giefnesse for hiera
māndǣde.

On 13 Æfter Gēol 532 cwōm micel geþrang and hrēoh þære Hippodroman for þæm
ræssum. Hiera cirm wæs "Blēo" oððe "Grēne" oððæt hie ānlǣhtedon hiera stefnas to
Nίκα, se is "Sigor" and hie abrāc and onsæccedon þæs Caseres Heall, and for fīf
dagum wæs Caseresele besæt, and hwīlum feaht Blēo wið Grēne. Fȳr ongann in
manigum læppan and bærnet micel dæl þæs ceasterscipes and his fyrmeste cirice,
Halgan Sophie.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Manitoba

Manitoba is underrīce on Canadan. He is land þāra brādra wongan and ðærin wunaþ
1.2 þūsenda þūsenda manna.

Beēasten þissum land līþ Ontario þæt underrīce and bewesten him is Sascatcewan.
Benorðen sind þā Norþwesterne Landscipas in þæm gefrōrenum landum and þisses
underrīces sūþernum landgemæro is wiþ Norþdakotan and Minnesotan þāra Geānedra
Rīca American.

Manitoban hēafodstōl is Winnipeg and swylce burg is ēac his mǣste burg. Ðis
underrīce fōn his naman of Manitobamere se is micel mere onmiddan þæm land.

Manitoba weard underrīce onmang Canadan in 1870 and ǣrror belimpede þis land se
Hudsones Byht Gyld, se heald landriht, sōc and sac and se gyld nemnede his land
Rupertsland. In 1867 þingode Canadan lēodweard to scepenne underrīce in þissum
land ac for þissum þinge Metis folc begannen uphebbung wiþ þæm lēodweard and þes
sæc hāt sēo Rēad Ēa Uphebbung and þā swican ceas þone nama 'Manitoba' for hiera
cynewīse. Æfterweard wæs gesetnes þærof weard þis land underrīce in Canadan
geþoftscipe be naman Manitoba.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/M%C3%B3na%C3%BE

Se mōnaþ is ānhād oþþe stycce tīman, gebrȳced mid gerīmbōcum, þe is ābūtan swā
lang swā sum gebyrde fæc gelenge þǣm færelde þæs mōnan (þ.i. "mōna-þ"). The
traditional concept arose with the cycle of moon phases; such months are synodic
months and last ~29.53 days. From excavated tally sticks, researchers have
deduced that people counted days in relation to the Moon's phases as early as
the paleolithic age. Synodic months are still the basis of many calendars.

The motion of the Moon in its orbit is very complicated and its period is not
constant. Moreover, many cultures (most notably those using the Hebrew (Jewish)
and Islamic calendars) start a month with the first appearance of the thin
crescent of the new moon after sunset over the western horizon. The date and
time of this actual observation depends on the exact geographical longitude as
well as latitude, atmospheric conditions, the visual acuity of the observers,
etc. Therefore the beginning and lengths of months in these calendars can not be
accurately predicted. Most Jews currently follow a precalculated calendar, but
the Karaites rely on actual moon observations.

The actual period of the Moon's orbit as measured in a fixed frame of reference
is known as a sidereal month, because it is the time it takes the Moon to return
to the same position on the celestial sphere among the fixed stars (Latin:
sidus): about 27 1/3 days on average. This type of "month" has appeared among
cultures in the Middle East, India, and China in the following way: they divided
the sky in 28 lunar stations, characterized by asterisms (groups of stars), one
for each day that the Moon follows its track among the stars.

It is customary to specify positions of celestial bodies with respect to the
vernal equinox. Because of precession, this point moves back along the ecliptic.
Therefore it takes the Moon less time to return to the equinox than to the same
point amidst the fixed stars. This slightly shorter period is known as tropical
month; cf. the analogous tropical year of the Sun. This type of month is not
used much.

Like all orbits, the Moon's orbit is an ellipse rather than a circle. However,
the orientation (as well as the shape) of this orbit is not fixed. In
particular, the position of the extreme points (the line of the apsides: perigee
and apogee), makes a full circle in about nine years. It takes the Moon longer
to return to the same apsis because it moved ahead during one revolution. This
longer period is called anomalistic month, and has an average length of about 27
1/2 days. The apparent diameter of the Moon varies with this period, and
therefore this type of month has some relevance for the prediction of eclipses
(see saros), whose extent, duration, and appearance depend on the exact apparent
diameter of the Moon.

The orbit of the Moon lies in a plane that is tilted with respect to the plane
of the ecliptic: it has an inclination of about five degrees. The line of
intersection of these planes defines two points on the celestial sphere: the
ascending and descending node. The plane of the Moon's orbit precesses over a
full circle in about 18.6 years, so the nodes move backwards over the ecliptic
with the same period. Hence the time it takes the Moon to return to the same
node is again shorter than a sidereal month: this is called the draconic month,
which has an average length of about 27 1/5 days. It is important for predicting
eclipses: these take place when the Sun, Earth and Moon are on a line. Now (as
seen from the Earth) the Sun moves along the ecliptic, while the Moon moves
along its own orbit that is inclined on the ecliptic. The three bodies are only
on a line when the Moon is on the ecliptic, i.e. when it is in one of the nodes.
The "draconic" month refers to the mythological dragon that lives in the nodes
and regularly eats the Sun or Moon at an eclipse.

The cause of the moon phases is that from the Earth we see the part of the Moon
that is illuminated by the Sun from different angles as the Moon traverses its
orbit. So the appearance depends on the position of the Moon with respect to the
Sun (as seen from the Earth). Because the Earth orbits the Sun, it takes the
Moon extra time (after completing a sidereal month, i.e. a full circle) to catch
up and return to the same position with respect to the Sun. This longer period
is called synodic month (from Greek syn hodô, with the way, i.e. the Moon
travelling with the Sun). Because of the perturbations of the orbits of the
Earth and Moon, the actual time between lunations may range from about 29.27 to
about 29.83 days.

Here is a list of the average length of the various astronomical lunar months
[1]. These are not constant, so I provide a first-order (linear) approximation
of the secular change:

Nōt: time expressed in ephemeris time (more precisely Terrestrial Time) with
days of 86400 SI seconds. y is years since the epoch (2000), expressed in Julian
years of 365.25 days. Note that for calendrical calculations, one would probably
use days measured in the time scale of Universal Time, which follows the
somewhat unpredictable rotation of the Earth, and progressively accumulates a
difference with ephemeris time called Delta-T.

[1] Derived from the ELP2000-85; see: M.Chapront-Touzē, J. Chapront (1991):
"Lunar Tables and Programs from 4000 B.C. to A.D.8000". Willmann-Bell, Richmond
VA; ISBN 0-943396-33-6

This is useful for designing purely lunar calendars, where months of 29 and 30
days occur in some pattern that repeats after some number of months. A recently
invented pure lunar calendar called the Yerm Calendar [1] makes use of all of
the above approximations.

More importantly, in lunisolar calendars, an integral number of synodic months
is fitted into some integral number of years. The average length of the tropical
year divided by the average length of the synodic month, i.e. the number of
synodic months in a year, is (for epoch J2000):

One mnemonic for remembering the lengths of the months is to hold up your two
fists with the index knuckle of your left hand against the index knuckle of your
right hand. Then, starting with January from the little knuckle of your left
hand, count knuckle, space, knuckle, space through the months. A knuckle
represents a month of 31 days, and a space represents a short month.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jan_Mayen

Ian Magen is Norþmanna īeg in þæm īsgebuden garsecge. Fȳrbeorg gewrohten is þēos
īeg and hie belimpeþ þæs Norrena rīce.

Ian Magen is 34 mīla lang (of sūþwest oþ norþeast) and hiere stede is 144 mīla
be þæm feowerscīte. Micel dǣl is be īsflōd bewrog ymbe þæm Beerenbeorg, se is
his mǣsta hlǣw. Þēos īeg hæfþ twegen dālas: here norþēastdǣl, Nord-Jan be naman
(se is ("Norþ-Ian"), and hiere lǣssa dǣl, Sør-Jan (se is "Sūþ-Ian") þara hlenc
is landhals healf twā mīla lang.

Þēos īeg līþ 400 mīla be norþēastan Īslande, 300 mīla be ēastan Grēnelande and
600 mīla be westan Norþweges Norþnǣsse. Beorgfæst is þēos īeg and hiere hēasta
topp is on Beerenbeorg, se is fȳrbeorg in þæm norþdǣl, and stent 7,470 fēt ofer
þæm brime. Lūh hæfþ Ian Magen on þæm landhals; Sørlaguna (se is Sūþ Mere), and
Nordlaguna (se is Norþ Mere). Þridde mere is Ullerenglaguna be naman.

Ian Magen belimpeþ Norrena Rīce and his Gereca is Nordlandes Scīrgerēfa, oððæt
ðe micel ealdordōm ofer Ian Magne hæfþ se cyning gegifen þæm wichlāforde þæs
heriges on þære īege.

Ian Magen næfþ hȳð and manige scipu habbaþ in wræcce on þissum rīm geweard
gebrōcen. For lyftcræfte is ān feld mid ceoslen rynweg: eahta lyftcræfte comon
hēr oþ Bodø ælc gear.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Englisca_Ingewinn

Se Englisca Ingewinn wæs blōdig ingewinn on Englum hwærin feahton þæs Cyninges
awreðiendas wiþ þæs Witenagemōtes awreðiendum in series of armed conflicts and
political machinations of 1642 oð 1651.

Þes wæl wæs in twǣim dalum þa hett man þā Forma Englisca Ingewinn (1642 - 1645)
and þā Oþer Englisca Ingewinn (1648 – 1649) gefeahten betwuht þæm geþafum of
Carles II Greatbryten Cyninges and þæm geþafum þæs Langan Witenagemōtes. Ēac in
1651 wæs þisse gūðe endmesta þing, þæt wæs sigelēasu fyrding be Carl II se
endode in his defeat æt þære Wigorneceastre Beadwe on 3 Hāligmonaþ 1651.

<-- wæs sēo endebyrdness gūða and and wealdscipiscra searwa þā gelumpon betweoh
witenagemōtes awreðiendum and cyninges awreðiendum fram þǣm 1642. gēare þæt
1651., þæt is þæt forme ingefeoht (fram þǣm 1642. oþ þæt 1645.) and þæt ōðer
(fram þǣm 1648. gēare oþ þæt 1649.) betweoh þǣm awreðiendum Charles I and þǣm
awreðiendum þæs Langan Witenegemōtes, and þæt unspēdige onginn fram Charles II
þæs ende wæs his oferdrīfung on þǣre Gūðe Wiogoraceastre on þǣm 3. Hāligmonaþes
þæs 1651. gēares.

Se Ingewinn wæs inextricably mixed mid series of sǣc and ingewinn betweonum 1639
and 1651 and þissa dǣl in þæm þrim rīcum þā wæron Englaland, Scotland and
Īrland, þā wæron sundra rīciu mid ānum ānwealdan, Carl I, forþæm het man þās
gecnyttedan sacas þā Gewinnas þara þrēora Cynerīca oððe þā "Bryttiscan
Ingewinnas".

Æt þæs Oþres Engliscan Ingewinnes ende wæs se ordāl Carles Cyninges and þe man
him behēafde. His sunu Carl II wæs on wræcce gesended, and in stede þæs
Engliscan cynedōmes wæs sēo Engla Cynewīse (1649 - 1653) and Weardscipe
(1653–1659) under Olivres Cromwelles agnum weald. Sēo gesetnes þærbe ne mōt man
attend weorðscipe ūtan þære Angelcirican endode and nīw oncwedend þegnhād wæs
gestaþoled on Īrum. Þās þing gestaðoledon principal þe se cyning ne mōt rīcan
būtan þæs Witenagemōtes geþafunge.

Engle þoleden ingewinn in sundrigum yldum, ac ǣr þis wæron swylce unfriþ ymbe
hwā meahte ricsian. Se Englisca Ingewinn wæs for in hwelcum wīse meaht þæt rīce
be gericsoden, hwǣrfor secgð stǣrwriteras þe he wæs seo Englisce Onwendung and
on þæs Cyninges folgendum in þæm dagum wæs he se Micla Wiðersæc.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carl_I_Bretta_Cyning

Carl I (19 Blōtmōnaþ 1600 – 30 Æfterra Gēol 1649) wæs Engla, Scotta and Ira
Cyning oð 27 Hrēþmōnaþ 1625 oð ðe man hin behēafdod in 1649. Carls hæfde geflit
for miht mid his Witenagemōte, þær þe he wolde scop bēodan þær þe sohted se
Witenagemōt to bætenne his cynelican frumgife. Manige on his Engliscum
underþeodum wiþ opposed his dǣdum, and sundorlice þe he hrinede þā Cirice and
hsi levying of scop būtan þæs Witenagemōtes andwyrdinge and hērbe man aliefde þe
se cyning be his dǣdum weard swa swa tyrannisc sundoranweald.

Sæc ofer ǣwe hæfde þōlde Carl in eallum his cynedōm. Ǣfæst menn ne geliefed þone
cyning forþæm þe he ne geaf ne fremfull fulltum þæm Oncwedendum rīcum on þæm
Þreotig Gearena Gewinn, and he bewodded Rōmciricefæst cwēne, Henrietta Maria,
Frencisce æþle hlāfdige. Gefyrhto hæfde Carles underþeodnas ymbe þæs cyninges
æfæstnesse and ēac þær geaf Carl fyrþringnesse swylcum ciricemannum swa swa
Richard Montagu, and Willelm Laud, þone anstealde he on Cantawararbyrige
biscopstōle. On Englum aliefdon manige þe swylce þing brohtedon þā Angelcirice
too close to the Rēmiscan Cirice. Þæn Carl wolde be niede bringan Scottena
Cirice under biscopum and his agnum bysne agann se Biscopena Gewinn. Be swylcum
þingum wæron þā Engliscan and Scyttiscan Witenagemōtas elnoden and þæs cyninges
feall brohtede nearr.

Þurh Carles' endlice gearas wæs se Englisca Ingewinn, hwærin feaht se Cyning wiþ
þreatum þāra Engliscum and Scyttiscum Witenagemōtum. Carl wæs geahined in þæm
Ǣrrsta Ingewinn (1642–45), hwæræfter aliefod se Witenagemōt þe se Cyning wolde
ceosan grundgesetness gebunden cynedōm, Ac Carl sohted geþoftscipe mid
Treowmannum on Scottum and he fliemede to Wiht.

Þæs Cyninges fleam ongann þone Ōðru Ingewinn (1648–49) and oþru sigeleasnesse
for Carle. Man him fang and beheafde for swicdōme.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cannae_Beadu

Cannae Beadu wæs micel feoht þære Oðran Puniscan Gūþe, which took place on 2.
Wēodmōnaþe in þæm geare 216 beforan Crīstes acennesse nēah Cannae tūn se is in
Apulialande in þæm sūþēastdǣl Italie.

On þissum wælfelde hæfde Cartainan here under Hannibal micel sige ofer herigum
þære Romaniscan Cynewīsan oððæt ðe þā Rōmware wæron manigfealde and Hannibales
rincgetæl mismicel. Þærbe fremmede Hannibal mǣrþe and man hycgþ þe þæs dæges wæl
wæs ān þāra mæstena wigweorcena in eallum þe ealda bēc teallaþ of wigcræft. Þa
hycþ man þæs wælgetæl, hē wæs Rōmbyrig grimsta wighryre æfter Arausio Beadwe.

Rōmware brōhton nīw fyrd þæm felde æfter hiere hryre æt Trebia in 218 wintru
beforan Cristes tōcyme and æt Trasimene in þæm niehstan geare, and hie ceas to
bringenne Hannibal to garmittunge æt Cannae.

In Cannae cwom Rēmisc þrēat, mid gefylce þe wæs ymbe 86,000 menn, Rōmware and
geþoftas. Þā Rōmware sætted hiera heofigan feðan in dēoprum setnunge þon wæron
hie gewuna.

Æfter þisne wæl æt Cannae, Capua and manig mǣre burgrīce on Eotolwarum
forswicoden of þære Rōmcynewīsan and cleofod to Cartaine.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/W%C3%A6tertyge

Wætertyge, oþþe wætergelād, is wæterfruma oþþe līðendlicu wæterþēote getimbrod,
to ferienne wæter. In modern engineering, is þæt word gebrocen for ænigre
endebyrdunge þēotena, dīca, wæterwega, crēpla, oþþe ōðra getimbrunga þe man
brȳcþ þǣrtō. Nearulīcor limpþ wætertyge (seldan wæterbrycg) tō ǣnigre brycge
oþþe ǣnigum rādtyge, þe wigþ wæter - on stealle pæðes, rāde, oþþe
īsernsceaftweges - ofer dwolman. Grēate līðendlice wætertygas brȳcþ man swā
fērungbend, swā geþēodung, for bātas and scipu. Wætertyge sceal spannen
oferfērunga æt þǣre ilcan smēþnesse swā þā wæterwegas on ǣlcum ende. Þæt word
cymþ of þǣm engliscan wæter and tyge (cymþ of "tēon" on mǣnunge 'tō lǣdenne').

Þēah þe gegæderode mid þǣm Rōmānum, wǣron wætertygas swīðe ǣrran in Grēclande
and þǣm Nēam Ēastan and Indiscum underworulddǣle, þǣr folc swā þā Egipte and
Harappan ātimbrodon built manigfealda gewæterunge endebyrdunga. Rōmānlice
wætertygas wǣron gebrocen swā ǣr swā in þǣre 7an ielde BC, hwonne þā Assyrige
ātimbrodon 80 km lang līmestānenne wætertyge, þe hæfde 10 m hēane dǣl tō
oferfērenne 300 m wīd dæl, tō fērenne wæter tō hira hēafodbyrg, Nineveh.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/W%C3%A6terdraca

Wæterdraca is ænig cynd þæs cynnes Crocodylidae. Se wordcwide mæge ēac beinnie
eall þāra hāda Crocodilia: þā wǣre wæterdracan, þā ālagetere, cǣgmanas,
gārigelan, and ēac þā crocodylmorpha, þe ealdwæterdracacynn beinnaþ.

Gesīþcynd þæs cynnes Crocodylidae sind micel wæterlic wyrmas þe þurh wearmstedum
in Affrican wuniaþ, Asian, Norðum and Sūðum Wīnlande, and Āstrelian. Wæterdracan
mǣste gadriaþ in frescwæterstedum gelic ēan, laga, wǣtland, and hwīlum in
sāmsealtwætere. Hīe etaþ mǣste hrycgdēor gelic fiscas, wyrmas, and sycedēor, and
hwīlum unhrycgdēor gelic molluscas and rindcynn.

Hīe habbaþ eald frumcynn, and man belīefþ þæt hweorfodon hīe swīðe seld siþþan
dinosaura tīman. Man belīefþ þæt bēoþ hīe 200 þūsenda þūsend gēar eald, þēah
dinosauras wurdon dēad fore 65 þūsenda þūsend gēar; wæterdracan þolodon
grēatdēaða gelimpas.

Wæterdracan sind sæthuntas, ābīdende for fiscum oþþe landdēorum to cumenne nēah,
þonne ræsende to feallenne. Wesende caldblōdige huntas, hīe habbaþ swīðe slāw
bodigswiftnesse, and þus magon langum tīdum līfan būtan fōd. Hīe bēoþ
hēafodhuntas in hiera ēðelum, and seah man missenlice cynd feallende and
cwellende scearcas.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pulgara_Cyning

Pulgara Cyningas be missenlicum titlum ricsoden on Pulgarum of þæs rīces forma
staþle (se hēt man þæt Forma Pulgara Rīce) in 681 oð thame dæg þan ahweafen
Communistas þone cynedōm in 1946. In his ylde þolede þisne cynedōm twone tīdas
under elelendiscum oferhlāfordscipe: healf ōðre hund geara unde þæm
Constantinipolis Rīce and ælmæst fīf hundred wintra þæs Oþomaniscan Rīces. Early
Pulgarisca rīcan hycgð man benyttedon þone naman Khan, later knyaz for scortum
tīde, and æfterwearde tsar.

Tsar seo titul (se is of þæm Wendiscum spræce þæs Læden wordes Caesar (se is
cāsere), and Pulgare nām þis word for hiera bregum for Simeon I, æfter his mæran
sige ofer þæm Constantinopolis Rīce in 913. Eall Simeones æftergengan nyttedon
þās title oð Pulgrara rīces feall þæm Turciscum Bregum in 1396.

Æfter þe þā Pulgare abrācon of þæm Turcum in 1878, cēas hiera forma cyning
Alexander I þe his titul biþ knyaz, ac his cynedōm næs sundorrīce in Turcena
ēagum oþ 1908 and on þæm dæge abannede Ferdinand Alexandres sunu þe he biþ Tsar,
se is 'Cyning'. Se nama tsar abād under Ferdinande his ierfum Boris III and
Simeon II.

Oððæt ðe tsar was onwendode "cāsere" in þæm Forma and Ōðrum Pulgara Rīcum
Empires, in þissum ylde hæfþ man onwended þæt word "cyning".

In þara fēam alibbendum Middelyldra Pulgariscum cynelicum bōcum, healdon
Pulgarena Cyningas mid langum titlum tobysene "In Criste se Wealdende se Trēowe
Cāsere and Autocrat of Eallra Pulgara" oððe gelicum þingum, and oft ēac "... and
Rōmwara, Crēaca, or Vlacha".

This list does not include the mythical Bulgar rulers and the rulers of Old
Great Bulgaria listed in the Nominalia of the Bulgarian khans as well as
unsuccessful claimants to the throne who are not generally listed among the
Bulgarian monarchs.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norrena_Cyning

Norrena cyningas beginað hiera getǣl in 872 in swylcum geare hæfde Harold
Fægrehar sige æt Hafrsfjord, hwǣrof wæs he cyning ofer eallum Norþwege – se
ærrsta cyning mid swylcum miclum rīce. Haroldes fæder rīce wæs Westfeald on
Osloflēotes westhealfe, ac Haroldes cynedōm wæs of þæm flēote oð þæm westsǣ and
oð Orcanege. Haroldes cynecynn, þæt Fægrehar Hūs, endode in his spearhealfe
æfter Haroldes sunsunan dēaþ, se wæs Harold II, in 970, ac Norrena cyningas oð
1387 nam þæt ilce hūs naman.

Ūtan wig wiþ Dēna cyningas in þæm 10. and 11. gearhundum wæs Norþweg sundorrīce
oð þæm 14. gearhund. In 1387, Norþweg and Swēoland wrohtedon ānnesse mid
Denemearce and Norþweges cynehelmes ierfe wæs Christian I Dēna Cyning in 1450.
Æfter þissum cyningas þæs setlas wæron æt in Ceapmannahæfne wæron Norþweges
cyningas oð 1814.

Norþmenn sohtedon sundorrīcehād eft in 1814 and ceason Christian Friþerice, Dēna
Æþeling to bēon cyning, ac Carl XIII Swēona Cyning onswōg þæt land forþæm þe hit
wæs his riht be friþgewrite and he weard Norrena cyning be naman Carl II. In
1905, beendod þās ānnese and Norþweg siððan 1905 hæfþ Norþweg his aga cyning, of
þæm Dēnisc cynecynn in þæs Sillende-Holstān-Sonderburg-Glücksburg Hūs.

In geardagum wæron Norrena cyningas be titul on Norðisc Konge til Norge Todæg
secgþ man Norges Konge, se is "Norþweges Cyning".



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nemniendlic_c%C4%81sus

Se nemniendlica cāsus (Nīwe Englisc: nominative case) is grammatisc cāsus for
namum. Sume wrīteras on Nīwum Englisce brūcaþ ēac þæt word subjective cāsus for
nemniendlicne, in order to draw attention to the differences between the
"standard" generic nominative and the way it is used in nīwum Englisce.

Se nemniendlica mearcaþ, generally, þā forþsetennesse sumes wordes. Nemniendlice
cāsas sind gefundene in Lǣden and Ealdum Englisce, ongemang ōðrum sprǣcum.
Englisc hæfþ gīet sume nemniendlice bīnaman, efenāmeten mid þǣm wregendlicum
cāse oþþ gebīegdum cāse: ic (wregendlic mec), wē (wregendlic ūsic), hē
(wregendlic hine), hēo (wregendlic hīe) and gē (accusative ēowic). On Englisce
habbaþ wē ēac þū, se ōðeres hāda bīnama (wregendlic þec) and manigfealdlic gē
(wregendlic ēowic). Syndriglīce spricþ man þāra bīnamena wit (wregendlic uncit)
and git (wregendlic incit), hwonne man spricþ ymbe twēgen menn.

se nemniendlica cāsus is þæt gewunelice, cynde ansīen (more technically, the
least marked) of certain dǣlas, such as nouns, adjectives, pronouns and less
frequently numerals and participles, and sometimes does not indicate any special
relationship with other parts of speech. Therefore, in some languages the
nominative case is unmarked, þæt is, the nominative word is the base form or
stem, with no flexion. Moreover, in most languages with a nominative case, the
nominative form is the one used to cite a word, to list it as a dictionary
entry, asf.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/N%C4%ABwe_Englisc

Sēo Nīwenglisce sprǣc (on Nīwenglisce: English) is Westgermanisc sprǣc, þe on
Englalande ārās. Hēo belimpeþ, swā sēo Þēodisce sprǣc and sēo Niðerlendisce
sprǣc tō þǣm Westernan twige þāra Germaniscra sprǣca.

Nū is Englisc sēo brādoste gesprǣdede sprǣc þǣre worulde, and hæfþ ymbe þæt
getæl sprecera þe Cīnisc hæfþ. In fela landum biþ Nīwenglisc sēo ǣreste fremðe
sprǣc gelǣred (Sēo Englisc (Scōl)) and is sēo ambihtlice sprǣc þāra mǣstena
betwixfolclicra gesetednessa. Fela þissa gesetednessa habbaþ ōðra ambihtlica
sprǣca. Nīwenglisc prōfaþ hēodæg swā woruldsprǣc.

Tōdæg biþ Englisc fram 340 millionena sprecenda swā mōdorsprǣc gesprecen. Gif
man īeceþ þā æfterran sprecend, cymþ man tō ymbe 510 millionena sprecenda.

Englisc cymþ of þǣre Ealdre Seaxiscre sprǣce and sibbum þēowsprǣcum þe wǣron
gebrōht tō Brytene fram Germaniscum gesittendum of syndrigum dǣlum norþwestes
Þēodisclandes. Sēo frume Englisce sprǣc wæs gehrinen folgiendlīce fram twǣm ȳðum
onrǣses. Se ǣresta onrǣs wæs fram sprecerum sprǣca Scedelendisces twiges þæs
Germaniscan sprǣchīredes, þe gebȳrdon in dǣlas Brytene in þǣm 8an and 9an
ieldum. Se ōðer onrǣs wæs mid Normandigsǣtum in þǣre 11an ielde, þe cynn
sprǣcon, Ealdes Frencisces.

Be þǣm Engliscan-Seaxiscan Cranice, ymbe þæt gēar 449, wǣron þā Engle gelaðode
fram Wyrtgeorne tō helpenne him wiþ þā Pihtas. Ongēan hira help gelendode hē þǣm
Englum in sūþēastum dǣle. Æfter sōhte hē māran help, and forþǣm cōmon þā Seaxe,
Engle, and Geate. Se Cranic spricþ ymbe fylgendne incyme gesittendra, þe
staðelodon on ende seofon cynerīcu. Tōdæges scōlerscipe behogeþ mǣst þisses
spelles tō bēonne spell and fram lēodweardrace gedōne.

Þās Germaniscan infarend oferrīcsodon þā fruman Celtisce sprǣcendan wuniend, þā
sprǣca þāra ālifdon mǣste on Scotland, Wealas, Cornweall, and Īrland. Þā
folcsprǣca, gesprecena fram þǣm ingengum, macodon þæt, þe man hēt Eald Englisc,
þe efenlǣcþ suma rimanþēowsprǣca, in (nū) landum norþwestes Þēodisclandes and
þāra Niðerlanda. Ufor wæs sēo sprǣc gehrinen fram þǣre Norþgermaniscre sprǣce
Norene, þǣra Wīcinga gesprecen, þe on þone norþēastan dǣl gesǣtton (sēo
Georfic).

For þǣm folgiendum 300 gēarum æfter þǣre Norþmandiscan Geþringunge in 1066
sprǣcon þā Norþmandiscan cyningas and sēo hēa duguþ cynn Frencisces āne. Micel
getæl Norþmandiscra worda wǣron inbrōht in Eald Englisc. Se Norþmandisca gehrine
gefæstnode þā gangendan hwierfunge þǣre sprǣce ofer fylgendum ieldum, oþ þǣre
sprǣce, nū Middelenglisc gehāten. Lareowas þǣre tunges lare ne laerdon;
leorneres heora spraec ne leornode. For þon þe þæt folc þāra Norþmanna þeowas
ȝeƿurdon, swa ealswa mot mon þæt 'Niwenglisc' beter 'þeowenglisc' ȝehatan.

In þǣre 15an ielde gewende sēo Micele Selfswēgendwendung þæt Middelenglisc, ēac
mid Lundencyndre sprǣce in lēodwearde and tōþegnunge, and þǣre
regolunggefremmunge gemǣlunge. Nīwenglisc cann gespyred bēon on bæc tō þǣre tīde
Willelmes Shakespeares.

Sēo Nīwenglisce sprǣc is dǣl þæs westernan undertwiges þæs Germaniscan twiges
þæs Indiscan-Europiscan sprǣca cynnes. Feorr þǣra Englisclǣhtan sprǣca swā Tok
Pisin oþþe Bislama, sind þā nīehstan Nīwenglisces Scyttisc (Lallans), mǣste on
Scotland and dǣl Norðernes Īrlandes gesprecen, and þǣræfter Fresisc, on
Þēodiscland and on þǣm Niðerlandum gesprecen. Swā Nīwenglisc is Scyttisc riht
æftergenga Englisces (Englisc-Seaxisc).

Ōðra sibba sprǣca, ac unsibbran þonne Fresisc oþþe Scyttisc, sind Þēodisc,
Seaxisc, Niðerlendisc, Scedelendisca sprǣca, and Afrikaanisc. Manig Frencisc
word sind ēac andgietfullicu tō Nīwenglisces sprecende (ac mid ōðrum
rihtstefne), for þǣm þe Nīwenglisc bedranc ormǣtlic rīm worda fram Frencisce
þurh þā Norþmandisce sprǣce æfter þǣre Norþmandiscan Oferswīðrunge and rihtlīce
of Frencisce in æfterrum ieldum; þǣrfor sind fela worda swīðe nēah þǣm
Frencisce, mid smalum wrītungscēadungum (on wordendungum oþþe mid Ealdes
Frencisces wrītungum, asf.), ēac swā hwīlum scēadunga on mǣnunge.

Englisc grammaticcræft hafaþ lȳtele gebīegunge in efenlǣcnesse mid ōðrum
Indoeuropicum sprǣcum. Tō bisene hæfþ Nīwenglisc, ungelīc Þēodisce,
Niðerlendisce, oþþe Rōmāniscum sprǣcum nān grammatisc cynn and nāne
tōgeīecendlice ānrǣdnesse. cāsu mearcung is æthwōn fullīce gedwinen of þǣre
sprǣce and ālifþ mǣste on þā bīnaman. Þā cynn strangra worda (t.b.
sprecan/spræc/sprǣcon/gesprecen) wiþ þā cynn wācra worda þe sēo sprǣc of
Germanisce ierfde is on weorðe gedwinen and þā lāfa gebīegunge (swā
manigfealdlicu mearcung) wurdon regolfæsta.

Þā seolfan tīd þǣre gebīegunge weorþgedwīnung in Englisce, scōp sēo sprǣc māran
getrēowunge in wīsan swā mōdword and worddiht tō getācnienne grammatisce
mǣnunge. Helpendu word brȳcþ man tō mearcienne tācnu swā frignunga, negativa, þā
underþēodendlican stefn, and gengende tīd

Mid Englisce brȳcþ man þā lǣdene stæfrǣwe būtan accentum, ac mid elþēodigum
wordum, swā résumé (Frencisc) cann man mid accentum wrītan. Mid manigum wordum,
swā night oþþe though is sēo wrītungwīse stǣrlicu (nā sprecendllicu), for þǣm þe
on Middelenglisce wrāt man night and though. Sēo wrītung worda oft ābȳgþ of hū
hīe gesprecen sind, and Nīwenglisc wrītung is oft geþōht sēo unēaðoste ǣnigra
sprǣca tō leornienne, in þǣm sprǣcum þe brūcaþ stæfrǣwa. Sēo Nīwenglisc
rihtwrītunge.

Englisc is ambihtsprǣc in þǣm fylgendum landum, þǣrin þæt getæl þāra
mōdorsprecera is gewriten, hwǣr cūþ:

Englisce sprǣc þegnaþ tō ēacan swā lingua franca in þǣm folgiendum landum and
landscipum:



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/M%C7%A3s

Sēo Mǣs (Niðerlandisce Maas) is Europisc hēafod ēa, rising in Francland and
flowing through Belgice and the Niðerland before draining into Norþsǣ. Hēo hæfþ
hāle lengþe 925 km (575 mīlena).

The Meuse rises on the Langres Plateau in France from where it flows northwards
past Sedan (the head of navigation) and Charleville-Mézières into Belgium. At
Namur it is joined by the River Sambre. Beyond Namur the Meuse winds eastwards,
skirting the Ardennes, and passes Liège before turning north. The river then
forms part of the Belgian-Dutch border, except that at Maastricht the border
lies further to the west. In the Netherlands it continues northwards past Venlo,
then turns towards the west, merging with the Rhine into an extensive delta
before finally flowing into the North Sea via the Nieuwe Waterweg and the
Hollands Diep. The river divides near Heusden into the Afgedamde Maas on the
right and the Bergse Maas on the left.

The Meuse is crossed by railway bridges between the following stations (on the
left and right banks respectively):



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iane_Grey_Hl%C3%A6fdige

Iane Grey (1536 oþþe 1537 – 12 Solmōnaþ 1554) wæs ansprecestre þāra Engliscan
and Īriscan Cynedoma. Hēo rīcsode ofer Englaland on nigon dagas in 1553, and þus
is oft cūþ swā Sēo Nigon Daga Cwēn, oþþe lēas gemǣne swā Sēo Cwēne Þritīene
Daga, forþǣm þā tōdǣlnessa ymbe þæt onginn hire mǣrsung rīcsonesse. Stǣrmenn
oncnāwaþ oþþe hire mǣrsungdæg swā Cwēn (10 Mǣdmōnþe), oþþe se ǣrmannes dēaþ (6
Mǣdmōnþe), swā þæt onginn.

Maria, Heanriges VIII iedsta dōhtor anām þone cyndōm of Iane þær hēo cwōm on
Lunden and Iane behēafded on 12 Solmōnaþ 1554.

Man cūþ Iane Hlǣfdige swā ān þāra wīsostra frēona hire tīman, and stǣrwritere
Alison Weir cwæþ þæt wæs hēo ān þāra "grēatostra wīfgemynda þæs gēarhundredes."
Sum menn reccaþ hīe swā Englalandes fyrmest Oferwealdende Cwēn.

Iane, ieldesta dohtor Heanrices Greyes and his wīfes, Frances Brandon Hlæfdige,
wæs æt Brādgeat Perrac geboren, in Lægreceastrescīre. Ǣror þancas wǣron þæt hēo
ymbe Winterfylleþ 1537 geboren wæs, ac sum menn nū gelīefaþ þæt hēo ǣror geboren
wæs, on uncūðum tīman in oþþe ieldum 1536 oþþe ǣror 1537.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ian_Magen

Ian Magen is Norþmanna īeg in þæm īsgebuden garsecge. Fȳrbeorg gewrohten is þēos
īeg and hie belimpeþ þæs Norrena rīce.

Ian Magen is 34 mīla lang (of sūþwest oþ norþeast) and hiere stede is 144 mīla
be þæm feowerscīte. Micel dǣl is be īsflōd bewrog ymbe þæm Beerenbeorg, se is
his mǣsta hlǣw. Þēos īeg hæfþ twegen dālas: here norþēastdǣl, Nord-Jan be naman
(se is ("Norþ-Ian"), and hiere lǣssa dǣl, Sør-Jan (se is "Sūþ-Ian") þara hlenc
is landhals healf twā mīla lang.

Þēos īeg līþ 400 mīla be norþēastan Īslande, 300 mīla be ēastan Grēnelande and
600 mīla be westan Norþweges Norþnǣsse. Beorgfæst is þēos īeg and hiere hēasta
topp is on Beerenbeorg, se is fȳrbeorg in þæm norþdǣl, and stent 7,470 fēt ofer
þæm brime. Lūh hæfþ Ian Magen on þæm landhals; Sørlaguna (se is Sūþ Mere), and
Nordlaguna (se is Norþ Mere). Þridde mere is Ullerenglaguna be naman.

Ian Magen belimpeþ Norrena Rīce and his Gereca is Nordlandes Scīrgerēfa, oððæt
ðe micel ealdordōm ofer Ian Magne hæfþ se cyning gegifen þæm wichlāforde þæs
heriges on þære īege.

Ian Magen næfþ hȳð and manige scipu habbaþ in wræcce on þissum rīm geweard
gebrōcen. For lyftcræfte is ān feld mid ceoslen rynweg: eahta lyftcræfte comon
hēr oþ Bodø ælc gear.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cham

Cham (חָם, Regollic Hebrēisc Ḥam, Tiberisc Hebrēisc Ḥām, Ḫām, Ge'ez Kam), be
þǣre Cynnreccnessa Cnēorisbōce, wæs sunu Noes and se fæder Chuses, Mizraimes,
Phutes, and Chananes. David Rohl gecnǣwþ þās þēode swā þā Pēne þæs Punt.

Þēawlīce is gecēpt þæt Cham wæs ān þāra suna Noes, þe tēah sūþwest intō Affrica
and dǣlas þæs nēan Middlan Ēastes, and wæs se forefæder þāra þēoda þǣr. Sēo
Biblioþēce belimpþ tō Egyptan swā "þæt land Chames" in (Saltere 78:51;
105:23,27; 106:22; 1Ch 4:40). Þǣt Hebrēisce word for Egyptan wæs Mizraim (gewēne
bōclīce mǣnþ þā tū land), and wæs se nama ānes suna Chames. Þæt Egiptisce word
for Egyptan wæs Khem, þe fægerlīce wæs se fruma þæs naman Cham, oþþe þurh
sōnhwierfune betwēonan sprǣcum. Þā naman Chames ōðra cildra efenlǣcaþ þā dǣlas
wiþinnan Egyptan rīcscunge - Kush, Chanan, and Phut.

Be Cnēorisbēc 9:20–25, ongann Noe tō tilienne wīnberian æfter þǣm flōde, and
druncnode sume dæge. Þā hwīle þe hē druncen wæs, læg hē þā limnacod in his
telde. Cham seah his fæder limnacodne, and cȳþde his brōðrum Seme and Iafethe
þǣrymbe. Sem and Iafeth ēodon in þæt teld mid hira andwlītan in bewrigenum, and
hine þeahton. Hwonne Noe wōc, wiste hē hwæt him belamp, and wiergde Chanan, sunu
Chames, tō bēone þā þēowas Semes and Iafethes.[1]



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C7%B7%C4%93odm%C5%8Dna%C3%BE

Wēodmōnaþ is se eahtoða mōnaþ þæs gēares in þǣre Gregoriscan gerīmbēc, and hæfþ
31 dagas. In nīwum Englisce, brȳcþ man þæt word August, and man nemnode hine tō
þances Augustes Cāseres. Se mōnaþ hæfþ 31 dagas for þǣm þe Augustus wolde swā
fela daga swā Iulies Cāseres Iulii. Agustus settede þæt nama mōnþes hēr forþȳ
Cleopatra cwēn Ǣgyptes aswealt in þissum mōnþe. Ǣror nemnedon þā Rōmaware þone
mōnaþ Sextilis in Bōclædene, for þǣm þe hit wæs se sixta mōnaþ in þǣm Romiscum
gēare, þe ongann in Hreþmōnþe.

In Īrlande, (in þǣm Īriscan sprǣc) is Wēodmōnaþ cūþ swā Lūnasa, swā menn nū
secgaþ þone Īriscan naman Lughnasadh, þe is genemned for þǣm gode Lugh. Se forma
dæȝ Wēodmōnþes hātte in þǣm Īriscum gēare (Lā Lūnasa) and in þǣre Īriscan
gerīmbēc is hē nū giet geþōht swā se ǣresta dæg hærfestes. Se forma Mōnandæg in
Wēodmōnþe is ān þāra Þēodlican Symbeldaga in þǣre Cynewīsan Īrlandes.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/W%C4%ABnlendisc_cystel

Wīnlendisc Cystel (Castanea dentata) is micel bēam þæs bēcan cynnes, þe þēodisc
Norðamerican is. Fore þone cystel blæc, hēo wæs ān þāra mǣste weorþlica
wudulanda bēama hire eardes. Þǣr sind nū feawe eald trēowu þisses cyndes, būton
hwǣr man hīe in unblæclicum eardum stealde.

Wīnlendlisc Cystel is swīfte weaxende sumorgrēne heardwudu bēam, þe oþ 100–150
fēt (30–45 m) micel and 10 fēt (3 m) brad wiext, and eardaþ fram Maine and
sūðernum Ontario tō Mississippi, and fram þǣm Atlantiscum waroðe tō þǣm
Appalaceanum Beorgum and Ohio Dene.

Þǣr sind mænig gesibbcynn cystela, beinnende þā Europisc Swētan Cystele, Cīnisc
Cystele, and þā Iapanisc Cystele. Hire lārcræftig nama, Castanea dentata, cymþ
of þǣm tōþum hire hlēafa, þe 5–8 yncas lang (14–20 cm) and 3–4 yncas brad (7–10
cm) sind. Þās sind lēohtlic scortor and brador þonna þe fram þǣm Swētum Cystele.
Sēo wiþblæclice Cīnisc Cystel nū biþ sēo mǣste folclice cystel þe man in þǣm
G.R. stelþ. Þā cystela bēoþ in þǣm bēcum cynne, mid bēce and ǣc, ac ne sind
gesibbod tō þǣre hors cystele, þe in þǣm cynne Sapindaceae is.

Sēo Wīnlendisc Cystel is grēatu berestre hnyta, mid þrēo hnutum in ǣlcum
scēaðgum burre. Þā hnyte weaxaþ þurh þǣre læstum healfe sumores, þā burras
ōpenende and tō þǣm grunde feallende nēah þone fyrst fylforst.

Sēo Wīnlendisc Cystel wæs swīðe weorþlic bēam for wildlīfe, giefende fela fōda
tō Hwīttægl Dēore and Wild Tyrcig. Sweart Beras cūðdon tō etenne þā hnyte for
oferwintera.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/T%C3%ADwesd%C3%A6g

Tīwesdæg is þǣre wuce dæg betwēonan Mōnandæge and Wēdnesdæge. Se Englisca nama
cymþ of þǣm Þēodisc gode Tīwe. And in Romam hit hātte Martis dies, þe is se dæg
þæs Romiscan gūðgodes Mars.

Gescrifen Tīwesdæg foregǣþ þone forman dæg Lenctenes in þǣre Crīstenan gerīmbēc.
And on Frencisce hātte hē Mardi Gras, þe segþ fæt Tīwesdæg, for þǣm þe on þǣm
dæge gēo man ǣt ealle ealde fōd þe wæs in hēddærnum and man ne miht gehabban hit
lengra, and in sumum landum þis wearþ symbel gehāten Carnival, þe in Bōclædene
wæs carni vale. And Lencten þus hǣtte for þǣm þe þonne in norðernum landum þā
dagas wurdon lengran. And gēo in Brytene in lenctene wæs wana fōdores in lande,
and giet nū in Brytene lēactūnweardas hātaþ þās mōnþas þā hungrigan ginnesse.

Tīwesdæg is se wunelica dæg for cystum in þǣm Geānlǣhtan Underrīcum. Þēodlice
cystas (þæt is Federale cystas) gelimpaþ on þǣm Tīwesdæge æfter þǣm forman
Mōnandæge in Blōtmōnþe; þēos tælmearc wearþ gesetted be lage þæs gēares 1845 for
foresittendlicum cystum (sundorlīge for þǣm cyre þæs Cystlican Colleges), and
wearþ gebrǣded tō cystum for þǣm Hūse Spelienda in 1875 and for þǣm Senate in
1914. Tīwesdæg wæs se ǣresta dæg þǣre wuce, þe cystum onhagode in þǣm fruman
19an gēarhundrede: burgmenn sceolden faran ǣnne hālne dæg tō macienne hira cyst,
and nolden faran on Sunnandæge, þe wæs weorðungum dæg for þǣm grīetestan dǣle
hira. Manig Americisc underrīcu habbaþ hira foresittendlican frumcystas on
"Super Tīwesdæge".

Blæc Tīwesdæg, in þǣm Geānlǣhtan Underrīcum, is se 29a dæg Winterfylleþes geares
1929, þonne ongann sēo grēata ege-geflyht þǣre gedǣlungcēapstōwe geares 1929.
Þes wæs se Tīwesdæg æfter Blacum Þunresdæge, þonne ongann sēo Grēata
Niðersincung.

In þǣre Grēciscan worulde, wierþ Tīwesdæg (se dæg þǣre wuce þæs Fealles
Constantinoplan) gecweden unspēdigne dæg. Se selfa is sōþ in þǣre
Spēonisc-sprecendan worulde, hwǣr bīword sægþ En martes, ni te cases ni te
embarques (On Tīwesdæge, ne sinhīwie ne onginne fare).



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Orosius

Paulus Orosius (c. 375 - c. 418) wæs crīsten stǣrwrītere, dryhtweorþ wrītere,
wita and Scte. Augustines lǣringmann. He wæs of Hispanie, wēnunga fram Bracara
Augusta. He lifde and wrāt æt þǣm ende þæs Rōmāniscan Ricum.

Orosius is cūþost for his bēc Historiarum Adversum Paganos Libri VII ("Seofen
Stærbēc wið þā Hǣðnas"), þa wrāt he ongēan þone gelēafan on folce þe þæs
Rōmāniscan Rīces amolsnung wæs þȳ hit hæfde onfangen Cristendōm.

Siþþan Orosius wearþ prēost, aspyrede hē þā Priscillianistas on Spēnum. Þā ēode
hē tō Scte Augustine æt Hippo in Norþaffrice in þǣm 413. gēare oððe þǣm 414.
Siþþan hē hæfde abiden sume þrāge in Affrice tō Augustines leornungcnihte, wæs
Orosius in þǣm 415. gēare of Augustine gesended tō Palestine mid pistole him tō
gecȳðenne Orosius tō Ierome, se wunede in Bethleheme. His ǣrend wæs þe Orosius
meahte habban mā lāre from Ierome on ymb þā wēna þāra Priscillianista and
Origenista. Nōþylæs, man segeð þe in sōþe wæs his bisgo fullǣst for Ierome and
ōþrum wið Pelagie, se, fram þǣm Cartaina synoðe in þǣm 411. gēare, wunede in
Palestine and þǣr fand frīend.

Æfter Orosies tōcyme, wæs oferstǣled Iohannes Biscop of Ierusaleme, to abannenne
synoð in þǣm Ǣrran Līðan þæs 415. Æt þissum synoðe getealde Orosius Cartaine
rǣdnessa and he rēd missenlice Augustines writunge wiþ Pelagie. Mære ascode
Pelagius Et quis est mihi Augustinus? ("Hwa me is Augustine?"). Sige nadde
Orosius on Crēcum, þa ne understōd Orosies Læden. Orosius gewonne Iohannes
biscopes word to sendenne pistolas and menn to þæm biscope of Rombyrige beforan
cwōm he ongean to Affrice

Historiarum Adversum Paganos ("Stær wiþ þæm Hæþnum") wrāt Orosius æt Augustines
scīenesse. Orosius cwēþ þe seo middangeard hæfþ weaxen tīlor siððan Cristendōmes
tōcyme. For andworde to þæm menn þa lociað to þisse ielde wēum, cwēþ he fram
ærdada wēum, þa cwōm beforan Cristendōme þa wæron rihte wiersa. Þeos bōc work,
an woruld-stær on þæm wēum þa habbaþ befeallan manncynn fram Adame oð ymbe 417,
wæs seo ærrest woruld-stærbōc swa stær of Godes hand swa manncynnes weard.
Eftsōn wæs seo bōc frēamære. Ælmæst twegen hundred biwriten bēc sind in
bōchordum ofer þære worulde.

Bono Giamboni awendede þæm boc in þæm Eotoliscan gereorde. Awendung þæs 14th
gearhundredes in þæm Aragoniscan gereorde, be Domingo de García Martín, wæs
gewyrhte fram Bono Giambonis Eotoliscan awendung. Historiarum Adversum Paganos
wæs in Arabisc awendede in Speonlande under al-Hakam II, Caliph of Cordoban.

Ælfred cyning wyrhte abridged, freo awendung þæs Stær wiþ þæm Hæþnum. Ælfredes
Orosius ne holdeþ fæst to Orosies ærest text; hit bringeþ manige þing to
Ælfredes dæge.

Seo bōc beginneþ mid biliþ þære worulde; "Hu ure ieldran ealne þisne middangeard
on þreo todældon". Ac seo woruld awended micle betweonum Orosies dæg and
Ælfredes and hēr towriteþ Ælfred þære landa Europes in his gearum, and on þæm
landum and folcum middangeardes. Ēac hæfþ seo bōc Wulfstanes talu in his færelde
to þæm Ostsæ to Denemearce, Norþwege, Sweolande and Estlande, and Ōhtheres talu
in his færelde ofer norþ to Beormalande.

Þæræfter folgieð Ælfredes cyninges bōc Orosies stær on þæm Engliscum gereorde,
fram Ninie Asiria cyninge and fram Sodome and Gomorre to Alerices cyninges dæge
in Italie.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ni%C3%B0erlendisc

Sēo Niðerlendisce sprǣc (Nīwenglisce: Dutch, Niðerlendisce: Nederlands) is
Westgermanisc sprǣc, þē fram Niðerlande ārās. Hēo is sēo eahta-and-fēowertigoðe
mǣste gelōmlice "ǣreste sprǣc", and hit hæfþ 23 millionan folces in 2007.
Gelōmlice is þæt cynn Niðerlandiscre sprǣce, þe is on Belgican gesprecen, þēo is
Flemisc gehāten. In Norþeastum dǣle þæs landes biþ sēo Niðerseaxisce sprǣc
gesprecen, Achterhoeks, Drents, Stellingwerfs, Twents and Gronings.

Þā mǣstan Niðerlendiscan word cumað of þǣre Ealdan Germaniscan sprǣce. Sum cumað
of Lǣdene and Crēacisce and fēawa of Nīwenglisce and Frencisce. Þæt word schip
cymð of seolfre orsprunge swā Englisc scip.

Eald niðerlendisc byð sēo ylce sprǣc swa sēo niðere Franconisc hātte (eastern
and western). Lange se niðerlendisc þōhton hira ieldeste writing wǣre:

Nū hycgeþ man þa þes cȳma cwide bēo eald Centisc and nis þæs ealdan
niðerlendiscan gereordes. Ac þenden sind gifundan oðre cwidas (on Hloðwices
rihtbēc be naman Lege Salica). Se ieldest byð:

Þēah eac sīe mihtelīce þæt ieldest niðerlendiscne bēon þās rún-stæfas læs
lēoðlican under-neoþan:



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/N%C4%ABwu_Englisc_spr%C7%A3c

Sēo Nīwenglisce sprǣc (on Nīwenglisce: English) is Westgermanisc sprǣc, þe on
Englalande ārās. Hēo belimpeþ, swā sēo Þēodisce sprǣc and sēo Niðerlendisce
sprǣc tō þǣm Westernan twige þāra Germaniscra sprǣca.

Nū is Englisc sēo brādoste gesprǣdede sprǣc þǣre worulde, and hæfþ ymbe þæt
getæl sprecera þe Cīnisc hæfþ. In fela landum biþ Nīwenglisc sēo ǣreste fremðe
sprǣc gelǣred (Sēo Englisc (Scōl)) and is sēo ambihtlice sprǣc þāra mǣstena
betwixfolclicra gesetednessa. Fela þissa gesetednessa habbaþ ōðra ambihtlica
sprǣca. Nīwenglisc prōfaþ hēodæg swā woruldsprǣc.

Tōdæg biþ Englisc fram 340 millionena sprecenda swā mōdorsprǣc gesprecen. Gif
man īeceþ þā æfterran sprecend, cymþ man tō ymbe 510 millionena sprecenda.

Englisc cymþ of þǣre Ealdre Seaxiscre sprǣce and sibbum þēowsprǣcum þe wǣron
gebrōht tō Brytene fram Germaniscum gesittendum of syndrigum dǣlum norþwestes
Þēodisclandes. Sēo frume Englisce sprǣc wæs gehrinen folgiendlīce fram twǣm ȳðum
onrǣses. Se ǣresta onrǣs wæs fram sprecerum sprǣca Scedelendisces twiges þæs
Germaniscan sprǣchīredes, þe gebȳrdon in dǣlas Brytene in þǣm 8an and 9an
ieldum. Se ōðer onrǣs wæs mid Normandigsǣtum in þǣre 11an ielde, þe cynn
sprǣcon, Ealdes Frencisces.

Be þǣm Engliscan-Seaxiscan Cranice, ymbe þæt gēar 449, wǣron þā Engle gelaðode
fram Wyrtgeorne tō helpenne him wiþ þā Pihtas. Ongēan hira help gelendode hē þǣm
Englum in sūþēastum dǣle. Æfter sōhte hē māran help, and forþǣm cōmon þā Seaxe,
Engle, and Geate. Se Cranic spricþ ymbe fylgendne incyme gesittendra, þe
staðelodon on ende seofon cynerīcu. Tōdæges scōlerscipe behogeþ mǣst þisses
spelles tō bēonne spell and fram lēodweardrace gedōne.

Þās Germaniscan infarend oferrīcsodon þā fruman Celtisce sprǣcendan wuniend, þā
sprǣca þāra ālifdon mǣste on Scotland, Wealas, Cornweall, and Īrland. Þā
