folcsprǣca, gesprecena fram þǣm ingengum, macodon þæt, þe man hēt Eald Englisc,
þe efenlǣcþ suma rimanþēowsprǣca, in (nū) landum norþwestes Þēodisclandes and
þāra Niðerlanda. Ufor wæs sēo sprǣc gehrinen fram þǣre Norþgermaniscre sprǣce
Norene, þǣra Wīcinga gesprecen, þe on þone norþēastan dǣl gesǣtton (sēo
Georfic).

For þǣm folgiendum 300 gēarum æfter þǣre Norþmandiscan Geþringunge in 1066
sprǣcon þā Norþmandiscan cyningas and sēo hēa duguþ cynn Frencisces āne. Micel
getæl Norþmandiscra worda wǣron inbrōht in Eald Englisc. Se Norþmandisca gehrine
gefæstnode þā gangendan hwierfunge þǣre sprǣce ofer fylgendum ieldum, oþ þǣre
sprǣce, nū Middelenglisc gehāten. Lareowas þǣre tunges lare ne laerdon;
leorneres heora spraec ne leornode. For þon þe þæt folc þāra Norþmanna þeowas
ȝeƿurdon, swa ealswa mot mon þæt 'Niwenglisc' beter 'þeowenglisc' ȝehatan.

In þǣre 15an ielde gewende sēo Micele Selfswēgendwendung þæt Middelenglisc, ēac
mid Lundencyndre sprǣce in lēodwearde and tōþegnunge, and þǣre
regolunggefremmunge gemǣlunge. Nīwenglisc cann gespyred bēon on bæc tō þǣre tīde
Willelmes Shakespeares.

Sēo Nīwenglisce sprǣc is dǣl þæs westernan undertwiges þæs Germaniscan twiges
þæs Indiscan-Europiscan sprǣca cynnes. Feorr þǣra Englisclǣhtan sprǣca swā Tok
Pisin oþþe Bislama, sind þā nīehstan Nīwenglisces Scyttisc (Lallans), mǣste on
Scotland and dǣl Norðernes Īrlandes gesprecen, and þǣræfter Fresisc, on
Þēodiscland and on þǣm Niðerlandum gesprecen. Swā Nīwenglisc is Scyttisc riht
æftergenga Englisces (Englisc-Seaxisc).

Ōðra sibba sprǣca, ac unsibbran þonne Fresisc oþþe Scyttisc, sind Þēodisc,
Seaxisc, Niðerlendisc, Scedelendisca sprǣca, and Afrikaanisc. Manig Frencisc
word sind ēac andgietfullicu tō Nīwenglisces sprecende (ac mid ōðrum
rihtstefne), for þǣm þe Nīwenglisc bedranc ormǣtlic rīm worda fram Frencisce
þurh þā Norþmandisce sprǣce æfter þǣre Norþmandiscan Oferswīðrunge and rihtlīce
of Frencisce in æfterrum ieldum; þǣrfor sind fela worda swīðe nēah þǣm
Frencisce, mid smalum wrītungscēadungum (on wordendungum oþþe mid Ealdes
Frencisces wrītungum, asf.), ēac swā hwīlum scēadunga on mǣnunge.

Englisc grammaticcræft hafaþ lȳtele gebīegunge in efenlǣcnesse mid ōðrum
Indoeuropicum sprǣcum. Tō bisene hæfþ Nīwenglisc, ungelīc Þēodisce,
Niðerlendisce, oþþe Rōmāniscum sprǣcum nān grammatisc cynn and nāne
tōgeīecendlice ānrǣdnesse. cāsu mearcung is æthwōn fullīce gedwinen of þǣre
sprǣce and ālifþ mǣste on þā bīnaman. Þā cynn strangra worda (t.b.
sprecan/spræc/sprǣcon/gesprecen) wiþ þā cynn wācra worda þe sēo sprǣc of
Germanisce ierfde is on weorðe gedwinen and þā lāfa gebīegunge (swā
manigfealdlicu mearcung) wurdon regolfæsta.

Þā seolfan tīd þǣre gebīegunge weorþgedwīnung in Englisce, scōp sēo sprǣc māran
getrēowunge in wīsan swā mōdword and worddiht tō getācnienne grammatisce
mǣnunge. Helpendu word brȳcþ man tō mearcienne tācnu swā frignunga, negativa, þā
underþēodendlican stefn, and gengende tīd

Mid Englisce brȳcþ man þā lǣdene stæfrǣwe būtan accentum, ac mid elþēodigum
wordum, swā résumé (Frencisc) cann man mid accentum wrītan. Mid manigum wordum,
swā night oþþe though is sēo wrītungwīse stǣrlicu (nā sprecendllicu), for þǣm þe
on Middelenglisce wrāt man night and though. Sēo wrītung worda oft ābȳgþ of hū
hīe gesprecen sind, and Nīwenglisc wrītung is oft geþōht sēo unēaðoste ǣnigra
sprǣca tō leornienne, in þǣm sprǣcum þe brūcaþ stæfrǣwa. Sēo Nīwenglisc
rihtwrītunge.

Englisc is ambihtsprǣc in þǣm fylgendum landum, þǣrin þæt getæl þāra
mōdorsprecera is gewriten, hwǣr cūþ:

Englisce sprǣc þegnaþ tō ēacan swā lingua franca in þǣm folgiendum landum and
landscipum:



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Manama

Manama (Arabisc: المنامة Al-Manāmah) is hēafodstōl Baraines and līþ be þǣm
Persisc Gulf, in ēastnorðe Bahrain Īege. Hit is mǣst stede Bahraines mid folcrīm
ymbe 150,000, fēorðlung þǣm full folcrīm Bahraines.

Islamisc cranicas namiaþ Manamane at least as far back as 1345. Hit þā
Portugliscmenn brǣcon in 1521 and æfter be þā Persiscmenn in 1602. Fram 1783 se
hīred Al-Khalifa habbaþ hit gehealden and gewealden, mid sceortum
underbrecungum. Man hēt Manaman swā frēohæfene in 1958, and in 1971 hit wearþ
hēafodstōl selfwealdendes Baraines.

The economical base for Manama is identical to Barain as a whole - petroleum,
oil refining, dhow building, fiscaþ and meregrot dyfung. Manama is served by
Barain International Flyhthæfen on þǣm īeglande Al Muharraq, to which it is
connected with a causeway. Manama ēac is ham for þone University of Barain,
which man āstealde in 1986.

Al Manamah was also one of the twelve municipalities of Barain, and it is now in
the Capital Governorate.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jacques-Yves_Cousteau

Jacques-Yves Cousteau wæs geboren on 11um Sēremōnþes, 1910 in Saint André de
Cubzac in Franclande and forþfērde on 25um Sēremōnþes, 1997 in Parise. Hē wæs
Frencisc sciptoga and explorer and researcher. Hē leornode þā sǣ and ealle þe
lifdon in wætre. Man cnǣwþ Cousteau in Franclande mǣste swā le commandant
Cousteau (Bebēodere Cousteau). Man sægþ his naman swā Cū·stō.

Man ālīefede hine in þǣm Ēcole Navale (Scipfierdlic Scōlu) in Breste. He wearþ
scēotunggerēfa þǣre Frenciscan Scipfierde, and þurh þis cwōm tō him byre ǣreste
cunnian under wætre. In 1936 he cunnode cynn underwæterlicra glasa, and mæg bēon
þæt of þissum cwōmon dȳfera ēagegriman.

In 1937 wīfode hē Simone Melchior. Hē fōhte in þǣre Ōðeran Woruldgūðe swā
dyrnscēawere for þǣre Frenciscan dyrnfierde, and þenden man fōhte hē fand tīd
for þǣm hē and Emile Gagnan macodon þæt forme cynnes ābiddungǣðmendra
lyftǣðmungsearwa, þe is se aqualung, in 1943, and of þissum cwōm mǣst þǣre
dȳfunge mid scuban in þǣre worulde. Hē sōhte gōd lyftǣðmungsearwu æfter þæt
twuwa mid oxygenongēanǣðmungsearwe hē hæfde oxygenfyllewærcas and geswogunge.

Æfter þǣre Ōðeran Woruldgūðe þenden hē wæs giet scipfyrde sciptoga, hē macode
weorcwegas tō findenne ūtberstendas in Franclandes hȳðum and swēawode in
gesuncenum scipum.

Man nemnede hine foresittend þāra Frenciscra Farunga tō Scēawianne þā Sǣwa. In
1950 he bōhte his mǣre scip Calypso, and in him hē fōr tō manigum sǣm and tō
sumum ēam. In þissum farungum he macode manige bēc and āstyriende gelīcnesse. Hē
gewann þrēo þæs myrcenses Oscar for þǣm āstyriendan gelīcnessum The Silent
World, The Golden Fish, World Without Sun, and manige ōðre hēam myrcelsas and in
þissum wǣron se Palme d'Or in 1956 æt þǣm Cannes Film Festival. Þurh his
geweorce þǣre worulde folc geleornode micel ymb underwæterlicre libbendcyþþe.

In 1963 Cousteau and Jean de Wouters searwodon þone underwæterlican
leohtātīefrend genemnedan "Calypso-Phot", and æfterra hē alīefede Nikon macian
hit and hit wearþ se "Calypso-Nikkor" and æfter se "Nikonos". ǣ Hē and Jean
Mollard macodon þone SP-350, þe is twǣm mannum undersǣbāt þe cūðe dȳfan 350
metras under sǣ. Spēow þissum, and in 1965 hē dȳfede tō 500m mid twǣm
undersǣbātum.

Man sette Cousteau swā stihtere þæs Sǣcræftlican Stǣrhēddærnes Monacos, and
Cousteau scōp þæt Undersǣs Þurhsmēagunggefēre in Toulone, wæs se lǣdere þæs
Conshelf Saturation Dive Program (long-term immersion experiments, the first
manned undersea colonies) and was one of the few foreigners that has been
admitted to the American Academy of Sciences.

Cousteau wearþ mǣrora. In Winterfylleðe 1960 EURATOM wolde āweorpan in sǣ
micelne radioactiviscne þreax. Cousteau organized a publicity campaign which
gained wide popular support. Wīfa and cildru sǣton on þǣm īrenwege and
forstoppodon þone gewægnoþ, and man þorfte senden þone þreax tō þǣm stede þanon
hit cwōm, and þæt plēo endode.

In þǣm æfterran Blōtmōnaðe Charles de Gaulle Francrīces foresittend ēode to
Monaco and þǣr wordum wrixlode ymb þæt þe gelamp on Winterfylleðe geares 1960
and wīdorlīce ymb cyrncræftlīe cunnungum.

Ǣrra Francrīces ambaht segde þæt betere wǣre gif Rainier æðeling ne sprece ymb
þis, ac man segde þæt se foresittend frēondlīce āscode Cousteau to be kind
toward nuclear researchers, and Cousteau (allegedly) replied: "No sir, it is
your researchers that ought to be kind toward us." During this discussion
Cousteau found out that the reason for French experiments and research was
American refusal to share its atomic secrets with its allies.

In 1974 he ongann þone Cousteau Society for the Protection of Ocean Life, and in
þissum nū sind māran þonne 300,000.

In 1977 man geaf him and Peter Scott þæt sigetācn gehāten "UN international
environment prize", and fēawe gēaru ǣfterra Jimmy Carter Foresittend geaf him
þone American Liberty Medal.

In 1992 inlāðode man hine tō Rio de Janeiro, Brazil for the United Nations'
international conference on environment and development, then he became a
regular consultant the UN and the World Bank.

Cousteau nemnode georne hine "oceanographic technician". He was in reality a
sophisticated lover of nature, especially that of the sea. His work allowed
people of all continents tō visit life under the ocean's surface and explore
through television the resources of the "blue continent".

The works that Cousteau produced also created a new kind of scientific
communication that caused some criticism by formal academics. The so-called
divulgationisme, a simple comprehensible form of sharing scientific concepts,
was soon used for other disciplines too and became one of the most important and
appreciated characteristics of modern TV broadcasting. The documentary
information found in Cousteau's words a linear scheme to follow.

Jacques Cousteau forþfērde on 25um Sēremōnþes 1997 and man byrgede hine in
Cousteau cynnes byrgenlande in Saint-André-de-Cubzac lictūne in Franclande.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hw%C4%ABt_Draca

Geoffrey of Monmūðe ƿrāt ymbe þone "Hƿītan Dracan" in þā "Ealdan Forebodunga
Merlines" and Historia Regum Brittaniae. Þēos mǣleþ ymbe beadu betƿeonan Rēadum
Dracan and Hƿītum Dracan. Monmūþ mǣnþ þæt se Rēada biþ for þǣm þēodiscum
Brytonum, and Hƿīt biþ for ȝesēċendum Seaxonum. Monmūþ nōm his þancas fram
ieldrum ȝeƿritum Nenniuses, þe spræc ymbe rēade and hƿīte ƿyrmas campende, þe
mǣnaþ dracan, þe mǣnaþ þā folc Brytona and Seaxna in þǣre bēċ Historia Britonum.
Naðer secgaþ þæt oþþe þā Seaxan oþþe þā Brittiscan brucon þis tācn.

Þǣr is missenliċ sēðung þe þā Englisc brucon dracan. Man mæȝ Dracan Fanan sēon
on þǣm Bayeux Tapestry, and þǣr is sēðung þæt man bruce dracan sƿā fanan æfter
þǣre Norþmandiscan Infare. Tacitus, Nennius, and sēo lār Bēoƿulfes namiaþ ēac
þone hƿītan dracan þāra Engla.

Sēo lār ymbe sanctan Georg and þone Hƿītan Dracan is ōðer stǣrliċ sēðung þæt se
hƿīta draca is tācn þāra Engla, forþǣm þe fana sancta Georges rōdum ƿæs tācn
þāra Normanna, sƿā ƿæs sancta Georg hiera fædersancta, hƿīl se Hƿīta Draca and
his fana ƿǣron tācn þāra Engla. Sēo lār ƿæs onstedeþanc for Beadum Hǣstingum.

Þyncaþ sumu clīeƿnu lēoda þæt se hƿīta draca biþ þæt ƿǣre tācn þāra Engla, ne
sēo rōd sancta Georges, forðy sumu clīewnu, sƿā þæt Engliscra Fanena Fryȝyld,
fandiaþ hine tō edcƿicienne.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/H%C4%93afod

On līclāre is þæt hēafod dēores se ceafllice dǣl (æfter līclārlicre legednesse)
þe gewunelīce stent on þǣm brægne, ēagum, ēarum, þǣre nase, and þǣm mūþe (eall
þāra helpiaþ maniga gefrēdnessa, swelce sihþ, gehīerness, stincung, and smæcc).
Sumu ānfealdran dēor nabbaþ hēafod, ac manige twisīdemnettendas sōþlīce habbaþ
swelc.

Tō mannum, þæt hēafod and hūru se andwlita sind þā hēafodlican gesundriendan
mearca betweox sundorlicum hādum for heora ēaðe gescēadendum mearcum swelce
hǣres and ēagena bleoh, and nase, ge ēagena, ge mūðes gesceapp, rifelunga, and
ōðru þing. Mennisce andwlitan sind ēaðe gescēadendlice mannum for heora brægnes
fōreþoncum tō scēadenne betweox missenlicum andwlitigum mearcum. Þǣr mann sēo
bemǣtende ungecūþ gecynd, ealle andwlitan þyncaþ tō wesenne nēan ful gelīce, and
mennisc bearn sind līfiglīce geset tō oncnāwenne lytela ungelīcnessa on
andwlitigum mearcum.

Hādas þā sind andgietfulran þonne sīe gewunelic sind hwīlum geēowod in
biliþspellum tō habbenne māran hēafdu, tō wīsan tō tācnienne þæt hīe habbaþ māre
brægn; in witancræftlicum lēasspellum, begeondeorþbūendas þe hæbbe grēat hēafod
is oft getācniendlic swīðre andgietfulnesse. Beūtan þisse getācniendlicre
ēowunge, sōþlīce habbaþ bētunga on fēlendseonulāre ēowod þæt sēo wyrcende
fǣgness þæs brægnes ēowaþ þæt ungelīcnessa on medumre brægnes micelnesse ne sind
nā gōd getācn micelnesse, gif hīe sīen tācn hire tō āhte, tōdāles on medumre
andgietfulnesse þe þǣr sīe betweox twǣm mannum.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fr%C4%93od%C5%8Dmes_%C3%BE%C5%8Dht

Frēodōmes þōht is þōht ymb frēodōm and gefērlice efennesse. Frēodōm is se
hēafodlica intinga on ealdwīslicum frēodōmes þōht, and efenness is hegifgre on
gefērlicum frēodōmes þōhte. Frēodōmes þōhtes fyrðrendas habbaþ grēate fǣgnesse
þōhta, æfter heora understandinge frēodōmes and gefērlicre efennesse, ac oft hī
heriaþ þōht swilce folcwealdes cēosunga, folcriht, frēodōm tīdunge, frēodōm
gelēafan, frēo mangung, and ānlēpig ǣhtgeweald.

Frēodōmes þōht ǣrost wearþ sundorlīc stēormǣles brǣdung under þǣre yldo
inlīhtunge, þǣr hit wearþ folclic ongemang ūþwitum and feohwendungwitum on
Europe and landum þā nēasibb him wǣron. Frēodōmes þōht awearp þā þōht þā wǣron
folclicu on þǣm tīman, swilce irfestōlas, rīca þēodscipas, forstrang ānweald,
and þā godcundan riht ānwealdena. Man sægþ oft þe John Locke staðolode þisra
daga frēodōmes þōht. John acwæþ þe menn hæfdon gecyndelicu riht līfes,
frēodōmes, and ǣhtgewealdes; and sægde þe lēodwearda ne scoldon awerdan þās riht
for þǣre gefērlican forewearde. Frēodōmes þōhtes fyrðrendas wiþstōdon selenessa
gehealdunge and wolde settan lahweald and aspelianda folcweald on stede
āngewealdes þurh bebodu.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Braddock

Edward Braddock Heretoga (Æfter Gēola 1695 –13 Mædmōnaþ 1755) wæs Bryttisc wiga
and hēafodgūþbrego for Norþamerice æt þǣre Frenciscan and Scræling Gūþe
onginnunge (1754–1763). Man hine mǣst gemann for þǣre hearmlican fierdinge, þā
hē forelædede wiþ Frenciscum landum in Americe in 1755, hwærin cringede he.

Edward Braddock wæs geboren in Perþscīre, on Scottum ymbe 1695. His fæder wæs
ēac heretoga; Edward Braddock Maior-Heretoga se fofērde in 1725.

Braddock wearð Oþer-Stedeholder in þǣm Coludesstrēam Weardas in 1710. In 1747
swa Under-Fierdstemmgerēfa þegned he under Orange Æþelinge in þǣm Niðerlandum æt
þǣre Bergen op Zoom besettunge. In 1753 wæs he genamed Fierdstemmgerēfa ofer þǣm
14. (Buccingahamscir) Weala Æðelinges Aganan Fōtfeða Fierdstemme, and in 1754
wearþ he maior-heretogan.

In 1754 hine genamed se cyning tō oferbēan wiþ þǣm Francum on Americe. He cwōm
on Uirginie on 19 Solmōnaþ 1755 mid twǣm Bryttiscum duguþ-fierdstemmum. Hē
metede fīf landbūnesgerecan æt Alexandrie on Uirginie on 14 Ēastermōnaþe. Hīe
āscodon hine tō gefremmenne felahrōr orlegweorc wiþ þǣm Francum.

Hīe sierwedon þe ān heretoga wolde onsacan æt Niagara-byrg, Johnson Heretoga æt
Cynebeag Ora Byrig, Monckton Fierdstemmgerēfa æt Beausejour Fæsten on Fundy
Byht. Braddock Heretoga wolde fierding forelædan wið Duquesne Fæstne æt þǣre
Ohio Ēa twislum, ofergān þæt fæsten and fāran norþweard tō Niagran.

Æfter monaþa tō gearcienne, hwærin hindrede he gedrēfnis and heregeatulēast ,
Braddockes dryht fōr forþ mid ceosenum mannum. In þǣm dryhte þegned George
Washington swa landfierd þegn.

Braddock ne træd lēohtlice in þǣre wealde; he fōr mid axmannum and his menn
built brād herpæþ for mannum and feldwæpnum. Þæt weorc wæs hefigtīeme and þa
menn wǣron werig mid þǣm weorce on þǣm fære, ac hīe getimbrode strang, brād
gelād tō Duquesne.

Se dryht fōr ofer Monongahela Ēa on 9 Mædmōnaþ 1755, and eftsona meteden
Scrælingisc and Frencisc þrēat. Braddock's wigan wæron forcumen and flīemed.
Braddock eftgecigode his menn tō hira stedum eft and eft, and feall siþlice, his
feohwund fram sceot þurh þā rihtearme and in þǣre lungan.

Washington bār Braddock fram þǣm wælfelde. He ācwæl on 13 Mædmōnaþ 1755, fēower
dagas æfter þǣre bēadwe. Beforan þe he forfērede geaf Braddock Washingtone his
gescriflica bend þone he werede mid his beaduhrægle. Man secgþ þe þurh eallum
his līfe nǣfre ēode Washington ahwǣr būton þisse bende.

His cempan begrōfon Braddock west þāra Micelra Mǣdwa, þa bād drytes lāf on his
wiðertrod. George Washington foresæt æt þǣre byrgunge þegnunge, forþǣm þe se
handprēost wæs wund. Þa menn begrōfon Braddock in þǣm weges middle and drifon
wægnas ofer his byrgenne þe scrælingas nolde findan and tōgælan his bānsele.

In 1758 John Forbes Heretoga cwōm tō Duquesne Fæsten; þa Francan āflīemedon æt
his tōcyme and forgrundon þæt fæsten. Þā Bretware timbrodon anīw on þǣm stede
Pitt Burg, þæt is nū Pittsburg.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carl_XIV_Sw%C4%93ona_Cyning

Carl XIV & III Iohannes (26 January 1763 – 8 March 1844) wæs Swēona Cyning (be
naman Carl XIV Iohannes) and Norrena Cyning (be naman Carl III Iohannes) of 1818
oð his dēaþ in 184 ac he þegnede de facto regent and rīceshēafod of 1810.
Beforan þe he weard Swēona Æþeling wæs he Pontecorvo Brego and ricsode in þæm
lande se is on þæm Eotolwarum and his rīce þærin was fram 1806 oþ 1810 for þæm
Napoleon I Francena Cāsere him geaf swylc rīce and title.

Carl Cyning wæs geboren on Francum and fōn fulluht mid þæm naman Jean-Baptiste
Bernadotte. and æfterwearde Jean-Baptiste Jules Bernadotte. Þan in 1801
gefædrede hine se Carl XIII Swēona Cyning, onfōn he þone naman Carl and ofgeaf
his eftnaman ‘Bernadotte’. Noþȳlæs, his iefan sind þæt 'Bernadotte Hūs' oððe
Bernadotte-Vasa.

Frencisc be cenning wæs Bernadotte and he þegnede lange in þæm Frenciscan Here.
Napoleon I asettede hine swa Mearscealh of Franclande, oððæt ðe oft cāfen hie.
His þegndōm on Francum endode in 1810, þan he wæs geceorren bidend-ierfa þæs
Swēoniscan cynedōmes. His laðung to Swēorīce wæs for þæm þe þæt Holstein-Gottorp
Hūs se wæs Swēona cynecynn wulde forþferian mid Carle XIII. Carl Otto Mörner
Þegn (22 May 1781 – 17 August 1868), se wæs Swēonisc hiredman and witenagemotes
gilda spāc for Bernadottes æftergengnesse.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/C._S._Lewis

Clive Staples Lewis, ēac on Englisce Cliff Staples Hlōþwīg (wæs geboren þæs 29.
dæges Blōtmōnaðes þæs 1898. gēares - cwæl þæs 22. dæges Blōtmōnaðes þæs 1963.
gēares), þe man oft hāteþ C. S. Lewis, and his frīend and cynn hine hēton Jack
(on Englisce Iohannes), wæs wrītere, lēoþwyrhta, lārgyldmann, midyldlārmann,
bōclīc dēma, costnunggewritmann, lǣwede godlārmann, and Crīsten lārlādere fram
Beal Fegrste on Norþīrum. Hē is gecūþ for his lēasspellum, tō bȳsne Þā
Tīdwrītunga Naria and Þā Þrēo Spell Rodores, and ēac for his eornostum gewritum,
tō bȳsne Ānfeald Crīstendōm.

Cliff and Iohannes Tolkien wǣron lēofe frīend. Begen wrīteras worhton onmiddan
þǣm lārhīrēde þǣre Engliscan sprǣce on Oxenafordeormengylde, and begen worhton
in þǣm ungesettan bōclīcan framscipe þe hātte "the Inklings", þe nēan mǣneþ "se
fruma ymbþonca".

Þæs 1956. gēares wīfode hē þā Geānedrīciscan wrīticgan Joy Davidman, þe wæs 17
gēara giengre þonne hē, and þē cwæl 4 gēara æfter for cancerādle. Cliff cwæl
þrim gēarum æfter his wīf cwæl for cropbyrste. Hē cwæl ānre wuce befōran his 65.
gebyrddæge. Sēo tīdungendebyrdness ne cȳðde fela ymbe his dēað for þȳ þe hit
gelomp þæs ilcan dæges þæs þe se Fōresittend þāra Geāndena Rīca Iohannes Kennedy
wæs myrðrod, and þæs þe ōðer brēme wrītere Aldous Huxley cwæl. Cliffes gewritu
wǣron awend tō mā þonne 30 sprǣca and þūsendþūsendlīce sind hīe cīpt. Þā bēc
Þāra Tīdwrītunga Narnia sind brēmosta and wǣron tō feorsīene, wæferstōwplegan,
and ūtweorpende gesetta.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/C%C5%8Dc%C4%ABega

Þā Cōcīega (Cōcīega Māorisce gehāten Kūki 'Āirani) sind selfwealdende gemōtlic
cynewīse in frēore gefērlǣhtnesse wiþ Nīwe Sǣland. Þā fīftīen lytelra īega in
þissum lande þæs sūðernan Sericus Gārsecges habbaþ fulle landes brǣdo of 240
fēorscētra þūsendmetera, ac þāra Cōcīega synderlic feohwendunglic geard þeceþ
1.8 þūsendum þūsenda fēorscētra þūsendmetera geofones.

Þā hēafodlican tūnas sind on þǣre īege Rarotonga (mid 14,153 lēoda on þǣm
2006.), þǣr þǣr is geondrīcisc flyhthæfen. Þǣr is ēac swīðe māre lēodrǣden
Cōcīegera in Nīwum Sǣlande, hūru on þǣre Norþīege. In þǣre lēodrīmunge þæs 2006.
gēares, 58,008 lēoda hēton hīe selfe lēodlic Cōcīega Māori.

Þǣr wǣron mā þonne 90,000 gesēcenda tō þǣm īegum in þǣm 2006 gēare; landscēawing
is þæs landes formest weorc, and se hēafodlicosta dǣl þǣre feohwendunge, swīðe
māre þonne elelendisc feohhealdung, meregrotu, and sǣlica and wæstma ūtsendunga.

Heora beorg is se borh Nīwes Sǣlandes, on gemōte mid þǣm Cōcīegum and þurh heora
ascunge. On þissum dagum habbaþ þā Cōcīega genumen ānstandendre ofersǣwisc
gerād.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/America%27s_Cup

America's Cup (on Englisce American Cuppe mǣnende) is sigebēacen þe is gifen þǣm
hēape þe oferwinþ þā wiþrǣsendan hēapas on sæglunge cræfte, and is þæt ieldeste
wyrcende sigebēacen on geondfolclicum pleginge.

Ǣrost "Royal Yacht Squadron Cup" hātte, hit ǣrost wearþ gehāten "America's Cup"
æfter þǣm ǣorstan plegscipe þe wann þæt sigebēacen, þæt America. Þæt sigebēacen
wæs gehealden fram þǣm New York Yacht Club fram þǣm 1887. gēare (þā þā se hēap
se þe oferwann þā Cuppan geald þæt sigebēacen þǣm gylde) ōþ þæt 1983. þā wæs sēo
Cuppe genumen be þǣm Royal Perth Yacht Club, mid heora plegscipe, Australia II,
endiende þone lengestan tīman siga on þǣm stǣre pleginge þisra daga.

Sēo American Cuppan winnung is gebēote gedrifen tæl gemacra rǣsa betweox twǣm
plegscipum þe is gedēmed fram þǣm Cartan Giefe þe wæs þæt þing þe wæs gebrocen
tō giefenne þā Cuppan tō þǣm New York Yacht Club. Ǣnig plegscipa gyld þe
fulfylleþ þā þearfa þā sindon gesett on þǣre Cartan Giefe hæfþ þæt riht tō
beclipienne þone plegscipa gyld þe hielt tā Cuppan. Gif se beclipenda plegscipa
gyld oferwinne þone ōðer on rǣse is þǣre Cuppan āgenung gifen tō þǣm plegscipa
gylde.

Fram þǣre þriddan gefæstnunge þǣre Cuppan on þǣm 1876. gēare ōþ þā twentigoðan
gefæstunge on þǣm 1967., þǣr wæs ā ān beclipiend and ān andfengend, þēah þe se
NYYC dyde andfengendes cēosunge tæl tō cēosenne þæt plegscip þe hī mōton
gebrūcan on rǣse. Fram þǣm 1970. gēare wæs cearu ymb beclipunge swā grēat þæt se
NYYC undegann tō lǣtenne manige beclipiendas to dōnne cēosunge winninge ongemang
him selfum, and se oferwinnend weorðende gesett tō Beclipiende and gānde forþ tō
þǣm sōðan American Cuppan rǣse. Fram ðǣm 1983. gēare ōþ þæt 2007., Louis Vuitton
awreðode þā Louis Vuitton Cup (þe mǣnþ "Loises Vuittones Cuppe") tō sigelēane tō
þǣm oferwinnende þæs beclipienda cēosunge getæles.

Æfter þǣre Ōðran Woruldgūðe wurdon nēan twentig gēar lēas becleopunge, and þæs
se Nīwes Eoferwīces Plegscipa Gyld macode hweorfunga on þǣre Cartan tō lǣtenne
þā smalran and læs dēoran twelfra metera gecyndes plegscipu tō winnenne, and þis
gecynd wæs genotod ōþ þæt 1987. þā þā his stede wæs genumen be þǣm Geondrīciscan
American Cuppan Gecynde.

Sēo American Cuppe þæs 2010. gēares wæs rǣsed in 90 fōta (27 metera) manighulum
plegscipum on twēgra bāta winnunge, þǣre agylda þe oferdrīfþ on þrim rǣsum fēhþ
sige, in Valencie in Spēonlande on Solmōnaðe þæs 2010. Se becleopiend BMW Oracle
Racing oferdrāf þone healdere Alinghi mid twǣm sigum wiþ nānne and nam þā Cuppan
for þǣm Gyldenes Geates Plegscipa Gylde.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Actium_S%C3%A6f%C4%93oht

Þæt Actium Sæfēoht wæs gefeaht on brime be Epirus on 2 Hāligmōnaþ in þæm geare
31 beforan Cristes tōcyme and wæs micel onsæcc þæs Rēmiscan ingewinnes. Þes
garmitting wæs geaf þone dōm in þæm Endmestan Gewinne þære Rōmānisce Cynewīse
þærin feahtede Octauianus wiþ Marcus Antonius for rīce. Æt Actie mēt Octauies
līþhere geānlǣhted þrēat of Marce Antonie and Cleopatran VII Ægyptus Cwēne, on
þæm Ioniscan Sǣ nēar Actium sēo burh, se wæs in Epirus Vetus Rōmāniscan
underrīce on Crēacum.

Octauianes scipheres heretoga wæs Marcus Uipsanius Agrippa, and Antonies
sciphere hæfde fultum of Ǣgyptes scipu gesended be Cleopatran Cwēne.

Octauian's sige geaf him þone cræft to bringenne in his handum weald ofer Rōme
and his rīce. He nām þone binaman Princeps, se is 'Forma mann' and eft geaf him
se Senatus ēac titul sēo is 'Augustus'. Be þissum naman wæs Octauinus gecenned
in folgendum iedum. Þȳ weard Octauianus Augustus Rōmes brego se endode þā
Rōmānisce Cynewīse and begann þæt Rōmānisc Rīce.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C4%AAslendisc_st%C3%A6fr%C7%A3w

Sēo andwearde Īslendisce stæfrǣw geþēah of þǣm regole þe wæs gestaðelod in þǣre
18an ielde, fram þǣm Deniscan sprǣccræftmenn Rasmus Rask hēafodlīce. Æt ende
hæfþ mǣst hire staðelunge of wrītungregole þe in þǣre 12an ielde gescapen wæs
fram dīegolfulum gewrite þe man nemde Þæt Ǣreste Grammatisce Lārspell, fram
uncūðum bōcere. Se regol wæs geþōht for þǣm þe his bōcere befēng tō bēonne
gemǣnu sprǣc Scedelandes, elles Noren. Næfde fela costung, hūru, æt þǣre tīde.

Se uferra Rasmus Raskes regol wæs wesendlīce edlagung þæs ealdan lārspelles, mid
fēawum hweorfungum tō geanlīcienne midbelimpende Germanisce þēawas, swā se
synderlica bryce þæs k þonne c. Syndriga ealda getācnunga, swā ð, hæfdon sōþlīce
nā fela bryces in uferrum ieldum, swā Raskes regol macode micele hweorfunge in
behogodnesse.

Uferran hweorfunga in þǣre 20an ielde sind brēmost sēo gewȳscednes þæs é, þe wæs
ǣr gewriten swā je (bīecneþ þā tōdæges geclipunge), and sēo dilegung þæs z in
1974, þe wæs lange geclǣnu wordwyrtlicu smalnes.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C3%86x-in-Profentse

Æx oðra naman Æx-in-Profentse is Franclandes burg, in þæs rīces sūþdǣle. Hiere
nama on Francum is Aix (man sægþ "eks"), oþþe Aix-en-Provence, forþǣm is Aix
nama be manigum wicum geboren þā stent ofer hātum wiellum. Hiere nama is of þǣm
Lǣden naman Aquae Sextiae.

Æx stent 189 mīla be norðen Marseille þǣre ceastre. He is in
Profentse-landscipe, and in þǣre Bouches-du-Rhône département, ðærof is hit
sous-préfecture (se is 'underþegndōm'). Þēos burg hæfþ ymbe 130,000 onwuniendas.

Se mētere Paul Cezanne wæs geboren in Æxe, and wunode and āmētede þǣr swā
geþogen.

Aix (Aquae Sextiae) wearþ geseted in 123 BC fram þǽm Rómániscan consule Sextius
Calvinus, þe his naman his springum geaf, swá "Aquae Sextiae Salluvorum." In 102
BC his neāhness wæs the scene of the Battle of Aquae Sextae when Romans under
Gaius Marius defeated the Cimbri and Teutones, with mass suicides among the
captured wifmannum, which passed into Roman legends of Germanic heroism (cf
Ierome, letter cxxiii.8, 409 A.D. [1]).

In the 4th century BC it became the metropolis of Narbonensis Secunda. It was
occupied by the Visigoths in 477. In the succeeding century was repeatedly
plundered by the Franks and Lombards, and was occupied by the Saracens in 731.
Aix, which during the middle ages was the capital of the county of Provence, did
not reach its zenith until after the 12th century, when, under the houses of
Aragon and Anjou, it became an artistic centre and seat of learning.

With the rest of Provence, it passed to the crown of Francland in 1487, and in
1501 Louis XII established there the parliament of Provence which existed until
1789. In the 17th and 18th centuries the town was the seat of the intendance of
Provence.

Aix-en-Provence is situated in a plain overlooking the Arc, about a mile from
the right bank of the river. The city slopes from North to South and the
Montagne Sainte Victoire can easily be seen to the Norþ East.

The Cours Mirabeau, a wide thoroughfare, planted with double rows of
plane-trees, bordered by fine houses and decorated by fountains, divides the
town into two portions. The new town extends to the south and west, the old town
with its wide but irregular streets and its old mansions dating from the 16th,
17th and 18th centuries lies to the north.

The cathedral of Saint-Sauveur, which dates from the 11th, 12th and 13th
centuries, is situated in this portion of Aix. It is preceded by a rich portal
in the Gothic style with elaborately carved doors, and is flanked on the north
by an uncompleted tower. The interior contains tapestry of the 16th century,
other works of art and a baptism pool from first century. The archbishop's
palace and a Romanesque cloister adjoin the cathedral on its south side. The
church of Saint-Jean-de-Malto, dating from the 13th century, contains some
valuable pictures.

The Hotel de Ville, a building in the classical style of the middle of the 17th
century, looks on to a picturesque square. It contains some fine woodwork and a
large library which includes many valuable manuscripts. At its side rises a
handsome clock-tower erected in 1505.

Se tún, which is the seat of an archbishop and court of appeal, and the centre
of an académie (educational circumscription), numbers among its public
institutions a Court of assizes, tribunals of first instance and of commerce,
and a chamber of arts and manufactures. It also has training-colleges, a lycée,
a school of art and technics, museums of antiquities, natural history and
painting, and several learned societies.

Aix is often referred to as séo burg þúsanda springa. Among them are the
Fontaine des Quatre Dauphins (Fountain of the Four Dolphins), built in 1667 by
Jean-Claude Rambot; King René's Fountain, built in the 19th century, of Roi René
holding a bunch of Muscat grapes, which he introduced into Provence; the
hot-water fountain dating back to 1734, which is covered in moss due to the
35 °C (93 °F) water; and the great fountain, from 1860, at La Rotonde, the large
roundabout at the center of town.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C3%86%C3%B0elst%C4%81n_Engla_Cyning

Æðelstān wæs Ēadweardes þæs Ieldran ieldesta sunu and iefa. Hē ricsode of 924 oð
his dēaþe in 939. Ǣr wæs he Westseaxna cyning and Miercna cyning of 924 and in
þǣm geare hæfde he his fædres cynestōl, and nām his coronbēag and his
underþēodna āðas of Westseaxum and of Miercum æt Cyningestūne se is on Sūþrige.

In 927 forþferde Sihtric Eoforwic Cyning and of þissum dǣge weard Æðelstān
cyning ofer eallum Englalande and wæs rihte se form Engla Cyning.

In 937 onswōg Anlāf Difelin Cyning þis land mid his herige and mid Stræclud
folce and mid Scottum þe Anlāf habbe his fædres rīcestōl on Norþhymbra rīce, ac
Æðelstān Cyning gewonn sige æt sæcce æt Brunanbyrig and eall Engle and eall
Brettas hæfde him ðe he bið hlāford. On his bōcum fint man swa swa his titul Rex
Totis Brittaniae, se is "Eallre Bretene Cyning".

Æðelstān næfde bearn ne wīf. His brōðor, Ēadmund Æðeling, wæs Engla cyning æfter
þǣm þe hē stearf. His ealder fæder wæs Ælfrēd Grēata



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Taprabane

Taprabane is rīce and īegland be Indealandes sūðernum strande in þǣm Indiscan
Gārsecge. Sēo īeg hæfþ tweontig þūsend þūsenda manna.

Tāprabane hæfþ in missenlicum gereordum mænige namen. Ealdcrēcas nemdon hīe
Taprobane (and Ælfred cyning geaf hire þone naman Tāpraban and Dēprobane. Þām
Arabum wæs hēo Serendib. Tō Marco Polo wæs hēo cūþ swā Seilan, and Ceilão wæs se
nama gegifan be Portugalwarum þā hīe cōmon to Tāprabane in þǣm 1505. gēare. On
NĪwum Englisce wæs þæs īeglandes nama Ceylon.

In þǣm 1972. gēare wæs þæs rīces ambihtlīc nama awended tō "Sri Lanka" (in
Sinhalisce śrī laṃkā, IPA: [ˌʃɾiːˈlaŋkaː]. Þæs īeglandes āgnan nama is in
Sinhalisce ලංකාව Laṃkāva, IPA: [laŋˈkaːʋə], and in Tamilisce இலங்கை ilaṅkai,
iˈlaŋgai). "Sri Lanka" is of Sanskrit worde laṃkā, þe is "boldwelena land", þe
wæs ēac his nama in ealdre Indiscre sægene þæs "Mahabharata" and þæs "Ramayana".
Sri is Sanskritisc titul of āre.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Street_Fighter_IV

Street Fighter IV (Strǣte Feohtere IV on Englisce) is 2008 feohtend gamen macod
by Capcome. Hit is þæt fyrst ȝetalod Street Fighter gamen for þǣm arcadum siþþan
1999. Man ālīesde þæt sceattȝeƿyrhtod arcade gamen in Iapane on 18 Mǣdmōnþes,
2008, and Norðamericanisc arcadan inbrōhton hīe siþþan Ƿēodmōnþe. Man ālīesde þā
gamensearufadung þæs PlayStation 3 and Xbox 360 on 12 Sōlmōnþes, 2009 in Iapane,
in Norðamerican on 18 Sōlmōnþes, and in Europan on 20 Sōlmōnþes. Man ālīeseþ
Windows fadung in þǣm ōðrum fēorðlinge 2009.

Þēah Street Fighter IV hæfþ þing and bæcgrund in 3D, se gamenpleȝ ofstenþ
ȝesetliċ 2D feld. Producer Yoshinori Ono cƿæþ þæt ƿold hē þæt gamen tō
ofstandenne ȝeliċ tō Street Fighter II. Man inlǣde nīƿ betƿeoxbend hātte "Focus
Attacks" ("Saving Attack", oþþe "Spariende Ȝefeoht," for þǣre Iapaniscan
fadunge), and "Ultra" ȝefeoht. Se ȝesetliċ siex-cnæpp handræd eftcymþ, mid nīƿum
mearcungum and oferȝefeohtum þæs āsettan betƿeoxbendes, blandende ȝesetliċ
gamenpleȝ mid ēacliċum þancƿyrhtum.

Þæt gamen hæfþ sƿīðe ȝeliċ mōd mid Super Street Fighter II Turbo, ac hæfþ ēac
fram Street Fighter III 3rd Strike mæniȝ mearcunga. Beȝen leoht ȝefeoht cnæppas
cnocende biþ ȝiet ƿyrpes, and beȝen strang ȝefeoht cnæppas bēoþ sārcƿides. Beȝen
middel ȝefeoht cnæppas bēoþ spariende ȝefeohtes. Þæt gamen hæfþ ēac cnossian and
sƿift standend. Crimson Viper is se efne mann þe mæȝ hēah hlēap fremman.

Man macaþ þā menn and stedas þæs gamenes sƿā 3D bisena mid mæniȝhealfum, ȝeliċ
tō þǣre Street Fighter EX underendebyrdnesse þe Capcom macode mid Arikan, ac
notiaþ syndriȝ tōhīȝung tō ȝiefenne him handȝetācnode ānsīen, mid ēagetōhīȝungum
þe ēast asian ƿritend hæfþ, bōcblæc clǣmend, and bōcblæc scūr on þǣm campum. Se
hēafodcynstmann and mannƿyrhta is Daigo Ikeno, þe ǣror on Street Fighter III 3rd
Strike ƿyrhtode.

Spariende Ȝefeoht sind nīƿ betƿeoxbend þe man in Street Fighter IV inlǣdeþ. Þæt
is ȝefeoht þe þone pleȝere līefþ tō scyldenne ȝefeoht, and fremeþ ƿiþȝefeoht.
Man fremeþ þis þȳ middlum fyste and middlum spurne tōgǣdre cnocende. Þǣr sind
tƿeȝen hēafodƿeardas þæs ȝefeohtes. In þǣm formestan hēafodƿearde, se mann macaþ
nīƿ standend, þȳ hē ān ȝefeoht scyldeþ fram þǣm ƿiþfeohtere. Se ōðer hēafodƿeard
biþ ƿiþȝefeoht. Þȳ mā hielt se pleȝa þā middel fyst and spurn cnæppas, þȳ
strangor ƿierþ þæt ȝefeoht. Ȝif man þā cnæppas ȝenug healde, þæt ȝefeoht macaþ
þone ƿiþfeohtere tō þǣm grunde āfielþ, ȝiefende þǣm pleȝere frēo ȝefeoht.

Mid oferfadungum syndriȝa ȝefeohta þe man in ǣrum Street Fighter gamenum
inlǣdode, sƿā Super Combos (Ofersamƿrædnessa) and EX Syndriȝ Ȝefeoht, þæt gamen
inlǣdeþ ēac nīƿ cynn syndriȝes ȝefeohtes þe hātte Ultra Combo (Grēate
Samƿrædnessa). Grēate Samƿrædnessa sind lang filmliċ ȝefeoht þe mæniȝfeald
samƿrædnessa fysta, spurna and ōðra ȝefeohta hæfþ.

Tīdlīċe ȝesettod betƿēonan þǣre Street Fighter II endebyrdnesse and þǣre Street
Fighter III endebyrdnesse, þā pleȝende menn þǣre arcadan fadunge beinnaþ þā menn
þæs fyrstan Street Fighter II, and fēoƿer nīƿ menn. Akuma fram Super Street
Fighter II Turbo ānȳƿeþ sƿā ȝehȳded pleȝende mann, and ȝehȳded ƿiþfeohtere. Þæt
gamen ēac beinnaþ tƿeȝen efne-CPU menn: Seth biþ se læste oferƿiþfeohtere þæs
gamenes, and Gouken sƿā ȝehȳded ƿiþfeohtere, þe ƿierþ 19 menn.

Þā hāmfadunga Street Fighter IV habbaþ mā menn sƿā ēac þe fram þǣre arcade
fadunge. Þā hāmfadunga habbaþ Cammy and Fei-Long fram Super Street Fighter II,
Dan and Rose fram Street Fighter Alpha, Sakura fram Street Fighter Alpha 2, and
Gen fram þǣm fyrstan Street Fighter.

Fore teohhode Yoshinori Ono þone þanc ymbe þæt gamen tō Capcomes R&D hēafodmann
Keiji Inafune, mannum þyncþ hit in Capcome þe ne sculde man nīƿu ȝetælod gamen
þǣre Street Fighter endebyrdnes ne macian. Ǣrest, mæniȝ menn ƿiþhæfdon Ones þanc
nīƿes gamenes æfter sƿā mæniȝ ȝēar æfter þǣm formeste. Þēah, þe sēo gōdu
folcliċnes Street Figher II Hyper Fighting on Xbox Live Arcade ƿæs cūþ tō
Capcome, þafode Inafune man þone ƿeorc tō beȝinnenne.

Þis ƿæs sēo formest fandung Ones nīƿes gamenes Street Fighter endebyrdnesse sƿā
ƿyrhta, þēah ƿyrhtode hē ǣror on Street Fighter III 3rd Strike sƿā sūnd
hēafodƿyrhta, and ǣror ƿyrhtode hē Capcom Fighting Jam. Se ƿeorc on Super Street
Fighter II Turbo ƿearþ se hēafodtæs Street Fighter IV ƿeorcscipetēames.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Perfume

Perfume ( パフューム Pafyūmu) is wīfmanna technopoplic trēpe fram Hirosciman, on
Iapane, þe stent on Ayano Ōmoto, Yuka Kashino and Ayaka Nishiwaki. Hī ætīwdon
stōwlīce þæs 2001. gēares and macodon hira fērnesse tō grēatre swēgdrihte on þǣm
2005. gēare. Fram þæs 2009. gēares Sēremōnaþe, se trēpe bær nigone ānfeadle
sangas mid grēatum forþgange. Fram þǣm 2003. gēare, Perfume is bewiten fram
Yasutaka Nakata þǣm leōdfruman Capsule trēpes and Contemode naman. Þæs trēpes
frymðelic swēg fram æfter Shibuya-kei dyde scearpe fērnesse tō electro-hūsdrēame
and technopop.

Þisses trēpes nama nis of þǣm Iapaiscum gereorde ac is Nīwenglisc, hwærin menþ
he æsceda oððe stenc.

On þǣm 2002. gēare, Perfume forþyppede twegen ametendlicu ānfealde sangas,
"Omajinai Perori" and "Kareshi Boshūchū", geseald ǣnlīcne on Hiroshima swā
Mimiji naman. Sēo mægþ wendede tō Tokyo æt 2003 bēon bewiste þæm Capsules
Yasutaka Nakata, and æt 2004 ūtālædede þrēo mārum ānfaldum: "Sweet Donuts",
"Monochrome Effect", and "Vitamin Drop", eallne ūtālædedon Bee-Hive Recordum.
Þære mægþe forme þrēo līfe fremminge wæron gegiefen ymbe þissum tīme, gietende
fylgend geþoftan mid hira unāseolcendlīcum fremmingum.

Perfume wendede tō grēatum naman æt 2005, ūtālædende "Linear Motor Girl" þurh
Tokuma Japan Communications on 21st Hāligmōnaþe of þæm gēare. Twā furþor
ānfaldan, "Computer City" and "Electro World", sāwon þā mægþe crīstnende sylfum
swā "nēah foreweard technopop dǣl". Hira hidercyme swēg-hord, Perfume ~Complete
Best~, mengede hira six geongest and stōd swā hēah swā #33 on þæm Oricon getalu
hwænne hit wæs forma ūtālædede. Þæt sanghord ingēong þæm getalum æfter
ūtālædende hira ōðer swēg-hord, rǣcende #25.

Perfumes forma mihtigne cīepinge forþgang com of hira ānfaldan "Polyrhythm", þæt
wæs brēac NHKe for hira Kankyō Recycle Campaign. On his līesinge dæg,
"Polyrhythm" ūtālædede æt #4 on þæm Oricon getalum, sittende æt #7 for wicelicne
hold; þæt ānfaldan sealde ofer 60,000 gelīobisenas. Scortlic æfter, Perfume
ūtālædede hira sixta ānfalde, "Baby Cruising Love/Macaroni", þæt hēgaede grēater
forþgange þanne "Polyrhythm" þurh hēgaende #3 on dæglicum and wicelicum getalum.
Hira ōðer swēg-hord, Game, becom þæt ōðer technopop swēg-hord in stǣre ūtālædan
æt #1, behindan Yellow Magic Orchestres Naughty Boys in 1983. Game wæs namede
twin-platinum þurh RIAJ for salan mid 500,000 gelīobisenas. Perfume befēng on
hira fora grēat hring in Iapan æt 27 Ēastermōnaþe tō 1 Sēremōnaþe of 2008. Þæt
hring, Perfume Forma Hring "GAME", wæs ūtālædede on DVD on 15 Winterfylleþe,
2008.

Æt 9 Mǣdmōnaþ, 2008, Perfumes seofoða grēatne naman ānfaldan, "Love the World",
ūtālædede on þæm Oricon salan getalum æt #1, becumende þonne forman technopop
sang ǣfre þus, brecende Yellow Magic Orchestres helm mid þæm "Kimi ni, Mune
Kyun." ūtālædende æt #2 in 1983. Twā folgende ānfaldan, "Dream Fighter" and "One
Room Disco", willedon æfnaþ efen-wel (þæt lætra rǣcende #1 on þæm Oricon tō.)
For þes tīma, Perfume began stōwlice fæstnunge līfe wæfta æt frēgeum stedum. Sē
forma swēg-stede, Budoukaaaaaaaaaan!!!!!, tōc plæce æt frēgene Nippon Budokan on
6 and 7 Blōtmōnaþe, 2008 and wæs fēng þurh sienasearu for brādweorpung on NHK
and wæs ūtālædede on DVD on 22 Ēastermōnaþe, 2009. Þæt ōðer, Disco!Disco!Disco!,
tōc plæce æt Yoyogi National Gymnasium on 9 and 10 Þrimilcemōnaþe, 2009. Perfume
began brādweorpung glīwerelic for feorrsīen namede Perfumes Chandelier House in
Ēastermōnaþe 2009, scortlīce æfter þære "One Room Disco" līesing. Perfume
ūtālædede hira þridda swēg-hord, Triangle, on 8 Mǣdmōnaþ, 2009, mid ōðerum hring
ymbe Iapan þæt began in Wēodmōnaþe. Triangle wæs namede platinum þurh RIAJ for
sellende ofer 250,000 gelīobisenas. In 2010, "Monochrome Effect" geat scēawunge
in þæm Norðamerica þā hit wæs on ānum American Dad!.

Perfume ābodede hira forma ānfaldan of 2010 sceal bēon ūtālædede on 14
Ēastermōnaþe. Þæt PV for Natural ni Koishite wæs pȳtede on YouTube þurh Tokuma
Iapan tramet. Natural ni Koishita biþ mid Iapanisc gescierplan naman NATURAL
BEAUTY BASIC. Hit wæs furþor ābodede þæt hit wæs bēon twā A-sīdan ānfaldan,
"Fushizen na Girl/Natural ni Koishite".



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nor%C3%BEamerica

Norðamerica (ēac Māre Norþerne Wīnland æfter Īslandiscum naman gehāten; on
Nīwenglisce: North America) is se norþerna worulddǣl of þǣm Americum, ligende on
Eorðan Norðernum Healftrendele and in þǣm Westernan Healftrendele. Hit is
bebyrded benorðan him þȳ Arctiscan Gārsecge, beēastan him þȳ Atlantiscan
Gārsecge, besūþēastan him þȳ Carabiscan Sǣwe, and benorþwestan him þȳ Sericus
Gārsecge; Sūðamerica ligeþ tō sūþēaste. Norðamerica þeceþ ymbe 24,709,000 km²
landes, nēan 4.8% of Eorðan fullre brǣdo oþþe 16.5% Eorðan landes. Swā fram
Mǣdmōnaþe þæs 2008. gēares, his landware wæs geteald swā nēan 529 milliona
manna. Hē is þridda worulddǣl æfter brǣdo, æfter Asia and Affrica, and fēorþa in
landware æfter Asia, Affrica, and Europe.

Middan þām þūsendum gēara þǣr inlendisca landwara wunedon on þǣm worulddǣle,
cynd wræsnaþ and getēon. Archæolocgistas oft namedon missenlicu cynd þā hī
afindaþ æfter þǣm lande þǣr hī wǣron afunden. Ān of ealdestum cyndum þe is ǣr
afunden is Clovis Cynd fram land þe is nū Nīwe Mexico. Ōðru geongu bisen is þæt
cynd hringa þe is gehāten Hlæw Byldan (ēac Fort Walton Cynd), þe wæs afunden be
þǣre Mississippi ēa. Hī blēowon fram 300 BCE tō 150 CE. * Fruma



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nor%C3%BE_America

Norðamerica (ēac Māre Norþerne Wīnland æfter Īslandiscum naman gehāten; on
Nīwenglisce: North America) is se norþerna worulddǣl of þǣm Americum, ligende on
Eorðan Norðernum Healftrendele and in þǣm Westernan Healftrendele. Hit is
bebyrded benorðan him þȳ Arctiscan Gārsecge, beēastan him þȳ Atlantiscan
Gārsecge, besūþēastan him þȳ Carabiscan Sǣwe, and benorþwestan him þȳ Sericus
Gārsecge; Sūðamerica ligeþ tō sūþēaste. Norðamerica þeceþ ymbe 24,709,000 km²
landes, nēan 4.8% of Eorðan fullre brǣdo oþþe 16.5% Eorðan landes. Swā fram
Mǣdmōnaþe þæs 2008. gēares, his landware wæs geteald swā nēan 529 milliona
manna. Hē is þridda worulddǣl æfter brǣdo, æfter Asia and Affrica, and fēorþa in
landware æfter Asia, Affrica, and Europe.

Middan þām þūsendum gēara þǣr inlendisca landwara wunedon on þǣm worulddǣle,
cynd wræsnaþ and getēon. Archæolocgistas oft namedon missenlicu cynd þā hī
afindaþ æfter þǣm lande þǣr hī wǣron afunden. Ān of ealdestum cyndum þe is ǣr
afunden is Clovis Cynd fram land þe is nū Nīwe Mexico. Ōðru geongu bisen is þæt
cynd hringa þe is gehāten Hlæw Byldan (ēac Fort Walton Cynd), þe wæs afunden be
þǣre Mississippi ēa. Hī blēowon fram 300 BCE tō 150 CE. * Fruma



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/N%C4%AB%C6%BFe_S%C7%A3land

Nīwe Sǣland is rīce þe standeþ on twǣm micelum īegum and fela læssena īega in
þǣm sūþwesternan dǣle Sericus Gārsecges. In þǣre Māwriscan sprǣce is Nīwe Sǣland
Aotearoa gehāten, þe in Māorisce mǣneþ "Land þæs Langan, Hwītan Wolcnes".

On Nīwes Sælandes fēower þūsenda þūsenda and fīf hundreda þūsenda manna, fornēan
þrēo þūsendu þūsenda wuniaþ on þǣre Norþīege and ān þūsend þūsenda manna on þǣre
Sūþīege. Þās īega sind ongemang þǣm brādostum in þǣre worulde and þæt heora
micelness ætsamne is gelīc þǣre þāra Bryttisca Īega oþþe Coloradorīces. Ēac
Aotearoa, Māorisc nama tō Nīwum Sælande wæs Niu Tireni, þe is of þǣm Engliscan
naman.

Nīwe Sǣland is ān betweox þǣm nīwostum gesetedum grēatum landum. Felaīegisc
gesettendas tōcōmon gelīce sumes tīman betweox þǣm 500. gēare and þǣm 1300.
gēare æfter Crīste, and cenedon þā inlendiscan Māwriscan folc.

Se forma þāra Europiscena þe sind gecūþ cuman tō Nīwum Sǣlande wǣron fram Abele
Janszoone Tasmane gelǣdd, þe oferseglode tō þǣm westernan sǣgemǣre þǣre Sūþīege
and þǣre Norþīege þæs 1642. gēares. Þā Niðerlendiscan wēndon þæt hit ān land
wǣre þe hī nemnedon Staaten Landt. Siþþan wæs hit "Nieuw Zeeland" gehāten æfter
þǣre stōwe on Batafie þǣr hī wǣron staðolodon, þe endebyrdlīce wæs gehāten æfter
heora scīre Sǣland. On þǣm 1769. gēare Hēafodmann James Cook ongann wīdlica
hāwunga þāra īega. Þēos fōreēode Europiscne hwælhuntað and endlīce hefige
Europisce landbūinge.

Nīwe Sǣland wearþ Englisc landbūness þurh þā Fōrewearde Waitangiges þæs 1840.
gēares, þe ēac gehēt "fullne hēafodmannscipe" (hāteþ tino rangatiratanga on
Māwrisce) þǣm Māwriscum cnēorissum Nīwes Sǣlandes. Oþ þisne tīman þæt andgiet
þǣre Fōrewearde is gīet gefliten.

Nīwe Sǣland wearþ selfwealdende rīce on þǣm 26. dæge Hāligmōnaþes þæs 1907.
gēares þurh cyninges hātunge. Ful sundorrīcehād wæs golden fram þǣm Gemōte þæs
Geāndan Rīces mid þǣre Asetnesse Westmynsteres þæs 1931. gēares; hit wæs
andfangen þurh þǣre Asetnesse gecorennesse fram þǣm Gemōte Nīwes Sǣlandes on þǣm
1947. gēare. Nū is Nīwe Sǣland cynerīce inne þǣre Þēodacynewīsan.

Nīwe Sǣland is staðolwritlīc cynedōm mid gemōtedum folcrīce. Æfter þǣre Nīwes
Sǣlandes Gesetednesse Cyninglicra Namena (þæs 1953. gēares), Elisabeþ II Cwēne
is Cwēne Nīwes Sǣlandes and is betǣcned tō hēafode þæs rīces fram þǣm
Cynespeliende.

Þæt Lǣstende Hūs is fram þǣm Forman Þegne gelǣdd, þe is nū John Key of þæs
medume drohtbewariendan Þēodlīcum Stēormǣlhēapes.

Gemǣna wealdcēosunga sind geworht ǣne on ǣlcum þrigēare; sēo nīwancumenoste
cēosung wæs geworht on þǣm 2011. gēare. Se Hēafodmann þæs Oferstealles wæs Phill
Goff, þe wearþ lādmann þæs Weorclican Gefēres on æfteran 2006. Nū is [[David
Shearer] se Hēafodmann þæs Oferstealles. On þissum dagum stent þæt Hūs on eahta
gefēra, þe fram þǣm 1996. gēare hæfþ geworden gecoren þurh wīsan andefenre
spelunge þe Mincgedum Dǣlnimendum Andefen gehāten is (oft on Nīwum Englisce
"MMP" æfter "Mixed Member Proportional" gehāten).

Nīwe Sǣland is dǣlnimend þǣre ANZUS borhes fōrewearde betweox Australie, Nīwum
Sǣlande, and þǣm Geānlǣhtum Rīcum American. On 1985 Nīwe Sǣland forweornde tō
lǣtenne Geānlǣhtra Rīca motige gefēd oþþe motige wǣpnded scipu tō ingangenne on
his hȳða; þis berēnode þā Geālǣhtan Rīcu tō tōwendenne his ANZUS borh tō Nīwum
Sǣlandelande on 1986. Nīwe Sǣland ne hæfþ be lage forlǣten þā fōrewearde.

Nīwe Sǣland hæfþ Hēah Gerēfearn (oþ 1980 wæs hit "Supreme Court" gehāten
(mǣnende "Hīest Gerēfearn")) and Gerēfearn Gesēcednesse (ǣr dǣl þæs Hīestan
Gerēfearnes), ēac tō underlinglicum gerēfearnum. Oþ 2004 cūðon gesēcednessa fram
cēosungum þæs Gerēfearnes Gesēcednesse on þǣm Dēmendum Gemōte þæs Witenagemōtes
on Lundene geseted wesan.

On 2003 wæs sēo Gesetedness þæs Hīestan Gerēfearnes geseted, tōwendende
gesēcednessa þǣm Witenagemōte, þe hæfþ geworden wyrcende siþþin 2004, and
staðoliende Hīehst Gerēfearn Nīwes Sǣlandes on Wellingtūne.

Þǣr hit wæs ǣrost fram Europiscum geseted wæs Nīwe Sǣlande gesundrod on scīrum.
Þās wǣron adilod on 1876 swā þæt þæt weald cūðe weorðan hēafodburge geseted for
sceattlicum intingum. Tō wæstme þisses hæfþ Nīwe Sǣland nān gesundrodlīce
gespelod underrīcisc dǣl landes, tō bȳsne scir, rīce oþþe landrīce būtan his
stōwlicum wealde. Nā þȳ lǣsÞā gāstas þāra scīra gīet libbaþ and þǣr is strang
feohtung on gamenum and þēawiscum weorcum.

Siþþin 1876 hæfþ stōwlic weald wealded þā missenlican geardum Nīwes Sǣlandes.
For his gesettunge stǣre wæs Nīwes Sǣlandes stōwlic weald geworht nēan æfter
Brytiscum stōwlicum wealdes wīsum, mid gecorenum burgum and fylca witenagemōtum.
Æfter gēarum habbaþ sume þisra witenagemōta geþoftod oþþe gefēred andwendunga be
gemǣnre andwyrdunge, and sumu nīwu ones wǣron geseted. On 1989 setede þæt
stōwlice weald on ful nīwe endebyrdnesse, brūcende þone twāendebyrdnessan timber
þisra daga landscipra witenagemōta and landrīca dōma.

Tōdæg hæfþ Nīwe Sǣland 12 gearda witenagemōtas tō þǣre dihtunge landes and
farunge and 74 landrīca dōmas þā þe dihtaþ strǣta macunge, adelsēaþes macunge,
timbrunga andwyrdunga, and ōðru stōwlicu þing. Þā landrīca dōmas sind 16 burga
witenagemōtas, 57 beganga witenagemōtas, and se Cīthāmīega Witenagemōt. Fēower
þāra landrīca witenagemōta (ān burg and þrīe begangas) and se Cīthāmīega
Witenagemōt ēac dō þæt weorc landscipes witenagemōtes and þæs sind gecūþ tō
geānlǣhtum dōmum. Landrīca dōma begangas ne sind sōþlīce underdǣl þāra landscipa
witenagemōta beganga, and sume heora gemengaþ landscipa witenagemōta mearca.

Nīwe Sǣland stent on twǣm grēatum īegum and missenlicum læssum īegum. Sēo
Sūðerne Īeg is sēo grēatoste landes brǣd, and is gesundrod andlang hire lengðe
be þǣm Sūðernum Alpisum, hwæs þe hīehst beorg is Aoraki / Cook Munt þe is 3754
metera hēahþe. Þǣr sind 18 beorgas þe standaþ hīehran þonne 3000 metera on þǣre
Sūðernan Īege. Sēo Norðerne Īeg is læs dūnlendisc þonne se Sūða, ac hire land is
geseted be fȳrbeorgum. Se hīehstan Norðerne Īege beorg, Ruapehu Munt (is 2797
metera), is wyrcende hornlic fȳrbeorg.

Sēo fulle brǣdness þæs landes Nīwes Sǣlandes, 268,680 þm²a, is hwæthwæge læsse
þonne sēo Iapanes oþþe þāra Brittiscena Īega, and hwæthwæge māre þonne
Coloradorīce on þǣm Geānlǣhtan Rīcum American. Þæt land is māre þonne 1600 þm
æfter his hēafodlican norþnorþēasternan eaxe.

Nīwe Sǣland is sēo landlecgende ānlēpigoste eallra þēoda. Þæt nīehste land,
Sūþland, is 2,000 þmum benorþwestan Nīwes Sǣlandes hēafodlicum īegum ofer þǣre
Tasmansǣwe. Þæt ān land besūðan him is se Andnorða, and benorðan him sind Nīwe
Caledonia, Ficgiege, and Tonga.

Þæt gewunelice medumweðer geond þæt land is mild, oftost fram cōlum gewedere oþ
milde wearm geweder, mid gewedere selden undersincende under oþþe ge 0°C ge
rīsende ofer 30°C. Byrdnessa gāþ fram wǣtum, caldum gewedere on Sūþlande and þǣm
Westriman þǣre Sūþīege, þǣr fielþ þæt grēatoste dǣl Nīwes Sǣlandes regnes, oþ
underwearmbeltisc geweder on Norþlande. On Wellingtūne is þæt medume læste
geweder on wintere 5.9°Ca and þæt medume mǣste geweder in sumere 20.3°Ca.

Nīwes Sǣlandes landlegedness hafaþ unhliden on manigum feorrsīene wæfersīnum and
scēawspellum . Hūru Ercol and Xena wǣron lēohgewriten be Auclande, Heofonlicu
Wiht in Crīstcirican. Peter Jackson lēohwrāt Se Hlāford þāra Hringa in
missenlicum stōwum geond þæt land, brūcende þā ānlican and andefne unahodenan
landlegednessa.

Hēafodlicu gewrite: Nīwes Sǣlandes dēor – Nīwes Sǣlandes wyrta – Getæl Nīwes
Sǣlandes fuglas – Nīwes Sǣlandes trēo

For his langan ānlēpnesse fram þǣm ōðrum landum þǣre worulde hæfþ Nīwe Sǣland
ungewunelice blōtsman and dēor. Oþ þone tōcyme þāra formena manna efne ānum
þūsendgēare oþþe twǣm ǣr, eahtig þæs landes wæs wuduland and, būtan twǣm cynnum
of hreaðemȳs, nān meolcsycend dēor fand man ūt þǣre brime. On stede þæs wǣron
Nīwes Sǣlandes wealda geset be missenlicum cynnum fugola (heora manige sind
fleohtlēase), crēopendas, and seoxsceancwyrm - heora manig nēan swā grēat swā
mūs (seoh þæt gewrit be lopphāmum).

Nīwe Sǣland hafaþ nīwlice, forðode feohwendunge. His hēafodlic ūtbǣru weorc sind
eorþbigeness, geardbigeness, fiscoþ, wudufellung and giwitnesse cræft. Þǣr is
ēacswā hwæthwega hefig landscēawinge weorc. Þā scēawspella and wīna weorc sind
geþōht wesan tōcumendu.

Siþþan 1984 habbaþ folgiendu geweald worhten grēate feohwendunge efttimbrunge,
andwendende Nīwe Sǣland from swīðe hāmcēapbeorgendre and gefadodre feohwendunge
on lȳsdre, frēocēapunglicre feohwendung. Būton tīmum strangre weaxunge in þǣm
middelum 1980 gēarum and ǣrum 1990 gēarum, sōþ ingangfēo habbaþ lytloden wiþ
þāre 1980 gēara micelnessa, and medume gēarlic feohwendunglic geþungenness hafþ
gebēon læsse þonne sēo þe wæs anbīdod and is swīðe getrīwende in micelum
micelnessum tōfarena tō ætīcenne his fulle rīcisce forþbǣro.

Þæs andweardes Nīwes Sǣlandes gewealdes feohwendunglice endas sind staðolode on
ǣre awendunge fram heora setting ongemang þāra læssena dǣl þāra OECDlicena rīca
tō mārum stede eft, sēcende frēocēapunglica forewearda, lytliende þā
ungelīcnessa betweox þǣm folcum, and timbriende "gewitnesse feohwendunge."

Ungelīce him on ǣrum tīengēarum, Nīwe Sǣland hæfþ nū forwierned cēapætēcenda
hefignessa, bēacniende forcēapætēcung hæfþ gebēon gesett on āgānum tīmum.

In þǣm 2004 gēare hit undergann tō geondsmēagenne frēocēapunge wiþ Cīne,
maciende hit ān þāra formena landa tō dōnne swā.

Under þǣm æfterrum 1980 gēarum , þæt Geweald Nīwes Sǣlandes cīepede manig miclu
cēapunge geweorc, ge his feorsprecera wrǣd, ge his rōdweges endebyrdnesse, ge
manige ūtweorpsenderas, ge tū gyldhūs in rǣwe nyttfēona cēpa. Þēah þæt Geweald
Nīwes Sǣlandes gīet gewealdeþ hefig tæl underginnunga, þā þe sind ætgædere
gecūða tō Rīcāgena Underginnunga; hīe sind gewealdeda þurh unbefealdena
dǣlnimunge gesetednessa swā ānstandenda underginnunga þe sind sculon wyrcan
nyttlīce, swā swā ǣnig ānlēpiglīce āgnu underginnung. Missenlicu dǣl beorgendre
gelagunge staðolaþ underginnunga endas ac forwiernaþ þæt dǣlnimendu geweald
hæbben wyrcen þā underginnunga gedæghwamlīce. Ǣrendþegnung, spearcaweorces
wrǣdas, ūtweorpsendunge and feorrsīene brādweorpendas, ēacswā lǣcehūs and ōðer
cēapunge underginnunga sind staðolod þus. Þā hēafodlican Rīces Þegnunga standaþ
on gewealdes mearcum and þegnungum þā hēafodlīce arēdiaþ gewealdes gelǣstunge,
rǣdes rǣd, laga gelǣstung, and fērlica þegnunga.

Hūhwega eahtige hundoðan Nīwes Sǣlandes folces sind of Europiscum lēodum
cennede. Māorisca lēoda sind þæt ōðerlīce mǣste folc (14.7% Nīwes Sǣlandes
folces). Betweox þæs 1996 gēares and þæs 2001 gēares folctellunge, þæt tæl lēoda
mid Asianiscum frumcynne (6.6% his lēoda) wearþ māre þonne þæt Seriscus
Gārsecges Īegbūenda (6.5% his lēoda) (understand þæt sēo folctellung lēt mann tō
wrītenne manige folcbendas). Sēo onfangenness Māoriscre līfwīsan gīet wiexþ,
ānlīce for þǣre nīwancumnan īnlāde Māoriscre feorrsīne þegnunge.

Þā hēafodlican Crīstnan cirican sind sēo Ænglisce Cirice, sēo Ealdormanna
Cirice, sēo Rōmanisce Cirice, and sēo Endebyrdnesse Cirice. Māre þonne þridde
dǣl þæs folces ne stent mid ānre cirican.

Sēo ēac: Nīwsǣlandisc Englisc, Nīwes Sǣlandes scēawcræft, Nīwes Sǣlandes
bōccræft, Nīwes Sǣlandes drēam, Māorisca þēoda

Nīwes Sǣlandes Geseted Tīma is twelfum stundu æforan Efenwyrcende Woruldwīd Tīma
(gehāten ēac tō sceortunge "UTC"). Betweox þǣm æftermestan Sunnandæge
Hāligmōnaðes ǣlces gēares and þǣm formestan Sunnandæge Eostormōnaðes þæs
folgiendan gīeres brȳcþ Nīwe Sǣland Dæges Lēohtes Settunge tīman.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/N%C4%93ohw%C3%A6l

Sē nēohwæl (Linnæus: Monodon monoceros, on Nīwenglisce narwhal oþþe narwhale,
swā gehāten for his scinnan blēo) is medume grēat hwæl þe wunaþ on þǣm Norðan.
Hē is ān þæs Monodonitidae cynnes ætædere mid þǣm hwītan hwæle; þæs hē grēatne
hornlicne tusc on hēafdes ceafles uferran wynstran healfe.

Nēohwælas wuniaþ oftost on þǣm Canadisc Norðan and Grēnelendiscum wæterum; hī
sind selden gefunden besūðan 65° norðernre landhīehþe and sind swīðe ānlīce
gested huntere for þǣm Norðan.

On Wintere etaþ hī oftost sǣgrundbūendu dēor, oftost efenfiscas, on dīepþum swā
dēop swā 1500 metera under fæstum īsflētum. Nēohwalas habbaþ gebēon gehuntod for
hire bānum and flǣsce tō heore fōdan be Scrælingum þūsendu gēara; efneted huntoþ
nēohwala is gīet geworht. Þēah þe heora hēafodrīm þynceþ stille wesan, se
nēohwæl is gedēmed ānlīce open cwellunge for gewedercyndes andwendunge and his
swīðe ānlicre fōdan etunge.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grendel

Grendel æglæca þærof wrāt se scop in Bēowulf þæm geweorce. He is ān þāra þrēora
feondra þærwiþ fēohteþ Bēowulf se beorn in þæm lēodweorces spelle: þā ōðran sind
Grendles mōdor and wyrm). Þes scopcræft wæs in þære ylde 700–1000 gewriten ac
his spell is of ealdyldum fore Englecyn wāt crīstendōm.

Grendel is brōga and þincþ man se is grim fīfel oððe eoten. Se scop writeþ se he
is onwōcen onmiddan manigum æglæcancyn and wæs of Caines cyn: "Wæs se grimma
gǣst Grendel, Caines cyn, -- ðanon untydras ealle onwócon, eotenas and ylfe and
orcneas, swylce gigantas". Eall men in þæm weorce sindon acol of Grendle būten
Bēowulf Æþeling.

Bēowulf se lēodweorc is fint man in þære Nowell Codex. Ðærin us tealleþ se scop
þe Hrōðgār Dēna Cyning timbrode Heorot his healle for his mēdosetle. Æglæca is
Grendel, and þes sceadugenga acymþ of þæm fennum þan he is astyred be æþlinga
dryhtes dynne, and þna swefað hie æfter symble cwōm se unhǣlo wiht onmiddan him
and slōg þā þegnas in Heorote. Ðar fareþ he on nihte and slegeþ Hrōðgāres
gesīþas þan slæpedon hie on Heorote. (Heaðowylma bād láðan líges ne wæs hit
lenge þā gēn þæt se ecghete.)

Bēowulf beebbeþe Geatena rīce þe he meahte slēan Grendel, þone he abād on þæm
heallrecede oð þder cwōm se brōga.

Æfter lange fēoht, fang Grendel his deaðbenn of Bēowulf. Grendel afliemede on
fenne and þær in luh stearf he. Æfterweard in þæm fennemere feahtede Bēowulf wiþ
Grendles mōdor under brimwylme, and hæfþ sige ofer hiere. Æfter hiere dēaþ fint
Bēowulf Grendel licgan aldorlēasne swá him aér gescód hild æt Heorote, hrá wíde
sprong, syþðan hē æfter déaðe drepe þrōwade heorosweng heardn, ond Bēwulf hine
þā hēafde becearf.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Genseric_Wendla_Cyning

Genseric wæs Wendla Cyning and Alana Cyning of 428 oþ 477 and mǣre wæs he þe he
staðolede þæt Wendlerīce on norðernum Affrican. Þurh Genseric cwōm micel æglǣc
þæs æfteweardan Westernan Rōmāniscan Rīces in þæm fifta gearhunde. Gensericces
cynedōm wæs ælmæst eahtig winter and in þissum ylde rærede he his lytel
Germanisc mægð þe swylc folc biþ mār Wendelsǣs rīce, and of his folce giefaþ we
þæm brime þone naman 'Wendelsǣ'. Æfter Genserices dēaþ begann swylce rīces slāwe
dryre.

Genseric fang to rīce æfter Gunderic his brōdor in ylde þan þā Wendlas healdon
rīce in Hispania Baetica, on Ispanie sūþēast dæle. In 428 æt Mérida Fēohte adrāf
Genseric onsæc þāra Swæfna and brōhtede eall his þēod, þærof wæron ymbe 80,000
menn, ofersǣ to Norþernum Affrican in þæm geare. Sum mann secgð ðe Bonifacius se
Rēmiscan Ealdormann geleaðede hine, þe he meahte atēon Wendelþēodes þrēat wiþ
þæs cāseres lēodweard.

Genseric wrohtede micel hryre in his ēastweardum fare fram Ercoles Sylan geond
Affrican. He feaht wið Bonifacius and gewonne sige in 430, and þan gecnyttede
þrēat of þāra Ēastrīces and Westrīces fōr wiþ Genseric, he gewonn ongean micel
sige.

In 435 sealde Gaiseric his hand on foremæl mid Rōmwarum þærbe heald Wendelþēod
Mauretania þæt underrīce and Numidie dæl þe hie bēon Rōmfolces gesiþþas. Noþȳlǣs
on 19 Hāligmōnaþ in 439, afang Gaiseric Cartainan, þæs rīces micel ceaster on
Affrican. In foremæle mid Rōmwarum in 442, Rōm oncnēow þæt Wendle rīce swa
sundorrrīce ofer Byzacena and Numidie dæle. Eftsōn heald Gaiserices liþhere
micel dæl þæs westernum brimes, and he cnyttede to his rīce þā Baleares,
Sardinia, Corsica, Melita and Sicilia.

Æfter þe Genseric forþferde in Cartaine æt 88 winterylde, wæs fang his sunu
Huneric to rīce.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/G%C3%A9ar

Gēar is hwyrftlic tīd þǣre eorðe tō ful gānne be þǣre sunnan. For wæccende on
eorðe, þēos stend wiþ þā tīd þe is geþorften fram þǣre sunnan tō endienne ānne
weg geond þone circulcræft andlang þǣm āsprungennesswege.

On tungolcræfte is þæt Iulianisce gēar is gemet tīman, tōmearcod tō 365.25um
daga þāre ǣlc hafaþ 86,400 Geondrīciscre Endebyrdnesse ēagantīda .

Þǣr nis nān woruldwīde andfenge tācn þæs gēares tō gemete tīde. Sēo Geondrīcisce
Endebyrdness Gemeta ne foreseteþ ān. Gemǣne sceortness gebrocen geondrīclīce is
a (æfter þǣm Lǣdnan worde annus).

For þǣre eorðe eaxisce hleoninge, se weg gēares fēreþ þā fernesse þāra tīmena,
gesundrode fram andwednungum in weðere, and on stundum dæges lēohtes, and þæs
ēac on wyrtum and eorþwēlan. In medumwearmum and undereaxlendiscum stedum,
oftost sind fēower tīman gecūðe: Lencten, Sumer, Hærfest and Winter, þe sind
tungollīce gesundrod þā sēo sunne cymþ tō þǣm tīdum efennihte and sunnstedes,
þēah þā medumweðerlice tīman latiaþ æfter heora tungollicum mearcum. In sumum
wearmbeltiscum and underwearmbeltiscum stedum is hit gemǣnre tō sprecenne be þǣm
regnigum (ēac "wǣt" gehāten) tīman wiþ þone drygan tīman.

Consulabēc gēar is nēahsagu þǣre eorðe hwirftlice tīde on sumre consulabēc.
Consulabēc gēar in þǣre Gregorianiscan consulabēc (ēacswā on þǣre Iulianiscan
consulabēc) hafaþ oþþe 365 (gemǣne gēar) oþþe 366 (bissextus) daga.

Þæt word "gēar" is ēac gebrocen tō tīdum þe sind nēahlīce gelīce ac ne ful gelīc
ge þǣm tungolican gēare ge þǣm consulabēc gēare, swelce þæt tīmisce gēar, þæt
feohhwyrftlice gēar oþþe þæt gyldisce gēar, and manig ōðru gēarcynd. Þurh
reccinge cann þæt word gēar mǣnan þā hwyrftlican tīde ǣniges dweligendes: tō
bȳsne, "Tīwlic gēar" is sēo tīd on þǣre Tīw dēþ his āgnan hwyrfte.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eormanr%C4%ABc

Eormanrīc (wæs geboren þǣre tīde betweoh þǣm 260. gēare and þǣm 276., cwæl
betweonan þǣm 370. gēare amd þǣm 376.) wæs Ōstgotena Cyning.

Tō cyninge rīcsode hē wīd rīce in Middelum Europe. Þā rihtan gemǣru his
landrīces sind dīegol, ac hit þynceþ þe hit wæs fram besūðan þǣm Pripet Fenlande
beteoh Danais Ēa and Dniester Ēa.

Eormanrīces nama in Gotisce wæs gelīce Aírmanareiks. He is genemnod on bōcum
geond þā Germaniscan land oft ōþ þæt 13. hundredgēare. For þissum is his nama on
fela wīsena: in Iordanes Getica is hē Ermanaricus, in þǣm Engliscan
gieddeBēowulf is hē Eormenrīc, in Ealdnorrene is hē Jörmunrekkr, and in Medume
Ealdum Hēahgermanisce Ermenrich. For þȳ se nama Heiðrekr wæs wel gelīc þǣm worde
"Ermanarīc", hē sī wēnunga Heiðrekr Ulfhamr self of þǣre Hervarar sagu.

Eormanrīc is genemnod in twǣm Rōmāniscum gewritum - ān is fram Ammianus and þæt
ōðer is Getica fram þǣm stǣrwritere Iordanes þæs 6. hundredgēares.

Æfter Ammianus, Eormanrīc wæs swīðe beaducræftig cyning þe lætemest dyde
selfcwalan, for þǣre berǣsunge þāra Hūna, þe anwōd his land on þǣm 378.
tīengēare. His cynedōm wæs adilegod and his folc wearþ gewealden fram þǣm Hūnum,
under þrāge nēan hūhwega 75 gēara.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/D%C8%B3fung

Sēo dȳfung gēo wæs hlēapung in wætre, ac nū hit oft is sund under wætre mid
sierwunge þe giefþ lyft tō ǣðmienne under wætre. And þēos sierwung oft nū hātte
scuba, þe cwōm of Nīwengliscum "Self Contained Underwater Breathing Apparatus".
And æt fruman "SCUBA" segde Americiscra gūþfroggamanna ǣðmungsierwunga.

And sume habbaþ micle lyftfatu and se dȳfere ǣðmaþ of þǣm lyftfæte and ūt in
wæter. And þēos sierwunge hātaþ in Nīwenglisce "open circuit", and hit ēac oft
hātte "aqualung". And Jacques-Yves Cousteau and Gagnan macodon þone ǣrestne
aqualung in gēare 1942. And mǣste hit wæs āna for geweorce oþþæt in gēare 1953
se National Geographical Magazine wrāt fore worulde ymb Sciptogan Cousteaus
geweorce under sǣ æt Grand Congloué īege neam Marseilles þǣr wæs eald scip þe
sanc þenden Rōm ricsode Europam, and forþȳ swīðe manige writon tō him tō
āscianne hwǣr man mihte bycgan aqualung. And gēo se aqualung oþþe air scuba næs
swā man nū siehþ wunelīc on sǣrīmum, ac his lyftwieldend [= regulator, demand
valve] wæs micel and behindan þæs dȳferes healse, and oft mid twǣm lyftfatum.
And oft nū þis ealde cynn scuban hātte se twēgra pīpa scuba.

And sume habbaþ lȳtle oxygenfatu and se dȳfere ǣðmaþ of poccan and eft ongēan in
poccan, and his līc nimþ oxygen and māra oxygen cymþ of fæte, and his līc macaþ
þone carbon dioxide, and in þǣre ǣðmungsyrwunge is fæt full þæs sodalīmes þe
iteþ þisne carbon dioxide, and forþȳ se dȳfere ne macaþ (bubbles), and mæg
swimman micle lengra under sǣ mid ǣðmungsierwunge mid samum gewihte. And þēs
sierwunge hātaþ eftǣþmendas and in Nīwenglisce rebreathers oþþe closed circuit.
And nū sind eftǣðmendas þe misciaþ nitrogen oþþe helium in þā ǣðmunge, swā hātte
'nitrox' and 'heliox' and 'trimix', tō þæs þe man mæg dȳfan dēopora þonne mid
ungemiscodum oxygene. And þū mæg sēon maniga gelīcnessa swilcra hēr .

Hēr is lȳtel āstȳriende biliþ dȳferes mid þǣm lȳtlan oxygeneftǣðmende Salvus þe
Siebe Gorman gēo macode in Lundene, and mid him man mihte dȳfan (oþþe weorcan in
atorlyfte) healf stunde oþþe lȳtle lengre, and hit is swīðe unhefig, and se
dȳfere miht swimman swā īeþ swā ēan sierwunge. And hēr is grēat gelīcnesse and
in hire be hȳþwætre geweorctoga bebīedeþ.

And swilce dȳferas oft hātton froggamenn, for þǣm þe on hira fōtum hīe habbaþ
scōs þe sind swā þā fēt froggan, and þēs hātton finnas. On winstran sīdan siehþ
man twēgen froggamenn þe rīdaþ in hȳðe dierne under wætere on rīdungfȳrramme.
Man macode ǣrest þis cynn froggamannberendes in Italiam for gūðe in gēare 1939
and þā Italiscan froggamenn nemnedon hit maiale, þe segþ 'swīn', for þǣm þe him
wǣron þā ǣrestan swīðe earfoþlīce to stȳrienne. Ac in Brytene nemnede man hit
manned torpedo oþþe human torpedo, oþþe oft chariot, þe segþ 'wīgcræt'. And man
mæg sēon þrēo þisra in Eden Camp þe is nēah Mæðeltūne (Nīwenglisc: Malton) on
Eoforwīcscīre on Englum. Hīe habbaþ þone Bryttiscan eftǣðmend CDBA þe Siebe
Gorman macode, þe segþ in Nīwenglisce "Clearance Diver's Breathing Apparatus",
and in Brytenes scipfyrde clearance diver is scipfyrdisc dȳfere þe dȳfeþ to
weorcanne and ne tō feohtanne.

Man siehþ twēgen froggamenn mid þǣm Russiscan eftǣðmende IDA71, and ān hira
rīdeþ þone Russiscan dȳfereberend Protei 5. And hēr sind þrēo dȳferas mid þǣm
IDA71.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canceler

Canceler (Lǣdene: cancellarius), ambihtlic tītul gebrocen fram mǣste þāra lēoda,
þe hæfdon land and laga þe ofcwōmon of þǣm Rōmāniscum Rīce. At different times
and in different countries it has stood and stands for very various duties, and
has been, and is, borne by officers of various degrees of dignity. The original
chancellors were the Cancellarii of Roman courts of justice- ushers who sat at
the cancelli or lattice work screens of a basilica or law court, which separated
the judge and counsel from the audience. A Chancellor's office is called a
chancellery or chancery.

The Chancellor of Austria or Bundeskanzler, is the title for the head of
government in Austria. In Austrian politics the Bundeskanzler position is
somewhat equivalent to that of a Fyrmestscealc.

The Þēodscmanna Canceler oððe Bundeskanzler, is Þēodsclandes rīces lēodweardes
hēafodman. Þær is Cancelerhād swa swa Forma Þegn in Brettaþēodna rīcum. Hiera
Bundeskanzler cēaseþ sē þēodisc Witenagemōt.

After the unification of Germany, in 1871, the Chancellor of the Reich or
Reichskanzler, served not only as head of government, but also as presiding
officer of the Bundesrat, the upper house of the German imperial parliament.
After the collapse of the German monarchy in 1918, the German chancellor no
longer presided over the upper house of parliament.

For centuries, the King of France appointed a Chancellor or Chancelier de
France, a Great Officer of the Crown, an office associated with that of keeper
of the seals. The chancelier was responsible for some judicial proceedings.
During the reigns of Louis XVIII, Charles X and Louis Philippe, the Chancellor
of France presided over the Chamber of Peers, the upper house of the royal
French parliament.

In Finnland the Chancellor of Justice (Oikeuskansleri, Justitiekanslern)
supervises the legality of actions taken by Government and monitors the
implementation of basic civil liberties. In this special function the Chancellor
also sits in the Finnish Cabinet, the Council of State.

In the Kingdom of Poland, from the 14th century, there was a royal chancellor.
In the Polish-Lithuanian Commonwealth (1569-1795), the four Chancellors
(Kanclerzs) were among the ten highest officials of the state. Poland and
Lithuania each had a Grand Chancellor and a Deputy Chancellor, each entitled to
a senatorial seat, responsible for the affairs of the whole Kingdom, each with
his own chancery. See Offices in Polish-Lithuanian Commonwealth.

In Sweden the Chancellor of Justice or Justitiekanslern acts as the Solicitor
General for the Swedish Government. The office was introduced by Charles XII of
Sweden in 1713. Historically there was also Lord High Chancellor or Rikskansler
as the most senior member of the Privy Council of Sweden. There is in addition
to this a University Chancellor or Universitetskansler, which leads the National
Agency for Higher Education.

In Russian Empire, the Chancellor was highest rank of civil service as defined
by Table of Ranks, on the same grade as Field Marshal and General Admiral. Only
the most distinguished government officials were promoted to this grade, such as
Foreign ministers Alexander Gorchakov and Alexey Bestuzhev-Ryumin.

In Spanish-speaking countries, the title of Chancellor (Spanish: Canciller) is
usually given to the government ministers (or equivalent Cabinet-level
positions) in charge of foreign policy or foreign language affairs.

In Swissland, the Federal Chancellor (Bundeskanzler, Chancelier fēdēral,
Cancelliere della Confederazione) is elected by the Swiss parliament. He or she
heads the Federal Chancellery, the general staff of the seven-member executive
Federal Council, the Swiss government. The Chancellor participates in the
meetings of the seven Federal Councilors with a consultative vote and prepares
the reports on policy and activities of the council to parliament. The
chancellery is responsible for the publication of all federal laws.

In the Geānlǣht Cynerīce, a number of cabinet ministers hold offices containing
the word Chancellor.

In the federal government of the United States, the only official granted the
title of chancellor is the Chancellor of the Smithsonian Institution, a largely
ceremonial office that has long been held by each Chief Justice of the United
States during his term. As the Smithsonian is an academic institution, however,
its use of the title is perhaps best thought of as akin to a university's
chancellor (see below).

A handful of U.S. states, like Delaware, still maintain a separate Court of
Chancery with jurisdiction over equity cases. Judges who sit on those courts are
called Chancellors.

The title is frequently used — particularly in Europe — to indicate the head of
a university. (Alternatively, the title rector is also popular.) Oxford and
Cambridge have both been headed by a Chancellor since medieval days, although
today the office is largely ceremonial, and the daily administration is in the
hands of a Vice-Chancellor. Many universities in the Commonwealth follow their
model.

Canadian universities follow the British tradition in having a figurehead
chancellor, but the day-to-day operations are typically handled by a
"president," "principal" or "rector" who also carries the title of
Vice-Chancellor.

In Australia, the Chancellor is Chairman of the University's governing body;
thus, as well as having ceremonial duties, the Chancellor participates in the
governance of the University (but not its active management). The Chancellor is
assisted by a Deputy Chancellor. The Chancellor and Deputy Chancellor are
frequently drawn from the senior ranks of business or the judiciary (it is one
of the few jobs considered compatible with judicial service). Some universities
have a Visitor, who is senior to the Chancellor, and is generally the state
Governor (or, for Catholic universities, a Bishop). Once upon a time, university
disputes could be appealed from the governing board to the Visitor (as is still
the case in the UK), but nowadays such appeal is generally prohibited by
legislation, and the position has only ceremonial functions. (In fact, little
function at all, since the Visitor will rarely attend University functions,
unlike the Chancellor and Deputy Chancellor, who frequently preside at functions
such as graduations.)

In the United States, universities usually call their heads "presidents," but
the name chancellor is sometimes seen, most commonly in a system of connected
state universities. A given state's university system is often headed by a
"chancellor" who serves as the system-wide chief, while individual campuses are
headed by presidents; a typical example is the California State University
system. Exceptions include the University of Alaska system, the University of
California system, University of North Carolina system, University of Illinois
system, and the University of Wisconsin System, within which the two titles are
reversed. So in California, for example, the CSU chancellor supervises the
presidents of CSU's 23 campuses, while the UC president supervises the
chancellors of UC's 9 campuses.

The College of William and Mary uses chancellor in the British way for a
figurehead leader, at present the former United States Secretary of State Henry
Kissinger. But the day-to-day head is an American-style "president," not a
"vice-chancellor."

In þǣm Crīstnum cirican, is se Canceler bisceopscīre lahwita þe spelaþ þā
cirican in lahlicum intingum.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bloomesd%C3%A6g

Bloomesdæg (Nīwenglisc: Bloomsday) is gemynding þærin mōt man begellan þæs līfes
James Joyce Īrisc writere and þes dæg is gemearcod in ælcum geare on þæm 16.
dæge monaþes. On þissum dæge eftlibbað menn þa belimpas þa þærof wrāt Joyce in
his bēc Ulysses. Eall se spell þære bēc takes place on 16 Seremōnaþ 1904 in
Difeline and his underburgum and forþæm heoldeþ man Bloomesdæg on þæm ilcan dæg
in ælcum geare 16 June in þære byrig. Þæs dæges naman is on þære bēc heafodman,
Leopold Bloom.

Joyce cēas the date 16 Seremōnaþ 1904 forþæm þe on þæm dæge fōr he ūt couting
Nora Barnacle heo wæs later his brȳd; hie wadedon to Ringsend Difelin suburb.

Se ærresta gewrit ymbe Bloomesdæge find man in epistol be Joyce to Miss Weaver
of 27 Seremōnaþ 1924: "There is a group of people who observe what they call
Bloom's day - 16 June."

On þæm dæg fiftige geare æfter 50th anniversary þære bēc belimpum gegædrede John
Ryan (artist, critic, elehūsweard and staðolere of Envoy magazine) and Brian
O'Nolan bōcwritere mid hiera frēondum for dæglang pilgrimage andlang þone
Ulysses ryne. Mid him wæron Patrick Kavanagh, Anthony Cronin, Tom Joyce (se wæs
tōþlæcce and James Joyces geswēor) and AJ Leventhal (Bōcere of Þrinesse
Felwascipe on Difeline). Hie hæfde Ryan twone mearhgetogne wægnas, of þæm
ealdtīdes wīsan þærin fōron Bloom and his friend in Ulysses þe hie drīfen to þæm
earman Paddy Dignames byrgen. Þes frēonhēap sōhtede to farenne ymbe þære byrig
þurh eall þone dæg, þe hie begaþ in turn þā stedas þæræt belamp þing in þære
bēc, and þe hi enden be nihte in þæm burgstede þe ǣr wæs Difelines sceandhūsena
ende, swylce stede nemnede Joyce 'Nihttūn'. Se fare wæs forscrāf healfweg, þan
þā werige menn eode in þæt Bailey elehūs and abādon in þæm hūs in druncenne and
geflīte. Þæt Bailey hūs Ryan then owned. In 1967 installed he þær þā duru to No.
7 Ecclesstrǣte (Leopold Bloomes strǣtduru), æfter þe he hæfde rescued it from
demolition.

In Difelin befealdaþ se dæg missenlice þing ūt bōccræfte on on him sind Ulysses
bōcrǣdinga and plegas, elehūsrȳnas and oþra belimpas, and micel is be þæm James
Joyce Centre berēnod, þæt stent in þære Norþ Micelgeorgiusstrǣte (North Great
Greorge Street). Oft gewǣdað menn hie in Ēadweardylde hrægle to begellenne
Bloomesdæg, and þærin folgað hie Bloomes ryne ymbe Difelin be mearcum to bysene
Davy Byrne's elehūs. Sum mann hæfþ in his mōde gedihted hele bōcrǣding þære
helum bēc and þis meaht læstan oþer healf dæg.

On þæm Sunnandæg in 2004 beforan þæm hundteontigoþa "geardæg" þāra spelles
belimpa, cwōmon 10,000 menn on Difelines wunenda for frēom, open-air, full Irish
breakfast on O'Connell Street consisting of sausages, rashers, toast, beans, and
black and white puddings.

"Every year hundreds of Dubliners dress as characters from the book ... as if to
assert their willingness to become one with the text. It is quite impossible to
imagine any other masterpiece of modernism having quite such an effect on the
life of a city."

On Bloomsday 1982, Joyces cennundæges hundteontigoþa eardæg, sand RTÉ ungebrōcen
30-hour dramatic performance of the entire text of Ulysses on radio.

Siððan 1994 hæbbaþ Ungere in Szombathely haefþ man begoll Bloomesdæg forþæm þe
is seo burg se cenningstōw of Leopold Bloomes fæder, Virág Rudolf, emigrant
Ungarisc Iudea. Þis is gedōn æt þæm Iseum, Isis tempules lāf sēo is of Rēmiscum
yldum, and æt þæm Blum-mansion, begollen to Joyce siððan 1997, æt 40–41
Fő-strǣt, and þis hūs wæs ǣr geagen be Iudisc cynn be naman Blum.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Africa

Affrica is þære woruldes ōðer-stōrest and ōðer mǣst eardfæste worulddǣl, æfter
Asie. Æt ymbe 30.2 þūsenda þūsenda km² midgetellende togegeōddum ēalandum, hit
bebrædeþ 6% of Eorðan mid 20.4% of Eorðan lande. Mid ān þūsenda þūsenda þūsenda
oneardendum(swa of 2009) in 61 ēðelmearca, hit talaþ for ymbe 14.72% þære
woruldes landwara.

Sēo worulddǣl is behlænede þisse Wendelsǣ benorþum, Suez Gedelf and Rēada Sǣ tō
norþwestum, se Indisca Garsecg besūþēastum, and Atlantic tō westum. Affrica hæfþ
manif rīcu, and man hie tellaþ to bēon 54 swylce mid Madagascar þǣm īeglande and
missenlica ēalandisc mægþa.

Affrica, mǣstlīce on his ēastān, is wīdlic ārede witancræfte gēfere swā bēon þæt
frumcynn land manna and þā grēata apas, mid gewitscipe for ǣrlīce hominidum and
hira ealdefæderum fram ymbe seofon þūsenda þūsenda geras agon. Þā ǣrlīcest menn
wæron fram Sigelhwaraland, sum 200,000 winter agon.

Affrica sitteþ on þæt Middelgyrdle and befæreþ manigum weder eordoras; hit is
ǣnlīc worulddǣl āreccan fram norðe midlenne tō sūþe midlenne eordoras.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C7%B7%C4%ABnlendisc_cystel/%E1%9A%B9%E1%9B%81%E1%9A%BE%E1%9B%9A%E1%9B%96%E1%9A%BE%E1%9B%9E%E1%9B%81%E1%9B%8B%E1%9A%B3_%E1%9A%B3%E1%9A%A3%E1%9B%8B%E1%9B%8F%E1%9B%96%E1%9B%9A

Wīnlendisc Cystel (Castanea dentata) is micel bēam þæs bēcan cynnes, þe þēodisc
Norðamerican is. Fore þone cystel blæc, hēo wæs ān þāra mǣste weorþlica
wudulanda bēama hire eardes. Þǣr sind nū feawe eald trēowu þisses cyndes, būton
hwǣr man hīe in unblæclicum eardum stealde.

Wīnlendlisc Cystel is swīfte weaxende sumorgrēne heardwudu bēam, þe oþ 100–150
fēt (30–45 m) micel and 10 fēt (3 m) brad wiext, and eardaþ fram Maine and
sūðernum Ontario tō Mississippi, and fram þǣm Atlantiscum waroðe tō þǣm
Appalaceanum Beorgum and Ohio Dene.

Þǣr sind mænig gesibbcynn cystela, beinnende þā Europisc Swētan Cystele, Cīnisc
Cystele, and þā Iapanisc Cystele. Hire lārcræftig nama, Castanea dentata, cymþ
of þǣm tōþum hire hlēafa, þe 5–8 yncas lang (14–20 cm) and 3–4 yncas brad (7–10
cm) sind. Þās sind lēohtlic scortor and brador þonna þe fram þǣm Swētum Cystele.
Sēo wiþblæclice Cīnisc Cystel nū biþ sēo mǣste folclice cystel þe man in þǣm
G.R. stelþ. Þā cystela bēoþ in þǣm bēcum cynne, mid bēce and ǣc, ac ne sind
gesibbod tō þǣre hors cystele, þe in þǣm cynne Sapindaceae is.

Sēo Wīnlendisc Cystel is grēatu berestre hnyta, mid þrēo hnutum in ǣlcum
scēaðgum burre. Þā hnyte weaxaþ þurh þǣre læstum healfe sumores, þā burras
ōpenende and tō þǣm grunde feallende nēah þone fyrst fylforst.

Sēo Wīnlendisc Cystel wæs swīðe weorþlic bēam for wildlīfe, giefende fela fōda
tō Hwīttægl Dēore and Wild Tyrcig. Sweart Beras cūðdon tō etenne þā hnyte for
oferwintera.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C5%8C%C3%B0re_Penisc_G%C5%AB%C3%BE

Se Ōðru Penisca Gewinn, þe Rōmware hetaþ elleswīse Se Hannibalisca Gewinn oððe
Seo Gūð wið Hannibale, oððe "Se Cartainisce Gewinn", wæs miclu gūþ of þære
Rōmāniscan Cynewīsan wiþ Cartaine þa burg. Þes sæcc læstede of 218 to 201
beforan Criste and his fēohtas wæron andlang Wendelsǣs rīmum of westen to
ēasten.

Þes wæs seo ōþru micle gūþ betwuh Cartaina and Rōme and þās tū rīcu hæfdon þreo
micel sæccas wiþ him ofer hiera ieldu þa hēt man þa "Peniscan Gewinnas" of
Rōmwara nama for Cartainafolce, Poeni, of Pene þæm folce of Wendelsǣs ēastrīme
þa gestaðoledon Cartaina.

In þissum sæcce gewonn Hannibal micel lof. He wæs Cartaine heretoga his mǣrostan
dædas wæron þe he brōhtede elpendas ofer Alpis þæm beorgum in Italie and his
micel sige æt Cannae. Hannibal fōr of Cartaine landrīcu on Ispanie and cwōm in
Gallie þære fulltumedon hine Galware. Þæn fōr his here mid his elpendum in
Italie.

In Italie hæfde Hannibal micel sige ofer Rōme æt Trebie and æt þæm miclan
sætnunge be Trasimene þæm mere. In þæm folgendan gear (216 bC), hæfde Hannibales
here ēac sige ofer Rōmwarum, æt Cannae in sūðernum Italie, and æt þissum
garmittunge wæron Rōmes legie eall forgrunden. Æfter þissum, manig byrig þa ær
wæron Rōmes geþoftan wendedon to Cartaine healfe, and forþæm bād wig on Italie
for tiene winter and lengre.
