https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romulus_Augustulus

Romulus Augustus wæs se endmesta Westrēmisca Cāsere. He wæs ymbe þæm geare 461
geboren and his dēaþ is ungecenned ac it wæs æfter 476, and man secgð þe he giet
alibbedede in 507 be bēc of þæm geare.) Romulus wæs cildcyning, abanned Cāsere
þæs westdǣl þæs Rōmāniscan Rīce æfter his fæder Orestes adrāf Iulius Nepos
Cāsere of Italie in 475. Romules cynedōm begann on 31 October 475 and endode
æfter ānum wintre on 4 Haligmōnaþ 476 þan Ēadwacer hine oferwearp. Stǣrwritas
secgaþ þe Romules dǣd þe he gesealde him in hande betæcneþ se ende þæs westrīce,
Ealdes Rōmes feall and þara Middelyldum angyn in Westernum Europan.

Þæs Cāseres nama wæs Momyllus Romulus and he ricsode be naman Romulus Augustus.
Be his binaman is he betste gecnawen se is "'Romulus Augustulus", þærin is
Augustulus 'Agustcynn' oððe Se 'Lytla Augustus'. Ealdran bēc nemnaþ hine Romulus
Momyllus oððe Momyllus Augustulus, and stǣrwriteras secgaþ þe Momyllus meaht
bēon being a corruption of Romulus.

Bēc of his ielde habbaþ fēa þing ymbe Romules līfe. He wæs abanned cāsere be
Orestes his fæder, se wæs wigenahlāford þæs Rōmānisc Here æfter he adrāf Iulius
Nepos Cāsere of Eotolware. Romulus wæs geong cild and his rīce wæs gedwimorlīce
for he wæs tæcencyning for his fædres rīce. Ūtan Italie aliefedon fēa þe he wæs
rihte cāsere ne meahten he abūgan to his wealde.

Tiene monaþlang wæs Romules cynedōm þan hine awearp Ēadwacer, æfter þe Ēadwacer
hæfde sige ofer Orestes and hine ofslōg. He sendede Romulus to wunienne in
Lucullanum þæm Byrig sēo is in Campanie and þæreft fordwīneþ Romulus Augustulus
of stǣrbōca spellum.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/R%C3%A6dwald_%C4%92astengla_Cyning

Rædwald (ēac (H)ræðwald), Tytilan sunu, wæs þæs Ēastengla cyning of ymb 600 oþ
his dēaþ in þǣm gēare 624. Fram 616 wearþ he sē rīcosta brytencyning besūþan
þǣre Humbran, and campes framscipum macede hē Norþanhymbranisc aloten dihtend tō
beorgenne willan his. Hē wæs forma Angel cyning begietan Crīstendōmes tæcinge
and fulwiht (fram þǣre Cantwarabyrig sande), and healp elnian hine wiþ þone
frambige of Ēastseaxum and Cent. Hē is se gecorenosta mann for þā namcūþan
Sūþtūn Hōh scipbyrgenna. In þǣm nigoðan hundgēare hē is reord in þǣm
Angelseaxiscum Cranicum tō wesenne Brytenwealda.

Þā forman and fullestan wrītunga be Rædwalde is Bēda þæm Stǣre Angelþeodes
cyricean, þe sægþ þæt his rīce betwēonum þǣre Augustiniscan sande cyme tō Cente
(on þǣm 597 gēare) and þǣre ǣwnunge and cierringe Ēadwines of Norþanhymbran
(fram 625 oþ 26). Consula æfterran trahtas (mid ungewislīcum dōme) secgaþ þæt
Rædwaldes dēaþ twā, æt 599 and 624, swā wēnunga þæt ofhende consula for 599 wæs
for Tytilan dēaþ and Rædwaldes āhafennesse.

For Rædwaldes geong līf wealdendeu hūs of ōþerum rīcum wæron becumende stranglic
fæstedon. Æðelbryht of Cent (forewesede 560-616) wæs weddede Berctan, Frankisc
Charibertes of Paris crīstene dohtor. Ceawlin West-Seaxna, mæst swīþ bregu sūþ
fram Humbre, æwde Æðelbryhtes infare fram Cent til 584, þā æfter feohtende þære
Brytena in Oxnafordscīr his rīce wanede and Æðelbryht āhte gelīc rīce. In Mierce
seo heolstoru līcnes Creoda, Iceles bearn, befæstede his cynnes grēatness. Norþ
fram Humbre ēa þā twā Deira rīcu (on Eoforwic) and þæt māra norþerne Bernice (on
Bamburgh) hæfdedon wiðerhȳdigu rīcu. Ælla of Deira racede til his dēaþ in 588,
lǣfende Acha dohtor and Edwin sunu swā mid þriddum siblinge. Þæt Bernicisc rīce
(gewæred cȳþþe West Seaxnan) wæs elnende rīcsunge, and Edwin gamolede in wræce
in Cadfan ap lago cafortūn of Gwynedde. In missenlicu wīg þæt Bernicisc Æðelfriþ
geānlǣcede Norþanhymbranisc rīce, and in 604 brōhte Deira under his ānwealde.

Rædwaldes gecynd fram Wuffan, Wuffinges genamed leōdfruma, is Bedes word. Hē wæs
geboren betweox þǣm 560 gēare and 580 and wæs (gelīce ieldra) Enian brōþor.
Wēnunga for þǣm 590um hē beweddede hæðenum wīfe mid hēagum cyste mōdstaðole hwæs
naman is ne cūþne. Fram hire hē hæfd be þæm læstan twā suna, Rægenhere (alder)
and Eorpwald. Ēac hē hæfd Sigeberht, ealder sunu oþþe stēopsunue.

Sē nama 'Sigeberht' is ne gelīc ænig ōþerne Wuffinga naman, ac hē is mǣnelic mid
þǣm Ēastseaxa rīce. Sledde Ēastseaxna Cyning (se rīcsode ymbe 587-604) beweddede
Ricula, Æðelbryhtes sweostor. Æðelbryht āhealp his nefan æfterfylgendnesse, hira
sunu, in Ēastseaxe, mid æfter þæm tūm cyningum becōmon of Crīstendōm. Hit is
manade þæt Rædwaldes wīf ǣr beweddede þæm cynnes gildan and Sigeberht wæs (swā
sægþ Willelm of Mælmesbeorge) Rædwaldes stēopsunu. Sigeberht (þæt grēow in
hæðenum hūse) earnode þā fēondrædenne Rædwaldes, þȳs drīfan him mid giestinge on
Galwalum, wēnunga weardian his āgenum blōde cynnes.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pasquier_Quesnel

Pasquier Quesnell (geboren 1634, dēadod 1719), wæs Frencisc Iansenisc
dryhtweorþ, geboren in Parise on þone 4an Mǣdmōnþes 1634.

Æfter þǣm þe hē his gradcinan āfēng in þǣm Sorbonne mǣrlīce in 1653, geþēodde in
þæt Frencisce Gebēdhūs. Þā wearþ hē welcūþ; ac his Ianseniscan efensārgunga
lǣddon tō his forewritennesse of Parise in 1681. Hē nōm hlēow mid þǣm
frēondlican Heorre Coisline, bisceope Aureliana; fēower gēarum ufor, hūru,
foreseah hē þæt nīwe ēhtnes wæs gearu tō cumenne, flēah hē tō Brysele, ongann
wunian mid Antoine Arnauld (q.v.).

Þǣr belāf hē oþ 1703, hwonne se hād þæs arcebisceopes Meclines hine hæftede.
Æfter þrim mōnþum hæftunge, ætflēah hē swīðe bealdlīce, and setlede æt
Amstelodamume, hwǣr hē þā lāfe his līfes brēac. Æfter Arnauldes dēaðe in 1694
hēold man Quesnell þone lǣdere þæs Ianseniscan gefēres; and his Réflexions
morales sur le Nouveau Testament dǣlnōm fullnēah swā micel dǣl in his bōccræfte
swā Iansens Augustinus self.

Swā his tītul getācnaþ, wæs þes ēstfulnestraht ymbe þā Hālgan Gewritu, þǣrin
Quesnell gefōr tō bereccenne endas and biliðu þæs Ianseniscan gefēre, bet þonne
gehwilc ǣrra wrītere hæfde gedōn; and be þǣm wearþ se traht sēo hēafodmearc
Iesuitisces rǣses. It appeared in many forms and under various titles, the
original germ going back so far as 1668; the first complete edition was
published in 1692. Þæt gewrit Unigenitus, in þǣm nā lǣs þonne 101 cwida of þǣm
Réflexions morales wǣron fordēmed swā eretic, wæs getilod on Clementum XI on
þone 8an Hāligmōnþes 1713. Quesnel dēadode æt Amsterdame on þone 2ne Gēolmōnþes
1719.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Napoleon_I_Francena_Casere

Napoleon I Francena Cāsere oððe Napoléon Bonaparte (wæs geboren þæs 15.
Wēodmōnþes þæs 1769. gēares – cwæl þæs 5. Þrimilcemōnþes þæs 1821.) wæs Frencisc
heretoga and rīca þe wearþ brēme under þǣre Frenciscan Onhebbinge and ōðrum
gelīcum wīgum.

Corsica þæt īegland wæs Napoleones gebyrdestede. Hē wæs geboren in Ajaccio byrg
in þǣm 1769. gēare, ānum wintre siþþan Francan hæfdon geboht þæt īegland fram
Genoa. His nama æt byrde wæs in þǣm Italiscan gereorde Napoleone di Buonoparte.
Þā eode hē on Francum nām hē Frencisce wīsan, Napoléon Bonaparte.

In þǣm 1779., æt ilde tīen wintra, fērde Napoleon tō þǣm cirican leornunghūse æt
Autun. Æfter Autun ēode hē tō þǣm heres leorninghūsum æt Briènne-le-Château and
þon þǣm æt Paris. He leornede tō wesenne feldwǣpengerēfa in Franclande.

In þǣm 1789. begann sēo Frencisce Tōwending and Napoleon ēode to Corsican, þǣr
wæs ungerec. In þǣm 1792. þā Loðewis XVIII Cyning wæs tōworpen and sēo Forme
Frencisce Cynewīse begann, genamode man Napoleon Hēafodmann.

Napoleones forme weorces ambiht wæs at Toulon, þā þegnede tō adrǣfenne Brittisce
and Spēonisce þrēatas fram þǣre hȳðe and þǣre byrg.

Tō Heretogan hædde hē micelne sige on Italie. He scōp þā Cisalpine Cynwīsan on
norþernre Italie and þā Heleuetisce Cynewīsan, þā seo Rōmānisce Cynewīse būton
þǣm Papiscan Rīce and þǣre Parthenopiscan Cynewīsan in eallre sūþernre Italie.
He gesōhte Ēastrīce þurh Alpis and be nīede nām Ēastrīce friþ and griþ wið
Francum.

In þǣm 1798. inswēog Napoleon Heretoga Ægypt. His liþ wæs be Horatio Nelson
adīleged æt Nīl Sǣfeohte and hē flēah on Francan.

In 1799, Bonaparte tōwearp þā Frenciscan Folcgesamnunge and leodwearde, and
gestaþoled hē þæt Consulatum, hwǣrin wæs hē se Forma Consul. Swa Consul reformed
hē þæt Francena rīce. He tōwendede eall stōwlicu rihtbēc and for rihte gesetede
hē ofer eallum Franclande þæt Code Napoleon. Þes Code Napoleon is nū þā grund
for riht ofer mæstum Europan, būton Bryten and Īrland.

Æfter fīf wintrum þæs Consulatum settede Napoleon corunbeag on his hēafod swa
Francena Casere.

In þǣr nigontieneþ gearhundrede forma tien gearum, forþsendede Napoleon þæs
Frenciscan Rīces herigas wiþ ælcum miclum Europiscan rīcum and underþeodede
Europe sigerōf in manigum beadwum, to bisene Austerlitz.

Napoleon Casere friþ gestaðolede ofer Europan, būton mid þǣm Bretwarum.
Francland þæt rīce beclyppede Francland, Holland, Tuscanie, Rōm and Dalmatie.
Napoleon wæs ēac Eotolwara Cyning. Ēastweard wǣron under þeodedan rīce; se Rīn
Āþgebēorscipe and Switzerland, and begeondan Warsaw Hēah Þeodenrīce (Polaland).
His brēþer and heretogum geaf hē cynestōlas geond Europan. His sweostru
gēmungedon æþelingas and cyningas. Prussia and Ēastrīce wǣron be niede mid him
in geþoftrædne.

Nōþylæs, þæt Geānlǣhte Cynerīce and Portugal onsōcon hine. On þǣm brime hæfde se
Bryttisca Cynelica Sciphere duguþmihte; Horatio Nelson forgrund Napoleones ligþ
æt Trafalgar Sǣfeohte and se Cynelice Sciphere besettede Frenciscan hyða þurh þā
gūþe. In Spēonlande and Portugal fēohtedon Bretware and Portugalþēod wiþ
Napoleones hergas and ādrufon hie fram þǣm landum.

In 1812 inswēog Napoleon Russland. Hēr endede his wīgblēd. His Micela Here
(Grande Armée) drēag cwealm in þǣre fierdinge and āwierpede nǣfre. In 1813 cōmon
þā Germaniscan Rīcu and Russland and sige hædde wiþ þǣm Frenciscan þrēat æt
Leipzig. Þā in 1814 inswēog hie Francland. In þǣm ilcan gēare fullfremmede
Wellington Spēonland to ofergān and inswēog Francland fram þæm sūþen.

Þā his fiend inswēog Francland flīemede Napoleon. Man him anām to Elban seo īeg
and him hie geag swa hiere brego.

Æfter læs þonne ānum gēare, ætlēop hē fram Elban and feng eft to rīce. He
ācwicede his Rīces hergas and fōr forþ tōweardes Bryseles. Wellington hine
oferdrāf æt þǣre Waterloo Beadwe on 18 Sēremōnaþ 1815. Þeos firstgemearc wæs "þā
Hundred Dagas".

Þā endemeste siexe gearu Napoleones Līfes spent hē on Sancte Elene Īege
ofersigon be þæm Brittiscan gereca. He forferede of gehrif cancere on 5
Þrimilcemōnaþ 1821.

In 1840 brōhte Loðwic-Philippus Cyning þæs Caseres bānas tō Paris. He licþ nū in
lof in Les Invalides.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/N%C4%ABwenglisc

Sēo Nīwenglisce sprǣc (on Nīwenglisce: English) is Westgermanisc sprǣc, þe on
Englalande ārās. Hēo belimpeþ, swā sēo Þēodisce sprǣc and sēo Niðerlendisce
sprǣc tō þǣm Westernan twige þāra Germaniscra sprǣca.

Nū is Englisc sēo brādoste gesprǣdede sprǣc þǣre worulde, and hæfþ ymbe þæt
getæl sprecera þe Cīnisc hæfþ. In fela landum biþ Nīwenglisc sēo ǣreste fremðe
sprǣc gelǣred (Sēo Englisc (Scōl)) and is sēo ambihtlice sprǣc þāra mǣstena
betwixfolclicra gesetednessa. Fela þissa gesetednessa habbaþ ōðra ambihtlica
sprǣca. Nīwenglisc prōfaþ hēodæg swā woruldsprǣc.

Tōdæg biþ Englisc fram 340 millionena sprecenda swā mōdorsprǣc gesprecen. Gif
man īeceþ þā æfterran sprecend, cymþ man tō ymbe 510 millionena sprecenda.

Englisc cymþ of þǣre Ealdre Seaxiscre sprǣce and sibbum þēowsprǣcum þe wǣron
gebrōht tō Brytene fram Germaniscum gesittendum of syndrigum dǣlum norþwestes
Þēodisclandes. Sēo frume Englisce sprǣc wæs gehrinen folgiendlīce fram twǣm ȳðum
onrǣses. Se ǣresta onrǣs wæs fram sprecerum sprǣca Scedelendisces twiges þæs
Germaniscan sprǣchīredes, þe gebȳrdon in dǣlas Brytene in þǣm 8an and 9an
ieldum. Se ōðer onrǣs wæs mid Normandigsǣtum in þǣre 11an ielde, þe cynn
sprǣcon, Ealdes Frencisces.

Be þǣm Engliscan-Seaxiscan Cranice, ymbe þæt gēar 449, wǣron þā Engle gelaðode
fram Wyrtgeorne tō helpenne him wiþ þā Pihtas. Ongēan hira help gelendode hē þǣm
Englum in sūþēastum dǣle. Æfter sōhte hē māran help, and forþǣm cōmon þā Seaxe,
Engle, and Geate. Se Cranic spricþ ymbe fylgendne incyme gesittendra, þe
staðelodon on ende seofon cynerīcu. Tōdæges scōlerscipe behogeþ mǣst þisses
spelles tō bēonne spell and fram lēodweardrace gedōne.

Þās Germaniscan infarend oferrīcsodon þā fruman Celtisce sprǣcendan wuniend, þā
sprǣca þāra ālifdon mǣste on Scotland, Wealas, Cornweall, and Īrland. Þā
folcsprǣca, gesprecena fram þǣm ingengum, macodon þæt, þe man hēt Eald Englisc,
þe efenlǣcþ suma rimanþēowsprǣca, in (nū) landum norþwestes Þēodisclandes and
þāra Niðerlanda. Ufor wæs sēo sprǣc gehrinen fram þǣre Norþgermaniscre sprǣce
Norene, þǣra Wīcinga gesprecen, þe on þone norþēastan dǣl gesǣtton (sēo
Georfic).

For þǣm folgiendum 300 gēarum æfter þǣre Norþmandiscan Geþringunge in 1066
sprǣcon þā Norþmandiscan cyningas and sēo hēa duguþ cynn Frencisces āne. Micel
getæl Norþmandiscra worda wǣron inbrōht in Eald Englisc. Se Norþmandisca gehrine
gefæstnode þā gangendan hwierfunge þǣre sprǣce ofer fylgendum ieldum, oþ þǣre
sprǣce, nū Middelenglisc gehāten. Lareowas þǣre tunges lare ne laerdon;
leorneres heora spraec ne leornode. For þon þe þæt folc þāra Norþmanna þeowas
ȝeƿurdon, swa ealswa mot mon þæt 'Niwenglisc' beter 'þeowenglisc' ȝehatan.

In þǣre 15an ielde gewende sēo Micele Selfswēgendwendung þæt Middelenglisc, ēac
mid Lundencyndre sprǣce in lēodwearde and tōþegnunge, and þǣre
regolunggefremmunge gemǣlunge. Nīwenglisc cann gespyred bēon on bæc tō þǣre tīde
Willelmes Shakespeares.

Sēo Nīwenglisce sprǣc is dǣl þæs westernan undertwiges þæs Germaniscan twiges
þæs Indiscan-Europiscan sprǣca cynnes. Feorr þǣra Englisclǣhtan sprǣca swā Tok
Pisin oþþe Bislama, sind þā nīehstan Nīwenglisces Scyttisc (Lallans), mǣste on
Scotland and dǣl Norðernes Īrlandes gesprecen, and þǣræfter Fresisc, on
Þēodiscland and on þǣm Niðerlandum gesprecen. Swā Nīwenglisc is Scyttisc riht
æftergenga Englisces (Englisc-Seaxisc).

Ōðra sibba sprǣca, ac unsibbran þonne Fresisc oþþe Scyttisc, sind Þēodisc,
Seaxisc, Niðerlendisc, Scedelendisca sprǣca, and Afrikaanisc. Manig Frencisc
word sind ēac andgietfullicu tō Nīwenglisces sprecende (ac mid ōðrum
rihtstefne), for þǣm þe Nīwenglisc bedranc ormǣtlic rīm worda fram Frencisce
þurh þā Norþmandisce sprǣce æfter þǣre Norþmandiscan Oferswīðrunge and rihtlīce
of Frencisce in æfterrum ieldum; þǣrfor sind fela worda swīðe nēah þǣm
Frencisce, mid smalum wrītungscēadungum (on wordendungum oþþe mid Ealdes
Frencisces wrītungum, asf.), ēac swā hwīlum scēadunga on mǣnunge.

Englisc grammaticcræft hafaþ lȳtele gebīegunge in efenlǣcnesse mid ōðrum
Indoeuropicum sprǣcum. Tō bisene hæfþ Nīwenglisc, ungelīc Þēodisce,
Niðerlendisce, oþþe Rōmāniscum sprǣcum nān grammatisc cynn and nāne
tōgeīecendlice ānrǣdnesse. cāsu mearcung is æthwōn fullīce gedwinen of þǣre
sprǣce and ālifþ mǣste on þā bīnaman. Þā cynn strangra worda (t.b.
sprecan/spræc/sprǣcon/gesprecen) wiþ þā cynn wācra worda þe sēo sprǣc of
Germanisce ierfde is on weorðe gedwinen and þā lāfa gebīegunge (swā
manigfealdlicu mearcung) wurdon regolfæsta.

Þā seolfan tīd þǣre gebīegunge weorþgedwīnung in Englisce, scōp sēo sprǣc māran
getrēowunge in wīsan swā mōdword and worddiht tō getācnienne grammatisce
mǣnunge. Helpendu word brȳcþ man tō mearcienne tācnu swā frignunga, negativa, þā
underþēodendlican stefn, and gengende tīd

Mid Englisce brȳcþ man þā lǣdene stæfrǣwe būtan accentum, ac mid elþēodigum
wordum, swā résumé (Frencisc) cann man mid accentum wrītan. Mid manigum wordum,
swā night oþþe though is sēo wrītungwīse stǣrlicu (nā sprecendllicu), for þǣm þe
on Middelenglisce wrāt man night and though. Sēo wrītung worda oft ābȳgþ of hū
hīe gesprecen sind, and Nīwenglisc wrītung is oft geþōht sēo unēaðoste ǣnigra
sprǣca tō leornienne, in þǣm sprǣcum þe brūcaþ stæfrǣwa. Sēo Nīwenglisc
rihtwrītunge.

Englisc is ambihtsprǣc in þǣm fylgendum landum, þǣrin þæt getæl þāra
mōdorsprecera is gewriten, hwǣr cūþ:

Englisce sprǣc þegnaþ tō ēacan swā lingua franca in þǣm folgiendum landum and
landscipum:



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mentha_aquatica

Balsminte (Mentha aquatica) is perennial plante in þǣm mentha cynde and is
gemǣne þurhūt Europe, būtan in þǣm ȳtemestan Norðe.

Hēo wiexþ ymbe 90 cm on hīehþe, although it may reach heights of 150 cm when
supported by taller vegetation and has a distinctly minty smell. It has ovate to
ovate-lanceolate, green (sometimes purplish), opposite, toothed, veined leaves
which can be either hairy or hairless. Þā stefnas sind oft purpurene. Flowers
are tiny, densely crowded, purple, tubular, pinkish to lilac in colour and bloom
from July to September. Water mint is pollinated by insects, but can easily be
propagated through root cuttings, like other species of mint.

Swā se ōðer nama wæterminte tācnaþ, findeþ man wætermintan in þǣm scealdum
margins and channels of streams, rivers, pools, dykes, ditches, canals, wet
meadows, marshes and fens. If the plant grows in the water itself, it rises
above the surface of the water. It generally occurs on mildly acid to calcareous
(it is common on soft limestone) mineral or peaty soils.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ma%C3%B0ante

Maðante (Frencisc: Mantes) is Francena burg sēo līð be Sigene ēa, þær iernð þā
strēam niþere Paris.

Maðante stōd healfweg betwēonum þǣm stōle þāra Eorles of Normandige æt Roðeme
and þāra Francena Cyninges æt Paris and in manigum wigum sōht eorl oððe cyning
þās burg.

In 1086 cwōm Willelm cyng of Normandige, þærin wæs hē ēac Eorl, into France mid
fyrde 7 hergode uppan his agenne hlaford Philippe þam cynge 7 sloh of his mannon
mycelne dæl 7 forbearnde þa burh Maðante 7 ealle þa halige mynstres þe wæron
innon þære burh.

In þǣm Hund Gearena Wige hwierfedon Engle and Francas Maðante oft. Philippus II
Francena Cyning, oðre naman Augustus, forðferde æt Maðante on 14 Sōlmōnað 1223.

On 9 August 1944, Patton Hertoga and his Þridde Here nām Maþantes brycg and þes
wæs þāra gefylceapena ǣrrsta brycghēafod ofer Sigene. Micel gebrōcenes wæs in
þǣre byrig and þæn cwōm frið wæs be niedemicel geweorc gedōn.

Mantes-sur-Seine se burgscipe wæs mid Gassicourt geāned in 1930 and
Mantes-Gassicourt wæs þæs nīwan burgscipes nama. In 1953 hit nām nīw naman:
Mantes-la-Jolie (se is "Manðante sēo Fægre").



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lundene

Lundene (Lǣden: Londinium, Nīwenglisc: London) is hēafodburg þæs Geānedan
Cynerīces and Englalandes, and is on ealre worulde þāra grīetestra burga ān. Hit
hæfþ seofon þūsendu þūsenda lēoda in Grēatrum Lundene (hātte Lundeneras).

His fyrmesta nama wæs Londinium, hēafodburg þæs Rōmāniscan underrīces þæs naman
Britannia wæs, and hit wierþ hēafodburg þæs Bryttiscan Rīces.

Lundenes ǣrest tūnscipe wæs se stede þǣre ealdan Romaniscan ceastre in þǣm
weallum. Under Ælfrede cyninge setledon þā Lundenware in þǣm weallum fram hira
ealdum wic, se is Ealdwic. Oþþæt þā wealla habbaþ gewiðged, sēo stōwe,
Lundenceaster, ābīdeþ swā Lundenes heorte and cēapung hēafodburg tō Bretene and
þǣre worulde.

Þæt micele ceasterisce land ymbe Lundene is Māre Lunden. Hit befēhþ nēan ealle
Middelseaxe, micele dǣlas geond Sūþrigan, Cent, and Ēastseaxe and Heortfordscīre
dǣlas.

Ofer Māran Lundene rīcsaþ þæt Māran Lundene Gerec, þæt is þæt Lundene Burgweald
and sēo Lundene Samnung.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Heafodburg

On stēormǣle is hēafodstōl (ēac hēafodburg and hēafodburh hātte) sēo hēafodlice
burg oþþe tūn gesibb hire wealde. Hēo is nēan ā sēo burg þe līchāmlīce befēhþ
þæt setlærn and þæt gemōtærn þæs setles wealdes and is geseted be lage.

Þā setlu wealdes on mægenum underrīciscum dōmum sind gewunelīce hēafodstōlas
gehāten, ac æfter læssum wealdendum underdǣlum, word swelce fylces tūn, fylces
setl, oþþe byrig setl sind ēac gebrocen.

Þǣr sind maniga gelimpunga þǣr rīcu oþþe ōðre ānstandendas habbaþ manige
hēafodstōlas. On Sūþaffrican, tō bȳsne, se wealdenda hēafodstōl is Pretoria, se
lagsettenda hēafodstōl is Næsstūn, and se dēmenda hēafodstōl is Blōtsmanwelle,
þe is þæt gelimp þæs gesēmes þætte gesciepede þæt Sūþaffrican Gæd on 1910.

On swelcum gelimpungum is sēo burg þe hielt þone wealdenda hēafodstō gewunelīc
understanden wesan se "rīcisca hēafodstō" ongemang elemanna. Tō bȳsne, Santiago
is understanden wesan se hēafodstōl of Cilan þēah hire Gemōt is in Falparegse.

Tō hēafodlicum stede wealdes þæs landscipes oþþe rīces, se hēafodstōl
gecyndelīce atihteþ þā stēormǣllīce geānmētedum and him þāra cræftas sind
þorftene tō welwyrcendum wealde swelce ǣswutolas, tīdingwrīteras, and folclices
rǣdes cneordlǣcendas. Ieldre hēafodstōlas habbaþ ēac oft grōwen on fornytte
stēormǣllice, līfwīsisce, oþþe andgietfule stōlas. Swelc is hūru sēo gelimpung
Parises on Franclande and Buenos Airese Argentinan ongemang rīciscra
hēafodstōla, and Irkutskes oþþe Saltlagburge on Utā on heora landscipum.
Nāþȳslæs swelc hālgung mæg wesan wiðerwinnende. Sēo settung of Brasilie in
Brasiles inlande wæs gedōn be dǣl tō ēowienne þæs gewealdes gesundrodnesse fram
þǣm crodenan and gewemedan ealdan hēafodstōle Rio de Janeiro. Þæt geweald
Sūþcorēan gehēt on 2004 þæt hit wege his hēafodstōl fram Seoule tō
Geongi-Gongtscu — þēah þe þæt word "Seoul" self mǣnþ "hēafodstōl" in þǣre
Corēiscan sprǣce.

Sēo gæderung wealdlices and feohhweorfunglices oþþe līfweglices dōmes nis nānum
wīsum woruldwīde. Þēawlice hēafodstōlas magon feohhweorfunglīce aþēostrian fram
bifylclicum ofersteallum, swā swā hit gelamp mid Thēbane, þe aþēostrode fram
Alexandrie, Nantscing fram Scanghai, oþþe Edinburg fram Glasgowe. Þæt geafeall
cynecynnes oþþe līfweges cūðe ēacswā wyrcean þone dēaþ his hēafodstōles, swā swā
hit gelamp be Bablōnie and Cahocie. Ēac wǣron manige nīwlice hēafodstōlas,
swelce Abuja and Ottawa, rǣdlīce geseted onweg fram feohhweorfunglicum stōwum
and nabbaþ gīet weaxen grēate tō nīwum feohhweorfunglicum burgum.

Andefen þǣra ēacnunge nīwlicra cāserrīca and geþēodrīca, hēafodstōlas habbaþ
worden tācn for heora rīcum heora gewealdu,, and gesetede be gewealdlicum
andgiete. Ungelīce midealdum ceastrum, þe wǣron geset ǣghwǣr wealda hēold his
gemōt, is sēo cēosung, edsettung, staðoling, oþþe se onfeng nīwlices
hēafodstōkes carful gelimpung. Tō bȳsne:



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harold_III_Norrena_Cyning

Harald Sigurdsson oððe Harold III (c. 1015 – 25 September 1066) wæs Norrena
Cyning of 1046 oð 1066 þær forþferde he on wælfelde. Æfterylde geafen him þone
etternaman Harðráði, se is “Heard ræd”. His ærrsta cynedōm wæs in Magnes dagum
cyning þær wæs Harold undercyning, ac æfter Magnes deaþ in 1047 wæs Harold
Norþmanna ānwealda.

In his dagum sohtede Harold ēac cynedom on Denum and on Englum ac he næfde
gelimpe in þissum. Beforan þe he wæs cyning, ferde Harold on wræcce. In þissum
wintrum wæs he heretoga on Russum æt Cænugearde, þe rīce gefundon be Swēonum,
and þæræft fōr he to Constantinopolis and þegned swa heretōga ofer þæm Wæringa
Wearde þæs Constantinopolis Rīces.

Þær wæs he fiftiene winter, in 1030, feahte Harold æt þære Stiklestad Beadwe mid
his healf-brodor Anlaf Haroldsson. Anlaf wolde eft gewinnan þone Norðmanna
cynedōm, þe he hæfde gelosen to þæm Dena cyning Cnut se Micel fore twegen
winter. On þæm wælfelde fremmeden Cnut sige, and Harold be niede fōr on wræcce
on Russe. On Russum anām he his byrne in þæm here þæs Hēah Brego Eoreslaf se
Wīs, and rās he to beon hēafodman. Ymbe 1034 fōr Harold to Constantinopolis. In
Constantinopolis, eftsōn rās to weodenne heretoga þæs Cāseres Wæringa Weard, and
he feaht in cempan on Wendelsǣ, in þære Lǣssan Asie, in Sicilie and on Pulgarum
(þær wæs his binama "Pulgareonbærna", and gewene ēac in þæm Hāligan Lande. In
Constantinopolis abrāc selefriþe and Harold him befeald in strīþe in þæm
cynehūs. Bēc secgað ðe Harold self ablindede Michael V Cāsere forþæm þe Zoe Cwēn
mōt habban weald in þæm rīce in his stede.

Æt Constantinopolis weard Harold swið rīce. He afōr of þære ceastre in 1043/4,
and fōr eft on Russe ðe he mōt sēcan cynedōm on Norþmannum. Þær cwōm Harold eft
on Norþmenn fund he þe Anlafes bastard sunu Magnus I Norrena Cyning, Haroldes
nefa, hæfde aworpen þā Dena of þæm lande and wæs þeodcyning, ac Harold sōhtede
þone cynehelm. Magnus nolde feohtan his agan ēam and begen gecwaþen þe Magnus
and Harold wolde bēon cyningas ætgædre and begen wolden bedælan Haroldes gold.
Æfter ānum winter forþferde Magnus and his wille wæs þe Harold biþ Norrena
cyning and Swegn biþ Dēna cyning. Þy weard Harold Norþweges anwealdend.

Harold ne ricsode on Dēnum forþæm þe in þæm rīce wealdede Swegn. Harold hæfde
crafunge for þæm cynedōme and ælc sumor oð 1064 fremmede he scipfyrdung on
Dēnum. Oððeæt ðe he hæfde sige on wælfelde næfre sæt he on þæm cynestōl þæs
rīces. Eftsōn æfter þe he ofgeaf his Denisc crafinge, cwōm him Tostig Godwinson,
se wæs Haroldes II Engla Cyninges brōðor, and Tostige gehātt Harold Sigurdsson
to sēcan þone Engliscan cynedōm. Tostig swār his trōþ to Harold and Norrena
Cyning brōhtede his sciphere on Eoferwicescīre in Hærfestmonaþ 1066. Þær
gewunnode Harold micel sige ofer þæm Englum æt Fulford Fēoht. His wynn endode æt
gūþe æt Standfordbrycge on 25 Hærfestmonaþ, þær feall he on þæm wælfelde, and
wæs be Haroldes Godwinessones þrēate geslēan.

Haroldes dēaþ at Standfordbrycge, hwæræt endode þā onswegunge, oft secgð man is
se ende þære Wicing Ylde. Harold is ēac gemæne held to have been se endmesta
micla Wicingcyning, and sum mann secgþ se endmesta micla Wicing.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grytviken

Grytviken is sē formesta tunstede on Sūþgeorgie. Hit standeþ on Ēadweard Cyning
Cofan in Cumbraland Byhte æt þære īege norþēasternum sǣrīman. Man hycgð ðe
Grytviken is þære īege tilosta hæfen. Æt Grytvikne is brād wong for boldum and
fersc wæter.

Gēo wæs Grytviken hwælhuntoþ wic and Sūþgeorgie mǣsta tūn. Þære īege gerecstōl
æt Ēadweard Cyning Næsse līþ nēah.

Carl Anton Larsen, Norþisc fiscere sciphlāford staþolode Grytvikenwic on 16
Blōtmōnaþ 1904 swa hwælhuntoþwic.

Grytvikenwic staðolede Carl Anton Larsen, Norþisc scipere, on 16 Winterfylleþ
1904 swa hwælhuntoþwic for his begang Compañía Argentina de Pesca. Swīðe
gesundful wæs hē. In þæm forman sumre fangon his menn þæs wices 195 hrānas.
Elpendseolcas ēac huntedon hie for fætte. Ymbe 300 menn weorcedon æt þæm wice in
his bisgum gearum, in þæm sūþernum sumre of Winterfylleþ oð Hrēþmōnaþ. Fēa menn
abad þone winter to maintain þā bātas and weorchūs.

Æt Sandefjord in Norþweg wæs Carl Anton Larsen, Grytviknes fundere, geboren, ac
hē weard Bryttisc ceastermann in 1910.

Under Larsenes hande, forþæm þe he wæs wicnere þæs Compañía Argentina de Pesca,
wæs Grytviken getimbrod. Getimbrod wæs hit be siextig Norþmannum in ōþrum healf
monaþum of 16 Blōtmōnaþ 1904.

Larsen ceas þone stede in his bisæcce in 1902 þær he wæs sciphlāford þæs
Swēoniscan scipes Antarctic. Þone naman "Grytviken" (Pottcofa) geaf Swēonisc
eorðwita Johan Gunnar Andersson þe gehāwode Geþacasteortes dǣl and fūnde manig
þing fram seolhhuntena hūsum and weorce, to bysene lytel bāt and costnungpottas
to seðenne seolhele.

Ernest Shackleton cwōm to Grytvikne æt þæm aginnesse his Woruldrīces
Geondantarctiscan Færeld and eftcwōm in 1916 æt his ende, froforsecend for his
sciplēasum mannum on wræcce on Elpendīege, be Antarctice. Of Grytvikne brōhtede
Shackleton Cilisc scip to þære feorre īege and his menn brōhtede on earde.

Binnan þære Folclandgewinne Grytviken fōn Argentinisc þrēat on 3 Ēastermonaþ
1982 æfter scortum beadwe mid Bryttiscum Cynelicum Scipfeðum. Þā Cynelica
Scipfeðan, SAS and SBS eftnām þone wic æfter þrim wucum būtan sceote.

Sēo forma beadu begann þær Argentiniscan scipu Guerrico and Bahía Paraíso
afeahton þā twegen and twentig menn þæs Cynelican Scipfeðena werod æt Grytvikne.
Æfter twæm stund hæfde þā Cynelica Scipfeðan severely damaged þæt Guerrico and
geāsceotedon Argentinisc helicopter. Þrie Argentinisc menn wæron ofslean and
oþru gewunded. On þære Bryttiscum healfe wæs ān mann gewunded. Argentinaware nām
þone Bryttiscan ealdor and manig menn of þære īege, ac 15 Brettas abādon ofer
þāra Argentinawara handum and næfre sæledon þā feond ealles Sūþgeorgie to
nimenne: Fugolīeg herewic, and feldwicu æt Schlieperbyht, Lyellīsēa and Sctes
Andreasbyht healdon Brettcynn.

On 25 Ēastermonaþ, sē Cynelica Sciphere sceat þā Argentinisce undersæbāt ARA
Santa Fe and hie nām æt Sūþgeorgie. Sē Argentinisca werod in Grytvikne alag
hiera ærmas būton sceotum. On þæm niehstan dæge geaf his handgang sē werod æt
Leþhæfne.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Geanl%C7%A3ht_C%C8%B3ner%C4%ABce

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce Grēatre Brytene and Norþīrlandes is cȳnerīce ofer norþenam
Europan. Man nemneþ hit sceortlīce Geānede Cynerīce oþþe UK (of Nīwum Englisce:
United Kingdom).

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce līþ on garsecges īeglandum be westnorðan Europan. His mǣste
īeg is Bryten (Nīwenglisc: Great Britain) and his oþru Īrland hwǣron licgaþ
siexe scīra þæs rīces. Eall ymbe þissum sǣrīman sind manigfealdum īege and
īegoþe.

Cynerīce is þæt Geānede Cynerīce, þærof is Elisabeþ II Cwēn. His hēafodstōl is
Westmynster (oþþe Lunden þærof is Westmynster nū dǣl). Sēo Cwēn hæfþ hiere stōl
hēr and hiere hām æt Windlesōran.

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce wearþ gescapen æfter syndrigum "Acts of Union", þæt habbaþ
þā sweotolan rīċu Englaland, Wēalas, Scotland, and Īrland geānlǣht under ān
rǣdena in Lundene. Mǣst þæs landes Īrlandes tōsyndrode of þǣm Geānlǣhtan
Cynerīce in 1922, and tōdæg is Īrland Cynewīse, ac se northēasterna dǣl þæs
īeglandes, Norðerne Īrland gehāten, gewunaþ in þǣm Geānedan Cynerīce.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/F%C4%ABfeldor

Fīfeldor (Denisc: Ejderen, Germanisc: Die Eider) is ēa sēo iernþ geond þǣm
landhals betwuh Germanie and Ēotalande. Nū līþ Fīfeldor on Sillende-Holstān,
Þēodsc land.

Þǣre ēa æwielme is nēah Bordesholme and flēowaþ be Kiel on Ostsǣ ecge, ac þonan
ierneþ westweard and ūt on Norþsǣ. Fīfeldores middeldǣl brycð sē Kiel Scipryne.

Gēo wæs Fīfeldor landgemære betwuh Angelcynn and Seaxe beforan þe þā mægþu
segledon ofer brād brime Breten secend, and lang þæræfter wæs he landgemære
betwuh Denemearc and Germanie. In æftergearum wæs hē mære betwuh Sillende and
Holstāne, begen heretogarīce under þǣm Dēna cynedōme.

In 1864 onswōgon Prēosse Sillende and Holstān and gehiersomedon eall þā land
oððæt ðe manige Dēne þǣr wonedon. Siððan þǣm geare hæfþ eall Fīfeldor in
Þeodsclande gelagen.

On īege on Fīfeldor, swa secgað ealdu tala, stōd Offa Engla Cyning and feoht
twegen æþelingas þāra Swæfa þone mearc to heoldenne. Man secgþ þeos beadu wæs æt
Hæþe.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Englum

Englaland is an mægþ (þe man England on nīwan Englisc hæt) þe is se dæl þæs
Geanedan Cynerices (þe man the United Kingdom on Modernan Englisc hæt). Hit norþ
ligeþ ymb Scottwara land and ymb Walewara land west and þus hit hafaþ
land-gemære mid Scottwara lande (þe man Scotland on Modernan Englisc hæt) and
mid Walewara lande (þe man Wales on Modernan Englisc hæt). Hit ligeþ on
westan-norþan Europe. Sæs þe þæt Englaland utanymblian sind be-westannorþan se
Irisc Sæ (the Irish Sea) and be-westansuþan se Celtlic Sæ (the Celtic Sea).

Englalandes nama cymþ of þǣm Englum, anum þriora mægþa Germania þe hie ofcomon
to Englande, oþerum twæm mægþum þe hie ofcomon to Englalande to eardian sind
Eald-Seaxa mægþ and Iota mægþ, þe habbaþ Englaland gesetled þǣm 5an and 6an
gēarhundredum. Siþþan 1707, þe man Grēate Bryten scōp, nu Englaland is ungewilde
þeod.

Englaland wæs in gēardagum cynerīce. Æþelstan cyning wæs sē ǣrresta cyning eall
Englacynn to geānlǣcenne in ānum rīce. Englalandes endemestan undercyning
aflīemed Ēadred Engla Cyning and Englarīce wæs an.

Mid Scottarīce wæs Englarīce geānlǣhte be Anne Cwēne in 1707, Grēate Bryten
Cynerīce to scieppenne.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/England

Englaland is an mægþ (þe man England on nīwan Englisc hæt) þe is se dæl þæs
Geanedan Cynerices (þe man the United Kingdom on Modernan Englisc hæt). Hit norþ
ligeþ ymb Scottwara land and ymb Walewara land west and þus hit hafaþ
land-gemære mid Scottwara lande (þe man Scotland on Modernan Englisc hæt) and
mid Walewara lande (þe man Wales on Modernan Englisc hæt). Hit ligeþ on
westan-norþan Europe. Sæs þe þæt Englaland utanymblian sind be-westannorþan se
Irisc Sæ (the Irish Sea) and be-westansuþan se Celtlic Sæ (the Celtic Sea).

Englalandes nama cymþ of þǣm Englum, anum þriora mægþa Germania þe hie ofcomon
to Englande, oþerum twæm mægþum þe hie ofcomon to Englalande to eardian sind
Eald-Seaxa mægþ and Iota mægþ, þe habbaþ Englaland gesetled þǣm 5an and 6an
gēarhundredum. Siþþan 1707, þe man Grēate Bryten scōp, nu Englaland is ungewilde
þeod.

Englaland wæs in gēardagum cynerīce. Æþelstan cyning wæs sē ǣrresta cyning eall
Englacynn to geānlǣcenne in ānum rīce. Englalandes endemestan undercyning
aflīemed Ēadred Engla Cyning and Englarīce wæs an.

Mid Scottarīce wæs Englarīce geānlǣhte be Anne Cwēne in 1707, Grēate Bryten
Cynerīce to scieppenne.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emma_Goldman

Emma Goldman (wæs geboren þæs 27. þæs Ǣrran Līðan þæs 1869. gēares on Liþþuanie
- cwæl þæs 14. Hrēþmōnþes þæs 1940. Torontwe on Canadan) wæs Geānedrīcisc
wealdlīste rǣdes fyrðrestre, friðes fyrðestre, frēos hǣmedes fyrðrestre, wīfa
rihta fyrðrestre, and godungelīfestre. Ēac is hēo brēme for hire byldunge
ungerne hǣstra onhebbinga.

On þǣm 1917. gēare wæs hēo gebroht on carcerne tū gēar on þǣm Geāndum Rīcum for
þȳ hēo wolde byldan menn tō ascūninge þǣre heres fornȳdinge. Siþþan hēo fram þām
carnerne cwōm wæs hēo fram burgweardum gehæfted and forsent tō hire ēðle
Russlande, ēac hundredum ōðerra hāda. Ǣrost awreðode hēo þā Bolsceficiscan
onhebbinge, ac æfter þǣre Cronstates onhebbinge wende hēo hire þōht and wrēgde
þā Bolsceficas for heora hǣste wiþ frēo sprǣce and frēo stēormǣl. Hēo wrāt þæt
hēo þǣr sēah on þǣre bēc My Disillusionment in Russia (on Englisce hātte Se Ende
Mīnre Bescwīcinge on Russlande).



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Denisc_and_Nor%C3%BEwegisc_st%C3%A6fr%C7%A3w

Sēo Denisce and Norþwegisce stæfrǣw is gestaðelod on þǣre Lǣdenan stæfrǣwe and
hæfþ 29 bōcstafa:

Se bōcstæf Å wæs inlǣded in Norþwegisc in 1917, nām steall þæs Aa. Gelīce wæs se
bōcstæf Å inlǣded in Denisc in 1948, ac the final decision on its place in the
alphabet was not made. The initial proposal was to place it first, before A. Its
place as the last letter of the alphabet, as in Norwegian, was decided in 1955.
Þone ǣrran twibōcstæf Aa findeþ man forþ nū in namum and ealdum cartum and gǣþ
nū swā sēo rihte þurhwendung, gif se bōcstæf nis gehende for mechaniscum racum.
Man handlaþ hine gelīc Å in stæfrǣwlic sorting, and handlaþ nā gelīc twǣm
nēahlicum bōcstafum A.

The difference betwēonan þǣre Deniscan-Norþwegiscan and þǣre Swēoniscan stæfrǣwe
is, þæt Swēonisc brȳcþ the variant Ä instead of Æ, and the variant Ö instead of
Ø — similar to Þēodisce. Also, the collating order for þissum þrim bōcstafum is
different: Å, Ä, Ö. Some scholars therefore have argued that Ä/Æ and Ö/Ø are
mere glyph variants of the same letters and should thus be encoded the same.

Additionally, in current Danish and Norwegian, W is now recognized as a separate
letter from V. In Denisce, wæs sēo oferhlēapung fullendod in 1980, before that
the W was merely considered to be a variation of the letter V and words using it
were alphabetized accordingly (e.g.: "Wales, Vallø, Washington, Wedellsborg,
Vendsyssel"). A common Danish children's song ymbe þā stæfrǣwe sægþ still states
þæt sēo stæfrǣw hæfþ 28 bōcstafa; the last line reads 28 skal der stå, i.e.
"that makes twenty-eight". Since 1980, the number of letters has been 29.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bloomsd%C3%A6g

Bloomesdæg (Nīwenglisc: Bloomsday) is gemynding þærin mōt man begellan þæs līfes
James Joyce Īrisc writere and þes dæg is gemearcod in ælcum geare on þæm 16.
dæge monaþes. On þissum dæge eftlibbað menn þa belimpas þa þærof wrāt Joyce in
his bēc Ulysses. Eall se spell þære bēc takes place on 16 Seremōnaþ 1904 in
Difeline and his underburgum and forþæm heoldeþ man Bloomesdæg on þæm ilcan dæg
in ælcum geare 16 June in þære byrig. Þæs dæges naman is on þære bēc heafodman,
Leopold Bloom.

Joyce cēas the date 16 Seremōnaþ 1904 forþæm þe on þæm dæge fōr he ūt couting
Nora Barnacle heo wæs later his brȳd; hie wadedon to Ringsend Difelin suburb.

Se ærresta gewrit ymbe Bloomesdæge find man in epistol be Joyce to Miss Weaver
of 27 Seremōnaþ 1924: "There is a group of people who observe what they call
Bloom's day - 16 June."

On þæm dæg fiftige geare æfter 50th anniversary þære bēc belimpum gegædrede John
Ryan (artist, critic, elehūsweard and staðolere of Envoy magazine) and Brian
O'Nolan bōcwritere mid hiera frēondum for dæglang pilgrimage andlang þone
Ulysses ryne. Mid him wæron Patrick Kavanagh, Anthony Cronin, Tom Joyce (se wæs
tōþlæcce and James Joyces geswēor) and AJ Leventhal (Bōcere of Þrinesse
Felwascipe on Difeline). Hie hæfde Ryan twone mearhgetogne wægnas, of þæm
ealdtīdes wīsan þærin fōron Bloom and his friend in Ulysses þe hie drīfen to þæm
earman Paddy Dignames byrgen. Þes frēonhēap sōhtede to farenne ymbe þære byrig
þurh eall þone dæg, þe hie begaþ in turn þā stedas þæræt belamp þing in þære
bēc, and þe hi enden be nihte in þæm burgstede þe ǣr wæs Difelines sceandhūsena
ende, swylce stede nemnede Joyce 'Nihttūn'. Se fare wæs forscrāf healfweg, þan
þā werige menn eode in þæt Bailey elehūs and abādon in þæm hūs in druncenne and
geflīte. Þæt Bailey hūs Ryan then owned. In 1967 installed he þær þā duru to No.
7 Ecclesstrǣte (Leopold Bloomes strǣtduru), æfter þe he hæfde rescued it from
demolition.

In Difelin befealdaþ se dæg missenlice þing ūt bōccræfte on on him sind Ulysses
bōcrǣdinga and plegas, elehūsrȳnas and oþra belimpas, and micel is be þæm James
Joyce Centre berēnod, þæt stent in þære Norþ Micelgeorgiusstrǣte (North Great
Greorge Street). Oft gewǣdað menn hie in Ēadweardylde hrægle to begellenne
Bloomesdæg, and þærin folgað hie Bloomes ryne ymbe Difelin be mearcum to bysene
Davy Byrne's elehūs. Sum mann hæfþ in his mōde gedihted hele bōcrǣding þære
helum bēc and þis meaht læstan oþer healf dæg.

On þæm Sunnandæg in 2004 beforan þæm hundteontigoþa "geardæg" þāra spelles
belimpa, cwōmon 10,000 menn on Difelines wunenda for frēom, open-air, full Irish
breakfast on O'Connell Street consisting of sausages, rashers, toast, beans, and
black and white puddings.

"Every year hundreds of Dubliners dress as characters from the book ... as if to
assert their willingness to become one with the text. It is quite impossible to
imagine any other masterpiece of modernism having quite such an effect on the
life of a city."

On Bloomsday 1982, Joyces cennundæges hundteontigoþa eardæg, sand RTÉ ungebrōcen
30-hour dramatic performance of the entire text of Ulysses on radio.

Siððan 1994 hæbbaþ Ungere in Szombathely haefþ man begoll Bloomesdæg forþæm þe
is seo burg se cenningstōw of Leopold Bloomes fæder, Virág Rudolf, emigrant
Ungarisc Iudea. Þis is gedōn æt þæm Iseum, Isis tempules lāf sēo is of Rēmiscum
yldum, and æt þæm Blum-mansion, begollen to Joyce siððan 1997, æt 40–41
Fő-strǣt, and þis hūs wæs ǣr geagen be Iudisc cynn be naman Blum.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bl%C5%8Dd%C4%93a_Gema%C3%B0el

Sēo Blōdēa Gemaðel wæs mǣre gemaðel forþcȳðed be Enoch Powell on 20 Ēastermōnaþ
1968. In gearum æfterweard cnawen he he his gemaþel 'se Beormingaham gemaðel' ac
tīdingscītas nemnedon hie Blōdēa fram wordum þærin.

In þæm æfne on 20 Ēastermōnaþ 1968, clipod Enoch Powell þone Gemæne Gemōt þæs
Westmidland Læppa Begealdenda Stēormælearn and hēr sprāc he wiþ lēorednesse in
Breten fram þære Þēodacynewīsan and wiþ rihtgesetnes wiþ toscēad. Powell wæs the
Behealdend Gemōtmann þæs Witenagemōtes for Heantun Sūþwest. Næfre sæd he 'blōd
ēa' ac he made allusion to a line from Æneid þære bēc be Uirgilius:

Þēos gemaþel wrōhtede wordsturm onmang st ēormaþlum and tīdingscītum and eall se
landfolc þingode on Enoch Powell. Ēadweard Heath se Behealdenda heretoga (se wæs
æfterweerd Forma Þegn) adrāf Powell of his hired, ac manig menn secgaþ þe
Powelles lof geaf þæm Behealdendum hiera sige in þæm gemǣnan ceosung in 1970.
Þæreft wæs Enoch Powell wiþercora to Heathes þegndōme.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Berewicsc%C4%ABr

Berewicscir is scīr on norþhealfe þæs Tuidi ea. Heo hæfþ mearc mid mid
Norþhymbralande be suðan, East Loðene and Midloðene be norðan. Be eastan is
særime. Berewicscir is seo suðeasternmest þara Scyttiscena scirena.

Berewicscir nimþ hiere naman fram Berewicburg, seo ær wæs micel sæport and
Berewicscire scirburg oððæt wæs hit gelosen to Englacyning endlice in 1482.

Berewicscir Scirgeþinge wæs uparæred in 1890. His ærest setl wæs in Dunse, æt
þæm ealdan Scirgerefa Stālærne.

Berewicscir nis nu gerecscir; se Scirgeþinge wæs geended in 1975. Nu feolþ heo
under þǣm Scyttisce Mearc geþingedome. Æfter 1975 oððæt 1995 wæron Berewicscire
nama, wæpen and mæst hiere gierde þurh boldgetale gebrucan.

Berewicscire scirburg, hwæræfter is hit genemed, wæs Berewic oððæt 1482, þa wæs
Berewicburg gelosen to Englum. (Man secgþ þe Berewic is nu burg in
Norþhymbralande.) Æfter 1482 wæs Berewicscire toþegnung gedon æt Dunse oððe æt
Laudere, oððæt in 1596 weard Grenehlǣw þa scirburg.

Berewicscir Scirgeþinge abaddon wæpengiefu in 1890. Se Lēo Hlāford Wǣpencyning
bryttade þone giefe in þæm ilcan geare. Þa wæpen gesceaweden beran in bende to
elme, seo wæs dæl þære wæpna Berewic-burgscipes, and wæs scild-cræftig gamen on
byriges and scire namum.

Oððæt ðe Berewicscire naman is be wealdlice gehyded, on þære scire folc nis he
geforged. Giet is The Berwickshire News gewídmærsed ælce wuce, and manige
gefērscipas and band habbað Berewicscir in hiera naman.

Se Berewicscir Burglufu Frygyld hegaþ gearlic Freoðiað Berewicscir Clæne Tilung,
gedemede ælc Þrimilcemonaþ. Nu tilaþ se Frygyld for radtæcne æt þæm ingangum
þære scire to secgenne 'Þu cymest in Berewicscire'



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beadu_%C3%BE%C3%A6s_Bogn

Seo Beadu þæs Bogne (Nīwenglisc: Battle of the Boyne) feahtan in 1690 twegen
crafendas þæs cynedōmes ofer Englum, Scottum and Īrum. Þās wæron Iacobus II and
Willelm III, forþæm þe in 1688 hæfde se Englisca Witenagemōt and se Scyttisca
Witenagemōt gesettedon Iacobus Cyning ūt of his cynedōme in þære Brēme Onwendung
ac in Īrland eft cwōm Iacobus mid Frenciscum fultume and þā cyninga þrēatum
hæfde hiera gārmittung in þæm lande.

Se wælfeld wæs in Lūþscīre, on Bogne ēa ofrum nēah Droheda (Īrlandes eastrīmes
hȳð). Willelm hæfde sige æt gūþe and hēr adrāf Iacobes menn swa micel in sige þe
Iacobus Cyning fliemede of Īrland on Francas. Æfter þissum feohte wæs fæst se
hild þæs Oncwedend Ealdordōmes on Īrum.

Sēo beadu wæs on 1 Mǣdmōnaþ 1690 in þæm eald, Iulianiscum Gerīmbēc" se is 11
Mǣdmōnaþ 1690 in þæm Gregorianiscum Gerīmbēc, oþþæt þe ǣr aleaf þe þes wæs 12
Mǣdmōnaþ on þæt ilcan dæge freolsiað Uladstires Oncwedendas þā Beadwe þǣm Boine.

For þisse garmittunge hefignesse is heo ān þāra gecyþed feohta in Bryttissum and
Iriscum stǣre and heo is heafodstede þære folclāre on Uladstire and for þæm
Orangehāde. Se Orangehād hæfð heafodstede todæg in freolsunge þā beadwe.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Asie

Asia is þǣre Eorðan grēatest worulddǣl in grīete and in landware, licgende
mǣstlic in þǣm norþernean and sūðernean healftryndlum. Hit þecþ 8.6% of Eorðan
fulne (oþþe 29.9% of hire lande) and mid ymbe 4 ðūsenda ðūsenda ðūsenda
onwunenda, hit behabbaþ 60% þā Eorðan tidgenge landware.

Asia is gemænelīc mearcaþ swā dǣl of land in Eurasia — mid þǣm westerneum þider
ende swā Europe — æt tō Suez Gedelfes ēastne, tō Riffenge Beorgum ēastne and
Caucasum þǣm Beorgum and hæfþ Caspia and Euxinus þā meras be sūþen. Hit is
endede be ēasten æt þǣm Sericus Garsecge, besūþen æt þǣm Indiscan Gārsecge and
benorþen be Īshæfe. Fram hire grīete and mise, is Asia māra ān mislic þing
ymbhabbende manig landas and lēoda þonne ānne þing.

Asia þisses welan tōscecgaþ micelne ongemang and wiþinnan his rīcu, forþæm his
grīete and grēatu manigu cynd, drohtaþas, stær and lēodwearda. For namede GDP,
Iapan hæfeþ grēatest welan worulddǣles, mid ōðerum in þære worulde, æfter þǣm
Geānedum Rīcum American. In strengþu for geēhtende, hæfeþ Cīna grēatest welan of
grīete in Asia and ōðerum grēatest in þære worulde.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C8%9Ce%C4%81nl%C7%A3ht_Cyner%C4%ABce

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce Grēatre Brytene and Norþīrlandes is cȳnerīce ofer norþenam
Europan. Man nemneþ hit sceortlīce Geānede Cynerīce oþþe UK (of Nīwum Englisce:
United Kingdom).

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce līþ on garsecges īeglandum be westnorðan Europan. His mǣste
īeg is Bryten (Nīwenglisc: Great Britain) and his oþru Īrland hwǣron licgaþ
siexe scīra þæs rīces. Eall ymbe þissum sǣrīman sind manigfealdum īege and
īegoþe.

Cynerīce is þæt Geānede Cynerīce, þærof is Elisabeþ II Cwēn. His hēafodstōl is
Westmynster (oþþe Lunden þærof is Westmynster nū dǣl). Sēo Cwēn hæfþ hiere stōl
hēr and hiere hām æt Windlesōran.

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce wearþ gescapen æfter syndrigum "Acts of Union", þæt habbaþ
þā sweotolan rīċu Englaland, Wēalas, Scotland, and Īrland geānlǣht under ān
rǣdena in Lundene. Mǣst þæs landes Īrlandes tōsyndrode of þǣm Geānlǣhtan
Cynerīce in 1922, and tōdæg is Īrland Cynewīse, ac se northēasterna dǣl þæs
īeglandes, Norðerne Īrland gehāten, gewunaþ in þǣm Geānedan Cynerīce.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C4%92adweard_se_Ieldra

Ēadweard se Ieldra (871? - 17 Mǣdmōnaþ, 924) wæs Engla Cyning of 899 oþ 924. Hē
wæs Ælfrēdes Miclan ieldesta sunu, and wearþ Westseaxna Cyning æfter his fæderes
dēaðe in 899.

Ēadweard mōt man secgan exceeded Ælfrēdes military achievements, eftbrohtede þæt
Denelagu be Engla rīce and he ricsode on Miercum of 918, æfter his sweostor
dēaþ, Æðelflǣd. Þæn fang he ǣrrste to rīce in his geoguðe be niede feaht he his
cousin Æþelwald, se wæs ǣroste Æthelrǣdes sunu forþǣm þe Æþelwald sohtede his
cynedōm and heald ān cuyninges tūn wiþ his nefan. Æfter þe Ēadweard Ǣþelweald
flīemede, cwōm Ǣþelweald on Norþanhymbrum and þā Norþmenn hæfde him to bēon
cyning on þǣm rīce, oð ðe Ēadweard slōg him on wælfelde.

Sēo gegifene onlīcnes included here is imaginary and was drawn together with
portraits of other Anglo-Saxon cyningum be ungecrawnum cræftere in þǣm 18,
gearhund.

Ēadweard Cyning hæfde onbūtan eahtatīene cildru of his þrim marriages, and may
have had an illegitimate bearn ēac. Hē forþferde in 924 his byrgen wæs æt
Wintanceastre.

His dohtor, Ēadgifu, ceorlode Carl III Francena Cyning, se hātte Carl se
Ānfealda. Hire sunu wearþ cyning Hloðwig IV Francena Cyning.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C3%9Er%C4%93o_Coreaniscu_Cyner%C4%ABcu

Þā Þrēo Coreaniscan Cynerīcu wǣron þā cynerī­cu Goguryeo, Baekje and Silla, þā
oferseten þæt Coreanisc healfīeg and Manchurie, betweox þæt forma hundredgēar BC
and 7e hundredgēar AD. Þis land hæfden lǣsse cynerīcu and undercynerīcu ǣr þǣm
tīd þǣm Þrim Cynerīcum, tō bisene Gaya, Dongye, Okjeo, Buyeo, Usan, Tamna, etc.

Þēos tīd onginnþ folclīce æt 57 BC, þonne þæt cynerīce Saro (lator hatte Silla)
in sūdeast þǣm healfīeg þeah selfdōm fram Cīnisc hēafodrīce Han dynasty.
Goguryeo in the north and the south of Yalu flōd (Amnok flōd in Coreaniscum
geþēodum) got independence from the Chinese in 37 BC. In 18 BC, twā Goguryeo
æþelingas sind fram æfterfylgendnesgūð geflogen, and habbaþ Beaekje in þǣm
sūþwestum healfīegum (todæg Seoul) gegrundweallod. His hēafodburg wǣs Ungjin
(todæag Gongju or Chongju) lator Sabi (todæag Puyo) in sūþwestum Seoulum. Þæt
cynerīce Gaya tōsundrode of Beakje in þǣm 1st hundredgēar A.D.

Gewered mit Tang dynasty of Cinalandum, Silla gewieldaþ Goguryeo in 668, æfter
hē gewieldaþ Baekje in 660, and stālode þæt Unified Silla tīd and endode þā Þrēo
Cynerīcu.

Man brȳcþ þone name "Samguk", oþþe "Þrēo Cynerīcum", in þǣm Koreaniscum tītulum
for tīrfæste trahtas Samguk Sagi and Samguk Yusa.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Woden

Wōden is nama ānes þāra Þēodiscum goda, hwæs nama is of Mercurie on Englisce
āreaht, for þǣm þe hē is þæt nīehste god tō Wōdne. His nama is oft gefunden in
cynnreccennessum Engliscra cynelicra mǣgscīra. His dǣl wæs manigfeald; hē wæs
god wīsdōmes and gūðes. Ēac lēodum þūhte þæt hē þæt god lēoðes wæs and
drȳcræftes and sīðes and þǣre huntunge.

His nama is, on Īslendisce/Norene Óðinn (Ōðen gehāten on Englisce); Swēonisce
Oden; Nīwum Englisce/Englisce (and Ealdum Seaxiscum) Wõden; Ealdum Franconisce
Wodan; Alemannisce Wuodan; Þēodisce Wotan oþþe Wothan; Lombardisce Godan, and in
Ealdgermanisce hit wæs *Wōðanaz, þe segde "se wōda" oððe "hē þǣre wōdnesse", for
þǣm þe æreste hē wæs gūðgod: gelīce in Ealdgrēcisce se Grēcisca gūðgod Arēs oft
hātte mainomenos þe segð "wōd".

Ac man wiþcwiþþ ymbe his rihtan andgiet in racum, as se nama is gemacod of òð
and -in. On Norene mǣnþ òð '"wit, soul" be selfum and in fēgungum "heaðumægen,
cāfnes" mǣnþ sēo endung -in "hǣsere, dryhten." Þus, Odin is dryhten þæs līfes
þrace.

Man geþēodode Óðen micle mid þǣm Wildan Huntoðe, farende hlūde þurh wolcnu
lǣdende micelne here þāra ofslægenena, gelīce þǣm gode Rudra þæs Hinduiscan
Rigvedasya. Ódinn and Frigg fōron ætgædre in þissum.

Snorri Sturlusones Edda ātīefreþ þæt Ōðen wilcumaþ þā micelan dēadan cempan þe
fēollon on beadwe in his sele, Valhalla. Þās gefeallenan, þā einherjar, feohtaþ
mid Ōðene and mid þæm ōðrum godum in þæt wæl þæs endes þǣre worulde, Ragnarök.

In þǣm Norþmanniscum spellum, Óðin oft scyrpeþ menn to gūðe and sendeþ his
Valkyrjur (þe segþ Wælcyrigan) tō sendanne sigu þǣr hē wysceþ and tō cēosanne þā
dēade. Þis is tō gaderianne þā beteste wīgendas in his greatan healle þe hātte
Valholl, þe segþ Wælheall, and hit hātte in Nīwenglisce Valhalla.

Hwīlum Óðinn scǣwþ hine selfne fore mannum. Sum wrītung sægde þæt æt ende þæs
gefeohtes æt Brávellir, Óðinn þider ēode tō fetianne þone ealdan cyning Harald
Hildetand. Helgi Hundingesbana wearþ genōg gūðmǣr and Dag his āðum wyscede þæt
hē wricþ his fæder þe Helgi ofslōh, and Óðinn onlǣnde his spere tō Dage, and Dag
ofslōh Helgi, þe ēode tō Valhallan and þǣr instæpe wearþ sum þāra lǣdendostra
wīgenda.

Man cnǣwþ lǣssa ymbe Óðine (oððe Wōdne) swā nimend þāra dēada swā gelīefdon þā
sūðerne Germanas. Se Romisca spellwrītere Tacitus wrāt þæt þā Germanas beēodon
Mercurium, ac is gelīc þæt þis tācnode Wōden, for þǣm þe Mercurius (þe in
Grēcisce hātte Hermēs) ēac wæs se sāwollǣdend (þe in Grēcisce is psychopompos).
And Iulius Caesar wrāt þæt Mercurius is se grēatost god þāra Germaniscena in his
bēc De Bello Gallico 6.17.1.

Paulus Diaconus (þe segþ Paulus se Dīacon) wrāt nēah þǣm ende þæs 8an
gēarhundrede, and þǣrinne he sægde þæt Wōden (þe hē wrāt Guodan) wæs se
hēafodgod þāra Langbearda, and hē and ǣrran wrīteras sægdon þæt Wōden wæs
Mercurius: sēo þā bōc History of the Langobards, I:9. Þurh þā samnesse, Paulus
wrāt þæt þā Germanas gelīefdon þæt Wōden wæs, and þæt þæs godes fruma wæs ne in
þissum tīde ac gēo and ne in Germaniam ac in Grēclande. Robert Wace ēac segþ þæt
Wotan is Mercurius. Viktor Rydberg in his bēc ymbe Teutonic Mythology, wrīteþ
ymbe sume ōðre gelīcnessa Wōdenes mid Mercuriō, and þæt bēgen brōhton
lēoðsangscip tō mannum.

Se Norþmannisca nama Ōðinn goes back to an earlier *Wōðinaz, consistent with the
initial consonant of the West Germanic form of the name. Adam von Bremen
etymologizes the god worshipped by the 11th century Scandinavian pagans as
"Wodan id est furor" ("Wodan, which means 'ire'."), a possibility still commonly
assumed today, connecting the name with Old English wōd, Gothic wōds, Old Norse
*ōðr (see Odr), Old High German wuot, all meaning "possessed, insane, raging".

In gemānum Proto-Germanisce se nama wæs *Wōðinaz, þe ēaðe mæg bēon of
Indo-Europeiscum *Watinos. Ac man seah þæt Englisc Woden nis riht sam-cynn
Germanisces Wotan, and þæt þǣrþurh folc gehweorf Wotan to folgienne þæt andgiet
"se wōda", and swīðe æfter þæt þā Germanas wurdon Crīstnas and man seah Wotan
swā deofol, ac þā Norþmenn and þā Engle hēoldon þone nama swā hit ǣrra wæs. And
gelīce in ealdum Grēcisce Arēs hira gūþgod oft hātte Arēs mainomenos þe segþ
"wōd Arēs".

Ān meahtlicnes is þæt se nama wæs geborgod of þǣm Wealhcynne, ymbe þā tīd
Tacites hwonne Germanisc and Wīelisc cynn wǣron wiþ hīe on ǣgðerre healfe þǣre
Rīne, and is gecynde þǣm Wīeliscan prēostlican gefērscipe þāra Vates. Þæt
Wīelisce word is æt ende genumen of þǣre ilcan wyrte (meahtlīce
Frum-Indisc-Europisc, ac gesōðod in Wīelisce and in Germanisce ānum) swā þā
Germaniscan word for "dēofolsēoc", ofer beclipod, *vāt-, mid with a more general
meaning of "spiritually excited", also preserved in the Irish word for "poet",
fáith. If the word is indeed a loan from the Celtic, it may be an important hint
to the dating of the Proto-Germanic sound changes.

Se Prose Edda segþ þæt Bestla and Borr ācennedon Óðin and þæt hē hæfde bróðru Vé
(þe is Wéo) and Vili (þe is Will) and þā þrēo gebrōðru niðerwurpon þone
forstþyrs Ymir and macodon þone woruld of Ymis līce. Man oft spræc ymbe þā þrēo
gebrōðru ætgædre.

Óðinn and Jorð ācennedon þone brēmostan sunu Þórr, and his nama segþ Þunor, and
Jorð segþ Eorþe. Ac his wīf and gemæcca wæs sēo gyden Frigg, and þā gecnāwenoste
ealdspell secgaþ þæt Frigg wæs sēo lufiende mōdor hira suna Baldr).

And se blinda god Hoðr þurh misgelimpe ofsloh his brōðor Baldr, and æfterra
Óðinn and þā þyrsen Rind ācennedon Vali, and Vali cwōm of Rindes cwiðe
fullweaxen and wæpned and hē swerode āþ þæt ne wolde dōn niht and ne baðian
oþþæt he wrece on Hoðe.

And manige cynecynnas sægron þæt Óðinn wæs sum hira ealdfædra þurh ōðre suno.
For traditions about Odin's offspring see Sons of Odin.

Óðinn hæfþ þæt eahtasceancan horse Sleipnir, and þæt ofhēawen hēafod þæs
dwearges Mímis and hit forewītegode þā forþgesceafte. His Valkyrjur þegnodon
hine gaderende þā sāwla beorna ofslægenra in gefeohte and brōhton hīe to
Wælhealle þǣr Óðinn wunode in Ásgarðe, þǣr þā sāwla wurdon þā Einherjar, þe
willon þurfan feohtan mid Óðine in þǣre gūðe æt Ragnaroke. And þæt nama
Einherjar segþ Ānheremenn, for in Wōdnes healle hīe sind ealle in ānum samum
herge, þéah þe ǣrra libbende on eorðan hie wǣron in manigum hergum and fyrdum.

Brynhildr, sum þāra Valkyrja, wearþ ūtgeworpen of his þegnscipe, ac Óðinn
gemiltsode and settede híe in healle and ymb hīe hring fȳres tō þæs þe ānne se
heardost mann mihte sēcan weddan hīe. And Sigurðr āhreddede hīe. And æfterra
Vali ofslōh Hoð.

Odin has a number of magical artifacts associated with him: the dwarven spear
Gungnir, which never misses its target, a magical gold ring (Draupnir), from
which every ninth night eight new rings appear, an eight-legged horse (Sleipnir)
and two ravens Huginn and Muninn (Thought and Memory) who travel the world to
acquire information at his behest. He also commands a pair of wolves named Geri
and Freki, to whom he gives his food for he himself consumes nothing but wine.
From his throne, Hlidskjalf (located in Valaskjalf), Ōðinn could see everything
that occurred in the universe.

The Norsemen gave Odin many nicknames; this was in the Norse skaldic tradition
of kennings, a poetic method of indirect reference, as in a riddle. See List of
names of Odin. The name Alföðr ("Allfather", "father of all") appears in Snorri
Sturluson's Younger Edda. It probably refers to the Christian God in that book,
but it may have referred to Odin at an earlier date. (It probably originally
denoted Tiwaz, as it fits the pattern of referring to Sky Fathers as "father".)

Englaþēod, Seaxcynn and Geotcynn brōhton Wōden tō Bretene ymbe þǣm 5th and 6th
gearhundedum, continuing his worship until conversion to Christianity in the 8th
and 9th centuries. Woden is the carrier-off of the dead, but not necessarily
with the attributes of Norse Odin. Woden is also the leader of the Wild Hunt.
The familial relationships are the same between Woden and the other Anglo-Saxon
gods as they are for the Norse.

Æfter þǣm Engla and Seaxna Cranice and þǣm Historia Britonum, Woden hæfde þās
sunas: Wecta, Bældæg, Casere and Wihtlaeg.

Wōdnesdæg ('Wōdenes dæg') is for him genemned, for þǣm þe his bend mid þǣm
dēadum gebȳraþ tō þǣm Rōmāniscan Mercurie. Þā Germaniscan lēode āreahton of
Lǣdene Mercuri dies on Englisc swā Wōdnesdæg.

Details of Migration period Germanic religion are sketchy, reconstructed from
artefacts, sparse contemporary sources, and later the later testimonies of
medieval legends and placenames. According to Jonas Bobiensis, the 6th century
Irish missionary Saint Columbanus is reputed to have disrupted a Beer sacrifice
to Wuodan (Deo suo Vodano nomine) in Bregenz. Wuodan was the chief god of the
Alamanni, his name appears in the runic inscription on the Nordendorf fibula.

Pagan worship disappeared with Christianization, from the 8th century in England
and Germany, lingering until the 12th or 13th century in Iceland and
Scandinavia. Remnants of worship were continued into modern times as folklore.

Many places are named after Odin, especially in Scandinavia, such as Odense
(Denmark) and Odensbacken (Sweden), but also places in other Germanic countries,
such as Wednesbury (Englaland), Wodensberg and Odenheim (Germany), and
Woensdrecht (Netherlands). Almost all German Gaue (Latin, pagi) had mountains
and other places named after him under such generic names as Wodenesberg,
Wuodenesberg, Godesberg and Gudensberg, Wodensholt, etc.

Odin wæs þæt āne god in Scandinavian mythology to demand human sacrifice at the
Blōts. Adam of Bremen relates that every ninth year, people assembled from all
over Sweden to sacrifice at the Temple at Uppsala. Male slaves, and males of
each species were sacrificed and hung from the branches of the trees. The
practice of sacrifice is one reason why Thor was much more popular among the
commonfolk. Committing suicide was also considered to be a shortcut to Valhalla.

As the Swedes had the right not only to elect king but also to depose a king,
the sagas relate that both king Domalde and king Olof Trätälja were sacrificed
to Odin after years of famine. Sēo ēac sacred king.

It was common, particularly among the Cimbri, to sacrifice a prisoner to Odin
prior to or after a battle. The Orkneyinga saga relates a (and uncommon) form of
Odinic sacrifice, wherein the captured Ella is slaughtered by the carving out of
a "blood eagle" upon his back.

More significantly, however, it has been argued that the killing of a combatant
in battle was to give a sacrificial offering to Odin. The fickleness of Odin in
battle was well-documented, and in Lokasenna, Loki taunts Odin for his
inconsistency.

Sometimes sacrifices were made to Odin to bring about changes in circumstance, a
notable example being the sacrifice of King Vīkar (detailed in Gautrek's Saga
and Saxo). Sailors in a fleet being blown off course drew lots to sacrifice to
Odin that he might abate the winds; the king himself drew the lot and was
hanged.

Sacrifices were probably also made to Odin at the beginning of summer, since
Ynglinga saga states one of the great festivities of the calendar is at sumri,
þat var sigrblōt "in summer, for victory"; Odin is consistently referred to
throughout the Norse mythos as the bringer of victory.

The Ynglinga saga also details the sacrifices made by the Swedish king Aun, who,
it was revealed to him, would lengthen his life by sacrificing one of his sons
every ten years; nine of his ten sons died this way. When he was about to
sacrifice his last son Egil, the Swedes stopped him.

The goddess Fricg is seen as an adept of the mysteries of seid (shamanism), a
völva, and it is said that it was she who initiated Odin into its mysteries. In
Lokasenna Loki abuses Odin for practising seid, condemning it as a unmanly art.
A justification for this may be found in the Ynglinga saga where Snorri opines
that following the practice of seid, the practitioner was rendered weak and
helpless. Another explanation is that its manipulative aspects ran counter to
the male ideal of forthright, open behaviour.

Odin was a compulsive seeker of wisdom, consumed by his passion for knowledge,
to the extent that he sacrificed one of his eyes (which one this was is unclear)
to Mimir, in exchange for a drink from the waters of wisdom in Mimir's well.

Further, the creation of the runes, the Norse alphabet that was also used for
divination, is attributed to Odin and is described in the Rūnatal, a section of
the Havamal. He hanged himself from the tree Yggdrasil, whilst pierced by his
own spear, to acquire knowledge. He remained thus for nine days and nights, a
number deeply significant in Norse magical practice (there were, for example,
nine realms of existence), thereby learning nine (later eighteen) magical songs
and eighteen magical runes. The purpose of this strange ritual, a god
sacrificing himself to himself because there was nothing higher to sacrifice to,
was to obtain mystical insight through mortification of the flesh; however, some
scholars assert that the Norse believed that insight into the runes could only
be truly attained in death.

Some scholars see this scene as influenced by the story of Christ's crucifixion;
and others note the similarity to the story of Buddha's enlightenment. it is in
any case also influenced by shamanism, where the symbolic climbing of a "world
tree" by the shaman in search of mystic knowledge is a common religious pattern.
We know that sacrifices, human or otherwise, to the gods were commonly hung in
or from trees, often transfixed by spears. (See also: Peijainen) Additionally,
one of Odin's names is Ygg, and the norse name for the World Ash
—Yggdrasil—therefore means "Ygg's (Odin's)horse". Another of Odin's names is
Hangatyr, the god of the hanged.

Ōðenes lufu for wīsdōme cann man ēac sēon in his weorc as a farmhand for a
summer, for Baugi, in order to obtain the mead of poetry. Sēo Fjalar and Galar
for more details.

Swā þæt hēafodgod ealra Germaniscra goda, onfēng syndrigne ymbþanc of þǣm frumum
spellbodum. For example, his day is the only day to have been renamed in the
German language from "Woden's day", still extant on Nīwum Englisce Wednesday to
the neutral Mittwoch ("mid-week"), while other gods were not deemed important
enough for propaganda (Tuesday "Tyr's day" and Frīgedæg "Frīge dæg" remained
intact in all Germanic languages). For many Germans, St. Michael replaced Wotan,
and many mountain chapels dedicated to St. Michael can be found, but Wotan also
remained present as a sort of demon leading the Wild hunt of the host of the
dead, e.g. in Swiss folklore as Wuotis Heer. However, in some regions even this
mythology was transformed so that Charlemagne led the hunt, not Odin.

In Englalande wæs Wōden was not so much demonized as rationalized, and in the
Anglo-Saxon Chronicle, he appears as a perfectly earthly cyning, only four
generations removed from Hengest and Horsa.

Snorri Sturluson's record of the Edda is striking evidence of the climate of
religious tolerance in medieval Iceland, but even he feels compelled to give a
rational account of the Aesir in his preface. In this scenario, Snorri
speculates that Odin and his peers were originally refugees from Troy,
etymologizing Aesir as derived from Asia. Some scholars believe that Snorri's
version of Norse mythology is an attempt to mould a more shamanistic tradition
into a Greek mythological cast. In any case, Snorri's writing (particularly in
Heimskringla) tries to maintain an essentially scholastic neutrality. That
Snorri was correct was one of the last of Thor Heyerdahl's
archeo-anthropological theories (see The search for Odin).

In manigum Germaniscum sprǣcum is se nama þæs fēorðan dæges þǣre wuce (if one
counts from Sunday) is frequently, "Wotanes Dæg" oþþe "Wōdenes Dæg", (Wōdnesdæg
on Englisce. Geefnett Norþwegisc, Denisc and Swēonisc onsdag, Niðerlendisc
woensdag; ǣnlīce se efenweorða dæg on Þēodisc is ānfealdlīce "mid wucu"
(Mittwoch)). This is thought to translate the Latin Dies Mercurii, "Mercury-day"
(cf. French mercredi), owing primarily to Tacitus' linking þāra twēgra goda.

Sēo endenīehste beadu, in þǣre þe þā Norenan tealdon sige tō Ōðene, wæs sēo
Beadu Lenan in 1208 [1]. The former Swedish king Sverker had arrived with a
large Danish army, and the Swedes discovered that the Danish army was more than
twice the size of their own. Naturally, the Danes got the upper hand and they
should have won. However, the Swedes claimed that they suddenly saw Odin riding
on Sleipnir. Accounts vary on how Odin gave the Swedes victory, but in one
version, he rode in front of their battle formation.

Scandinavian folklore also maintained a belief in Odin as the leader of the Wild
Hunt (Åsgårdsreia in Norwegian). His main objective seems to have been to track
down and kill the forest creature huldran or skogsrået. In these accounts, Odin
was typically a lone huntsman, save for his two wolves. Originally, he was armed
with a spear, but in later accounts this was sometimes changed to a rifle.

Washington Freedom, hƿæs nama is Hƿæsingatūn Frēodōm on Englisce, is Americanisc
frēona clīeƿen fōtball tēam Hƿæsingatūnes, D.C., þe in Women's Professional
Soccer pleȝaþ. Man onstealdon þā Freedom ǣror in 2001 in þǣm unȝeþēododum
Women's United Soccer Association. Siþþan 2004, sēo Freedom pleȝodon hiera
hāmmæccan æt þone Maryland SoccerPlex.

Se tēam pleȝode his hāmmæccan æt Robert F. Kennedy Memorial Stadium in
Hƿæsingatūne, D.C., hƿǣr þā tēamscīr ēac stōdon. Þā onstellende pleȝestran þæs
tēames ƿǣron Mia Hamm, Siri Mullinix, and Michelle French. Man ȝeaf þās
pleȝestran þæs þēodliċan tēames tō ǣlċum WUSA tēame. Man ƿēnode þæt ƿierþ hīe ān
þāra bestan tēama þæs sportcampes, ac ȝeƿunnon hīe seofoða of eahtum tēamum ofer
hiera fyrstum tīman.

Þēah, þis ȝeƿinn ȝeaf him þæt sundorriht tō ċēosenne Abby Wambach sƿā hiera
fyrst ċyre þæs 2002 WUSA draftes. Mā āƿendunga manna, pleȝestra betera
fremminga, and Mia Hammes ȝehǣled cnēoƿ ȝeaf hīe betera ȝeƿinn, sƿā Hƿæsingatūn
ƿæs unfyled on hiera læstan eahtan mæccum, and ȝeƿinnodon þridda beste þisses
ȝēares, efne tƿeȝen puntas fram fyrste. In þǣm æftertīman, hīe ȝeƿunodon hiera
healflæst mæcca ƿiþ þā Philadelphia Charge, 1–0, and ēodon forþ tō þǣm Founders
Cup, se WUSA ċeampscipe mæcca, hƿǣr þā Carolina Courage hīe fyledon, 3–2.

In 2003, se Freedom ƿearþ bærlīċe ƿeorþful þāra rancmæccan, healdende fēorða
stede and tƿeȝen mæccan þurhstandende. Þēah, hīe nōmon siȝe ofer þā ċeampmenn
Boston Breakers in þǣm healflæstan mæccan, 0–0 (3–1 scriftspurn scēotend), and
þonne nōmon siȝe ofer Atlanta Beat in þǣm Founders Cup, 2–1, in ofertīde.

Se Washington Freedom is ān seofona tēama þæs Women's Professional Soccer heres,
þe pleȝ begann in 2009.

On 16 Hāliȝmōnaþ, 2008, man fremede þone fyrst pleȝestre ȝiefend; ȜR Frēona
Þēodliċ Tēam pleȝestran Abby Wambach, Cat Whitehill and Ali Krieger ēodon tō þǣm
Freedome. Se ȝiefend ȝeaf Wambach eft tō þǣm Freedome, hƿīl Krieger pleȝode mid
þǣm Washington Freedom Reserves in 2004 and 2005, and for þǣm W-League tēame in
2007.

On 24 Hāliȝmōnaþ, 2008, man fremede þone 2008 WPS Ȝeondþēodliċ Mann-nimende; man
ȝeaf ēac Iapanisc pleȝestre Homare Sawa, Frenċisc pleȝestran Sonia Bompastor and
Louisa Necib, and Austrealisc forƿeardmann Lisa De Vanna tō þǣm Freedome.

On 6 Ƿinterfylleþ, 2008, se 2008 WPS Riht Mann-nimende fremede. Hƿæsingatūn nōm
pleȝestran Sarah Huffman, Becky Sauerbrunn, Lori Lindsey, and Emily Janss. Ealla
þissa pleȝestra pleȝodon mid Hƿæsingatūne in þǣm W-League in 2008.

On 16 þǣm Æfterrum Ȝēole, 2009, se WPS Beȝinnende Mann-nimende fremede. Se
Freedom nōm Allie Long, Alex Singer, Jill Gilbeau, Parrissa Eyorokon, Briana
Scurry, Rebecca Moros, Sarah Senty, and Kati Jo Spisak. Ēac, se Freedom onfēng
þā riht Joanna Lohman in mannċīepe mid Saint Louis Athletica. Ealla þāra
pleȝestra būton Long, Eyorokon, and Scurry pleȝodon mid þǣm W-League tēame
Freedomes.

https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unmeaht

Unmeaht (on Nīwenglisce hātte "disability") is brād word þe is fram þǣre Worulde
Hǣlðe Þēodnesse in Nīwenglisce þus tōmearcod: "Disabilities is an umbrella term,
covering impairments, activity limitations, and participation restrictions. An
impairment is a problem in body function or structure; an activity limitation is
a difficulty encountered by an individual in executing a task or action; while a
participation restriction is a problem experienced by an individual in
involvement in life situations. Thus disability is a complex phenomenon,
reflecting an interaction between features of a person’s body and features of
the society in which he or she lives.'"

Þes traht is awended fornēan þus: "'Unmeaht' is brād wordgemeare, begangende
wanunge, gemǣtgunga macunge, and dǣlnimunge gehaftunga. Wanung is wōh
līchāmlices weorces oþþe timberes; gemǣtung macunge is earfoþ on gelǣstunge
ǣrendes oþþe macunge þe is gefēred fram menn; ac dǣlnimunge gehaftung is wōh þe
is gefēred fram menn on steallum līfes. Þæs is unmeaht manigfeald þing, þe ēowaþ
efenweorc betweox þǣm mearcum menn līces and þǣm mearcum þæs drohtaðes þǣm þe
man wunie.'"

Þēah þe hit wordlīce mǣnþ ǣnig þing on þǣm þe mann nis cræftig, hit is oftost
gebrocen tō worde tācnende ungewunelica oþþe ungecyndelica unmeahta.

Virginia (Nīwe Englisc: Virginia) is ān þāra frumra 13 rīca þāra Geānlǣhtra Rīca
þe ongēan Brytta gewealde ūpārās on þǣre American Oferweorpennesse. Hēo biþ
gemǣnelice geteald tō dǣle þæs Sūðdǣles. His ambihtlica nama is þæt
Gemǣngestrēon Virginian; hēo is ān fēower Gemǣngestrēona of þǣm fīftig
Geānlǣhtum Rīcum.

Kentucky and West Virginia wǣron dǣlas Virginie æt þǣre tīde þǣre staðelunge
þāra Geānlǣhtra Rīca, ac se ǣrra wearþ underfangen in þā Geānlǣcunge swā
sundorrīce in 1792 and se ōðer oþbærst of Virginie in þǣm Americaniscan
Ingefeohte.

Virginia is gecweden "Foresittenda Mōdor" for þǣm þe wǣron mā U.S. Foresittendra
(8) on þissum rīce geboren þonne on ǣnigum ōðrum. Fīf þāra wǣron geedcoren tō
ōðerre ambihttīde: George Washington and Thomas Jefferson, James Madison and
James Monroe and Woodrow Wilson. Þā ōðre Virginiānisce Foresittend sindon
William Henry Harrison and John Tyler and Zachary Taylor.

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce Grēatre Brytene and Norþīrlandes is cȳnerīce ofer norþenam
Europan. Man nemneþ hit sceortlīce Geānede Cynerīce oþþe UK (of Nīwum Englisce:
United Kingdom).

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce līþ on garsecges īeglandum be westnorðan Europan. His mǣste
īeg is Bryten (Nīwenglisc: Great Britain) and his oþru Īrland hwǣron licgaþ
siexe scīra þæs rīces. Eall ymbe þissum sǣrīman sind manigfealdum īege and
īegoþe.

Cynerīce is þæt Geānede Cynerīce, þærof is Elisabeþ II Cwēn. His hēafodstōl is
Westmynster (oþþe Lunden þærof is Westmynster nū dǣl). Sēo Cwēn hæfþ hiere stōl
hēr and hiere hām æt Windlesōran.

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce wearþ gescapen æfter syndrigum "Acts of Union", þæt habbaþ
þā sweotolan rīċu Englaland, Wēalas, Scotland, and Īrland geānlǣht under ān
rǣdena in Lundene. Mǣst þæs landes Īrlandes tōsyndrode of þǣm Geānlǣhtan
Cynerīce in 1922, and tōdæg is Īrland Cynewīse, ac se northēasterna dǣl þæs
īeglandes, Norðerne Īrland gehāten, gewunaþ in þǣm Geānedan Cynerīce.

Taprabane is rīce and īegland be Indealandes sūðernum strande in þǣm Indiscan
Gārsecge. Sēo īeg hæfþ tweontig þūsend þūsenda manna.

Tāprabane hæfþ in missenlicum gereordum mænige namen. Ealdcrēcas nemdon hīe
Taprobane (and Ælfred cyning geaf hire þone naman Tāpraban and Dēprobane. Þām
Arabum wæs hēo Serendib. Tō Marco Polo wæs hēo cūþ swā Seilan, and Ceilão wæs se
nama gegifan be Portugalwarum þā hīe cōmon to Tāprabane in þǣm 1505. gēare. On
NĪwum Englisce wæs þæs īeglandes nama Ceylon.

In þǣm 1972. gēare wæs þæs rīces ambihtlīc nama awended tō "Sri Lanka" (in
Sinhalisce śrī laṃkā, IPA: [ˌʃɾiːˈlaŋkaː]. Þæs īeglandes āgnan nama is in
Sinhalisce ලංකාව Laṃkāva, IPA: [laŋˈkaːʋə], and in Tamilisce இலங்கை ilaṅkai,
iˈlaŋgai). "Sri Lanka" is of Sanskrit worde laṃkā, þe is "boldwelena land", þe
wæs ēac his nama in ealdre Indiscre sægene þæs "Mahabharata" and þæs "Ramayana".
Sri is Sanskritisc titul of āre.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sw%C3%A9oland

Swēoland þæt Cynerīce (Swēonisc: Konungariket Sverige) is Norþmannisc land in
Scedelande, in Norðernre Europan. Ymb his mearce licgaþ Norþweg be westan,
Finnland be norþēastan, se Skagerrak and se Kattegat be sūþwestan, and se Ostsǣ
and se Botmlandsǣ be ēastan. For þǣm þe sēo folces þiccnes is hwæthwēgra smæl,
is þæt Swēonisce land cūþ for his stilnesse, micelum wudum, and beorgwēstenne.

Swēoland hæfð mild weder oððæt ðe hit is norðern, forþæm þe se Gulfstrēam wearmþ
Ostsǣ. In þisses landes sūþdǣle is welig mid lēaf-berendum trēowum, and in his
norþdǣl is furhwudu and heard birc stent in eallum þǣm lande. On norðernum
Swēolandes beorgum is ceald weder mid snawe and īs. Be norþen þǣm norðworulde
hring, seteð se sunne næfre in sumor and ne rīseð hit in winter; seo winter niht
is unendende.

Be easten Swēolande is Ostsǣ and his norðdǣl se Botmsǣ. Þȳ hæfþ þis land lang
sǣrīm. In his westdǣl sindon Scedelandes beorgas, þā bedālað Swēonas of þǣm
Norþmannum.

Swēolandes sūðdǣl is gebūrland mid micel weald se oferwriēhþ þæt land, þiccor
norðweard. Onmiddan þǣm lande sind twā luge and Mälaren meres dæl is gemearc, in
Öresund.

Sweoland hæfþ fēower and twēontig landscipas oððe fīf and twēontig gif man hygð
ðe Norþbotten is his agan land and nis Westbottnes dæl. Þās landscipas næbbað
tōþegnung þing ac hie sindon hēafod bedælunge ðæs rīces.

Oþre landscipas of ealdtīde sind in Finnland, þæt land hæfþ gebēon gelosen.
Terfinnland is þæt ānne landscipe genomen be landbūnesse.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Starcraft_II

Steorracræft II is þrisnes herȝes cunninglēasspelles spearcatella gamenes þe
Blizzard Entertainment maciaþ, sƿā ōðer hiera gamen SteorraCræftes. Man ǣrest
þyncodon SteorraCræft II tō bēonne enfe ān gamen, ac æt BlizzCon 2008, hīe
cƿǣdon þæt ƿierþ hit þrines, cūþ sƿā Wings of Liberty (Feðra Frēodōmes), Heart
of the Swarm (Middel Sƿearmes), and Legacy of the Void (Lāf Nahtnesse).

Se ānpleȝend forþƿeȝ mōd þæs gamenes and his underseta ǣlċ ƿierþ spreċen, ymbe
þā lār þēoddǣles, ǣr mid þǣm Terranum onȝinnende, þonne þā Zerg, and læste þā

ne sind nān ālīesendtīd for þǣre þrinesse.

Mihtelic se betstcūþ and betstcīepend stēamwægn wæs Stanley Steamer, macod fram

wægnas, and wæs ōðerbetst tō efne Columbia Electric in þǣm G.R. Hit breac smæl

https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sci%C3%BE%C3%BEisc_%C4%ABsm%C3%A6%C8%9Dden

Þæt Sciþþisc īsmægden is Pazyryk byrgen þe Natalia Polosmak fand in 1993,
seldcūðu bisen ānwīfes þe hæfde ful trēowen byrgen in þǣm fīftan gēarhundrede,
gefolged mid siexum horsum. Hit wæs for 2,400 wintrum byrged in līcbeorge þe man
macode of geholedum learctrēo. Ūtweard þǣre līcbeorge wǣron biliðas dēora and
snāwpænþra, intō leðere corfen.

Þæt mægdnes welgeāspared līc, nēodlīce geāspared mid mēose and bēamrinde, legþ
on hire rihtum handa swelce slǣpende. Hēo wæs geong; hire hǣr giet fæger, and
wæs 5 fēt, 6 ynca micel. Þā dēormōd tācnunga wǣron on hire āblæcum scynne
geāspared: dēor mid hornum þe weorðaþ hwæt blostmlic.

Man macode hire līcbeorg micel genug for þǣre hēahan hēafodgearwan þe werode
hēo, þe man ontō hire fīftīene trēowan briddas sēowede. Man þōhte þæt hire serc
wild tussahseolc wæs, ac betere scēawung onwrāh þæt se onfeng nis Cīnisc, ac of
