https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sunnand%C3%A6%C8%9D

Sunnandæg is þǣre wuce dæg betwēonan Sæternesdæge and Mōnandæge. His nama is
genumen of Sunne, þǣm Seaxiscan Sunnes gyden, ēac hātte Sōl be þǣm Norþmannum.

Sunnandæg is sometimes held to be the last day of the week (especially in modern
Europe and South America), and sometimes the first day (a traditional view
derived from ancient Jews and ancient Egyptians).

In orthodox Christian families and communities some activities are not done,
e.g. working, doing something that requires somebody else to work such as buying
goods or services (including the use of public transport), driving a car,
gardening, washing a car, etc. Exceptions which are allowed are making use of
religious services, and, usually, using electricity, and urgent medical matters.

In þǣm folclēoðe, "Þæt cild geboren on Sunnandæge is fæger and wīs and gōd and
gāl".

In ancient Jewish tradition Sæternesdæg is the sabbath. Mænig geþēodu forþoliaþ
ānlīelpigra worda for "Sæternesdæge" and "Sabate". Eastern Orthodox churches
distinguish between the sabbath (Sæternesdæg) and the Lord's day (Sunnandæg).
Roman Catholics put so little emphasis on that distinction that many among them
follow -- at least in colloquial language -- the Protestant practice of calling
Sunnandæg the sabbath.

Sunnandæg is se ōðer dæg þæs wucende and is hāligdæg in landum of Christian
tradition, se dæg þæt Crīstenfolc most commonly attend cirice.

In þǣm Geānlǣhtum Underrīcum, professional football is usually played on
Sunnandæg, although Sæternesdæg and Mōnandæg (via Tīwesniht Fōtball) also see a
some professional games. College fōtball gelimpþ usually on Sæternesdæge, and
high-school football tends to take place on Sunnandæg. It is not uncommon for
church attendance to shift on days when a late morning or early afternoon game
is anticipated by a local community.

Manig Americisc feorransēora nettweorc and stations ēac broadcast their
political interview shows on Sunnandæg mornings.

Manig American newspapers publish a larger edition on Sunnandæge, þe oft
includes color comic strips and a coupon section.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Steorracr%C3%A6ft

SteorraCræft is spærcletelle gamen macod be Blizzard Entertainment for Microsoft
Windows, Mac OS and Nintendo 64. Þæt stǣr spricþ ymbe gūþ betweox þrīe woruldrum
cynd: þā Terrans, þā woruldrum-ellorwihta Zerg, and þā mannlīce Protoss
gūþrincas.

SteorraCræft wæs þæt betst-cīepende spærcletelle gamen þæs 1998 and wann þæt
Origins Award for Betst Mōdgeþance Spærcletelle Gamen þæs gēares. SteorraCræft
wæs on IGNes "Cnoll 100 Gamena þæs Ealle Tīman" swā #7, and in 2006, underfēng
Tungol on þǣm Wād þæs Gamenes æt Metreon, San Fransisco. In Sēremōnaþ 2006,
SteorraCræft cīepode ofer 9,500,000 styccum, maciende his ān þāra betst-cīepende
spærcletelle gamenes in stǣre. Hit is swīðe notod in Sūþ Corea. Blizzard ǣreste
wold þæt stǣr mid SteorraCræft: Gāst þurhstandan, hwīc wæs gestillen. Þæt ōðer,
SteorraCræft II, wæs āboden 19 Þrimilcemōnaþ, 2007, in Seoul, Sūþ Corea.

SteorraCræftes gamenplegen is ymbe gadraþ twā onstale: gimmas and vespene lyft.
Hīe sind be weorhtum hærfestode. Gimmas, þe sind for eallum regollicum styccum
nodode, ætīewþ æs blæwenum gimmum fram þǣm grunda. Vespene lyft, þe is for
gelyfdum styccum and beteras nodod, ætīewþ æs grēnre lyfte.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stalin

Iosep Fissarionofic Stalin (geboren swā Ioseb Besarionis dse Iughascfili on þǣm
18 dæge Ǣrran Gēolan þæs 1878 gēares and cwæl on þǣm 5 dæge Hrēþmōnaðes þæs 1953
gēares) wæs se forma Gemǣna Lǣdend þæs Sofietre Gesamnunge Middelan Gyldes fram
þǣm 1922 gēare oþ his dēaþ in þǣm 1953 gēare. In þǣm gēarum æfter Lenines dēaðe
in þǣm 1924 gēare, hē rās and wearþ se lǣdend þǣre Sofietan Gesamnunge.

On Georgia wæs Ioseb Besarionis dse Iughascfili geboren and he wenod þe he wolde
weordan prēost, ac he alēt his lārhūse and feaht in þǣre Russiscan Onwendung in
1917 and weard hēah in þǣm nīwan Communistan lēodweard se ricsode ofer Russlande
and his rīce. In þissum gearum nām he his binaman "Stalin", se is "Stǣl-mann".

Stalin undergann gewealdede feohwendunge, þe namm þone stede þæs Nīwan
Feohwendunge Rǣdes þāra æfterrena 1920 gēara and setede on his stede þā Rǣd Fīfa
Gēara and undergann tīde swifte weorcsettunge and feohwendunge gemōtsettunge.
Þæt bræc in þǣre eorþbigenesse forestōp fōre þā forþbǣre ǣtes, þætte cwōm micel
hunger, and of þissum wæs se Sofietisca hunger of 1932–1933, þe man in þǣm
Ucrægne hētt be naman Holodomor, se is "Eallhunger".



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/St%C7%A3rlicu_sc%C4%ABr

Þæt Geāned Cynerīce hæfþ twa and hundnigontige scīra. Ēac hātaþ þisse scīra
eardfæstan scīra oððe gamola scīra.

Þisse scīra nabbað ane gerecþegnung, æfter mdccclxxxviiij, oððæt ðe to
mdcccclxxviiij stōwlicu āstyrung bād gestaðolod on hieran gierdum.

In Uladstire, stowlica ræden edniwung in mdcccclcciij arærde twa-endebyrdnes
stowlica ræden æt regio and læppa had; eall Uladstir wearþ seo regio.

On Engla and Norþ-wealum, þæt Local Government Act 1972 arærde scira for þæm
gesetnesa forþsetennesse utweard Grietran Lundene and Sylliege. Þa gerecþegnung
scira on Wealum wæron endedon in mdcccclxxxxvj.

In Englalande wæron mænigefealde læppan gesundrede fram hierum scirum æfter
mdcccclxxxx. Ælc "anfeald eard" (buton þa fram Bearrucscire) is scir be selfe
for þære gesetnesa, mid ānan læppan geond hierum halum earda, and hiere geþinge
is sēo geþinge þære scīre oððe sēo geþinge þæs læppan.

Scotland and Norþwealas habbaþ an-endebyrdnes "geþingedomas" and "fyrmestan
earde", þa on Wealum sume hetaþ "scīra" and sume "scīr-burgscipas".

Þæt Grietra Lunden eard (seo ne hatan næfre "scīr") wæs gearæred in mdcccclxv.
Þæt Grietra Lunden Gerec (Se Lundene Burgeald and Lundene Samnung) wæs in mm
gearæred.

On 1 Ēastermōnaþ 2009 (mmuiiii) weard þā Scīrgeþingas for Cornweallum,
Dunholmscīre, Norþhymbralande, Scrobbesbyrigscīre and Wiltunscīre ælc ānfeald
scīr. Beadanfordscīre and Ceasterscīre Scīregeþingas wæron beendedon.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/St%C4%93am_w%C3%A6gn

Mihtelic se betstcūþ and betstcīepend stēamwægn wæs Stanley Steamer, macod fram
1896 oþ 1924. Betwēonan 1899 and 1905, Stanley ūtcēapede ealle gæsolīnmihtode
wægnas, and wæs ōðerbetst tō efne Columbia Electric in þǣm G.R. Hit breac smæl
fȳrpīpesīeða tō gemægnne twinnafremmende tū-fȳrþyrel mihta. Forþǣm þe grēatum
spinmihte þe hæfde hit on eallum mihtaswiftnesum, man tīegede þone mihte þæs
stēamwægnes eallrihte tō þǣre bæceaxle, būton þearfende grāpe oþþe mænigfealde
swiftfulnes gearwebox. Oþ 1914, Stanley stēamwægnas ūtblēow hiere dism eallrihte
intō þǣre lyfte, and þurfdon lōme eftfyllendas þæs wæterfæt; æfter 1914, ealle
Stanleys hæfdon condenser þe hiere wæteressunge āþynnede.

In 1906, Stanley stēamwægn bræc þā landswiftnesgemynde, þe Fred Marriot drāf, æt
127 mīla ǣlc stund æt Ormond Strande, Floridan.

Man fandodon tō bringenne tō þǣre cēapstōwe mā gelyfed stēamwægnas, se grēatost
bēonde Doble stēamwægn, þe scortaþ styrttīd mid swīðe cræftful ānpīpe stēammaca
þe hæteþ lǣssre wæterandefne, and swīðlicum selfwyrhtende bærnes and
wæterfēdgewealdes. Be 1924, man meahte Dobles stēamwægnas styrtan fram ceald
bēonde mid þǣm wend cæges, and hine drīfan in lǣs þonne 40 secondas.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Smallville_(TV_l%C4%ABne)

Smallville is Americanisc feorransīen endebyrdnes þe ongann in 2001 on Þæt WB
Feorransīen Nettweorc. Gescapen fram Alfred Gough and Miles Millar, sēo
endebyrdnes folgaþ þǣm sīðum þæs geongan Clark Kent in þǣm tūne Smallville, ǣr
þǣm þe hē wearþ Supermann.

Smallville wæs gestaðolod on þǣm swīðe folccūðum DC Comics Supermann swēg. Hē
wricþ þæt spell Ċlark Kentes swā geong mann þe wunaþ in þǣm tūne Smallville,
Kansase, hū hē handlaþ coping with geoguðe þā hwīle þe hē grēwþ ofermennisce
cræftas, āspyreþ his eleorþlice fruman, and winþ tō findenne his gewyrde.

Sēo endebyrdnes oft styreþ þā lēode in Clarkes līfe: his gefædriende mennisce
ealdras, Jonathan Kent and Martha Kent; his frīend, Chloe Sullivan, Pete Ross;
his lufu, Lana Lang; and gewislīce his frēondscipe mid geongum Lex Luthor.

Þæt gesceaft Kryptonite is gebrocen swā edcierrende lārsearu þurhūt þā
endebyrdnesse. Kryptonite is geīewed tō hæbbenne fremeða and latienda fremmunga
on menniscum bodigum adn se geonga superhæle oft sceal feohtan gecierrede þȳ
rūmstāne fīend, þe grēowon ungemǣne cræftas, swilc swā þanc-cræftas,
hīwcierrung-cræftas, and ōðere begeondanmǣne cræftas.

Hāweras oft sēoþ healfgemynegunga in ānsīene þæs gesprǣces, swēghrægles, and
ymbganggesceaftes gebrocen þurhūt þā endebyrdnesse, healfgemynegunga tō þǣm
Supermannes ātiefredbōcum and filmennum.

Smallville wæs swīðost on filmen geþrāwen in Vancouveres Niðer Mægenland in and
ymbe Clǣfrandæl, Bryttiscne Columbian, Canadan. Se tūn hæfþ bēacen æt his
ingange þe sægþ "Home of Smallville".



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sisavang_Vatthana

Sisavang Vatthana (þæs fullnama wæs Samdach Brhat Chao Mavattaha Sri Vitha Lan
Xang Hom Khao Phra Rajanachakra Lao Parama Sidha Khattiya Suriya Varman Brhat
Maha Sri Savangsa Vadhana) wæs Lao Cyning of his fæder deaþe in 1959 oþ 1975 þan
man hine ahwearf. Þæræfter hæfþ nān cyning gericsod on Laowarum.

Sisavang Vatthana wæs geboren æt Luang Phrabang on 13. Blōtmōnaþ 1907 þan wæron
eallum Lao rīcu under Frenciscum weardscipe. Þæt Lao Cynerīce ānedaþ Francas in
@ and Laoland weard sundorrīce in 1954. Sisavang Vatthana fang to rīce in 1959
æfter his fæder dēaþ. In eallum his lande wæs unfriþ and se cyning ne meahte
gedihtan his rīce. His rīce endode þan wæs Laoland ætfang be Paþet Lao sēo
Gemōtscipes gyld in 1975. Se Paþet Lao lēodweard sendede þone cynnig and his
cynn to 'getenyswice' and þær stearfon hie. Man hycgð ðe se cyning stearf on 13
May 1978 ac perhaps as late as 1984.

On 23 Wēodmōnaþ 1975 cwōm Pathet Lao þrēat in Vientiane, and þēos ceaster wæs
sēo endmeste burg þe hie ætfang. Se lēodweard weard wealdlēas and on 2 Gēolmōneþ
be niede forscrah Vatthana his rīce and þā Pathet Lao abanned þe se cynedōm be
beendod. Hie geafon þone cyning æmtig ambeht þe he bēon "Ealdorrǣdbora þæs
Foresittend". He forsōc to fliemene Laoland and in 1976 ageaf he his cynehealle
þæm Lao Leodwearde and fang to nēah gebūr þærin leah he under hūshæfte.

In Hrēþmōnaþ 1977 behæftede se Gemōtscipica lēodweard Vatthana Cyning for hiera
egsan þe meahte flieman in þæt land and lædan wiþerstand. Hie ætfang þone Cyning
mid þære Cwēne and his bearnum and gebrōðor and sendede hie to carcerewic æt Sam
Neua: hēr "Wic Gerīm Ān" heald hēah ambihtmenn þæs ærlēodwardes. Oft in þissum
dagum cwōmon menn þæs nīwan lēodweardes hired and ēac his Foresittend to mētenne
þone Cyning. He wæs se ieldsta numa in þæm wice.

In 1978, þæs lēodweardes bodan sæd þe that Vatthana Cyning, Khamphoui Cwēn, and
Vong Savang se Ierfa-Æþeling hæfdon forþferdon fram unlyfte. Nīworu talu secgþ
þe se Cyning forþferde in Hrēþmōnaþ 1980. Kaysone Phomvihane secgþ þe Vatthana
Cyning stearf in 1984, æt 77 wintra ylde.

Æfetr Vatthanan dēaþ and e-ac his ierfan weard þæs Cyninges iengsta sunu
Sauryavong Savang Æþeling hēafod þæs Laoisc cynecynn swa weardhlāford for his
nefan Soulivong Savang Ierfa-Æþeling.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Se_%C3%A6fterra_G%C4%93ola

Se æfterra Gēola oððe Gēola se æfterra is se ǣresta mōnaþ þæs gēares on þǣre
Gregoriscan gerīmbēc, and hæfþ 31 daga. His Lǣden nama, Januarius, is genumen of
þǣm Rōmāniscan gode Ianus, þǣm Rōmāniscan gode dura and inganga.

Æfterra Gēola and Solmōnaþ wǣron þā endemestan twēgen mōnþas, þe man īehte intō
þǣre gerīmbēc, siþþan þā Rōmwaran hæfdon fyrst winter for mōnaþlēasum fæce. Þēah
þe Hrēþmōnaþ fyrst se forma mōnaþ wæs, stang se æfterra Gēola on þone stede for
þǣm þe sē wæs þæt fæc hwonne consulas geþeawe wurdon gecoren.

Se forma dæg þæs mōnþes is gecnāwen swā Forweardes Gēares Dæg oþþe ānfealdlīce
Gēares Dæg.

Se Ielde Cymes dæg in Iapane is se ōðer Mōnandæg þæs Æfterran Gēolan, for þǣm þe
weorðaþ 20-wintre in þǣm nīwum . Hē is þēodlic symbeldæg. Se dæg stendeþ sīþ
1948, ac fēoll on 15an Æfterran Gēolan oþ 1999, hone man hine cierrde of þǣm
Iapaniscum lēodwearde in onginne tō hebbenne ūp þone earfoþdōm mid þȳ þe hī
maciaþ mā symbeldaga folgendra.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sc%C4%ABra_%C3%BE%C3%A6s_Ge%C4%81nl%C7%A3htan_Cyner%C4%ABces

Þæt Geāned Cynerīce hæfþ twa and hundnigontige scīra. Ēac hātaþ þisse scīra
eardfæstan scīra oððe gamola scīra.

Þisse scīra nabbað ane gerecþegnung, æfter mdccclxxxviiij, oððæt ðe to
mdcccclxxviiij stōwlicu āstyrung bād gestaðolod on hieran gierdum.

In Uladstire, stowlica ræden edniwung in mdcccclcciij arærde twa-endebyrdnes
stowlica ræden æt regio and læppa had; eall Uladstir wearþ seo regio.

On Engla and Norþ-wealum, þæt Local Government Act 1972 arærde scira for þæm
gesetnesa forþsetennesse utweard Grietran Lundene and Sylliege. Þa gerecþegnung
scira on Wealum wæron endedon in mdcccclxxxxvj.

In Englalande wæron mænigefealde læppan gesundrede fram hierum scirum æfter
mdcccclxxxx. Ælc "anfeald eard" (buton þa fram Bearrucscire) is scir be selfe
for þære gesetnesa, mid ānan læppan geond hierum halum earda, and hiere geþinge
is sēo geþinge þære scīre oððe sēo geþinge þæs læppan.

Scotland and Norþwealas habbaþ an-endebyrdnes "geþingedomas" and "fyrmestan
earde", þa on Wealum sume hetaþ "scīra" and sume "scīr-burgscipas".

Þæt Grietra Lunden eard (seo ne hatan næfre "scīr") wæs gearæred in mdcccclxv.
Þæt Grietra Lunden Gerec (Se Lundene Burgeald and Lundene Samnung) wæs in mm
gearæred.

On 1 Ēastermōnaþ 2009 (mmuiiii) weard þā Scīrgeþingas for Cornweallum,
Dunholmscīre, Norþhymbralande, Scrobbesbyrigscīre and Wiltunscīre ælc ānfeald
scīr. Beadanfordscīre and Ceasterscīre Scīregeþingas wæron beendedon.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/SF4

Street Fighter IV (Strǣte Feohtere IV on Englisce) is 2008 feohtend gamen macod
by Capcome. Hit is þæt fyrst ȝetalod Street Fighter gamen for þǣm arcadum siþþan
1999. Man ālīesde þæt sceattȝeƿyrhtod arcade gamen in Iapane on 18 Mǣdmōnþes,
2008, and Norðamericanisc arcadan inbrōhton hīe siþþan Ƿēodmōnþe. Man ālīesde þā
gamensearufadung þæs PlayStation 3 and Xbox 360 on 12 Sōlmōnþes, 2009 in Iapane,
in Norðamerican on 18 Sōlmōnþes, and in Europan on 20 Sōlmōnþes. Man ālīeseþ
Windows fadung in þǣm ōðrum fēorðlinge 2009.

Þēah Street Fighter IV hæfþ þing and bæcgrund in 3D, se gamenpleȝ ofstenþ
ȝesetliċ 2D feld. Producer Yoshinori Ono cƿæþ þæt ƿold hē þæt gamen tō
ofstandenne ȝeliċ tō Street Fighter II. Man inlǣde nīƿ betƿeoxbend hātte "Focus
Attacks" ("Saving Attack", oþþe "Spariende Ȝefeoht," for þǣre Iapaniscan
fadunge), and "Ultra" ȝefeoht. Se ȝesetliċ siex-cnæpp handræd eftcymþ, mid nīƿum
mearcungum and oferȝefeohtum þæs āsettan betƿeoxbendes, blandende ȝesetliċ
gamenpleȝ mid ēacliċum þancƿyrhtum.

Þæt gamen hæfþ sƿīðe ȝeliċ mōd mid Super Street Fighter II Turbo, ac hæfþ ēac
fram Street Fighter III 3rd Strike mæniȝ mearcunga. Beȝen leoht ȝefeoht cnæppas
cnocende biþ ȝiet ƿyrpes, and beȝen strang ȝefeoht cnæppas bēoþ sārcƿides. Beȝen
middel ȝefeoht cnæppas bēoþ spariende ȝefeohtes. Þæt gamen hæfþ ēac cnossian and
sƿift standend. Crimson Viper is se efne mann þe mæȝ hēah hlēap fremman.

Man macaþ þā menn and stedas þæs gamenes sƿā 3D bisena mid mæniȝhealfum, ȝeliċ
tō þǣre Street Fighter EX underendebyrdnesse þe Capcom macode mid Arikan, ac
notiaþ syndriȝ tōhīȝung tō ȝiefenne him handȝetācnode ānsīen, mid ēagetōhīȝungum
þe ēast asian ƿritend hæfþ, bōcblæc clǣmend, and bōcblæc scūr on þǣm campum. Se
hēafodcynstmann and mannƿyrhta is Daigo Ikeno, þe ǣror on Street Fighter III 3rd
Strike ƿyrhtode.

Spariende Ȝefeoht sind nīƿ betƿeoxbend þe man in Street Fighter IV inlǣdeþ. Þæt
is ȝefeoht þe þone pleȝere līefþ tō scyldenne ȝefeoht, and fremeþ ƿiþȝefeoht.
Man fremeþ þis þȳ middlum fyste and middlum spurne tōgǣdre cnocende. Þǣr sind
tƿeȝen hēafodƿeardas þæs ȝefeohtes. In þǣm formestan hēafodƿearde, se mann macaþ
nīƿ standend, þȳ hē ān ȝefeoht scyldeþ fram þǣm ƿiþfeohtere. Se ōðer hēafodƿeard
biþ ƿiþȝefeoht. Þȳ mā hielt se pleȝa þā middel fyst and spurn cnæppas, þȳ
strangor ƿierþ þæt ȝefeoht. Ȝif man þā cnæppas ȝenug healde, þæt ȝefeoht macaþ
þone ƿiþfeohtere tō þǣm grunde āfielþ, ȝiefende þǣm pleȝere frēo ȝefeoht.

Mid oferfadungum syndriȝa ȝefeohta þe man in ǣrum Street Fighter gamenum
inlǣdode, sƿā Super Combos (Ofersamƿrædnessa) and EX Syndriȝ Ȝefeoht, þæt gamen
inlǣdeþ ēac nīƿ cynn syndriȝes ȝefeohtes þe hātte Ultra Combo (Grēate
Samƿrædnessa). Grēate Samƿrædnessa sind lang filmliċ ȝefeoht þe mæniȝfeald
samƿrædnessa fysta, spurna and ōðra ȝefeohta hæfþ.

Tīdlīċe ȝesettod betƿēonan þǣre Street Fighter II endebyrdnesse and þǣre Street
Fighter III endebyrdnesse, þā pleȝende menn þǣre arcadan fadunge beinnaþ þā menn
þæs fyrstan Street Fighter II, and fēoƿer nīƿ menn. Akuma fram Super Street
Fighter II Turbo ānȳƿeþ sƿā ȝehȳded pleȝende mann, and ȝehȳded ƿiþfeohtere. Þæt
gamen ēac beinnaþ tƿeȝen efne-CPU menn: Seth biþ se læste oferƿiþfeohtere þæs
gamenes, and Gouken sƿā ȝehȳded ƿiþfeohtere, þe ƿierþ 19 menn.

Þā hāmfadunga Street Fighter IV habbaþ mā menn sƿā ēac þe fram þǣre arcade
fadunge. Þā hāmfadunga habbaþ Cammy and Fei-Long fram Super Street Fighter II,
Dan and Rose fram Street Fighter Alpha, Sakura fram Street Fighter Alpha 2, and
Gen fram þǣm fyrstan Street Fighter.

Fore teohhode Yoshinori Ono þone þanc ymbe þæt gamen tō Capcomes R&D hēafodmann
Keiji Inafune, mannum þyncþ hit in Capcome þe ne sculde man nīƿu ȝetælod gamen
þǣre Street Fighter endebyrdnes ne macian. Ǣrest, mæniȝ menn ƿiþhæfdon Ones þanc
nīƿes gamenes æfter sƿā mæniȝ ȝēar æfter þǣm formeste. Þēah, þe sēo gōdu
folcliċnes Street Figher II Hyper Fighting on Xbox Live Arcade ƿæs cūþ tō
Capcome, þafode Inafune man þone ƿeorc tō beȝinnenne.

Þis ƿæs sēo formest fandung Ones nīƿes gamenes Street Fighter endebyrdnesse sƿā
ƿyrhta, þēah ƿyrhtode hē ǣror on Street Fighter III 3rd Strike sƿā sūnd
hēafodƿyrhta, and ǣror ƿyrhtode hē Capcom Fighting Jam. Se ƿeorc on Super Street
Fighter II Turbo ƿearþ se hēafodtæs Street Fighter IV ƿeorcscipetēames.

Sēo Sōðe Iesus Cirice (on Nīwum Englisce:True Jesus Church) is selfdēmendlicu
Crīstnu cirice þe wæs gestaðelod fram Paul Wei in þǣm 1917. gēare in Beijinge on
Cīne.

Tōdæg hæfþ sēo cirice oþþe 1.5 þūsenda þūsenda oþþe 4 þūsenda þūsenda agyldena
in twǣm and fīftigum landum and seox worulddǣla. Hēo is cildcirice þǣre
Pentecostencirican Crīstendōmes þe tōcōm on þǣm ǣrran 20. hundgēare. Sēo cirice
ne frēolsaþ ne Crīstesmæssan ne Langfrīgedæg. Sēo cirice ungeþwǣraþ ymb þone
Þrillihād.

"Onfō þone gehātnan Hālgan Gāst, ǣboren þurh sprǣcunge on tungum, is se weard
ūrre erfeweardnesse on Heofones Rīce."

"Wæterfulwiht is se hāligdōm for þǣre forgifnesse synna and for ednīwunge. Se
fulwiht sceal gelimpan in gecyndelicum libbendum wætere, swā in þǣre ēa, sǣ,
oþþe fynt.

Se Bæzere, þe ǣr onfēng bæþ wæteres and þæs Hālgan Gāstes, fullaþ þurh naman þæs
Dryhtnes Iesus Crīstes. And se mann þe onfēhþ þone fulwiht sceal bēon fullīce
bedyped in wætere mid gebogenum hēafde and niðerweardum nebbe". (Iohannes 3:5;
Math. 3:16; Dǣda 2:38, 10:48).

"Se hāligdōm fōta wæsces lǣteþ þæt man dǣlnime mid Iesus. Hit þegnaþ ēac swā
gengu myndgung þæt man sceolde habban lufe, hālignesse, scamfæstnesse,
ālǣtnesse, and þegnunge.

Ǣlc mann þe onfēng wæteres fulwiht sceall habban his fēt gewæscen þurh naman
Iesus Crīstes. Frēondlic fōta wæsc bēo gedōn þǣr hē sī gehæp". (John 13:1-7)

"Sēo Hūselhālgung is hāligdōm tō gemunenne þæt cwealmbealu þæs Dryhtnes Iesus
Crīstes.

Hit lǣteþ ūs tō dǣlnimme þæs blōdes and þæs flǣsces ūres Dryhtnes and tō wesenne
on ānnesse mid Him swā þæt wē cunnen habban ēcelic līf and wesan rǣred on þǣm
æftermestan dæge. Þis hāligdōm biþ gehealden swā oft swā sī meahtlic. Synerlīce
ān þeorf hlāf and wīnberigena sēaw is gebrocen".

"Se Restdæg, se seofoða dæg þǣre wuce (Sæternesdæg), is hālig dæg, gebletsod and
gehālgod fram Gode. Hē biþ gehealden under þæs Dryhtnes āre tō þǣm gemynde Godes
gesceaftes and sparunge and mid þǣm hopan tō restienne ā on þǣm cumendan līfe."

"Iesus Crīst, þæt Word þe wearþ flǣsc, wæs cweled on þǣre rōde for þǣre animunge
gylta gyltera, ūp rǣred on þǣm þriddan dæge and astāg tō Heofonum. Hē is se
nergend manna, se Meotod þāra Heofona and þǣre eorðan, and se ān sōða God".

"Sēo Hālige biblioþēce, þe stent on þǣre Ealdan Gecȳðnesse and Nīwan Gecȳðnesse,
is ēðod fram Gode, þæt āncynne lagfæste sōþ, and þæt gemet Crīstna lifunge".

"Hreddung is gegifen fram þǣre giefe Godes þurh gelēaffulnesse. Gelīefendas
sculon hangian on þǣm Hālgan Gāste tō gesēcenne hālignesse, tō ārienne God, and
tō lufienne menn."

"Sēo Sōðe Iesus Cirice, gestaðelod fram ūserum Dryhtne Iesus Crīste, þurh þone
Hālgan Gāst in þǣre tīde þæs 'æfterran rīces', is sēo edstaðelode cirice þǣre
apostoliscan tīde."

"Þæs Dryhtnes Ōðer Cyme gelimpþ on þǣm æftermestan dæge þǣr hē niðer gǣþ fram
Heofonum tō dēmenne þā worulde: Þā gōdan sculon fōn ēcelic līf, ac þā yfelan
bēoþ ā aniðerod."



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/R%C4%ABma%C8%9Diefun%C8%9D

Rīmagiefung (on Nīwenglisce hātte algebra) is dǣl rīmcræftes be þǣre
cneordlǣcinge þāra laga of weorcunge and gesibbnessum, and þǣm timbrum and
oncnāwnessum þe arīsaþ from heom, ēac besetednessum, manigsetednessum,
efenweorðfindungum, and rīmagiefunglicum endebyrdnessum. Andefen eorþmetes,
arāflunge, stōwlāre, tellingalāre, and rīma flītcræftes is rīmagiefung ān þāra
hēafodlicena dǣla smǣtes rīmcræftes.

Þā þā Plato cōm, Crēcisc rīmcræft hæfde gefēred micele andwendunge. Þā Crēcas
sciepedon eorþmetlice rīmagiefunge on þǣre þe besetednessa wǣron tācnod fram
sīdum eorþmetlicra þinga, oftost līna, þā hæfdon stafan geþēote wiþ hīe.
Diophantus (þe lifode on þǣm 3. hundgēare æfter Crīste), þe hwīlum is gehāten
"se fæder rīmagiefunge", wæs Alexandrianisc rīmcræftmann and se wrītere
endebyrdnesse bōca þā hātaþ Rīmcræft. Þās gewritu standaþ be þǣre arāflinge
rīmagiefunglicra efenweorþfindunga.

Rīmagiefunge staðol biþ gefunden on gamolum Indiscum rīmcræfte, þe Muhammad ibn
Mūsā al-Khwārizmī (lifode fram þǣm 780. gēare oþ þæt 850. gēar) hefige onfēng on
mōde. Hē leornode Indiscne rīmcræft and inlēd hīe in þā Allahdōmiscan dǣlas þǣre
worulde þurh his wīdcūð rīmcræftlic gewrit, Bōc be Ēacnunge and Animunge æfter
þǣre Wīsan þāra Indiscena. Hē lator awrāt Sēo Sceortlice Bōc be Rīmweorcinge
þurh Fulfillinge and Efensettung, þe gesette rīmagiefunge tō rīmlāriscum cræfe
se is ānstandende fram eorþmete and grundrīmcræfte.

Þā staðolas rīmagiefunge cunnon wesan gefunden on þǣm gamolum Babyloniscum , þā
forðodon forðode rīmmetende endebyrdnesse þurh þā þe hīe cūðdon dōn rīmweorcunga
in rīmendebyrdnessiscre wīsan. Þā Babyloniscan forðodon endebyrdnessa tō
weorcienne arāflunga cnottena þe sindgewunelīce arāfled tōdæg be þǣre nytte
līnlicra efenweorþfindunga, fēowerscētra efenweorþfindunga, and unrīmra līnlicra
efenweorþfindunga. Tō ungelīcnesse, þæt mǣste dǣl Egyptiscena þisre tīde, and
Crēciscena and Cīniscena rīmlārmanna in þǣm 1 þūsendgēare fōre Crīste,
gewunelīce arāflede swelca efenweorþfindunga þurh eorþmetlica endebyrdnesse,
swelce þās amearcod in þǣm Rhind Rīmlāriscan Papyrus, Euclides Gesceaft, and Þā
Nigone Hēafodwearda on þǣm Rīmcræfte. Þæt eorþmetlice weorc þāra Crēciscena,
ēowod in þǣre bēc Gesceaft, macode þæt grundweorc for þǣre gewuneliclǣcunge
endebyrdnessa begeondan þā arāflunge sumra cnottena on maniga gewunelica
endebyrdnessa secgunge and arāflunge efenweorþfindunga, þēah þe þis ne scolde
wesan gecūþ oþ þā midealdan Alladōmiscan rīmcræftmenn.

Þā Crēciscan rīmcræftmenn Hero Alexandrie and Diophantus and Indisce
rīmcræftmenn, swelce Brahmagupta, hēoldon þā þēawas Ægyptes and Babilōnie, þēah
þe Diophantus Arithmetica and Brahmaguptan Brahmasphutasiddhanta standaþ on
hīeran efenette. Tō bȳsne, sēo forme fulle rīmcræftisce arāfling (befōne
nāwihtrīm and underran arāflunga) fēowerscētra efenweorþfindunga wæs amearcod
fram Brahmaguptan in his bēc Brahmasphutasiddhanta. Þǣræfter, Arabisce and
Muslime rīmcræftmenn forðodon rīmagiefungisca endebyrdnessa on swīðe hīeran
strengðe manigfealdnesse. Þēah Diophantus and þā Babylōniscan brucon oftost
ānlica endebyrdnessa tō arāflenne efenweorþlǣcinga, Al-Khwarizmi wæs se forma þe
arāflede efenweorþlǣcinga þā hwīle þe hē brēac brāda endebyrdnessa. Hē arāflede
þā līnlican unfæstlican efenweorþlǣcinga, fēowerscēta efenweorþlǣcinga,
unfæstlica efenweorþlǣcinga þǣre ōðerre endebyrdnesse and efenweorþlǣcinga mid
manigfealdum unfæstrīmum.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/R%C3%A6dwald

Rædwald (ēac (H)ræðwald), Tytilan sunu, wæs þæs Ēastengla cyning of ymb 600 oþ
his dēaþ in þǣm gēare 624. Fram 616 wearþ he sē rīcosta brytencyning besūþan
þǣre Humbran, and campes framscipum macede hē Norþanhymbranisc aloten dihtend tō
beorgenne willan his. Hē wæs forma Angel cyning begietan Crīstendōmes tæcinge
and fulwiht (fram þǣre Cantwarabyrig sande), and healp elnian hine wiþ þone
frambige of Ēastseaxum and Cent. Hē is se gecorenosta mann for þā namcūþan
Sūþtūn Hōh scipbyrgenna. In þǣm nigoðan hundgēare hē is reord in þǣm
Angelseaxiscum Cranicum tō wesenne Brytenwealda.

Þā forman and fullestan wrītunga be Rædwalde is Bēda þæm Stǣre Angelþeodes
cyricean, þe sægþ þæt his rīce betwēonum þǣre Augustiniscan sande cyme tō Cente
(on þǣm 597 gēare) and þǣre ǣwnunge and cierringe Ēadwines of Norþanhymbran
(fram 625 oþ 26). Consula æfterran trahtas (mid ungewislīcum dōme) secgaþ þæt
Rædwaldes dēaþ twā, æt 599 and 624, swā wēnunga þæt ofhende consula for 599 wæs
for Tytilan dēaþ and Rædwaldes āhafennesse.

For Rædwaldes geong līf wealdendeu hūs of ōþerum rīcum wæron becumende stranglic
fæstedon. Æðelbryht of Cent (forewesede 560-616) wæs weddede Berctan, Frankisc
Charibertes of Paris crīstene dohtor. Ceawlin West-Seaxna, mæst swīþ bregu sūþ
fram Humbre, æwde Æðelbryhtes infare fram Cent til 584, þā æfter feohtende þære
Brytena in Oxnafordscīr his rīce wanede and Æðelbryht āhte gelīc rīce. In Mierce
seo heolstoru līcnes Creoda, Iceles bearn, befæstede his cynnes grēatness. Norþ
fram Humbre ēa þā twā Deira rīcu (on Eoforwic) and þæt māra norþerne Bernice (on
Bamburgh) hæfdedon wiðerhȳdigu rīcu. Ælla of Deira racede til his dēaþ in 588,
lǣfende Acha dohtor and Edwin sunu swā mid þriddum siblinge. Þæt Bernicisc rīce
(gewæred cȳþþe West Seaxnan) wæs elnende rīcsunge, and Edwin gamolede in wræce
in Cadfan ap lago cafortūn of Gwynedde. In missenlicu wīg þæt Bernicisc Æðelfriþ
geānlǣcede Norþanhymbranisc rīce, and in 604 brōhte Deira under his ānwealde.

Rædwaldes gecynd fram Wuffan, Wuffinges genamed leōdfruma, is Bedes word. Hē wæs
geboren betweox þǣm 560 gēare and 580 and wæs (gelīce ieldra) Enian brōþor.
Wēnunga for þǣm 590um hē beweddede hæðenum wīfe mid hēagum cyste mōdstaðole hwæs
naman is ne cūþne. Fram hire hē hæfd be þæm læstan twā suna, Rægenhere (alder)
and Eorpwald. Ēac hē hæfd Sigeberht, ealder sunu oþþe stēopsunue.

Sē nama 'Sigeberht' is ne gelīc ænig ōþerne Wuffinga naman, ac hē is mǣnelic mid
þǣm Ēastseaxa rīce. Sledde Ēastseaxna Cyning (se rīcsode ymbe 587-604) beweddede
Ricula, Æðelbryhtes sweostor. Æðelbryht āhealp his nefan æfterfylgendnesse, hira
sunu, in Ēastseaxe, mid æfter þæm tūm cyningum becōmon of Crīstendōm. Hit is
manade þæt Rædwaldes wīf ǣr beweddede þæm cynnes gildan and Sigeberht wæs (swā
sægþ Willelm of Mælmesbeorge) Rædwaldes stēopsunu. Sigeberht (þæt grēow in
hæðenum hūse) earnode þā fēondrædenne Rædwaldes, þȳs drīfan him mid giestinge on
Galwalum, wēnunga weardian his āgenum blōde cynnes.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/R%C3%A6d%C6%BFald

Rædwald (ēac (H)ræðwald), Tytilan sunu, wæs þæs Ēastengla cyning of ymb 600 oþ
his dēaþ in þǣm gēare 624. Fram 616 wearþ he sē rīcosta brytencyning besūþan
þǣre Humbran, and campes framscipum macede hē Norþanhymbranisc aloten dihtend tō
beorgenne willan his. Hē wæs forma Angel cyning begietan Crīstendōmes tæcinge
and fulwiht (fram þǣre Cantwarabyrig sande), and healp elnian hine wiþ þone
frambige of Ēastseaxum and Cent. Hē is se gecorenosta mann for þā namcūþan
Sūþtūn Hōh scipbyrgenna. In þǣm nigoðan hundgēare hē is reord in þǣm
Angelseaxiscum Cranicum tō wesenne Brytenwealda.

Þā forman and fullestan wrītunga be Rædwalde is Bēda þæm Stǣre Angelþeodes
cyricean, þe sægþ þæt his rīce betwēonum þǣre Augustiniscan sande cyme tō Cente
(on þǣm 597 gēare) and þǣre ǣwnunge and cierringe Ēadwines of Norþanhymbran
(fram 625 oþ 26). Consula æfterran trahtas (mid ungewislīcum dōme) secgaþ þæt
Rædwaldes dēaþ twā, æt 599 and 624, swā wēnunga þæt ofhende consula for 599 wæs
for Tytilan dēaþ and Rædwaldes āhafennesse.

For Rædwaldes geong līf wealdendeu hūs of ōþerum rīcum wæron becumende stranglic
fæstedon. Æðelbryht of Cent (forewesede 560-616) wæs weddede Berctan, Frankisc
Charibertes of Paris crīstene dohtor. Ceawlin West-Seaxna, mæst swīþ bregu sūþ
fram Humbre, æwde Æðelbryhtes infare fram Cent til 584, þā æfter feohtende þære
Brytena in Oxnafordscīr his rīce wanede and Æðelbryht āhte gelīc rīce. In Mierce
seo heolstoru līcnes Creoda, Iceles bearn, befæstede his cynnes grēatness. Norþ
fram Humbre ēa þā twā Deira rīcu (on Eoforwic) and þæt māra norþerne Bernice (on
Bamburgh) hæfdedon wiðerhȳdigu rīcu. Ælla of Deira racede til his dēaþ in 588,
lǣfende Acha dohtor and Edwin sunu swā mid þriddum siblinge. Þæt Bernicisc rīce
(gewæred cȳþþe West Seaxnan) wæs elnende rīcsunge, and Edwin gamolede in wræce
in Cadfan ap lago cafortūn of Gwynedde. In missenlicu wīg þæt Bernicisc Æðelfriþ
geānlǣcede Norþanhymbranisc rīce, and in 604 brōhte Deira under his ānwealde.

Rædwaldes gecynd fram Wuffan, Wuffinges genamed leōdfruma, is Bedes word. Hē wæs
geboren betweox þǣm 560 gēare and 580 and wæs (gelīce ieldra) Enian brōþor.
Wēnunga for þǣm 590um hē beweddede hæðenum wīfe mid hēagum cyste mōdstaðole hwæs
naman is ne cūþne. Fram hire hē hæfd be þæm læstan twā suna, Rægenhere (alder)
and Eorpwald. Ēac hē hæfd Sigeberht, ealder sunu oþþe stēopsunue.

Sē nama 'Sigeberht' is ne gelīc ænig ōþerne Wuffinga naman, ac hē is mǣnelic mid
þǣm Ēastseaxa rīce. Sledde Ēastseaxna Cyning (se rīcsode ymbe 587-604) beweddede
Ricula, Æðelbryhtes sweostor. Æðelbryht āhealp his nefan æfterfylgendnesse, hira
sunu, in Ēastseaxe, mid æfter þæm tūm cyningum becōmon of Crīstendōm. Hit is
manade þæt Rædwaldes wīf ǣr beweddede þæm cynnes gildan and Sigeberht wæs (swā
sægþ Willelm of Mælmesbeorge) Rædwaldes stēopsunu. Sigeberht (þæt grēow in
hæðenum hūse) earnode þā fēondrædenne Rædwaldes, þȳs drīfan him mid giestinge on
Galwalum, wēnunga weardian his āgenum blōde cynnes.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pitcearn%C4%ABeg

Þā Pitcearnīgga (on Pitcearnisce hātāþ hīe Pitkern Ailen), gesetedlīce hātaþ
Pitcearn-, Hendersunu-, Ducie- and Oeno- Īega, stent on þrim of fēowra
fȳrbeorglicra īega in þǣm sūðernan Sericus Gārsecge. Þā īega sind Bryttisc
ofersǣwisc landscipe, se æftermesta þe gīet stent in þǣm Sericus Gārsecge.

Þā fēower īega – gehāten Pitcearn (gehāten Pitcairn on Nīwum Englisce),
Hendersunu, Ducie, and Oeno – licgaþ ofer sumum hundum mīla geofones and habbaþ
a fulle brǣdu of about 18 fēowerscētra mīla. Efne Pitcearrn, sēo þridde þurh
brǣdu and wīd 2 mīla, is geseted.

Þā īega sind gecūðosta tō botle þāra cildra þāra Bounty geswīcena and þāra
Tahitiscena wīfa þā mid him fōron, þe is gelimpung eft teald oft on manigum
bōcum and scēawspellum. Þis spell is gīet gesewenlic in þǣm cūþnamum þāra
īegbūenda.

Mid efne 50 landbūendum (of nigonum cynnum), Pitcearn is ēac mearcweorþ tō
wesenne se læst folcseteda and gesundrodosta dōm in þǣre worulde (þēah hit nis
wealdende rīce). Hit is þæt læst folcsetede land in þǣre worulde. Þāre Geāndena
Þēodscipa Gemōt Unfolcsetunge befēhþ þā Pitcearnīega on þǣm Geānedra Þēodscipa
getæl Unselfwealdendra Landscipa.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/O%C3%B0re_Punisc_G%C5%AB%C3%BE

Se Ōðru Penisca Gewinn, þe Rōmware hetaþ elleswīse Se Hannibalisca Gewinn oððe
Seo Gūð wið Hannibale, oððe "Se Cartainisce Gewinn", wæs miclu gūþ of þære
Rōmāniscan Cynewīsan wiþ Cartaine þa burg. Þes sæcc læstede of 218 to 201
beforan Criste and his fēohtas wæron andlang Wendelsǣs rīmum of westen to
ēasten.

Þes wæs seo ōþru micle gūþ betwuh Cartaina and Rōme and þās tū rīcu hæfdon þreo
micel sæccas wiþ him ofer hiera ieldu þa hēt man þa "Peniscan Gewinnas" of
Rōmwara nama for Cartainafolce, Poeni, of Pene þæm folce of Wendelsǣs ēastrīme
þa gestaðoledon Cartaina.

In þissum sæcce gewonn Hannibal micel lof. He wæs Cartaine heretoga his mǣrostan
dædas wæron þe he brōhtede elpendas ofer Alpis þæm beorgum in Italie and his
micel sige æt Cannae. Hannibal fōr of Cartaine landrīcu on Ispanie and cwōm in
Gallie þære fulltumedon hine Galware. Þæn fōr his here mid his elpendum in
Italie.

In Italie hæfde Hannibal micel sige ofer Rōme æt Trebie and æt þæm miclan
sætnunge be Trasimene þæm mere. In þæm folgendan gear (216 bC), hæfde Hannibales
here ēac sige ofer Rōmwarum, æt Cannae in sūðernum Italie, and æt þissum
garmittunge wæron Rōmes legie eall forgrunden. Æfter þissum, manig byrig þa ær
wæron Rōmes geþoftan wendedon to Cartaine healfe, and forþæm bād wig on Italie
for tiene winter and lengre.

Wiþ Hannibales cræfte on þæm felde nyttedon Romware þone Fabianiscan wigcræfte
þe hie awerie Cartainie þreat.

In þæm ilcan ield slog Publius Cornelius Scipio Roamanisc heretoga Cartainisc
cræft in Ispanie; þær nam Scipio Carthago Nova þa ceastre and heald eall Iberia
æfter Ilipa thaare Beadwe. Þæræfter seglod Scipio on Affrice and his endmesta
feoht þæs gewinnes wæs at Zama fore Cartaine þære ceastre self. On þæm dæge
feohte Scipio wið Hannibal and Hannibal wæs sigeleas. Cartaina weard Rōmes
underrīce.

Ðæn feahtedon Rōm wiþ Cartaine in Wendelsǣs westdæle, be ēasten wæs se Forma
Mæcedonisca Gewinn, ac naht wolde hilde gesceadan hēr. Swylc wig wæs sæcc in
Wendelsǣs ēastdæl and in þæm Ioniscan Sǣ.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Normandi%C8%9D

Normandig is stede in Franclande, be Franclandes norðan. Hit wæs gesetlod fram
Norþmenn.

Normandig hæfþ 3.2 þūsenda þūsenda landbūenda, mid landware þiccnesse 107/km2.
Þæt is hwega under þǣm gemǣnan rīme Franclandes, and in uferran Normandige gǣþ
þæt rīm tō 145. Þā hēafodbyrg sind: Roðem (on Frencisce: Rouen) (385,000
burgwara, mid underburgum), se hēafod uferran Normandiges and gēo þæs hālan
landdǣles; Le Havre (247,000); Caþum (on Frencisce: Caen (200,000), þæt hēafod
niðeran Normandiges; and Kiæresburh (on Frencisce: Cherbourg) (89,000).

Se landscipe bebyrdeþ andlang þāra norðernra rimena þā Sūþsǣ. Þā sind granitisc
cleofu west and cealcstānes cleofu ēast. Þā sind ēac lang sporu riman in þǣm
middan þæs landscipes. The bocage, patchwork of small fields with high hedges,
typical of the western areas caused problems for the invading forces in the
Battle of Normandy. There are meanders of Sigene as it approaches its estuary
which form a notable feature of the landscape.

The Pont de Normandie crossing the estuary of the Seine is regarded as a feat of
modern engineering.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nemniendlic

Se nemniendlica cāsus (Nīwe Englisc: nominative case) is grammatisc cāsus for
namum. Sume wrīteras on Nīwum Englisce brūcaþ ēac þæt word subjective cāsus for
nemniendlicne, in order to draw attention to the differences between the
"standard" generic nominative and the way it is used in nīwum Englisce.

Se nemniendlica mearcaþ, generally, þā forþsetennesse sumes wordes. Nemniendlice
cāsas sind gefundene in Lǣden and Ealdum Englisce, ongemang ōðrum sprǣcum.
Englisc hæfþ gīet sume nemniendlice bīnaman, efenāmeten mid þǣm wregendlicum
cāse oþþ gebīegdum cāse: ic (wregendlic mec), wē (wregendlic ūsic), hē
(wregendlic hine), hēo (wregendlic hīe) and gē (accusative ēowic). On Englisce
habbaþ wē ēac þū, se ōðeres hāda bīnama (wregendlic þec) and manigfealdlic gē
(wregendlic ēowic). Syndriglīce spricþ man þāra bīnamena wit (wregendlic uncit)
and git (wregendlic incit), hwonne man spricþ ymbe twēgen menn.

se nemniendlica cāsus is þæt gewunelice, cynde ansīen (more technically, the
least marked) of certain dǣlas, such as nouns, adjectives, pronouns and less
frequently numerals and participles, and sometimes does not indicate any special
relationship with other parts of speech. Therefore, in some languages the
nominative case is unmarked, þæt is, the nominative word is the base form or
stem, with no flexion. Moreover, in most languages with a nominative case, the
nominative form is the one used to cite a word, to list it as a dictionary
entry, asf.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ne%C3%B0erlandisce_ge%C3%BE%C3%A9ode

Sēo Niðerlendisce sprǣc (Nīwenglisce: Dutch, Niðerlendisce: Nederlands) is
Westgermanisc sprǣc, þē fram Niðerlande ārās. Hēo is sēo eahta-and-fēowertigoðe
mǣste gelōmlice "ǣreste sprǣc", and hit hæfþ 23 millionan folces in 2007.
Gelōmlice is þæt cynn Niðerlandiscre sprǣce, þe is on Belgican gesprecen, þēo is
Flemisc gehāten. In Norþeastum dǣle þæs landes biþ sēo Niðerseaxisce sprǣc
gesprecen, Achterhoeks, Drents, Stellingwerfs, Twents and Gronings.

Þā mǣstan Niðerlendiscan word cumað of þǣre Ealdan Germaniscan sprǣce. Sum cumað
of Lǣdene and Crēacisce and fēawa of Nīwenglisce and Frencisce. Þæt word schip
cymð of seolfre orsprunge swā Englisc scip.

Eald niðerlendisc byð sēo ylce sprǣc swa sēo niðere Franconisc hātte (eastern
and western). Lange se niðerlendisc þōhton hira ieldeste writing wǣre:

Nū hycgeþ man þa þes cȳma cwide bēo eald Centisc and nis þæs ealdan
niðerlendiscan gereordes. Ac þenden sind gifundan oðre cwidas (on Hloðwices
rihtbēc be naman Lege Salica). Se ieldest byð:

Þēah eac sīe mihtelīce þæt ieldest niðerlendiscne bēon þās rún-stæfas læs
lēoðlican under-neoþan:



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Napoleon

Napoleon I Francena Cāsere oððe Napoléon Bonaparte (wæs geboren þæs 15.
Wēodmōnþes þæs 1769. gēares – cwæl þæs 5. Þrimilcemōnþes þæs 1821.) wæs Frencisc
heretoga and rīca þe wearþ brēme under þǣre Frenciscan Onhebbinge and ōðrum
gelīcum wīgum.

Corsica þæt īegland wæs Napoleones gebyrdestede. Hē wæs geboren in Ajaccio byrg
in þǣm 1769. gēare, ānum wintre siþþan Francan hæfdon geboht þæt īegland fram
Genoa. His nama æt byrde wæs in þǣm Italiscan gereorde Napoleone di Buonoparte.
Þā eode hē on Francum nām hē Frencisce wīsan, Napoléon Bonaparte.

In þǣm 1779., æt ilde tīen wintra, fērde Napoleon tō þǣm cirican leornunghūse æt
Autun. Æfter Autun ēode hē tō þǣm heres leorninghūsum æt Briènne-le-Château and
þon þǣm æt Paris. He leornede tō wesenne feldwǣpengerēfa in Franclande.

In þǣm 1789. begann sēo Frencisce Tōwending and Napoleon ēode to Corsican, þǣr
wæs ungerec. In þǣm 1792. þā Loðewis XVIII Cyning wæs tōworpen and sēo Forme
Frencisce Cynewīse begann, genamode man Napoleon Hēafodmann.

Napoleones forme weorces ambiht wæs at Toulon, þā þegnede tō adrǣfenne Brittisce
and Spēonisce þrēatas fram þǣre hȳðe and þǣre byrg.

Tō Heretogan hædde hē micelne sige on Italie. He scōp þā Cisalpine Cynwīsan on
norþernre Italie and þā Heleuetisce Cynewīsan, þā seo Rōmānisce Cynewīse būton
þǣm Papiscan Rīce and þǣre Parthenopiscan Cynewīsan in eallre sūþernre Italie.
He gesōhte Ēastrīce þurh Alpis and be nīede nām Ēastrīce friþ and griþ wið
Francum.

In þǣm 1798. inswēog Napoleon Heretoga Ægypt. His liþ wæs be Horatio Nelson
adīleged æt Nīl Sǣfeohte and hē flēah on Francan.

In 1799, Bonaparte tōwearp þā Frenciscan Folcgesamnunge and leodwearde, and
gestaþoled hē þæt Consulatum, hwǣrin wæs hē se Forma Consul. Swa Consul reformed
hē þæt Francena rīce. He tōwendede eall stōwlicu rihtbēc and for rihte gesetede
hē ofer eallum Franclande þæt Code Napoleon. Þes Code Napoleon is nū þā grund
for riht ofer mæstum Europan, būton Bryten and Īrland.

Æfter fīf wintrum þæs Consulatum settede Napoleon corunbeag on his hēafod swa
Francena Casere.

In þǣr nigontieneþ gearhundrede forma tien gearum, forþsendede Napoleon þæs
Frenciscan Rīces herigas wiþ ælcum miclum Europiscan rīcum and underþeodede
Europe sigerōf in manigum beadwum, to bisene Austerlitz.

Napoleon Casere friþ gestaðolede ofer Europan, būton mid þǣm Bretwarum.
Francland þæt rīce beclyppede Francland, Holland, Tuscanie, Rōm and Dalmatie.
Napoleon wæs ēac Eotolwara Cyning. Ēastweard wǣron under þeodedan rīce; se Rīn
Āþgebēorscipe and Switzerland, and begeondan Warsaw Hēah Þeodenrīce (Polaland).
His brēþer and heretogum geaf hē cynestōlas geond Europan. His sweostru
gēmungedon æþelingas and cyningas. Prussia and Ēastrīce wǣron be niede mid him
in geþoftrædne.

Nōþylæs, þæt Geānlǣhte Cynerīce and Portugal onsōcon hine. On þǣm brime hæfde se
Bryttisca Cynelica Sciphere duguþmihte; Horatio Nelson forgrund Napoleones ligþ
æt Trafalgar Sǣfeohte and se Cynelice Sciphere besettede Frenciscan hyða þurh þā
gūþe. In Spēonlande and Portugal fēohtedon Bretware and Portugalþēod wiþ
Napoleones hergas and ādrufon hie fram þǣm landum.

In 1812 inswēog Napoleon Russland. Hēr endede his wīgblēd. His Micela Here
(Grande Armée) drēag cwealm in þǣre fierdinge and āwierpede nǣfre. In 1813 cōmon
þā Germaniscan Rīcu and Russland and sige hædde wiþ þǣm Frenciscan þrēat æt
Leipzig. Þā in 1814 inswēog hie Francland. In þǣm ilcan gēare fullfremmede
Wellington Spēonland to ofergān and inswēog Francland fram þæm sūþen.

Þā his fiend inswēog Francland flīemede Napoleon. Man him anām to Elban seo īeg
and him hie geag swa hiere brego.

Æfter læs þonne ānum gēare, ætlēop hē fram Elban and feng eft to rīce. He
ācwicede his Rīces hergas and fōr forþ tōweardes Bryseles. Wellington hine
oferdrāf æt þǣre Waterloo Beadwe on 18 Sēremōnaþ 1815. Þeos firstgemearc wæs "þā
Hundred Dagas".

Þā endemeste siexe gearu Napoleones Līfes spent hē on Sancte Elene Īege
ofersigon be þæm Brittiscan gereca. He forferede of gehrif cancere on 5
Þrimilcemōnaþ 1821.

In 1840 brōhte Loðwic-Philippus Cyning þæs Caseres bānas tō Paris. He licþ nū in
lof in Les Invalides.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Napol%C3%A9on_Bonaparte

Napoleon I Francena Cāsere oððe Napoléon Bonaparte (wæs geboren þæs 15.

Napoleon Casere friþ gestaðolede ofer Europan, būton mid þǣm Bretwarum.
Francland þæt rīce beclyppede Francland, Holland, Tuscanie, Rōm and Dalmatie.
Napoleon wæs ēac Eotolwara Cyning. Ēastweard wǣron under þeodedan rīce; se Rīn
Āþgebēorscipe and Switzerland, and begeondan Warsaw Hēah Þeodenrīce (Polaland).
His brēþer and heretogum geaf hē cynestōlas geond Europan. His sweostru
gēmungedon æþelingas and cyningas. Prussia and Ēastrīce wǣron be niede mid him
in geþoftrædne.

Nōþylæs, þæt Geānlǣhte Cynerīce and Portugal onsōcon hine. On þǣm brime hæfde se
Bryttisca Cynelica Sciphere duguþmihte; Horatio Nelson forgrund Napoleones ligþ
æt Trafalgar Sǣfeohte and se Cynelice Sciphere besettede Frenciscan hyða þurh þā
gūþe. In Spēonlande and Portugal fēohtedon Bretware and Portugalþēod wiþ
Napoleones hergas and ādrufon hie fram þǣm landum.

In 1812 inswēog Napoleon Russland. Hēr endede his wīgblēd. His Micela Here
(Grande Armée) drēag cwealm in þǣre fierdinge and āwierpede nǣfre. In 1813 cōmon
þā Germaniscan Rīcu and Russland and sige hædde wiþ þǣm Frenciscan þrēat æt
Leipzig. Þā in 1814 inswēog hie Francland. In þǣm ilcan gēare fullfremmede
Wellington Spēonland to ofergān and inswēog Francland fram þæm sūþen.

Þā his fiend inswēog Francland flīemede Napoleon. Man him anām to Elban seo īeg
and him hie geag swa hiere brego.

Æfter læs þonne ānum gēare, ætlēop hē fram Elban and feng eft to rīce. He
ācwicede his Rīces hergas and fōr forþ tōweardes Bryseles. Wellington hine
oferdrāf æt þǣre Waterloo Beadwe on 18 Sēremōnaþ 1815. Þeos firstgemearc wæs "þā
Hundred Dagas".

Þā endemeste siexe gearu Napoleones Līfes spent hē on Sancte Elene Īege
ofersigon be þæm Brittiscan gereca. He forferede of gehrif cancere on 5
Þrimilcemōnaþ 1821.

In 1840 brōhte Loðwic-Philippus Cyning þæs Caseres bānas tō Paris. He licþ nū in
lof in Les Invalides.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/N%C3%ADwe_Englisc_spr%C7%BDc

Sēo Nīwenglisce sprǣc (on Nīwenglisce: English) is Westgermanisc sprǣc, þe on
Englalande ārās. Hēo belimpeþ, swā sēo Þēodisce sprǣc and sēo Niðerlendisce
sprǣc tō þǣm Westernan twige þāra Germaniscra sprǣca.

Nū is Englisc sēo brādoste gesprǣdede sprǣc þǣre worulde, and hæfþ ymbe þæt
getæl sprecera þe Cīnisc hæfþ. In fela landum biþ Nīwenglisc sēo ǣreste fremðe
sprǣc gelǣred (Sēo Englisc (Scōl)) and is sēo ambihtlice sprǣc þāra mǣstena
betwixfolclicra gesetednessa. Fela þissa gesetednessa habbaþ ōðra ambihtlica
sprǣca. Nīwenglisc prōfaþ hēodæg swā woruldsprǣc.

Tōdæg biþ Englisc fram 340 millionena sprecenda swā mōdorsprǣc gesprecen. Gif
man īeceþ þā æfterran sprecend, cymþ man tō ymbe 510 millionena sprecenda.

Englisc cymþ of þǣre Ealdre Seaxiscre sprǣce and sibbum þēowsprǣcum þe wǣron
gebrōht tō Brytene fram Germaniscum gesittendum of syndrigum dǣlum norþwestes
Þēodisclandes. Sēo frume Englisce sprǣc wæs gehrinen folgiendlīce fram twǣm ȳðum
onrǣses. Se ǣresta onrǣs wæs fram sprecerum sprǣca Scedelendisces twiges þæs
Germaniscan sprǣchīredes, þe gebȳrdon in dǣlas Brytene in þǣm 8an and 9an
ieldum. Se ōðer onrǣs wæs mid Normandigsǣtum in þǣre 11an ielde, þe cynn
sprǣcon, Ealdes Frencisces.

Be þǣm Engliscan-Seaxiscan Cranice, ymbe þæt gēar 449, wǣron þā Engle gelaðode
fram Wyrtgeorne tō helpenne him wiþ þā Pihtas. Ongēan hira help gelendode hē þǣm
Englum in sūþēastum dǣle. Æfter sōhte hē māran help, and forþǣm cōmon þā Seaxe,
Engle, and Geate. Se Cranic spricþ ymbe fylgendne incyme gesittendra, þe
staðelodon on ende seofon cynerīcu. Tōdæges scōlerscipe behogeþ mǣst þisses
spelles tō bēonne spell and fram lēodweardrace gedōne.

Þās Germaniscan infarend oferrīcsodon þā fruman Celtisce sprǣcendan wuniend, þā
sprǣca þāra ālifdon mǣste on Scotland, Wealas, Cornweall, and Īrland. Þā
folcsprǣca, gesprecena fram þǣm ingengum, macodon þæt, þe man hēt Eald Englisc,
þe efenlǣcþ suma rimanþēowsprǣca, in (nū) landum norþwestes Þēodisclandes and
þāra Niðerlanda. Ufor wæs sēo sprǣc gehrinen fram þǣre Norþgermaniscre sprǣce
Norene, þǣra Wīcinga gesprecen, þe on þone norþēastan dǣl gesǣtton (sēo
Georfic).

For þǣm folgiendum 300 gēarum æfter þǣre Norþmandiscan Geþringunge in 1066
sprǣcon þā Norþmandiscan cyningas and sēo hēa duguþ cynn Frencisces āne. Micel
getæl Norþmandiscra worda wǣron inbrōht in Eald Englisc. Se Norþmandisca gehrine
gefæstnode þā gangendan hwierfunge þǣre sprǣce ofer fylgendum ieldum, oþ þǣre
sprǣce, nū Middelenglisc gehāten. Lareowas þǣre tunges lare ne laerdon;
leorneres heora spraec ne leornode. For þon þe þæt folc þāra Norþmanna þeowas
ȝeƿurdon, swa ealswa mot mon þæt 'Niwenglisc' beter 'þeowenglisc' ȝehatan.

In þǣre 15an ielde gewende sēo Micele Selfswēgendwendung þæt Middelenglisc, ēac
mid Lundencyndre sprǣce in lēodwearde and tōþegnunge, and þǣre
regolunggefremmunge gemǣlunge. Nīwenglisc cann gespyred bēon on bæc tō þǣre tīde
Willelmes Shakespeares.

Sēo Nīwenglisce sprǣc is dǣl þæs westernan undertwiges þæs Germaniscan twiges
þæs Indiscan-Europiscan sprǣca cynnes. Feorr þǣra Englisclǣhtan sprǣca swā Tok
Pisin oþþe Bislama, sind þā nīehstan Nīwenglisces Scyttisc (Lallans), mǣste on
Scotland and dǣl Norðernes Īrlandes gesprecen, and þǣræfter Fresisc, on
Þēodiscland and on þǣm Niðerlandum gesprecen. Swā Nīwenglisc is Scyttisc riht
æftergenga Englisces (Englisc-Seaxisc).

Ōðra sibba sprǣca, ac unsibbran þonne Fresisc oþþe Scyttisc, sind Þēodisc,
Seaxisc, Niðerlendisc, Scedelendisca sprǣca, and Afrikaanisc. Manig Frencisc
word sind ēac andgietfullicu tō Nīwenglisces sprecende (ac mid ōðrum
rihtstefne), for þǣm þe Nīwenglisc bedranc ormǣtlic rīm worda fram Frencisce
þurh þā Norþmandisce sprǣce æfter þǣre Norþmandiscan Oferswīðrunge and rihtlīce
of Frencisce in æfterrum ieldum; þǣrfor sind fela worda swīðe nēah þǣm
Frencisce, mid smalum wrītungscēadungum (on wordendungum oþþe mid Ealdes
Frencisces wrītungum, asf.), ēac swā hwīlum scēadunga on mǣnunge.

Englisc grammaticcræft hafaþ lȳtele gebīegunge in efenlǣcnesse mid ōðrum
Indoeuropicum sprǣcum. Tō bisene hæfþ Nīwenglisc, ungelīc Þēodisce,
Niðerlendisce, oþþe Rōmāniscum sprǣcum nān grammatisc cynn and nāne
tōgeīecendlice ānrǣdnesse. cāsu mearcung is æthwōn fullīce gedwinen of þǣre
sprǣce and ālifþ mǣste on þā bīnaman. Þā cynn strangra worda (t.b.
sprecan/spræc/sprǣcon/gesprecen) wiþ þā cynn wācra worda þe sēo sprǣc of
Germanisce ierfde is on weorðe gedwinen and þā lāfa gebīegunge (swā
manigfealdlicu mearcung) wurdon regolfæsta.

Þā seolfan tīd þǣre gebīegunge weorþgedwīnung in Englisce, scōp sēo sprǣc māran
getrēowunge in wīsan swā mōdword and worddiht tō getācnienne grammatisce
mǣnunge. Helpendu word brȳcþ man tō mearcienne tācnu swā frignunga, negativa, þā
underþēodendlican stefn, and gengende tīd

Mid Englisce brȳcþ man þā lǣdene stæfrǣwe būtan accentum, ac mid elþēodigum
wordum, swā résumé (Frencisc) cann man mid accentum wrītan. Mid manigum wordum,
swā night oþþe though is sēo wrītungwīse stǣrlicu (nā sprecendllicu), for þǣm þe
on Middelenglisce wrāt man night and though. Sēo wrītung worda oft ābȳgþ of hū
hīe gesprecen sind, and Nīwenglisc wrītung is oft geþōht sēo unēaðoste ǣnigra
sprǣca tō leornienne, in þǣm sprǣcum þe brūcaþ stæfrǣwa. Sēo Nīwenglisc
rihtwrītunge.

Englisc is ambihtsprǣc in þǣm fylgendum landum, þǣrin þæt getæl þāra
mōdorsprecera is gewriten, hwǣr cūþ:

Englisce sprǣc þegnaþ tō ēacan swā lingua franca in þǣm folgiendum landum and
landscipum:



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moretoin

Moretoin is tūn on Normandige in westnorþenum Franclande, nu on his ‘’Manche’’
scīre. Se tūn stent on stænenum beorge se stigð ofer þæm crundle þærin flēoweþ
Cance sēo ēa, Sélune ēa tributary.

In þære Middelyldan wæs Moretoin hēafodstōl ofer important eorldōme (Frencisc:
comté), in þæm handum þæs cynecynnes Normandiges and of þæm hūs wæron his
eorlas. Ymbe 1027 wæs þes eorldom gestaþoled for Roðbeart, se wæs aliefþ man
Ricardes Eorles bastard. Æfter Roðbeartes ierfa wæs Willelm Warlenc, Roðbeartes
sunu. In 1049 oððe ymbe þæm geare anām Willelm Normandiges Eorl þone eorldom of
Willelm Warlenc and geaf hine his healfbrēder, Roðbeart, se wæs þæræfter "Eorl
of Moretoine," and his micel agnunge on Englum æfter þæm Gehiersumunge in 1066
geaf naman "þæm lytlum tūnum Moretoines," þā ahtedon læss þegnunge his hlāforde
þonne oþru.

Æfter Roðbeart ierfede Willelm Eorl of Moretoin his sunu, and Willelm feahtede
wiþ Heanric I Cyning, and wæs gefengen æt the Tenercebrai Beadwe in 1106 and for
his dǣd losede eall his agnung. Æfter fēwum wintrum geaf Heanric Cyning his
nefan Stepne þone eorldōm. Stepne fang to rīce on Englum and on Normandige in
1135. On Stephen's dēaþ in 1154 weard Willelm his sunu Eorl of Moretoin, ac on
þæn forþferde Willelm būton bearnum in 1159 nām Heanric II Cyning þone eorldōm
and his land and title. Ricard I Cyning (1189) geaf Moretoin his brōþor
Iohannes, and he wæs be title Eorl of Moretoin oð he fang to rīce in 1199.
Iohannes losede Normandig and mid his landum losede he ēac Moretoine. Noþȳlǣs
æfter eftnām se Lonceastre Hūs Normandig, wæs Ēadmund Beaufort, Iohannes of
Gaunt sunusunu, gebanned Eorl of Moretoin and bār swylc title oð 1441 þan wæs he
Eorl of Dorsætum.

In Wēodmōnaþ 1944 in Moretoin wæs miclu gārmitting betwuh Germaniscum and
Americaniscum wigum. Ofer siexe nihtum feahtede hwæte se 30. Fēðan Bedælunge
fought wiþ Germaniscum byrnewægnum in Operation Lüttich, þe hie preserve the
breakout staþolede in Operation Cobra. J D Salinger writere feahtede in þæm
Americaniscum þrēate and of þisre onfundelnesse sæd his dōhtor cwōm his līfes
gnornsorg.

Moretoines scild is in þara bodan gereorde: Azure, semy de lys Or, a bend
compony argent and gules.

Sēo tūncirice be naman Halga Evroult is magnificent example of the transitional
style of the early 13th century. Close to the town is the Abbaye Blanche,
founded as a Benedictine convent in 1105 and soon afterwards affiliated to
Cîteaux. The church is a perfect example of a Cistercian monastic church of the
late 12th century, and portions of the 12th-century cloisters also survive. The
ruins of a castle was once the home of the cruel Sir Guillaume de Moretoin and
the site of the Gap of Goeblin.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Modern_english

https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mirai_Nagasu

Mirai Aileen Nagasu (geboren 16 Ēastermōnaþ, 1993) is Americanisc lēoðlic
scātestre. Hēo is 2008 G.R.A. Þēodlic Ceamp and 2007-2008 Geong Grand Prix Final
Ceamp. Nagasu wann þone seolfor tācn æt þǣm 2007 Woruld Junior Lēoðlican
Scātunge Ceampgelimpe and þone bræs tācn æt þǣm 2008 Woruld Geongan Lēoðlican
Scātunge Ceampgelimpe.

Nagasu is sēo gingesta mægþ siþþan Tara Lipinski in 1997 tō winne þone
ceampscipe G.R. ealdra wīfa, and is sēo ōðer gingesta in stǣre. Hēo is sēo forma
mægþ siþþan Joan Tozzer in 1937 and 1938 tō winne in endebyrdum gēarum þā
geongan and ealdoran þēodlīce ceampscipas.

Nagasu wæs in Montebelle, Los Angeles Scīre Californian geboren, and eardaþ in
Arcadian, Californian. Hire ealdras cymþ of Iapane and hēo is Iapanamericanisc.
Hire nama Mirai is Iapanisc word þe wyrd mǣnþ. Man mæg hire nama writan on
Iapanisce mid kanji swā 長洲未来 oþþe mid kana swā ミライ・ナガス.

Forþǣm Nagasu wæs in þǣm G.R. geboren, ac begen hira ealdra wǣron in Iapane
geboren, hēo hæfþ twinne landwarehād mid þǣm G.R. and Iapane. Be þȳ Iapanisce
lage, hēo þearf cēosan hwelce landwarehād tō healdenne fore hire 22e beorþdæg.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mihtesetl

On stēormǣle is hēafodstōl (ēac hēafodburg and hēafodburh hātte) sēo hēafodlice
burg oþþe tūn gesibb hire wealde. Hēo is nēan ā sēo burg þe līchāmlīce befēhþ
þæt setlærn and þæt gemōtærn þæs setles wealdes and is geseted be lage.

Þā setlu wealdes on mægenum underrīciscum dōmum sind gewunelīce hēafodstōlas
gehāten, ac æfter læssum wealdendum underdǣlum, word swelce fylces tūn, fylces
setl, oþþe byrig setl sind ēac gebrocen.

Þǣr sind maniga gelimpunga þǣr rīcu oþþe ōðre ānstandendas habbaþ manige
hēafodstōlas. On Sūþaffrican, tō bȳsne, se wealdenda hēafodstōl is Pretoria, se
lagsettenda hēafodstōl is Næsstūn, and se dēmenda hēafodstōl is Blōtsmanwelle,
þe is þæt gelimp þæs gesēmes þætte gesciepede þæt Sūþaffrican Gæd on 1910.

On swelcum gelimpungum is sēo burg þe hielt þone wealdenda hēafodstō gewunelīc
understanden wesan se "rīcisca hēafodstō" ongemang elemanna. Tō bȳsne, Santiago
is understanden wesan se hēafodstōl of Cilan þēah hire Gemōt is in Falparegse.

Tō hēafodlicum stede wealdes þæs landscipes oþþe rīces, se hēafodstōl
gecyndelīce atihteþ þā stēormǣllīce geānmētedum and him þāra cræftas sind
þorftene tō welwyrcendum wealde swelce ǣswutolas, tīdingwrīteras, and folclices
rǣdes cneordlǣcendas. Ieldre hēafodstōlas habbaþ ēac oft grōwen on fornytte
stēormǣllice, līfwīsisce, oþþe andgietfule stōlas. Swelc is hūru sēo gelimpung
Parises on Franclande and Buenos Airese Argentinan ongemang rīciscra
hēafodstōla, and Irkutskes oþþe Saltlagburge on Utā on heora landscipum.
Nāþȳslæs swelc hālgung mæg wesan wiðerwinnende. Sēo settung of Brasilie in
Brasiles inlande wæs gedōn be dǣl tō ēowienne þæs gewealdes gesundrodnesse fram
þǣm crodenan and gewemedan ealdan hēafodstōle Rio de Janeiro. Þæt geweald
Sūþcorēan gehēt on 2004 þæt hit wege his hēafodstōl fram Seoule tō
Geongi-Gongtscu — þēah þe þæt word "Seoul" self mǣnþ "hēafodstōl" in þǣre
Corēiscan sprǣce.

Sēo gæderung wealdlices and feohhweorfunglices oþþe līfweglices dōmes nis nānum
wīsum woruldwīde. Þēawlice hēafodstōlas magon feohhweorfunglīce aþēostrian fram
bifylclicum ofersteallum, swā swā hit gelamp mid Thēbane, þe aþēostrode fram
Alexandrie, Nantscing fram Scanghai, oþþe Edinburg fram Glasgowe. Þæt geafeall
cynecynnes oþþe līfweges cūðe ēacswā wyrcean þone dēaþ his hēafodstōles, swā swā
hit gelamp be Bablōnie and Cahocie. Ēac wǣron manige nīwlice hēafodstōlas,
swelce Abuja and Ottawa, rǣdlīce geseted onweg fram feohhweorfunglicum stōwum
and nabbaþ gīet weaxen grēate tō nīwum feohhweorfunglicum burgum.

Andefen þǣra ēacnunge nīwlicra cāserrīca and geþēodrīca, hēafodstōlas habbaþ
worden tācn for heora rīcum heora gewealdu,, and gesetede be gewealdlicum
andgiete. Ungelīce midealdum ceastrum, þe wǣron geset ǣghwǣr wealda hēold his
gemōt, is sēo cēosung, edsettung, staðoling, oþþe se onfeng nīwlices
hēafodstōkes carful gelimpung. Tō bȳsne:



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Merewif

Meremægden is gelēaflic wæterwiht mid menniscum hēafde and bodige, and þǣm tægle
wæterdēores, swylce fisc. Þæt ƿord meremægden wearþ mermaid on Nīwum Englisce
gecweden. Se werlic efengemæcca is merewer, þēah man brȳceþ ēac þone wordcwide
meremægden for werlicum wihtum. Mænig land þǣre worulde gelīca wihta habbaþ,
gemǣne būtan clāðas.

Micel gelīc sirena, meremægdnu sungon tō lēodum and godum, and hīe besungon,
tōstregdende hīe fram hiera weorc, āfylaþ hīe of hiera scipum, oþþe hiera scipu
on grunde stīeran. In ōþrum lārum, hīe þringaþ sencende menn hwīlum fandiaþ hīe
tō sparienne. Man gelīefeþ ēac þæt meremægdnu bringaþ menn tō hiera
undermererīcum. In Hans Christian Andersenes Lȳtlum Meremægdne, man þynceþ hit
þæt meremægdnu forgietaþ þe menn underwæter āblāwan ne magon, hwīlum ōþra menn
gelīefaþ þæt meremægdnu menn āsencaþ forþǣm hiera wræðe.

Man þynceþ Grēcisc hǣðenscipes sirena hwīlum bēoþ in laterum folclāre
meremægdenlic; sum sprǣca brūcaþ þæt ælce word for begen bridd and fiscwihta,
swylce þæt Maltesisc word 'sirena.' Ōðer sibbcynna gelēaflicra wihta sind
wæterylfe and selkies, dēor þe fram sǣcūm intō mannum weorðaþ.

In Bryttiscum folclāre, man þenceþ hit þæt meremægdnu unspēdlica hwata wǣron -
begen forebodende misgelimp, and hīe wiðeriende. Mænig cynn þæs cwidegieddes Sir
Patrick Spens hæfþ meremægden mid þǣm dēaþwyrdodum scipum sprecende; in sumum,
hēo sægeþ þæt næfre sēoþ hīe land ongēan, and in ōþrum, hēo sægeþ þæt hīe nēah
stæþ bēoþ, ac hīe sind wīs genōg tō witenne þæt begen ælce bēoþ. Hīe magon ēac
tācn unwederes bēoþ.

Meremægdn magon ēac up īe swimman, tō færscwæterum lagum. On ānum dæge, in læge
nēah his hūs, Lornties Hlāford wīfmann sēah, and fandode hīe tō sparienne; his
þegn warnode þæt hēo meremægden wæs, and þæt meremægden begeal þe hēo hine
cwellan, gif ne forþǣm his þegn.

Meremægdnu magon ēac mā helpfulle bēon, sellende mannum gescēad hǣle. Sum tala
āsciaþ þā frignunge gif meremægdnu þurhlīfende sāwla hæfden. Man þynceþ hit ēac
þæt mereweras wildera and mā unfæger bēoþ þonne meremægdnu, ac ne reccaþ menn.

Þæt meremægden, oþþe syrenka, is Warsawes tācn. Man brēac meremægdenbiliðas on
Warsawes tācnscielde swā hiera tācn siþþan middlunge þæs 14ª gēarhundredes.
Mæniga gesegena tōefnaþ gelēaflic Triton mid þǣre byrig, þe mæg se fruma bēon
þæs meremægdnes geþēodes mid þǣre byrig.

Oninnan þǣm Nīwum Taíno þēodum þāra Caribbean īega, þæt meremægden Aycayia
hātte. Hire mearcunga sind gelīc þā gydenne Jagua, and þā hibiscus blōstm þæs
majaguabēam Hibiscus tiliaceus. Bisena ōðra sidaþinga beinniaþ þā Mami Wata of
Westum and Middlum Affrica, þā Jengu of Cameroon, sēo Merrow of Scotlande and
Īrlande, þā Rusalkas of Russlande and Ucrægne, þā Iara fram Brazil and þā
Grēcisc Oceanids, Nereids, and Naiads. Ān fræscwæter meremægdenlic wiht
Ēoropisces folclāre is Melusine, þe twegen fisctæglas hæfþ, ac ōðer fadunga
habbaþ hīe mid þǣm nǣdres niðerhealfe. Man þynceþ hit þæt in Iapane, etenne þone
ningyes flǣscmete unealdiende undēadlicnesse seleþ. In sumum Ēoropiscum
gesegenum meremægdnu bēoþ unspēdlic.

Meremægdnu sind cūþ for hiera rence, ac ēac for hiera unsceaþfulnesse. Hīe oft
lufiaþ menn, and swīðe willaþ hiera lufe for werum sōðian (sēo meremægdendeorf).
Mislimplīce, gewisse mid geongum meremægdnum, hīe oft forgīetaþ þe menn ne magon
underwæter āblāwan. Mereweras seldbeþencaþ ymbe mennisc gelimpas, ac in
Finniscum hǣðenscipe merefolc magon wysca bēodan, sēocnessa hǣlan, wyrgþa
forniman, wyrtdrincas brēowan and ēac mattuc beran. Meremægdnu ēac habbaþ sumra
þissa mearcunga.

Gerǣswoda gesihþa ymbe dēad oþþe līfende meremægdnu cwōm of stedum swylce swā
Java and Bryttiscum Columbian. Þǣr sind twā Canadisca cȳþþa of Vancouver and
Victorian, sum fram betweonan 1870 and 1890, and sēo ōþran fram 1967.

In Wēodmōnaðe 2009, Qiryat Yam þorp in Israele bēad $1,000,000 lēan for ǣnige þe
meremægdnu sōðian in hiera rimum, æfter mænigra twelfa lēode cūðdon meremægden
sēonende, hlēapende ūt þǣm wætere gelīc delfin and fremmende lyftsealta fore tō
þǣm dēopum eftgānde.

Of Dorothy Dinnersteines bēc Þæt Meremægden and se Werbula, mennisc-dēorisc
dōcas swylce þā werbula and meremægden bēoþ ealdmanna understandnes þæt menn and
dēor begen syndrig and ælce sind, and manna "mearcunga sind inweardlic unefen,
þe ūre þurhstandnes mid, and ūre sundornes fram, eorðan ōþrum dēordum tō mannum
rūnisc and dēop bēoþ; and of þissum þurhstandnessum, and þissum sundornessum,
habbaþ begen on eorðe fremdnes and mihtelicne þēaw tō þencenne hēr æt hām."

John William Waterhouse macode getæse biliþ fram 1895 oþ 1905, hātte Meremægden
(sēo þæt hēafod þisses gewrites). Late Bryttisc Academyes cynstweorcmōd, man
onwrāh þās mētinge mid gōdum dōme (þe him earnode þone Cynelices Academyes
geþēodscipe), ac intō sundorhorde tōfōr and ne oþ þā 1970a ne eftcwōm. Hit is nū
in Andrew Lloyd-Webberes sundorhorde.

Þæt mǣste welcūðe weorc nīwlic gēarhundredes is Hans Christian Andersenes
folcatalu Þæt Lȳtle Meremægden (1836), þe man ontō mænigum sprǣcum āwendode.
Andersenes tācnung, þe man fæst macode mid bræsene hēahgræfte in
Cēapmannahæfnhȳðe, wearþ sēo Westerne rihtbisen siþþan hēo wrīten wæs. Þæt
meremægden, swā Andersen gewrāt, mæg efne þurhstandende sāwle begīetan bȳ
beweddiende mann.

Þæt mǣste welcūðe glīwweorc ymbe meremægdnu sind þās of Felix Mendelssohn in his
Fair Melusina glīwsange and þā þrēo "Rīnisc dohtor" Richard Wagneres Der Ring
des Nibelungen. Lorelei, se nama ān þāra Rīnisc meremægda, wearþ tācnung
sirenes. Mā nīwlicu tācnung glīwes is Taiwanisc glīwwyrhta Fan-Long Ko's Þæt
Wēpende Meremægden.

Sue Monk Kidd gewrāt bōc gehāten Se Meremægdenstōl. Se nama cymþ of meremægdne
þe unwǣre sanctas wearþ.

Film ymbe meremægdnu beinnaþ 1984 lustfilm Splash, mid Daryl Hannah. Scēawung
1963 feorrsīenendebyrdnesse Route 66, Sēo Wælhrēoƿoste Sǣ hātte, wæs ymbe wǣre
meremægden þe in Weeki Wachee wæterperroce swanc. Man hæfde ēac meremægdnu in
þǣre gelēaflicum feorrsīenendebyrdnesse Charmed, and þonne þǣre
dohtorendebyrdnesse Mermaid. Tācniscu film beinniaþ Disneyes glīwisce fadunge
Andersenes tale, and Hayao Miyazakies Ponyo.

In herewealdscipe, þæt biliþ meremægdnes gemǣne camb and scēawere hæfþ, and cūþ
swā 'meremægden in hire īdelnesse' is. Man brēac Merefolc tō tācnienne
cræftignesse and fægernesse in sprǣce.

Scield- and sweordwieldende meremægden (Syrenka) is on þǣm wǣrum Warsawes
herewealdscield, sēo hēafodburg Polalandes. Sēo burg Norþfolc, Virginia ēac
brȳceþ meremægden swā hiera tācn, and byrgisc cynstweorc mid missenlicum
gefægrodum meremægdengræfte bēoþ geond þǣm burhstede. Sēo hēafodburh Hamilton,
Bermuda hæfþ þæt meremægden on hire herewealdscielde, þe man mæg geond þǣre
byrig gesēon.

Michaëlle Jeanes sundorherewealdscield, Canada's Governor General, hæfþ twegen
Simbi, meremægdenlicu wihta fram Haitisc Fūdū, swā bearwan.

sirenes. Mā nīwlicu tācnung glīwes is Taiwanisc glīwwyrhta Fan-Long Ko's Þæt
Wēpende Meremægden.

Sue Monk Kidd gewrāt bōc gehāten Se Meremægdenstōl. Se nama cymþ of meremægdne
þe unwǣre sanctas wearþ.

Film ymbe meremægdnu beinnaþ 1984 lustfilm Splash, mid Daryl Hannah. Scēawung
1963 feorrsīenendebyrdnesse Route 66, Sēo Wælhrēoƿoste Sǣ hātte, wæs ymbe wǣre
meremægden þe in Weeki Wachee wæterperroce swanc. Man hæfde ēac meremægdnu in
þǣre gelēaflicum feorrsīenendebyrdnesse Charmed, and þonne þǣre
dohtorendebyrdnesse Mermaid. Tācniscu film beinniaþ Disneyes glīwisce fadunge
Andersenes tale, and Hayao Miyazakies Ponyo.

In herewealdscipe, þæt biliþ meremægdnes gemǣne camb and scēawere hæfþ, and cūþ
swā 'meremægden in hire īdelnesse' is. Man brēac Merefolc tō tācnienne
cræftignesse and fægernesse in sprǣce.

Scield- and sweordwieldende meremægden (Syrenka) is on þǣm wǣrum Warsawes
herewealdscield, sēo hēafodburg Polalandes. Sēo burg Norþfolc, Virginia ēac
brȳceþ meremægden swā hiera tācn, and byrgisc cynstweorc mid missenlicum
gefægrodum meremægdengræfte bēoþ geond þǣm burhstede. Sēo hēafodburh Hamilton,
Bermuda hæfþ þæt meremægden on hire herewealdscielde, þe man mæg geond þǣre
byrig gesēon.

Michaëlle Jeanes sundorherewealdscield, Canada's Governor General, hæfþ twegen
Simbi, meremægdenlicu wihta fram Haitisc Fūdū, swā bearwan.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lunden-ceaster

Lundenceaster is ceaster þæs Geāndan Cynerīces, æt Lundenbyrige heortan. Hēo is
lytel burg be landgemete, ac hēo is ēac sēo rīcoste stōw þæs rīces.

Lundenceaster is Lundenes stǣrfæst cyrnel þǣrymbe, ēac Westmynstere, þisses
dæges Māran Lundene wēox. Sēo Ceastre landgemearc hæfþ awunedon oþ þā
Middelieldu, and sēo is nū lytel dǣl þæs Lundene burgscipes. Oft hātte man
Lundenceastre efne Sēo Ceaster.

Lundenceaster is in Lundene heorte, ac būtan feohgestreōngeornesse, Lundene
mǣste ceasterlicu geornes hæfþ his hām on Lundene Westende.

Tōdæg is Lundenceaster micel bysig stede feohhūsa. Hēo is se fyrmesta staðolwang
for eormenum fēohhūscræfte. (Se nīehsta, Nīwe Eoforwīc Burg, is nēah ōþer.)

Lundenceaster hæfþ þæt Lundenceastre Gyld. Þæt Gild hæfþ riht ofer eallum
stōwlicum tōþegnungfeldum and ofer þǣm burgwac. Hit hæfþ onweald ofer ealdfæstre
ceastre cēapstōwum begeondan þā ceastre and āh micel land begeondan þǣre ceastre
mearce.

Æfter Beadwe Hæstinga, Willelm Bastarð cōm to Lundene, ac þa Lundenburhware
āmieredon hine æt Suþweorce and he ne ofercierrede Lundenbrycg. Willelm
ofercierrede Temes ēa æt Wallingford and hergade ealne þone ende þe he
oferferde, oð þæt he com to Beorhhamstede, and þær him com ongean Ealdred
arcebiscop, and Eadgar cild, and Eadwine eorl, and Morkere eorl, and ealle þa
betstan men of Lundene, and bugon þa for neode þa mæst wæs to hearme gedon. In
1075 geaf Willelm Lundenwarum nīwu bōc.

In 1132, geaf Heanrig I Lundenceastre scīr-weald, and be 1141 hycgeþ man ealle
burgware swa swa an gild. Þes wæs Lundenceaster Gildes frymþ.

Þæt Gild nis gelīc anum ōðrum stōwlicum geþinge þæs rīces. His ǣrost gesceap wæs
þæt Cnihtagild in Eadgares Cyninges dagum. Siþþan þǣm dagum hæfþ Lundenceaster
getæl cynelicra bōca tō āfæstnienne his staðol and onweald.

Lundenceastre Gildes cwide is "Domine dirige nos", þæt meahte man āwendan swā
"Hlaford, gestīere us".



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Laos

Laoland oðre naman sēo Lao Folcescynewīse is a landbegyrded rīce in Asie
sūþēastdæle, þæt hæfþ his mearcas mid Burman and Cīnan be westnorþen him, mid
Fietname beēasten him, Cambodie besūþen him, and Thailand to the west. Siððan
1975 hæfþ þis land geþoled under Marxist Gemōtscipes lēodwearde. His þēod wæs be
his getæle 6.8 þūsenda þūsend in 2014.

In þæs Frencisce gereorde is þis land and his landfolc "Laos" þærof habbað manig
gereord hiera naman þærof and þes nama is in þæm mænigfealdum getele for Lao,
swylces landmanna nama, þȳ mænþ Laos on Englisce 'Laoware'.

Laowara stǣr fint man oþ Lan Xang þæt cynerīce, þæt geþēah of þæm 14. gearhunde
oþ þæm 18. gearhund þan wæs hit in þrim rīcum bedæled. In 1893 weard Laoland
Frencisc gerēfland þærin waron his þrēo rīcu geānlǣhted þā wæron Luang Phrabang,
Vientiane and Champasak.

Laos weard his agan sundorrīce in 1953 and wæs cynerīce mid grundgesetnesse
cynedōme under Sisavang Vong Cyning. Gemōtscipe folc be naman Pathet Lao fang to
rīce in 1975 and þone cynedōm onwearpen.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kesc%C6%BFisc_spr%C7%A3ccynn

Þæt Kescwisce sprǣccynne (on Nīwum Englisce hāteþ Quechua, on Spēonisce quechua,
and on Kescwisce qheshwa oþþe runa simi, þe tācnaþ "sēo sprǣc þæs folces") is
sprǣccynn þætte mann spriceþ on Sūðamerican, on þǣm Andes. Hit hæfþ hūhwēga tīen
þūsenda þūsenda sprecenda, þēah þe hit is swīðe earfoþ tō witenne gewisslīce hū
fela sprecenda þǣr sind; and sind þǣr manige ānlīce on Bolifie, Perwe, and
Ecuadore, ac ēac on Argentinan, Cilan, Brasile, and Colombie.

Hit is þæt gesprecenoste sprǣccynn þāra inlendiscena Wīnlandes. Sōþlīce is hit
betere tō hātenne hit "sprǣccynn" þonne "sprǣc" for þȳ þe hit is swīðe missenlīc
betweox þǣm undersprǣcum. Oft ne cann mann þe spriceþ āne undersprǣce his
forstandan ōðerne mann þe spriceþ ōðre undersprǣce his. Þǣr sind þrēo
hēafodundersprǣccynn his: Norþkescwisc sprǣc, Midkescwisc sprǣc, and Sūþkescwish
sprǣc, þe hæfþ þæt mǣste rīm sprecenda eallra þāra undersprǣca. Þis sprǣccynn is
gecūþ tō "þǣre sprǣce þāra Incena", for þȳ þe hit heora hēafodsprǣc wæs.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Stalin

Iosep Fissarionofic Stalin (geboren swā Ioseb Besarionis dse Iughascfili on þǣm
18 dæge Ǣrran Gēolan þæs 1878 gēares and cwæl on þǣm 5 dæge Hrēþmōnaðes þæs 1953
gēares) wæs se forma Gemǣna Lǣdend þæs Sofietre Gesamnunge Middelan Gyldes fram
þǣm 1922 gēare oþ his dēaþ in þǣm 1953 gēare. In þǣm gēarum æfter Lenines dēaðe
in þǣm 1924 gēare, hē rās and wearþ se lǣdend þǣre Sofietan Gesamnunge.

On Georgia wæs Ioseb Besarionis dse Iughascfili geboren and he wenod þe he wolde
weordan prēost, ac he alēt his lārhūse and feaht in þǣre Russiscan Onwendung in
1917 and weard hēah in þǣm nīwan Communistan lēodweard se ricsode ofer Russlande
and his rīce. In þissum gearum nām he his binaman "Stalin", se is "Stǣl-mann".

Stalin undergann gewealdede feohwendunge, þe namm þone stede þæs Nīwan
Feohwendunge Rǣdes þāra æfterrena 1920 gēara and setede on his stede þā Rǣd Fīfa
Gēara and undergann tīde swifte weorcsettunge and feohwendunge gemōtsettunge.
Þæt bræc in þǣre eorþbigenesse forestōp fōre þā forþbǣre ǣtes, þætte cwōm micel
hunger, and of þissum wæs se Sofietisca hunger of 1932–1933, þe man in þǣm
Ucrægne hētt be naman Holodomor, se is "Eallhunger".



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jesus

Iesus (oþþe Ihesus, Jesus) is se weorþlic wiht on crīstendōme. Þā Crīstnas hine
nemnaþ Iesus Crist (of Hebrēisce יהושע [Yĕhošūa‘], and Crēacisc: Χριστός
(Christos)]). Hē hatte ēac Iesus Nasarenisc forþǣm hē wunode on Nazareth, þēah
þæt hē wæs on Bethleheme geboren.

Crīstnas gelīefaþ hē wǣre gewyrdelic man and hē lifde fram ymbe (6–4 BC oþ ymbe
AD 29–33), and manig (ac nā eall) woruldlic scōleras cnāwaþ þā sceaf Iesuse.
Crīstnas ēac gelīefaþ, be þǣre gewitegunge þǣre feowera godspella, þe sind þā
forman bēc þǣre Nīwu Gecȳþnes on þǣre Biblia, þæt Iesus wæs se Hælend and se
Sunu Godes. Se nama Christos secgeð þæt he wǣre "gesealfod," þæt is þæt God hine
of werum gesundrode tō hālignesse. Tō æthreddenne us fram þǣm ǣwigan deaðe in
þǣre Helle, hē stearf for ūrum synnum on þǣm Crístesmǣle (on þǣre rōde) æt
Golgota, ǣgyltas þe wē dōþ wiþ Gode and wiþ ǣghwilcum ōðrum. Tō āwinnenne þone
deaþ, nam Jesus se Hælend sige ofer þǣm deaðe on ðriddum dæge. Hē āstōd fram
dēaðe and þæt græf opennode.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Janice_Rogers_Brown

Janice Rogers Brown Dēmestre (geboren on 11 Þrimilcemōnaþ, 1949) is dēma in þǣm
Ambihte Rihtes on þǣm Geānlǣht Rīcu Dōmærn Hālsunga for þǣm Columbianscīre
Ymbwyrfte. Hēo wæs gēo Efendēma þæs Californian Ealdordōmærnes, hæfde þōne stede
siþþan 2 Þrimilcemōnaþ, 1996. Spellwrīteras oft nōtiaþ þæt hēo is gehyldendlicu
blacu dēmestre. US Foresittend George W. Bush hīe nemnode tō hire nīwlicum stede
in 2003, ac hūru wæs hire genemnung geslāwod 2 gēarum for þā Democratas for hire
gehyldendlicne gelēafan. Oft nemnaþ man hīe swā mihtiglicu genemnodu for þǣm
Geānlǣhtes Rīces Ealdordōmærn. Gif genemnod, þonne biþ hēo sēo ǣreste blace
wīflice dēmestre.

Brown Dēmestre leornode in Californian be Californianrīce Hēahleornungstede of
1967 oþ 1969, and of 1972 oþ 1974 tō earnienne hire B.A. gewis. Of 1974 oþ 1977
wæs hēo be Hēahleornungstede Californian Lage Scōle and earnode hire J.D. gewis.
Of 2002 oþ 2004 earnode hēo hire LL.M. be Hēahleornungstede Virginian Lage
Scōle.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jane_Grey_Hl%C7%A3fdige

Iane Grey (1536 oþþe 1537 – 12 Solmōnaþ 1554) wæs ansprecestre þāra Engliscan
and Īriscan Cynedoma. Hēo rīcsode ofer Englaland on nigon dagas in 1553, and þus
is oft cūþ swā Sēo Nigon Daga Cwēn, oþþe lēas gemǣne swā Sēo Cwēne Þritīene
Daga, forþǣm þā tōdǣlnessa ymbe þæt onginn hire mǣrsung rīcsonesse. Stǣrmenn
oncnāwaþ oþþe hire mǣrsungdæg swā Cwēn (10 Mǣdmōnþe), oþþe se ǣrmannes dēaþ (6
Mǣdmōnþe), swā þæt onginn.

Maria, Heanriges VIII iedsta dōhtor anām þone cyndōm of Iane þær hēo cwōm on
Lunden and Iane behēafded on 12 Solmōnaþ 1554.

Man cūþ Iane Hlǣfdige swā ān þāra wīsostra frēona hire tīman, and stǣrwritere
Alison Weir cwæþ þæt wæs hēo ān þāra "grēatostra wīfgemynda þæs gēarhundredes."
Sum menn reccaþ hīe swā Englalandes fyrmest Oferwealdende Cwēn.

Iane, ieldesta dohtor Heanrices Greyes and his wīfes, Frances Brandon Hlæfdige,
wæs æt Brādgeat Perrac geboren, in Lægreceastrescīre. Ǣror þancas wǣron þæt hēo
ymbe Winterfylleþ 1537 geboren wæs, ac sum menn nū gelīefaþ þæt hēo ǣror geboren
wæs, on uncūðum tīman in oþþe ieldum 1536 oþþe ǣror 1537.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Israel

Israhēl þæt land (Hebrēisce: מְדִינַת יִשְׂרָאֵל; Medinat Yisra'el; Arabisce:
دَوْلَةْ إِسْرَائِيل, Dawlat Isrā'īl) is land in þǣm Middlum Ēaste on þǣm
ēasternan riman þæs Wendelsǣs. Hē is folcgemōtisc lēodþing and se āna Iudēisc
landrīce þǣre worulde. Se nama "Israēl" cymþ of þǣre Hebrēiscan Biblioþēcan, þa
þe hātte Tanakh, þǣrinn Iacobus biþ ednemnod Israēl æfter þǣm þe hē wrixlode mid
diernum fīend ("wer", and ufor "god" æfter þǣre Cnēorisbēc 32:24-30; oþþe "se
engel", æfter þǣm Hosean 12:4).

Se ymbeþanc þæs "Israhēlisces Land", cnāwen in Hebrēiscre spræce swā Eretz
Yisrael (oþþe Eretz Yisroel), wæs and is wihtig and hālig for Iudeiscum lēode
siþþan bibliþēcanlican tīman. In þǣre Ǣ, weddod God þæt land tō þǣm þrim
Lēodfrumum þæs Iudeisces lēode. On þǣm staðole ǣ, se rūm þæs þrēora Lēodfruman
is geseted gehwǣr in þæs ǣrlicum ōðerum þūsandgēar BCE, and se ǣrost Israhēlisc
Cyningdōm wæs staðolod ymbe þǣm endleofeða hūndredgeare BCE. Nēahfolgiende
Israhēlisc cyningdōmas and rīcu gewealden intermittently ofer þǣm nīehst fēower
hūndred geara, and sind cnāwen fram syndrig frumum ūtan þǣre Biblioþece.

Se norðlic cyningdōm Israhēlisces, swā swā Philistine burg rīcu gefylled in 722
BCE, þēah þæs sūþernes Iudea Cyningdōm and ānlīep Phoenician burg rīcu āwunod
hira bistandung swā þǣm landscipe gecumen under Assyrian wealdung. Mid þæt
cumung of Babylonians, Iudah wæs gefylled ēac.
