https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hypnosis

Oferswefn (on Nīwum Englisce and hwīlum on Englisce hypnosis gehāten) is mōdig
byrdness oftost geworht þurh endebyrdnesse þe is oferswefnlic settung gehāten.
Oferswefnbǣre cwidas magon fram oferswefnsettende gegifen wesan oþþe magon fram
selfe gegifen wesan. Sēo nytt oferswefnes tō hǣlenne is "oferswefnes hǣlu"
gehāten (oþþe ānfealdlīce "oferswefnhǣlu").

Þæt word "oferswefn" is geworht of þǣm geþōhte þæt sēo byrdness is gesibb
swefne, ac on witunge is hit hīere þonne swefn, oþþe "ofer" swefne. Hit is fram
þǣm worde "hynosis" (þe is fram "neuro-hypnosis", wordlīce
"(fēlend)-seonu-swefn", fram þǣm Scotiscan lǣce Jamese Braide ymb 1841 gemacod)
selfe ēðod; þæt word "hypnosis" self is efne gebrocen on þǣm mǣstum dǣle ōðerra
sprǣca. James self scēop his weorc on þǣm geforðod fram Franze Mesmere and his
folgiendum ("Mesmerscipe" oþþe "dēora blōmtēong" ), ac he ne gelīefde swā swā
Franz ymb þǣre wīsan be þǣre þe sēo endebyrdness worhte.

Wiþ folclicne gelēafan þæt oferswefn is gecynd unwitunge gelīc swefne, andweard
cneordlǣcung ēowaþ þæt hit is sōþlīce þurhwacol byrdness ānmōdes and grēatran
befæstendes cræftes, mid gelytlodre ōran sihþe. In þǣre forman bēc be þǣre lāre,
Neurypnology (1843), Braid tōmearcod "hypnotism" ("oferswefn") tō byrdnesse
līchāmlicre slacunge gefērlǣced and beworht be mōdigre ānmōdsettunge
("abstraction").



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hw%C3%A6lsang

Hwælsang is the collection sōna macodon fram hwalum tō communicate. The word
"song" is used in particular to describe the pattern of predictable and
repetitious sounds made by certain species of whales (notably the humpback
whale) in a manner that to cetologists is reminiscent of human singing.

The biological processes used to produce sound vary from one family of cetaceans
to another. However, all whales, dolphins, and porpoises are much more dependent
on sound for communication and sensation than their terrestrial cousins because
the absorption of light by water makes sight difficult and because the
relatively slow movement of water compared to air decreases the effectiveness of
the sense of smell. Increased ambient noise in the world's oceans due to
shipping gives rise to environmentalists' concerns that humans are destroying
this important feature of the marine habitat.

Mennisc scellaþ by expelling air through the larynx. The vocal cords within the
larynx open and close as necessary to separate the stream of air into discrete
pockets of air. These pockets are shaped by the throat, tongue, and lips into
the desired sound.

Cetacean sound production differs markedly from this mechanism. The precise
mechanism differs in the two major sub-families of cetaceans: the Odontoceti
(toothed whales—including dolphins) and the Mystceti (baleen whales—including
the largest whales, such as the blue whale).

Toothed whales do not make the long, low-frequency sounds known as the whale
song. Instead they produce rapid bursts of high-frequency clicks and whistles.
Single clicks are generally used for echolocation whereas collections of clicks
and whistles are used for communication. Though a large pod of dolphins will
make a veritable cacophony of different noises, very little is known about the
meaning of the sound. Frankell (1998) quotes one researcher characterizing
listening to such a school as like listening to a group of children at a
playground.

The sounds themselves are produced by passing air through a structure in the
head rather like the human nasal passage called the phonic lips. As the air
passes through this narrow passage, the phonic lip membranes are sucked
together, causing the surrounding tissue to vibrate. These vibrations can, as
with the vibrations in the human larynx, be unconsciously controlled with great
sensitivity. The vibrations pass through the tissue of the head to the melon,
which shapes and directs the sound into a beam of sound for echolocation. Every
toothed whale except the Sperm Whale has two sets of phonic lips and is thus
capable of making two sounds independently. Once the air has passed the phonic
lips it enters the vestibular sac. From there the air may be recycled back into
the lower part of the nasal complex, ready to be used for sound creation again,
or passed out through the blowhole.

The French name for phonic lips—museau de singe—translates to "monkey lips,"
which the phonic lip structure is supposed to resemble. New cranial analysis
using computed axial and single photon emission computed tomography scans in
2004 showed that, at least in the case of bottlenose dolphins, air may be
supplied to the nasal complex from the lungs by the palatopharyngeal sphincter,
enabling the sound creation process to continue for as long as the dolphin is
able to hold their breath (Houser et al., 2004).

While the complex and haunting sounds of the Humpback Whale (and some Blue
Whales) are believed to be primarily used in sexual selection (see section
below), the simpler sounds of other whales have a year-round use. While toothed
dolphins (including the orca) are capable of using echolocation (essentially the
emission of ultra-sonic beams of sound waves) to detect the size and nature of
objects very precisely, baleen whales do not have this capability. Further,
unlike some fish such as sharks, a whale's sense of smell is not highly
developed. Thus given the poor visibility of aquatic environments and the fact
that sound travels so well in water, human-audible sounds play a role in such
whales' navigation. For instance, the depth of water or the existence of a large
obstruction ahead may be detected by loud noises made by baleen whales.

Two groups of whales, the Humpback Whale and the subspecies of Blue Whale found
in the Indian Ocean, are known to produce the repetitious sounds at varying
frequencies known as the whale song. Marine biologist Philip Clapham describes
the song as "probably the most complex [songs] in the animal kingdom" (Clapham,
1996).

Interest in the whale song was aroused by researchers Roger Payne and Scott
McVay, who analysed the songs in 1971. The songs follow a distinct hierarchical
structure. The base units of the song (sometimes loosely called the "notes") are
single uninterrupted emissions of sound that last up to a few seconds. These
sounds vary in frequency from 20 Hz to 10 kHz (the typical Human range of
hearing is 20 Hz to 20 kHz). The units may be frequency modulated (i.e., the
sound may go up, go down, or stay the same during the note) or amplitude
modulated (get louder or quieter).

A collection of four or six units is known as a sub-phrase, lasting perhaps ten
seconds. A collection of two sub-phrases is a phrase. A whale will typically
repeat the same phrase over and over for two to four minutes. This is known as a
theme. A collection of themes is known as a song. The whale will repeat the same
song, which last perhaps twenty minutes, over and over again over the course of
hours or even days. This "Russian doll" hierarchy of sounds has captured the
imagination of scientists.

Mǣst balēnra hwala scellaþ æt ymbe 15–20 hertza. Hūru, sǣlic biologists æt þǣre
Woods Hole Oceanographic Insetenne meldodon in þǣm New Scientist in Gēolmōnþe
2004 þæt hīe wǣron on spyrunge hwæl in þǣm Norðum Pacifiscum geond 12 gēara fec
þe wæs "on singunge" æt 52 Hz. Þā cræftmenn ne cunnon nū sweotolian þās
mægenscēadunge of þǣm regole; hūru, is him witodlic þæt se hwæl is balēn and
borlīce gelīclic tō bēonne nīwe cynn, and þis manaþ þæt nū cūþ cynn hæbben
wīdran swēgendlican fāgunge þonne ǣr geþōht.

Mǣst ōðra hwala and delfina scellaþ of varying degrees of complexity. Of
particular interest is the Beluga (the "sea canary") which produces an immense
variety of whistles, clicks and pulses.

Though some observers suggest that undue fascination has been placed on the
whales' songs simply because the animals are under the sea, most marine mammal
scientists believe that sound plays a particularly vital role in the development
and well-being of cetaceans. It may be argued those against whaling have
anthropomorphized the behaviour in an attempt to bolster their case. Conversely
pro-whaling nations are perhaps disposed to downplay the meaning of the sounds,
noting for example that little is taken in the "moo" of cattle.

Researchers use hydrophones (often adapted from their original military use in
tracking submarines) to ascertain the exact location of the origin of whale
noises. Their methods allow them also to detect how far throughout an ocean a
sound travels. Research by Dr Christopher Clark of Cornell University conducted
using thirty-years worth of military data showed that whale noises travel up to
3,000 km. As well as providing information about song production, the data
allows researchers to follow the migratory path of whales throughout the
"singing" (mating) season.

Prior to the introduction of human noise production, Clark says the noises may
have travelled right from one side of an ocean to the other. His research
indicates that ambient noise from boats is doubling each decade. This has the
effect of halving the range of whale noises. Those that do believe the whale
songs are significant to the continued well-being of well-populations are
particularly concerned by this increase in ambient noise. Other research has
shown that increased boat traffic in, for example, the waters off Vancouver, has
caused some orca to change the frequency and increase the amplitude of their
sounds, in an apparent attempt to get themselves heard. Environmentalists fear
that such boat activity is putting undue stress on the animal as well as making
it difficult to find a mate.

Hrānhuntoþ in Grēnelande is sƿīðe ƿeorþliċ for þǣm Kalaallitþēodum Grēnelandes
and gamenhuntum, beȝen þēodisc and elþēodisc. Hrānas bēoþ ƿeorþliċ frumas
flǣscmetes, and for hiera stǣre and selenesse. Huntoþsetnes biþ ƿeorþliċ for þǣm
hrānum, þǣre ƿelnesse līfes þāra skrælinga, and þǣm metegræsstedum. Hrānhuntoþ
biþ tō þǣm skrælingum sƿær ȝelimp, and plihtas and lēan hæfþ.

Hrānhuntoþ by mannum hæfþ dēop stǣr, and hrānas "mæȝ þæt dēor bēon grēatostes
ƿeorþliċnesse eallra ȝeƿrita ymbe huntoþ."

In Grēnelande, þā skrælingas huntaþ þā hrānas for fōde, clāðum, hāmum, and
tōlum. Hīe brūcaþ crūcbogas, bogas, træppas, and nū nīƿlīċe gunnan. Hīe brūcaþ
eall þæs hrān, beinnende hǣr, scynn, hornas, and bān. Mǣste man hunteþ hīe for
hiera flǣscmete, ac ieldra hrānas mid grēatum hornum gōd for siȝebēacn bēoþ.

Man hunteþ mā hrānas in Grēnelande þonne ǣniȝ ōðer miċel gamen landsyċedēor.
Hrān flǣscmete biþ sƿīðe ƿeorþliċ fōd in mǣstum hāmum, and bīdaþ þā lēode ȝeorne
þǣm fylhuntoþtīman tō beȝinnenne.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hockey

Hocig is plega þǣr twegen hēapas plegaþ ǣlc wiþ ōðerne, sēcende tō drīfenne
cliewen oþþe efencliewen in þæt getælgeat oþþe nett þæs wiþstandendan hēapes.

Īshocig (gemǣne gehāten hocig in landum þǣr þis þæt gemǣnoste hocigcynn is) is
hēapplega þe man on īse plegeþ, þǣr slīdendas brūcaþ styccas tō drīfenne
efencliwen in þæt getælgeat þæs wiþstealles. Hit biþ swīðe swift and stearc
gamen. Īshocig oftost līcaþ mannum on stedum þe cealde genōh sind tō þeccenne
þone grund mid īse tīdmǣlum, swelce Canada, þā norðernan Geāndan Rīcu, þā
Norðiscan rīcu (hūru Swēoland and Finland), Russland, þā Bealtiscan rīcu, þæt
Cecisce Folcrīce, and Slofacia. Mid þǣm cræflican īshringa cyme, hit wearþ brēme
geondgēarlic gamen in þissum stedum. Īshocig is ān þāra fēowra grēatena gamena
Norðamerican. Geond þā worulde, se National Hockey League (NHL) þynceþ se
hīehsta dōm īshociges mannum, and ge se Canadian Women's Hockey League (CWHL) ge
se Western Women's Hockey League (WWHL) sind þā hīehstan dōmas for frēoum. Hit
is ēac Canadan folcriht folclic winterlic gamen, þǣr hit līcaþ manigum mannum.

Man plegeþ feldhocig (ēac feldswingoþ tō smǣtran worde gehāten) on ceosele,
gecyndum græse, sandgeardum oþþe wætergeardum mannorhtre turfe, mid lytlum,
heardum cliewenum. Þæt gamen līcaþ manigum werum and frēom in manigum stedum
þǣre worulde, hūru on Europan, Asian, Australian, and Sūðaffrican. In manigum
rīcum, mann plegeþ þæt gamen betwēonen āncund þrēatum, þēah hīe māgon missencund
wesan.

Se ānwealdenda dōm is se International Hockey Federation (FIH) mid 116 gesīðum.
Mann plegede wera feldhocig æt ǣlcum Sumores Olympiscum Gamenum siþþan 1908
(būton 1912 and 1924), and plegede mann frēona feldhocig æt ǣlcum Sumores
Olympiscum Gamenum siþþan 1980.

Strǣthocig (ēac strǣtswingoþ gehāten) is ōðer cynn hociges. Hit is oftost
gepleged mid ilcum lagum īsswingoðes oþþe weolchociges, ac hit is gepleged on
strǣte oþþe ōðrum gelīcum stede. Oftost is cliewen gebrocen on stede
efencliewenes, for þǣm þe efencliewen wyrceþ tō micel gedreog on līme and
eorþtirwan and ne slīt wel. Strǣthocig is gepleged geond þæt fulle gēar.

Iane Grey (1536 oþþe 1537 – 12 Solmōnaþ 1554) wæs ansprecestre þāra Engliscan
and Īriscan Cynedoma. Hēo rīcsode ofer Englaland on nigon dagas in 1553, and þus
is oft cūþ swā Sēo Nigon Daga Cwēn, oþþe lēas gemǣne swā Sēo Cwēne Þritīene
Daga, forþǣm þā tōdǣlnessa ymbe þæt onginn hire mǣrsung rīcsonesse. Stǣrmenn
oncnāwaþ oþþe hire mǣrsungdæg swā Cwēn (10 Mǣdmōnþe), oþþe se ǣrmannes dēaþ (6
Mǣdmōnþe), swā þæt onginn.

Maria, Heanriges VIII iedsta dōhtor anām þone cyndōm of Iane þær hēo cwōm on
Lunden and Iane behēafded on 12 Solmōnaþ 1554.

Man cūþ Iane Hlǣfdige swā ān þāra wīsostra frēona hire tīman, and stǣrwritere
Alison Weir cwæþ þæt wæs hēo ān þāra "grēatostra wīfgemynda þæs gēarhundredes."
Sum menn reccaþ hīe swā Englalandes fyrmest Oferwealdende Cwēn.

wæs æt Brādgeat Perrac geboren, in Lægreceastrescīre. Ǣror þancas wǣron þæt hēo
ymbe Winterfylleþ 1537 geboren wæs, ac sum menn nū gelīefaþ þæt hēo ǣror geboren

https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Habs

Þā Montreal Canadiens (Frencisc: Les Canadiens de Montréal) sind andƿīs
īshociȝtēam steald in Montreal, Quebec, Cænadan. Hīe sind ȝesīðas þæs Norþēastes
Dǣles þæs Ēasternes Þoftscipes þæs National Hockey League (NHL). Se tēam is
rihtcūþ sƿā le Club de hockey Canadien. Frenċisc ymbenaman for þǣm tēame
beinniaþ Les Canadiens (oþþe Le Canadien), Le Bleu-Blanc-et-Rouge, La
Sainte-Flanelle, Le Tricolore, Les Glorieux (oþþe Nos Glorieux), Les Habitants
and Le Grand Club. On Inglisce, þæs tēames hēafodymbenama is þā Habs ("Hæbs"),
scortnes "Les Habitants". (Ēac on Inglisce, man brȳcþ āƿa þone Frenċisc
bōcstæfing, Canadiens.)

Onsteald in 1909, þā Canadiens sind se langost þurhstande fremmende andƿīs
īshociȝtēam, and se efne nū NHL tēam þe fore NHL onstelle onsteald ƿæs, ēac ān
þāra ieldostra Ƿīnlendiscra indryhtetēama. Se tēam is ān þāra "Formestra Siexa"
tēama; tēamas þe ȝeþēoded mid þǣm NHL ƿǣron, fram 1942 oþ þā 1967 āþenunge. Þȳ
unȝeþēodunge þāra Quebec Nordiques in 1995, þā Canadiens se efne NHL tēam in
Quebec sind. Se tēames ċeampscipetīma in 1992–93 ƿæs se læst tīma Cænadisc tēam
þone Stanley Cup ƿann.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/H%C3%A6mus

Hæmus þā beorgas oferwrēogaþ in Illyrices ēastdæle. Þes hlāwhēap rynþ 350 mīla
of Vrashka Chuka þæm beorge on þære landgemearce betwuh Pulgarum bewesten and
Serbum beēasten þurh Pulgaralandes middeldæle to Æmonnæsse on Euxines sǣrīme.
His hēastan dūnas sindon in Middelpulgaralande. Se hēasta topp is Botev, se
stent æt 7,792 fōtum ofer þæm brīme.

In þissum beorgum is micel fæger and gefrǣge blōmacynn and dēorcynn. Eþelhwīt
blōweþ hēr in Kozyata stena þæm lande. Hēalic land sind in þæm Middelhæmus
Þēodiscan Edisce mid hid stēopum hliþum, Illyrices hēastan wæterfeal and rīc
wyrtcynn. Europan micel dēor oneardiaþ þissum dūnas; her sind beran, wulfas,
bāras, chamois and heortas.

In geardagum hataþ þā beorgas on Crēacum Αἷμος þærof wrāt Rōmware Haemus Mons on
Lædne. In þære Pulgariscan gereorde and on Serbisce secgþ man Стара планина
(Stara planina) se menþ, "Se Ealda Beorg".

Leorneras ne witaþ hwærof cymþ swylc nama 'Hæmus'. Hie hycgað þe he mōtan of
Crēacna worde αἷμα bēon (se is 'blōd') oððe of worde þæs Traciscan gereorde þone
naman wit ac hie hycgaþ *saimon, menþ 'beorghēap'.

Folclār þāra Ealdcrēac secgþ þe Zeus hiere deofolgield feaht Typhon dūnes
æghlæc, and Zeus derode Typhon mid þunre þe Typhones blōd feall on þæm dūnlande
and for thisssum þing habbaþ þās hlāwas þone naman Αἷμος, se is 'blōd'.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gyanendra_Nepal_Cyning

Gyanendra Bir Bikram Shah Dev (Bysen:Lang-ne; Jñānendra Śāh) is Nepal Cyning and
he ricsode in þæm lande oð ðe wealdsēcendas hine awearp in 2006.

On 7 Mǣdmōnaþ 1947 wæs Gyanendra geboren þan wæs his fæder Mahendra se
ierfe-æþeling. In Gyanendra cildhād in 1950 fliemedon his fæder and his
ealdfæder Tribhuvan se cyning of þæm rīce and se forma þegn abannede þe
Gyanendra biþ cyning. In þæm niehstan geare edcwōm Tribhuvan Cyning. In 2001 wæs
micel wæl in Nepales cynehealle þærin Gyanendran brōðorsunu, Dipendra Æþeling,
slōg his agen fæder Birendra Cyning, his mōdor and manig elleswīse, beforan þe
Dipendra ofsceat his agen hēafod. Æfter Birendran Cyninges dēaþ and Dipendran
dēaþ æfter þrim nihtum fange Gyanendra to rīce.

Gyanendran Cyninges rīce wæs eall unfriþ. His brōðor Birendra Cyning hæfde
gestaðoled grundgestnes and toþegnung wæs gedōn be lēodweardes þegnum getēon of
þæm witenagemōte, ac þēos bysen wæs lef and ateorigendlic þan weax unrǣd þāra
Gemōtscipe aliefenda and hiera camp forwiernde spelena cyst. Þȳ in 2005 fang se
Cyning ānweald þe he meaht oferdrifan þēos unfriþ, ac se cirm þāra strǣta wæs
hlūde wiþ his wīsum dǣdum and se Cyning cygde þone ealdne wintenagemōt in
Ēastermōnaþ 2006 and swylca wealdsēcendas in hiera gyrnwrace swuteloden þe se
Cyning næfde weald in þæm lande and æfter twǣm wintrum sæd þe se cynedōm biþ
awearpen and þe Nepal wæron cyninglēasu cynewīse.

Gifica wæs Burgenda Cyning in þǣre endhealfe þæs 4. gēarhundes ōþ his dēað in
oððe ymbe þæt 407. Hē wæs fæder tō Guðorm I, Giselhere and Gūðhere. Hē is rinc
in sagum ac ēac in stǣre forþǣm þe Gundobad Burgenda Cyning wrāt of his cynedōme
in his rihtbēc, Lex Burgundionum.

Þæs cyninges naman is on manigum þēoda sagum. In missenlicum gereordum is his
nama Gjúki, Gibica, Gebicar, Gibicho or Gippich.

Se scop þæs Wīdsīðes sanges wrāt þe Gifica wæs Burgenda rīca ac segeþ nā mā. In
þæm Norðiscan geweorce Atlakviða be naman (se is 'Ætla Lēod') hātte hēGjúki, and
se scop segeþ þe Gifica wæs Gūþheres fæder. In þǣm geweorce hē is ǣr cyning on
þǣm Nifelingum and of him is þæt cynn genemned Gjúkungar, se is 'Gificingas'.

Snorri Sturluson segeþ in Edda his bēc þe Gifica ('Gjúki') hæfde twegen sunan -
Gūþhere ('Gunnar') and Hagenan ('Hogni') – and āne dōhtor, Gūðrūne. Gotþorm
(Sigefriþes bana) is his stēopsunu of his wīfe Grimhilde ǣrran hǣmedes.

In Edda lēoðe is ēac Gudny, Gifican and Grimhilde ōðru dōhtor. In þǣm
Guðrunarkvida is þēos dōhtor Gullrond be naman.

Georgisc gewritcræft (ქართული კალიგრაფია) is gewritcræftes cynn, oððe searulic
writing in þæm Georgiscan gereorde and þes cræft nytt þæs gereordes þrēo
Georgiscan stæfrǣwan.

Georgia hæfþ yldlang geselenesse of fægrum gewritcræfte. Handgewritna bēc of
ǣryldum weardon micel þing on Georgieþēode. Cristendōm wæs æt his heorte and sēo
Georgiscu Orthodox Cirice and hiere muncas geaf micel līf to Georgisc gewrite
forþæm þe hie wrāten bēc and eall þæs folces stǣrlica gewritas.

Ælc gear on 14. Ēastermōnaþ, begellaþ Georgiaware þone "Dæg þæs Georgiscan
gereordes". Gearlice on þissum dæge heoldaþ manig byrig on Georgie gewritcræft
gewin, and sigorlēan gewinneþ se man se writeþ betste.

Georgiaware atȳdredon cræftiga weorcas begen of æfæstnesse and of lāre in the
stedum ūt Georgie in mynstrum getimbrode be Georgiscum munucum oððe in swylcum
ðærin būedon hie and onmang swlycum hūsum sind:

On þæm Georgiscum landum wæs Tao-Klarjeti þæt rīce þæs þēodes heort for
scopcræfte and hēr arāsen þā sēlostan magistras in lēoþcræfte, scopcræfte,
orþance and timbercræfte.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Geanl%C3%A6ht_Cynerice

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce Grēatre Brytene and Norþīrlandes is cȳnerīce ofer norþenam
Europan. Man nemneþ hit sceortlīce Geānede Cynerīce oþþe UK (of Nīwum Englisce:
United Kingdom).

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce līþ on garsecges īeglandum be westnorðan Europan. His mǣste
īeg is Bryten (Nīwenglisc: Great Britain) and his oþru Īrland hwǣron licgaþ
siexe scīra þæs rīces. Eall ymbe þissum sǣrīman sind manigfealdum īege and
īegoþe.

Cynerīce is þæt Geānede Cynerīce, þærof is Elisabeþ II Cwēn. His hēafodstōl is
Westmynster (oþþe Lunden þærof is Westmynster nū dǣl). Sēo Cwēn hæfþ hiere stōl
hēr and hiere hām æt Windlesōran.

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce wearþ gescapen æfter syndrigum "Acts of Union", þæt habbaþ
þā sweotolan rīċu Englaland, Wēalas, Scotland, and Īrland geānlǣht under ān
rǣdena in Lundene. Mǣst þæs landes Īrlandes tōsyndrode of þǣm Geānlǣhtan
Cynerīce in 1922, and tōdæg is Īrland Cynewīse, ac se northēasterna dǣl þæs
īeglandes, Norðerne Īrland gehāten, gewunaþ in þǣm Geānedan Cynerīce.

rǣdena in Lundene. Mǣst þæs landes Īrlandes tōsyndrode of þǣm Geānlǣhtan
Cynerīce in 1922, and tōdæg is Īrland Cynewīse, ac se northēasterna dǣl þæs
īeglandes, Norðerne Īrland gehāten, gewunaþ in þǣm Geānedan Cynerīce.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ge%C4%81nl%C7%A3ht_Cyner%C4%ABce

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce Grēatre Brytene and Norþīrlandes is cȳnerīce ofer norþenam
Europan. Man nemneþ hit sceortlīce Geānede Cynerīce oþþe UK (of Nīwum Englisce:
United Kingdom).

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce līþ on garsecges īeglandum be westnorðan Europan. His mǣste
īeg is Bryten (Nīwenglisc: Great Britain) and his oþru Īrland hwǣron licgaþ
siexe scīra þæs rīces. Eall ymbe þissum sǣrīman sind manigfealdum īege and
īegoþe.

Cynerīce is þæt Geānede Cynerīce, þærof is Elisabeþ II Cwēn. His hēafodstōl is
Westmynster (oþþe Lunden þærof is Westmynster nū dǣl). Sēo Cwēn hæfþ hiere stōl
hēr and hiere hām æt Windlesōran.

Þæt Geānede Cynerīce wearþ gescapen æfter syndrigum "Acts of Union", þæt habbaþ
þā sweotolan rīċu Englaland, Wēalas, Scotland, and Īrland geānlǣht under ān
rǣdena in Lundene. Mǣst þæs landes Īrlandes tōsyndrode of þǣm Geānlǣhtan
Cynerīce in 1922, and tōdæg is Īrland Cynewīse, ac se northēasterna dǣl þæs
īeglandes, Norðerne Īrland gehāten, gewunaþ in þǣm Geānedan Cynerīce.

https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ge%C3%BEacasteort

Geþacasteort (Nīwenglisc: Thatcher Peninsula) (54°17′00″S 36°32′00″W﻿ /
﻿54.2833°S 36.5333°W﻿ / -54.2833; -36.5333) is Sūþgeorgie steortland hwæron
standaþ Ēadweard Cyning Næss, þæs landscipes hēafodstōl, and Grytviken, his
mæsta wic.

Ūt strecceþ Geþacasteortes in norþernum Sūþgeorgie betwuh Cumbraland Ēastbyhte
and Moraine Flēote be ēastan and Cumbraland Westbyhte be westan, mid Ēadweard
Cyning Cofan on his ēastrīman. Dynig is hē. Lyell Īsflōd and Hamberg Īsflōd
licgaþ æt his hēafde.

Sē steortland næfde naman beforan þā Folcland Gewinne. In þæm sæcce wæs
Sūþgeorgia þæt ærste land þe sē Bryttisc þrēat eftnām. Æfter þære gūþe sē GC
Antarctisca Stōwnaman Ræd acwæþ þe þæt land hwæron stōd sē hēafodstōl meaht
beran naman æfter Margaret Thatcher, sēo wæs Forma Þegn in þæm dagum and sēo
gereccede to sendenne þone þreat þā īega to hreddenne. Vivian Fuchs, Cniht,
foresittend þæs Antarctiscan Stōwnaman Rædes, cwæþ þe hēo wæs "micel mann in
Sūþgeorgie stǣre". Thatcher wæs, swa swa secgþ hiere friend, 'geficed and
getǣtted' be þissum āre.

https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/F%C3%A6%C8%9Der_h%C7%A3r/%E1%9A%B1%E1%9A%A2%E1%9A%BE

Fæger is hǣrhīw þe man mæg in sumum lēodum findan, þe habbaþ lȳtel þæs deorcan
scinnhīwes melanine. Þæt ānsīene hīw cymþ of missenliċum þingum, ac awa hæfþ
gylden hīw, fram āblæc tō rēadisc "strēawberge" fægrum hǣre, þe hæfþ mā
eumelanin.

Þæt word fæger cymþ of Ealdorliċum Þēodisce *fagraz, and his sweostorword in
ōðrum sprǣcum sind Eald Norðisc fagr, Eald Hēah Þēodisc fagar, and Geatisc
fagrs.[1]

Þæt Nīwe Englisc word for fæger hǣr is blonde, þe man ēac wrīteþ swā blond. Wrāt
man þis word ǣrest in 1481, and cymþ hit of þǣm Eald Frenċisc word blont þe mǣnþ
"hīw þe is healf betwēonan gylden and lēoht ċisten." Man nū brūceþ þis word in
þǣm stede þæs Ealdan Engliscan wordes fæger. Þæt Englisc word, and þus ēac þæt
Frenċisc word blonde hæfþ twegen mihteliċ frymðas. Sum sprǣcmenn cweðaþ þæt cymþ
hit of þǣm Middlan Ieldan Lǣdnan worde blundus, mǣnþ gēolu, fram Ealdum
Francisce *blund, hwelċ gesibb hit mid Ealdum Englisce blonden-feax, ēac cuþ swā
greg hǣred, fram blanden.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/F%C3%A6%C8%9Der_h%C7%A3r

Fæger is hǣrhīw þe man mæg in sumum lēodum findan, þe habbaþ lȳtel þæs deorcan
scinnhīwes melanine. Þæt ānsīene hīw cymþ of missenliċum þingum, ac awa hæfþ
gylden hīw, fram āblæc tō rēadisc "strēawberge" fægrum hǣre, þe hæfþ mā
eumelanin.

Þæt word fæger cymþ of Ealdorliċum Þēodisce *fagraz, and his sweostorword in
ōðrum sprǣcum sind Eald Norðisc fagr, Eald Hēah Þēodisc fagar, and Geatisc

greg hǣred, fram blanden.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/English

Sēo Nīwenglisce sprǣc (on Nīwenglisce: English) is Westgermanisc sprǣc, þe on
Englalande ārās. Hēo belimpeþ, swā sēo Þēodisce sprǣc and sēo Niðerlendisce
sprǣc tō þǣm Westernan twige þāra Germaniscra sprǣca.

Nū is Englisc sēo brādoste gesprǣdede sprǣc þǣre worulde, and hæfþ ymbe þæt
getæl sprecera þe Cīnisc hæfþ. In fela landum biþ Nīwenglisc sēo ǣreste fremðe
sprǣc gelǣred (Sēo Englisc (Scōl)) and is sēo ambihtlice sprǣc þāra mǣstena
betwixfolclicra gesetednessa. Fela þissa gesetednessa habbaþ ōðra ambihtlica
sprǣca. Nīwenglisc prōfaþ hēodæg swā woruldsprǣc.

Tōdæg biþ Englisc fram 340 millionena sprecenda swā mōdorsprǣc gesprecen. Gif
man īeceþ þā æfterran sprecend, cymþ man tō ymbe 510 millionena sprecenda.

Englisc cymþ of þǣre Ealdre Seaxiscre sprǣce and sibbum þēowsprǣcum þe wǣron
gebrōht tō Brytene fram Germaniscum gesittendum of syndrigum dǣlum norþwestes
Þēodisclandes. Sēo frume Englisce sprǣc wæs gehrinen folgiendlīce fram twǣm ȳðum
onrǣses. Se ǣresta onrǣs wæs fram sprecerum sprǣca Scedelendisces twiges þæs
Germaniscan sprǣchīredes, þe gebȳrdon in dǣlas Brytene in þǣm 8an and 9an
ieldum. Se ōðer onrǣs wæs mid Normandigsǣtum in þǣre 11an ielde, þe cynn
sprǣcon, Ealdes Frencisces.

Be þǣm Engliscan-Seaxiscan Cranice, ymbe þæt gēar 449, wǣron þā Engle gelaðode
fram Wyrtgeorne tō helpenne him wiþ þā Pihtas. Ongēan hira help gelendode hē þǣm
Englum in sūþēastum dǣle. Æfter sōhte hē māran help, and forþǣm cōmon þā Seaxe,
Engle, and Geate. Se Cranic spricþ ymbe fylgendne incyme gesittendra, þe
staðelodon on ende seofon cynerīcu. Tōdæges scōlerscipe behogeþ mǣst þisses
spelles tō bēonne spell and fram lēodweardrace gedōne.

Þās Germaniscan infarend oferrīcsodon þā fruman Celtisce sprǣcendan wuniend, þā
sprǣca þāra ālifdon mǣste on Scotland, Wealas, Cornweall, and Īrland. Þā
folcsprǣca, gesprecena fram þǣm ingengum, macodon þæt, þe man hēt Eald Englisc,
þe efenlǣcþ suma rimanþēowsprǣca, in (nū) landum norþwestes Þēodisclandes and
þāra Niðerlanda. Ufor wæs sēo sprǣc gehrinen fram þǣre Norþgermaniscre sprǣce
Norene, þǣra Wīcinga gesprecen, þe on þone norþēastan dǣl gesǣtton (sēo
Georfic).

For þǣm folgiendum 300 gēarum æfter þǣre Norþmandiscan Geþringunge in 1066
sprǣcon þā Norþmandiscan cyningas and sēo hēa duguþ cynn Frencisces āne. Micel
getæl Norþmandiscra worda wǣron inbrōht in Eald Englisc. Se Norþmandisca gehrine
gefæstnode þā gangendan hwierfunge þǣre sprǣce ofer fylgendum ieldum, oþ þǣre
sprǣce, nū Middelenglisc gehāten. Lareowas þǣre tunges lare ne laerdon;
leorneres heora spraec ne leornode. For þon þe þæt folc þāra Norþmanna þeowas
ȝeƿurdon, swa ealswa mot mon þæt 'Niwenglisc' beter 'þeowenglisc' ȝehatan.

In þǣre 15an ielde gewende sēo Micele Selfswēgendwendung þæt Middelenglisc, ēac
mid Lundencyndre sprǣce in lēodwearde and tōþegnunge, and þǣre
regolunggefremmunge gemǣlunge. Nīwenglisc cann gespyred bēon on bæc tō þǣre tīde
Willelmes Shakespeares.

Sēo Nīwenglisce sprǣc is dǣl þæs westernan undertwiges þæs Germaniscan twiges
þæs Indiscan-Europiscan sprǣca cynnes. Feorr þǣra Englisclǣhtan sprǣca swā Tok
Pisin oþþe Bislama, sind þā nīehstan Nīwenglisces Scyttisc (Lallans), mǣste on
Scotland and dǣl Norðernes Īrlandes gesprecen, and þǣræfter Fresisc, on
Þēodiscland and on þǣm Niðerlandum gesprecen. Swā Nīwenglisc is Scyttisc riht
æftergenga Englisces (Englisc-Seaxisc).

Ōðra sibba sprǣca, ac unsibbran þonne Fresisc oþþe Scyttisc, sind Þēodisc,
Seaxisc, Niðerlendisc, Scedelendisca sprǣca, and Afrikaanisc. Manig Frencisc
word sind ēac andgietfullicu tō Nīwenglisces sprecende (ac mid ōðrum
rihtstefne), for þǣm þe Nīwenglisc bedranc ormǣtlic rīm worda fram Frencisce
þurh þā Norþmandisce sprǣce æfter þǣre Norþmandiscan Oferswīðrunge and rihtlīce
of Frencisce in æfterrum ieldum; þǣrfor sind fela worda swīðe nēah þǣm
Frencisce, mid smalum wrītungscēadungum (on wordendungum oþþe mid Ealdes
Frencisces wrītungum, asf.), ēac swā hwīlum scēadunga on mǣnunge.

Englisc grammaticcræft hafaþ lȳtele gebīegunge in efenlǣcnesse mid ōðrum
Indoeuropicum sprǣcum. Tō bisene hæfþ Nīwenglisc, ungelīc Þēodisce,
Niðerlendisce, oþþe Rōmāniscum sprǣcum nān grammatisc cynn and nāne
tōgeīecendlice ānrǣdnesse. cāsu mearcung is æthwōn fullīce gedwinen of þǣre
sprǣce and ālifþ mǣste on þā bīnaman. Þā cynn strangra worda (t.b.
sprecan/spræc/sprǣcon/gesprecen) wiþ þā cynn wācra worda þe sēo sprǣc of
Germanisce ierfde is on weorðe gedwinen and þā lāfa gebīegunge (swā
manigfealdlicu mearcung) wurdon regolfæsta.

Þā seolfan tīd þǣre gebīegunge weorþgedwīnung in Englisce, scōp sēo sprǣc māran
getrēowunge in wīsan swā mōdword and worddiht tō getācnienne grammatisce
mǣnunge. Helpendu word brȳcþ man tō mearcienne tācnu swā frignunga, negativa, þā
underþēodendlican stefn, and gengende tīd

Mid Englisce brȳcþ man þā lǣdene stæfrǣwe būtan accentum, ac mid elþēodigum
wordum, swā résumé (Frencisc) cann man mid accentum wrītan. Mid manigum wordum,
swā night oþþe though is sēo wrītungwīse stǣrlicu (nā sprecendllicu), for þǣm þe
on Middelenglisce wrāt man night and though. Sēo wrītung worda oft ābȳgþ of hū
hīe gesprecen sind, and Nīwenglisc wrītung is oft geþōht sēo unēaðoste ǣnigra
sprǣca tō leornienne, in þǣm sprǣcum þe brūcaþ stæfrǣwa. Sēo Nīwenglisc
rihtwrītunge.

Englisc is ambihtsprǣc in þǣm fylgendum landum, þǣrin þæt getæl þāra
mōdorsprecera is gewriten, hwǣr cūþ:

Englisce sprǣc þegnaþ tō ēacan swā lingua franca in þǣm folgiendum landum and
landscipum:



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Englisc_Ingefeoht

Se Englisca Ingewinn wæs blōdig ingewinn on Englum hwærin feahton þæs Cyninges
awreðiendas wiþ þæs Witenagemōtes awreðiendum in series of armed conflicts and
political machinations of 1642 oð 1651.

Þes wæl wæs in twǣim dalum þa hett man þā Forma Englisca Ingewinn (1642 - 1645)
and þā Oþer Englisca Ingewinn (1648 – 1649) gefeahten betwuht þæm geþafum of
Carles II Greatbryten Cyninges and þæm geþafum þæs Langan Witenagemōtes. Ēac in
1651 wæs þisse gūðe endmesta þing, þæt wæs sigelēasu fyrding be Carl II se
endode in his defeat æt þære Wigorneceastre Beadwe on 3 Hāligmonaþ 1651.

<-- wæs sēo endebyrdness gūða and and wealdscipiscra searwa þā gelumpon betweoh
witenagemōtes awreðiendum and cyninges awreðiendum fram þǣm 1642. gēare þæt
1651., þæt is þæt forme ingefeoht (fram þǣm 1642. oþ þæt 1645.) and þæt ōðer
(fram þǣm 1648. gēare oþ þæt 1649.) betweoh þǣm awreðiendum Charles I and þǣm
awreðiendum þæs Langan Witenegemōtes, and þæt unspēdige onginn fram Charles II
þæs ende wæs his oferdrīfung on þǣre Gūðe Wiogoraceastre on þǣm 3. Hāligmonaþes
þæs 1651. gēares.

Se Ingewinn wæs inextricably mixed mid series of sǣc and ingewinn betweonum 1639
and 1651 and þissa dǣl in þæm þrim rīcum þā wæron Englaland, Scotland and
Īrland, þā wæron sundra rīciu mid ānum ānwealdan, Carl I, forþæm het man þās
gecnyttedan sacas þā Gewinnas þara þrēora Cynerīca oððe þā "Bryttiscan
Ingewinnas".

Æt þæs Oþres Engliscan Ingewinnes ende wæs se ordāl Carles Cyninges and þe man
him behēafde. His sunu Carl II wæs on wræcce gesended, and in stede þæs
Engliscan cynedōmes wæs sēo Engla Cynewīse (1649 - 1653) and Weardscipe
(1653–1659) under Olivres Cromwelles agnum weald. Sēo gesetnes þærbe ne mōt man
attend weorðscipe ūtan þære Angelcirican endode and nīw oncwedend þegnhād wæs
gestaþoled on Īrum. Þās þing gestaðoledon principal þe se cyning ne mōt rīcan
būtan þæs Witenagemōtes geþafunge.

Engle þoleden ingewinn in sundrigum yldum, ac ǣr þis wæron swylce unfriþ ymbe
hwā meahte ricsian. Se Englisca Ingewinn wæs for in hwelcum wīse meaht þæt rīce
be gericsoden, hwǣrfor secgð stǣrwriteras þe he wæs seo Englisce Onwendung and
on þæs Cyninges folgendum in þæm dagum wæs he se Micla Wiðersæc.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Englisc_In%C8%9Defeoht

Se Englisca Ingewinn wæs blōdig ingewinn on Englum hwærin feahton þæs Cyninges
awreðiendas wiþ þæs Witenagemōtes awreðiendum in series of armed conflicts and
political machinations of 1642 oð 1651.

Þes wæl wæs in twǣim dalum þa hett man þā Forma Englisca Ingewinn (1642 - 1645)
and þā Oþer Englisca Ingewinn (1648 – 1649) gefeahten betwuht þæm geþafum of
Carles II Greatbryten Cyninges and þæm geþafum þæs Langan Witenagemōtes. Ēac in
1651 wæs þisse gūðe endmesta þing, þæt wæs sigelēasu fyrding be Carl II se
endode in his defeat æt þære Wigorneceastre Beadwe on 3 Hāligmonaþ 1651.

<-- wæs sēo endebyrdness gūða and and wealdscipiscra searwa þā gelumpon betweoh
witenagemōtes awreðiendum and cyninges awreðiendum fram þǣm 1642. gēare þæt
1651., þæt is þæt forme ingefeoht (fram þǣm 1642. oþ þæt 1645.) and þæt ōðer
(fram þǣm 1648. gēare oþ þæt 1649.) betweoh þǣm awreðiendum Charles I and þǣm
awreðiendum þæs Langan Witenegemōtes, and þæt unspēdige onginn fram Charles II
þæs ende wæs his oferdrīfung on þǣre Gūðe Wiogoraceastre on þǣm 3. Hāligmonaþes
þæs 1651. gēares.

Se Ingewinn wæs inextricably mixed mid series of sǣc and ingewinn betweonum 1639
and 1651 and þissa dǣl in þæm þrim rīcum þā wæron Englaland, Scotland and
Īrland, þā wæron sundra rīciu mid ānum ānwealdan, Carl I, forþæm het man þās
gecnyttedan sacas þā Gewinnas þara þrēora Cynerīca oððe þā "Bryttiscan
Ingewinnas".

Æt þæs Oþres Engliscan Ingewinnes ende wæs se ordāl Carles Cyninges and þe man
him behēafde. His sunu Carl II wæs on wræcce gesended, and in stede þæs
Engliscan cynedōmes wæs sēo Engla Cynewīse (1649 - 1653) and Weardscipe
(1653–1659) under Olivres Cromwelles agnum weald. Sēo gesetnes þærbe ne mōt man
attend weorðscipe ūtan þære Angelcirican endode and nīw oncwedend þegnhād wæs
gestaþoled on Īrum. Þās þing gestaðoledon principal þe se cyning ne mōt rīcan
būtan þæs Witenagemōtes geþafunge.

Engle þoleden ingewinn in sundrigum yldum, ac ǣr þis wæron swylce unfriþ ymbe
hwā meahte ricsian. Se Englisca Ingewinn wæs for in hwelcum wīse meaht þæt rīce
be gericsoden, hwǣrfor secgð stǣrwriteras þe he wæs seo Englisce Onwendung and
on þæs Cyninges folgendum in þæm dagum wæs he se Micla Wiðersæc.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Englalandes

Englaland is an mægþ (þe man England on nīwan Englisc hæt) þe is se dæl þæs
Geanedan Cynerices (þe man the United Kingdom on Modernan Englisc hæt). Hit norþ
ligeþ ymb Scottwara land and ymb Walewara land west and þus hit hafaþ
land-gemære mid Scottwara lande (þe man Scotland on Modernan Englisc hæt) and
mid Walewara lande (þe man Wales on Modernan Englisc hæt). Hit ligeþ on
westan-norþan Europe. Sæs þe þæt Englaland utanymblian sind be-westannorþan se
Irisc Sæ (the Irish Sea) and be-westansuþan se Celtlic Sæ (the Celtic Sea).

Englalandes nama cymþ of þǣm Englum, anum þriora mægþa Germania þe hie ofcomon
to Englande, oþerum twæm mægþum þe hie ofcomon to Englalande to eardian sind
Eald-Seaxa mægþ and Iota mægþ, þe habbaþ Englaland gesetled þǣm 5an and 6an
gēarhundredum. Siþþan 1707, þe man Grēate Bryten scōp, nu Englaland is ungewilde
þeod.

Englaland wæs in gēardagum cynerīce. Æþelstan cyning wæs sē ǣrresta cyning eall
Englacynn to geānlǣcenne in ānum rīce. Englalandes endemestan undercyning
aflīemed Ēadred Engla Cyning and Englarīce wæs an.

Mid Scottarīce wæs Englarīce geānlǣhte be Anne Cwēne in 1707, Grēate Bryten
Cynerīce to scieppenne.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dylan_Thomas

Dylan Marlais Thomas (27 October 1914 – 9 November 1953) wæs Brittisc scop and
writere þæs weorces belimpaþ manig mǣre gid: he wrāt se 'stemmapleg' be naman
'Under Meolcwude' and swylc gid "Gān ne bleaþe in þā gōde nihte" (Do not go
gentle into that good night) and "And dēaþ ne sceall habban ne rīce" (And death
shall have no dominion) and manig spellas wrāt he for lēafe and for stemme,
tobysene 'Cildes Cristmæsse on Wēalum' (A Child's Christmas in Wales) and
'Gelicnes þæs Cræftan swa Geong Hund'.

In Swegnesīege se is on Glamorgane wæs Dylan Thomas geboren in 1914 and hū self
gecneaw, þe he wæs Wēalh, is strang in his fitte.

Dylan Thomas weard gelufod of mannum in his dagum for his cræfte. Noþȳlǣs, oððæt
ðe his scopcræft wæs fæger, yfel wæs his līf. Æt his dēaþ in Nīweoferwicceastre
bār 39 winter, and menn ceann him þe he wæs oferdrincere and libbede in
gæglbǣrnesse.

Dylan Thomas wrāt in þæm Nīwengliscan gereorde. Man secg þe he wæs onmang
Wēalacynnes hēastum scopum þæs 20. gearhundes for his searwe plege mid wordum
and wordbiliþum.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Diablo_(gamen)

Dēofol, hātte Diablo on Nīwum Englisce (þe is Spēonisc fōr "Dēofol"), is
spærcletelle gamen fram Blizzard Norðe gemacod, and fram Blizzard Entertainment
ālīesed, on Gēolmōnaðe, 1996.

Standende in þǣm Cānduras rīċe þǣre worulde þæs Friþhūses, Dēofol hæfþ þone
plēgere ān anlīepe hæleðe wieldeþ, swā hē oþþe hēo fiehteþ tō cwellenne Eges
Hlāford. Under þǣm tūne Tristram, sīðeþ se plēgere þurh sixtīene burgum tō
feohtenne ætnīehstan Dēofol and his hildedēoflas.

Dēofol wæs betstgeċīept, and æfter þǣre folclicnesse þæs ǣrestan gamenes,
underset gamen, hātte Dēofol: Hellfȳr, wæs on 1997 ālīesed. Þis wæs be rihte
ōðre gefolgod, Dēofol II, in 2000.

Sēo lār Dēofles is ymbe gūðe betwēonan Heofene and Helle. Se tūn Tristrames is
under gewealce be hildedēoflum gecumen, and se plēgere sceal þǣm tūne beorgan,
and ēac, þǣre worulde, be endebyrdeþ þone Eges Hlāford. Swā dilfþ se plēger intō
þǣre underworulde, sum dǣl þæs spelles ymbe þā gūðe betwēonan Heofene and Helle,
samod swā ongietenes ymbe Dēofle hine selfne, sind þurh miċlum bōcum onwrigen,
þe sind þurh þǣm burgum gefunden.

Dēofol is se Hlāford þæs Eges and ān þāra Þrēora Hēafodyfla þǣre Helle, þā
mǣstan mihtigan hlāfordas þæs hildedēofolcynnes. Lange ǣr þǣm belimpum þæs
gamenes, wæs hē be dīegolre gefadunge scinncræftigra gefangen, cūþ þā Horadrim.
Þā Horadrim oferfēngon ǣlċ Hēafodyfel in Sāƿolstāne; Dēofles rēad stān wæs in
eorþscræf gebyrged, under þǣm tūne þes Tristrames, and swā þā tīman forþgān, wæs
forgiten. Þēah his carċernung mǣneþ ēċe bēon, sēo miht þæs sawolstānes wācode
þurh tīman, ænextan geþafiende Dēofol tō brūcenne mǣte miht fram beinnan þǣm
stāne. Hē feorrþance gewearðaþ wīcing Tristrames, Lazarus Arċebiscop, intō þēowe
his. Swā þæt Dēofol mæg fram þǣm sawolstāne āfaran, Dēofol þearf mann āgan. Þurh
his þēow Lazarus Arċebiscop, hē ǣrest fandode Leoric cyning wealdan, ac Dēofol
wæs tō unmihtig, and ne meahte Leoric gewieldan.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Deprobane

Taprabane is rīce and īegland be Indealandes sūðernum strande in þǣm Indiscan
Gārsecge. Sēo īeg hæfþ tweontig þūsend þūsenda manna.

Tāprabane hæfþ in missenlicum gereordum mænige namen. Ealdcrēcas nemdon hīe
Taprobane (and Ælfred cyning geaf hire þone naman Tāpraban and Dēprobane. Þām
Arabum wæs hēo Serendib. Tō Marco Polo wæs hēo cūþ swā Seilan, and Ceilão wæs se
nama gegifan be Portugalwarum þā hīe cōmon to Tāprabane in þǣm 1505. gēare. On
NĪwum Englisce wæs þæs īeglandes nama Ceylon.

In þǣm 1972. gēare wæs þæs rīces ambihtlīc nama awended tō "Sri Lanka" (in
Sinhalisce śrī laṃkā, IPA: [ˌʃɾiːˈlaŋkaː]. Þæs īeglandes āgnan nama is in
Sinhalisce ලංකාව Laṃkāva, IPA: [laŋˈkaːʋə], and in Tamilisce இலங்கை ilaṅkai,
iˈlaŋgai). "Sri Lanka" is of Sanskrit worde laṃkā, þe is "boldwelena land", þe
wæs ēac his nama in ealdre Indiscre sægene þæs "Mahabharata" and þæs "Ramayana".
Sri is Sanskritisc titul of āre.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dave_Dobbyn

Dave Dobbyn (mid þǣm titul ONZM) is Nīwsǣlendisc hēahgieffōnde drēamere,
sangere, sangwrītere, and drēamhordforþberend. On his ǣrran weorcwege wæs hē
agylda þæs weolcdrēamlīcan hēapes Th' Dudes and þæs gēogoþdrēamlīcan hēapes DD
Smash. Þǣræfter hafaþ hē forþboren þæt mǣste dǣl his drēamhorda tō ānscēawere.

Dobbynes ǣrost spēd cōm mid þǣm weolcdrēamhēape Th' Dudes, þæs agylda hē wearþ
hraðe æfter hē lēt Sacred Heart College on þǣre underbyrig Glen Innes Auclandes.
Þæs trēpes spēd "Be Mine Tonight" (þe mǣnþ "Wes Mīn Tōniht") feng sigebēacen tō
ānsange þæs gēares on þǣm 1979 gēare on Nīwum Sǣlande, þā hwīle se sang "Bliss"
hæfþ hefigtācne (and smicerhīwunglīce, for þȳ hit ǣrost wæs tō wiþmedulīcum
sange gewriten) Nīwsǣlendisc medusang.

Þǣr DD Smash tōfōron, Dobbyn undergann tō gānne on spēdgum ānlēpgum weorcwege;
hē awrāt þone drēam þæs līflīcan fullan īwungspelles Footrot Flats: The Dog's
Tale]] on þǣm 1986 gēare. Þæt īwungspell hæfde twegen spēdge ānsangas: "Oughta
Be in Love" and þone getæloferwinnendan sang "Slice of Heaven", þe wæs
swēgwriten mid þǣm trēpe Herbs. Æfter þǣre forþsettunge þæs īwungspelles, "Slice
of Heaven" wearþ ān Dobbynes gecūðostra sanga, oft gebrocen on landsōcncȳþþum
gedōn on Australiscre feorrsihþe þā byldaþ lēoda tō sēcenne Nīwe Sǣland. Tō
wæstme þisses, manige Australisce unearnostlīce hēton þone sang Nīwes Sǣlandes
rīcisc sang.

Dobbynes spēdig sang "Loyal" (þæs 1988 gēares) wæs gebrocen tō sange þæs
Nīwsǣlendiscan Hēapes on þǣm asprungenan beorge America's Cup. Hē hæfþ ēac
forþboren drēamhord þǣm Australiscan sangere Grante McLennane and hæfþ geforðod
drēamhordum fram Jenny Morris, Gyane Evanse, Bice Rungan, and ōðrum. Hē hæfþ ēac
befaren mid Rungan and Time Finne, þe wæs gemyndod on þǣm wæfersīnlīcan
drēamhorde Together in Concert: Live, on þǣm 2000 gēare.

Dobbynes drēamhord Available Light, þe wæs forþboren on þǣm 2005 gēare, andfeng
folclīce and dēmendlīce befæstunge. On þǣm 2005 gēare plegede Dobbyn þone
lādānsang fram Available Light, "Welcome Home" (þe mǣnþ "Wilcume Hām") be þǣre
New Zealand Music Awards hēahgiefa gifte. Under þǣre wæfersīne, Ahmed Zaoi, þe
wæs sēcende wiþ fæstnesscartan gifen for rǣswedum bandum egesherum, cōm on þǣre
wæferstōwe mid Dobbyne.

His forþberung þæs drēamhordes Anotherland on þǣm 2008 gēare cōm on þæt NZ Top
40 Album Charts mid þǣre ōðerre endebyrdnesse and belāf on þǣm getæle 6 wuca,
endlīce fōnde goldene setnesse.

Dobbyn is eftgeboren Crīsten, and hafaþ geworden wīfod on Anneliesje under þǣm
mǣstan dǣle his weorcweges. Þā tū habbaþ tū cildru cened.

On Ǣrran Gēolan þæs 1984 gēares, DD Smash wæs tēonde be ūtanweardre wæfersīne on
Aoteaplæsan on Auclande. Under heora tīman wæs þǣr spearccræftapringness þe
dydon dǣl þæs gemanges unstillu. Heora sumu undergunnon tō weorpenne bēorflæscan
and burgweardas hīe ætfeahton. Sēo gelimplīcness wearþ gewersod and sume þæs
hrēamswēotes wæs abannen. Dobbyn dydon unsǣlgu word be þǣm burgweardum þe
wēnendlīce ahyrtede þǣm hrēame. Sēo wæftersīn wæs fōresteped fram þǣm
burgweardum and dǣl þæs gemanges dydon bolgenlīce, tōbrecende cēaphūsa ēagdura
on Cwēnstǣte on Auclande. Se forma þegn David Lange hēt ǣrend ascunge and tō
wæstme wæs sacung wīt Dobbyn gedōn, þæt hē hrēam hēte. Þā sprǣce weargnesse
wǣron on þǣm Ǣrran Līðan þæs 1985 gēares undergunnen. His forespreca spēdiglīce
hine bearg and hē wæs gelādod fram þǣre sacunge "gebǣres wīsan þe gelīce
anstelle hǣste wiþ hād oþþe ǣhte and nytte bismerworda".

Be þǣm New Zealand Music Awards þæs 2001 gēares andfōh Dobbyn Līftīman
Þurhtēounge Hēafgiefe. On þǣm 2002 gēare wearþ hē Ambeht þǣre Nīwes Sǣlandes
Endebyrdness Weorðes|Nīwes Sǣlandes Endebyrdnesse Weorðes tō þonce his 'cræfta
and geforðunga'. On þǣm 2005 gēare and þǣm 2006 gēare andfōh hē þā hēahgiefe þæs
"Formestan Sangwrīteres þæs Gēares" and þæs "Betstan Werlīcan Ānsangeres" on
ilcan endebyrdnesse, heora bū for his weorce tō Available Light.

https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/D%C3%BDfung

Sēo dȳfung gēo wæs hlēapung in wætre, ac nū hit oft is sund under wætre mid
sierwunge þe giefþ lyft tō ǣðmienne under wætre. And þēos sierwung oft nū hātte
scuba, þe cwōm of Nīwengliscum "Self Contained Underwater Breathing Apparatus".
And æt fruman "SCUBA" segde Americiscra gūþfroggamanna ǣðmungsierwunga.

And sume habbaþ micle lyftfatu and se dȳfere ǣðmaþ of þǣm lyftfæte and ūt in
wæter. And þēos sierwunge hātaþ in Nīwenglisce "open circuit", and hit ēac oft
hātte "aqualung". And Jacques-Yves Cousteau and Gagnan macodon þone ǣrestne
aqualung in gēare 1942. And mǣste hit wæs āna for geweorce oþþæt in gēare 1953
se National Geographical Magazine wrāt fore worulde ymb Sciptogan Cousteaus
geweorce under sǣ æt Grand Congloué īege neam Marseilles þǣr wæs eald scip þe
sanc þenden Rōm ricsode Europam, and forþȳ swīðe manige writon tō him tō
āscianne hwǣr man mihte bycgan aqualung. And gēo se aqualung oþþe air scuba næs
swā man nū siehþ wunelīc on sǣrīmum, ac his lyftwieldend [= regulator, demand
valve] wæs micel and behindan þæs dȳferes healse, and oft mid twǣm lyftfatum.
And oft nū þis ealde cynn scuban hātte se twēgra pīpa scuba.

And sume habbaþ lȳtle oxygenfatu and se dȳfere ǣðmaþ of poccan and eft ongēan in
poccan, and his līc nimþ oxygen and māra oxygen cymþ of fæte, and his līc macaþ
þone carbon dioxide, and in þǣre ǣðmungsyrwunge is fæt full þæs sodalīmes þe
iteþ þisne carbon dioxide, and forþȳ se dȳfere ne macaþ (bubbles), and mæg
swimman micle lengra under sǣ mid ǣðmungsierwunge mid samum gewihte. And þēs
sierwunge hātaþ eftǣþmendas and in Nīwenglisce rebreathers oþþe closed circuit.
And nū sind eftǣðmendas þe misciaþ nitrogen oþþe helium in þā ǣðmunge, swā hātte
'nitrox' and 'heliox' and 'trimix', tō þæs þe man mæg dȳfan dēopora þonne mid
ungemiscodum oxygene. And þū mæg sēon maniga gelīcnessa swilcra hēr .

Hēr is lȳtel āstȳriende biliþ dȳferes mid þǣm lȳtlan oxygeneftǣðmende Salvus þe
Siebe Gorman gēo macode in Lundene, and mid him man mihte dȳfan (oþþe weorcan in
atorlyfte) healf stunde oþþe lȳtle lengre, and hit is swīðe unhefig, and se
dȳfere miht swimman swā īeþ swā ēan sierwunge. And hēr is grēat gelīcnesse and
in hire be hȳþwætre geweorctoga bebīedeþ.

And swilce dȳferas oft hātton froggamenn, for þǣm þe on hira fōtum hīe habbaþ
scōs þe sind swā þā fēt froggan, and þēs hātton finnas. On winstran sīdan siehþ
man twēgen froggamenn þe rīdaþ in hȳðe dierne under wætere on rīdungfȳrramme.
Man macode ǣrest þis cynn froggamannberendes in Italiam for gūðe in gēare 1939
and þā Italiscan froggamenn nemnedon hit maiale, þe segþ 'swīn', for þǣm þe him
wǣron þā ǣrestan swīðe earfoþlīce to stȳrienne. Ac in Brytene nemnede man hit
manned torpedo oþþe human torpedo, oþþe oft chariot, þe segþ 'wīgcræt'. And man
mæg sēon þrēo þisra in Eden Camp þe is nēah Mæðeltūne (Nīwenglisc: Malton) on
Eoforwīcscīre on Englum. Hīe habbaþ þone Bryttiscan eftǣðmend CDBA þe Siebe
Gorman macode, þe segþ in Nīwenglisce "Clearance Diver's Breathing Apparatus",
and in Brytenes scipfyrde clearance diver is scipfyrdisc dȳfere þe dȳfeþ to
weorcanne and ne tō feohtanne.

Man siehþ twēgen froggamenn mid þǣm Russiscan eftǣðmende IDA71, and ān hira
rīdeþ þone Russiscan dȳfereberend Protei 5. And hēr sind þrēo dȳferas mid þǣm
IDA71.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Communism

Gemǣnre ǣhte rǣd (on Nīwenglisce hātte Communism) is gefērscipes endebyrdness in
þǣm þe gefērscipes gradu sind adeligod and ǣht is gemǣnlīce gewealden; hit is
ēac stēormǣllic oncnāwness and gefērsciplīc brǣdung þe tīemeþ and seteþ self tō
scieppenne swelce gefērrǣdene.

Karl Marx sægde þæt gemǣnre ǣhte rǣd bēo sēo æftermeste byrdnesse in
gefērrǣdene, þe wǣre gedōn þurh weorcmanna onhebbunge and wǣre ānlīce mihtlīc
æfter middel byrdness macaþ þā forþberendan mihta, þe inlǣde oferblǣd gōda and
þegniscipa.

"Smǣte gemǣnre ǣhte rǣd" in þǣm Marxiscan andgiete tācnaþ ge gradlēase, ge
rīclēaes, ge ofþricnesslēase gefērrǣdne[sēðung þurfed] þǣr cēosunga be þǣm þe
man forþbirþ and be þǣm rǣdum þe mann wolde gesēcan sind gedōn
folcwealde,[sēðung þurfed] þe lǣteþ ǣlcne dǣlnimend gefērrǣdene tō dǣlnimenne
þæs cēosunge macunge weorces in ge þǣm stēormǣllīcum and feohwendunglīcum dǣlum
līfes. In nīwlīcre nytte is þæt word "gemǣnre ǣhte rǣd" oft gebrocen tō hātenne
þā rǣd þāra missenlīcena gemǣnǣhtrǣdlicena rīca, þā wǣron ānwealdendu weald þe
hæfdon middellīce wealdena feohwendunga and ǣhte eallra þāra middela forþbǣro.
Se mǣsta dǣl gemǣnǣhtrǣdlicra wealda staðolode heora geþeaht on Marxleniniscum
rǣde.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carl_I_Gr%C4%93atre_Bryten_Cyning

Carl I (19 Blōtmōnaþ 1600 – 30 Æfterra Gēol 1649) wæs Engla, Scotta and Ira
Cyning oð 27 Hrēþmōnaþ 1625 oð ðe man hin behēafdod in 1649. Carls hæfde geflit
for miht mid his Witenagemōte, þær þe he wolde scop bēodan þær þe sohted se
Witenagemōt to bætenne his cynelican frumgife. Manige on his Engliscum
underþeodum wiþ opposed his dǣdum, and sundorlice þe he hrinede þā Cirice and
hsi levying of scop būtan þæs Witenagemōtes andwyrdinge and hērbe man aliefde þe
se cyning be his dǣdum weard swa swa tyrannisc sundoranweald.

Sæc ofer ǣwe hæfde þōlde Carl in eallum his cynedōm. Ǣfæst menn ne geliefed þone
cyning forþæm þe he ne geaf ne fremfull fulltum þæm Oncwedendum rīcum on þæm
Þreotig Gearena Gewinn, and he bewodded Rōmciricefæst cwēne, Henrietta Maria,
Frencisce æþle hlāfdige. Gefyrhto hæfde Carles underþeodnas ymbe þæs cyninges
æfæstnesse and ēac þær geaf Carl fyrþringnesse swylcum ciricemannum swa swa
Richard Montagu, and Willelm Laud, þone anstealde he on Cantawararbyrige
biscopstōle. On Englum aliefdon manige þe swylce þing brohtedon þā Angelcirice
too close to the Rēmiscan Cirice. Þæn Carl wolde be niede bringan Scottena
Cirice under biscopum and his agnum bysne agann se Biscopena Gewinn. Be swylcum
þingum wæron þā Engliscan and Scyttiscan Witenagemōtas elnoden and þæs cyninges
feall brohtede nearr.

Þurh Carles' endlice gearas wæs se Englisca Ingewinn, hwærin feaht se Cyning wiþ
þreatum þāra Engliscum and Scyttiscum Witenagemōtum. Carl wæs geahined in þæm
Ǣrrsta Ingewinn (1642–45), hwæræfter aliefod se Witenagemōt þe se Cyning wolde
ceosan grundgesetness gebunden cynedōm, Ac Carl sohted geþoftscipe mid
Treowmannum on Scottum and he fliemede to Wiht.

Þæs Cyninges fleam ongann þone Ōðru Ingewinn (1648–49) and oþru sigeleasnesse
for Carle. Man him fang and beheafde for swicdōme.

Þis is getalu byrig in þǣm fīftig Geānlǣhtum Rīcum as well as U.S.-owned
territories (Puerto Rico, the United States Virgin Islands, Guam, the Northern
Mariana Islands, and American Samoa) and the District of Columbia. For a more
exhaustive list of cities in a particular state or territory, see the main

United States.

Hēafodgewrit: List of cities in Utah (which includes towns and census-designated

Hēafodgewrit: Ceastra in Virginia (Note: Virginia brūceþ þone þanc þǣre
"selfstandendu burg" for mǣste wǣrum byrig, swā sumum þissum stede mæg scīra,

https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Br%C5%8Dcminte

Mentha sylvestris (gelīce naman Mentha longifolia L., Mentha tomentosa D'Urv,
and Mentha incana Willd.) is cynn in þǣm cynde Mentha (Minte). Gemǣnelīce is hēo
cūþ swā Horsminte in Englalande, oþþe Wildu minte. Man mæg hīe ēac opene mintan
nemnan, and efne hwīlum brōðorwyrt. (Þes æftemesta nama ne sceolde bēon gemenged
wiþ þæt eallmislice cynn Mentha pulegium, gemǣnelīce brōðorwyrt gehāten.)

Mentha sylvestris is a crēopendu ēcu hwæs lēaf stincaþ swāa peppermint scented
aroma. Gelīc manigum mintum, is Mentha sylvestris crēopendu plante. Hire lēaf
geweaxaþ on healmlēas wīn and sind healsrefeðerlice, getēðede, and
grǣggrēnehǣwene. Mentha sylestris ācenne lilac, blācbaswe, or hwīte blōstmas
andlang nearwiendlicra gāda. Sēo plante gespringe fram 16yn oþ 48yn (40cm to
1.2m) lang. Hēo sprǣdeþ þurh forþhealde stelan and wiexþ tō geþeccenne
uncūðelice mearce.

Gelīc mǣst ealle mintan, Mentha sylvestris is onwadendlicu. Man gīeme hwonne hīe
plantie in unheaðorodum flōrum.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blonde_hair

Fæger is hǣrhīw þe man mæg in sumum lēodum findan, þe habbaþ lȳtel þæs deorcan
scinnhīwes melanine. Þæt ānsīene hīw cymþ of missenliċum þingum, ac awa hæfþ
gylden hīw, fram āblæc tō rēadisc "strēawberge" fægrum hǣre, þe hæfþ mā
eumelanin.

Þæt word fæger cymþ of Ealdorliċum Þēodisce *fagraz, and his sweostorword in
ōðrum sprǣcum sind Eald Norðisc fagr, Eald Hēah Þēodisc fagar, and Geatisc
fagrs.[1]

Þæt Nīwe Englisc word for fæger hǣr is blonde, þe man ēac wrīteþ swā blond. Wrāt
man þis word ǣrest in 1481, and cymþ hit of þǣm Eald Frenċisc word blont þe mǣnþ
"hīw þe is healf betwēonan gylden and lēoht ċisten." Man nū brūceþ þis word in
þǣm stede þæs Ealdan Engliscan wordes fæger. Þæt Englisc word, and þus ēac þæt
Frenċisc word blonde hæfþ twegen mihteliċ frymðas. Sum sprǣcmenn cweðaþ þæt cymþ
hit of þǣm Middlan Ieldan Lǣdnan worde blundus, mǣnþ gēolu, fram Ealdum
Francisce *blund, hwelċ gesibb hit mid Ealdum Englisce blonden-feax, ēac cuþ swā
greg hǣred, fram blanden.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Berewicscir

Berewicscir is scīr on norþhealfe þæs Tuidi ea. Heo hæfþ mearc mid mid
Norþhymbralande be suðan, East Loðene and Midloðene be norðan. Be eastan is
særime. Berewicscir is seo suðeasternmest þara Scyttiscena scirena.

Berewicscir nimþ hiere naman fram Berewicburg, seo ær wæs micel sæport and
Berewicscire scirburg oððæt wæs hit gelosen to Englacyning endlice in 1482.

Berewicscir Scirgeþinge wæs uparæred in 1890. His ærest setl wæs in Dunse, æt
þæm ealdan Scirgerefa Stālærne.

Berewicscir nis nu gerecscir; se Scirgeþinge wæs geended in 1975. Nu feolþ heo
under þǣm Scyttisce Mearc geþingedome. Æfter 1975 oððæt 1995 wæron Berewicscire
nama, wæpen and mæst hiere gierde þurh boldgetale gebrucan.

Berewicscire scirburg, hwæræfter is hit genemed, wæs Berewic oððæt 1482, þa wæs
Berewicburg gelosen to Englum. (Man secgþ þe Berewic is nu burg in
Norþhymbralande.) Æfter 1482 wæs Berewicscire toþegnung gedon æt Dunse oððe æt
Laudere, oððæt in 1596 weard Grenehlǣw þa scirburg.

Berewicscir Scirgeþinge abaddon wæpengiefu in 1890. Se Lēo Hlāford Wǣpencyning
bryttade þone giefe in þæm ilcan geare. Þa wæpen gesceaweden beran in bende to
elme, seo wæs dæl þære wæpna Berewic-burgscipes, and wæs scild-cræftig gamen on
byriges and scire namum.

Oððæt ðe Berewicscire naman is be wealdlice gehyded, on þære scire folc nis he
geforged. Giet is The Berwickshire News gewídmærsed ælce wuce, and manige
gefērscipas and band habbað Berewicscir in hiera naman.

Se Berewicscir Burglufu Frygyld hegaþ gearlic Freoðiað Berewicscir Clæne Tilung,
gedemede ælc Þrimilcemonaþ. Nu tilaþ se Frygyld for radtæcne æt þæm ingangum
þære scire to secgenne 'Þu cymest in Berewicscire'



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beethoven

Ludwig van Beethoven (spricþ "LUD-vih fan BĒ-to-ven", 16 Gēolmōnaþ 1770 – 26
Hrēþmonaþ 1827) wæs Germanisc songcræftmann and pianoplegere. Hē wæs weorþliċ
þæs hweorfendan tīman þāra Classiscan and Rōmantiscan ylda, and swā ān þāra
grēatost sangcræftmanna eallan yldan ofstenþ.

In Bonne geboren, fōr hē tō Wīene and þǣr wunode in his ǣr twentigwintrum, mid
Joseph Haydne leornende and ƿæs swiftlic cūþ swā cræftful pianoplegere. Þēah
wearþ hē dēaf in his ǣr twentigwintrum, þurhstōd hē tō ācræftenne and plegenne.

Beethoven ƿæs dohtorsusu Flemisc glīwdrēammann þe ēac Ludwig van Beethoven hǣtt
(1712–1773). Siþþan 1733 wæs se ielda Beethoven bass singere þæs geardes Cylnes,
þe Kapellmeister wearþ. Se ieldra Beethoven hæfde ān sunu, Johann van Beethoven
(1740–1792), þe swā þēow worhte, ēac tǣcende piano and fiðel tō earnienne gield.

Johann wīfode Maria Magdalena Keverich in 1744. Hēo wæs dohtor Johannes
Heinriches Keveriches, þe hēafodcōc þæs geardes Ercebiscopes Treueris wæs.

Of þissum wīfunge wæs Beethoven in Gēolmōnþe 1770 geboren, and wæs on 17
Gēolmōnþe gefullede. Cildru þæs tīman oft wǣron gefullode on þǣm dæge æfter
beorþ, ac biþ hit tō menn uncūþ gif gefullode wæs Beethoven. Hit is cūþ tō menn
þæt his cynn, and his lærere Johann Albrechtsberger mǣrsodon his beorþdæg on 16
Gēolmōnþes.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Balsminte

Balsminte (Mentha aquatica) is perennial plante in þǣm mentha cynde and is
gemǣne þurhūt Europe, būtan in þǣm ȳtemestan Norðe.

Hēo wiexþ ymbe 90 cm on hīehþe, although it may reach heights of 150 cm when
supported by taller vegetation and has a distinctly minty smell. It has ovate to
ovate-lanceolate, green (sometimes purplish), opposite, toothed, veined leaves
which can be either hairy or hairless. Þā stefnas sind oft purpurene. Flowers
are tiny, densely crowded, purple, tubular, pinkish to lilac in colour and bloom
from July to September. Water mint is pollinated by insects, but can easily be
propagated through root cuttings, like other species of mint.

Swā se ōðer nama wæterminte tācnaþ, findeþ man wætermintan in þǣm scealdum
margins and channels of streams, rivers, pools, dykes, ditches, canals, wet
meadows, marshes and fens. If the plant grows in the water itself, it rises
above the surface of the water. It generally occurs on mildly acid to calcareous
(it is common on soft limestone) mineral or peaty soils.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Autaugaville%2C_Alabama

Autaugaville is tūn þe ligþ in Autaugan Scīre, Alabaman. Æfter þǣre 2000
folcrīmunge, is þæt tūnscipes rīm 820.

Be þǣm U.S. Folcrīmungambihte, hæfþ se tūn a æltæwe area of 20.5 km² (7.9 mi²).
20.0 km² (7.7 mi²) his is land and 0.4 km? (0.2 mi²) his is wæter. The æltæwe
area is 2.15% water.

Æfter þǣre folcrīmunge2 of 2000, sind þǣr 820 lēoda, 316 hūscipa, and 219
families wuniende in þǣm tūne. The population density is 41.0/km² (106.1/mi²).
There are 384 housing units at an average density of 19.2/km² (49.7/mi²). The
racial makeup of the town is 32.32% White, 65.98% Blæc, 0.24% Native American,
0.24% from other races, and 1.22% of twǣm oþþe mārum cynnum. 0.98% of the
population are Hispanic or Latino of any race.

Þǣr sind 316 gehūsscipa, and of þǣm þabbaþ 34.5% cildru under þǣre ielde 18 þe
wuniaþ mid him, 39.6% sind married couples living together, 25.0% habbaþ
wīflicne bondan mid nānum hūsbondan andweardum, and 30.4% are non-families.
28.5% of all households are made up of individuals and 13.6% have someone living
alone who is 65 years of age or older. Sēo midde gehūsscipes micelnes is 2.59
and sēo midde hīredes micelnes is 3.18.

Þæt midde feohsceatt for gehūsscipe in þǣm tūne is $22,563, and þæt midde
feohsceatt for hīrede is $35,417. Weras habbaþ middel feohscheatt $29,688 wiþ
$19,821 for wīfum. Þæt for hēafde feohsceatt for þǣm tūne is $12,586. 27.1% þæs
tūnscipes and 27.4% hīwena sind under þǣre iermþlīnan. Of þǣm hālan tūnscipe,
31.2% þāra lēoda under þǣre ielde 18, and 23.2% þāra 65-wintra and ieldrena sind
under þǣre iermþlīnan.

Autaugaville is dǣl þǣre Autauga Scīr Scōl Endebyrdnes and is hām tō
Autaugaville Scōle for for-kindergarten tō grādes 12 leornerum.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Austria

Sēo Cynewīse Ēastrīces (on Þēodisce Republik Österreich) is sǣstrandlēas land in
Middelre Europan. Hit is mōtlic þringgeweald. Ēastrīce hæfþ gebēon agylda þāra
Geāndena Lēodrīca siþþan þǣm 1955 gēare, and þǣre Europiscan Gesamnunge siþþan
þǣm 1995 gēare. Hit ligþ be Þēodisclande and Ceclande benorðan him, Slofacie and
Ungerlande beēastan him, Slofenie and Italie besūðan him, and Swisslande and
Lēohtenstāne bewestan him.

Æfter þe gehiersumode þis land Lǣdenware, Hunnas, Langbeardas, Ēastgotan,
Bægware and Francan, wæs Ēastrīce geweald fram þǣm Babenbeorges rīce fram þǣm
tēoðan hundgēara oð þæt þrēotēoðe hundgēare. Æfter þæt Babenbeorges hūs afylgode
þā Habsburgas, þæs hūs rīcsode Ēastrīce oþ þæt 1918 gēar.

Æfter þǣre adilegiunge þæs Hālgan Rōmāniscan Rīces on þǣm 1806 gēare, Ēastrīces
Casererīce (Germanisc: Kaisertum Österreich) gestaðolode Francis II. On þǣm 1867
gēare andwendede Franz-Iosef I Casere þis casererīce on þǣm twifealdan cynedōme
Ēastrīce-Ungerlande. Þæt Casererīce wæs adǣled on sumu ānstandendu rīcu æfter
þǣm unsige þāra Middelena Dōma on þǣre Ǣrestan Woruldgūðe, þe worhte Ēastrīce
swā hit is tōdæg.

In þǣm 1918 gēare wearþ Ēastrīce cynewīse, þe gelǣstede oþ þæt 1934 gēar, þā þā
Engelbert Dollfuß Canceler staðolode tictatorscipe cwæl.

Ēastrīce wæs be Adolf Hitler befangen for Þēodisclande, on þǣm 1938 gēare (seoh
þæt gewrit be Þēodnesse). Hitler wæs self on Ēastrīcþēode geboren. Æfter þǣre
oferdrīfunge þāra Nazea, þā Gefēran gesetedon Ēastrīce fram þǣm ende þǣre Ōðran
Woruldgūðe oþ þæt 1955 gēar, þā þā þæt land eft wearþ ful ānstandende lēodaþing
under þǣm gerāde be þǣm þe hit belufe ungewǣred (seoh ēac: Ēastrīclic Rīces
Nǣming). Hūru æfter þǣm geafealle mōtscipes on Ēasternre Europe, Ēastrīce wearþ
ǣfre gewyrcendre on Europiscum gelimpungum, and in þǣm 1995 gēar, Ēastrīce
geþoftode wiþ þā Europiscan Gesamnunge, and sēo Euro wearþ þæt gestede rīcisce
fēos gemitta on þǣm 1999 gēare.

Se Þēodisca nama Österreich cann wesan understanden sāmwell in Englisce swā
"ēasterne rīce", þe is of Ealdum Þēodisce Ostarrîchi. Se nama gelīce wæs
staðolod þurh lēodþēawisce āwendunge þæs Midieldisclǣdnan naman tō þǣm
landscipum: Marchia orientalis, þe mǣnþ "ēasterne landmearc," for þǣm þe hit læg
æt þǣm ēasternan ōran þæs Hālgan Rōmāniscan Rīces. Care weorðe is hit þæt sēo
forðung þæs Lǣdnan naman fram þǣm forman Ealdþēodiscan naman wōrhte þā nytte of
"Aust-" swā "ēast", ǣr þonne "sūþ" swā on Ealdum Lǣdne.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australisca_Witenagem%C5%8Dt

Se Australie Witenagemōt (Nīwenglisc: Parliament of Australia), se is ēac be
naman se Cynewīsan Witenagemōt (Commonwealth Parliament) oþðe Geþoftscipes
Witenagemōt, is Australie witenagemōt hwærin sind gesetnessa gewrōhten and
spricð þæs rīces lēodweard.

Ðes witenagemōt hæfð sēo Cwēn and tū hūs; se Senatus and þæt Spalena Hūs. On
Australie stent se Gemæne Gereca in þǣre Cwēne stede.

His bysen is se Witenagemōt þæs Geānedan Cynerīces forðæm is nemnð man ðās bysen
Sēo Westmynster Bysen.

Se Senatus is of þāra rīcum geceorren and hæfþ 76 witan, þā sindon twelf of
ælcum rīce and twegen of ælcum inlendiscum landscipe. Þæt Spalena Hūs hæfþ 150
hiredmenn.

Ðā tū hūs gadriaþ sundorlice æt Witenagemōt Hūs on Hēafodstōdbeorge on
Canberran, swylce tūn is in þǣm Australiscan Hēafodburg Landscipe.

The Cynewīsan Witenagemōt wæs on 9 Þrimilcemōnaþ 1901 on Melbūrnan (se is on
Uictorie rīce) be Georgius Æþeling, se wæs æfterweard Georgius V Cyning.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anna_%C4%92astengla_Cyning

Anna wæs Ēastengla Cyning of ymb þǣm 640. gēare ōð his dēaþ. Of Wuffingum wæs
hē, þā wǣron Ēastengla cynecynn. Annan fæder wæs Eni se rīcsode on Ēastenglum,
and he fēng to rīce siþþan Ecgric wæs geslagen on sæcce of Pendan Miercna
Cyninge. Þrēo suna hæfde Eni Cyning.

Bēda lofode Annan for his ǣfæstnesse on Crīstendōme and of his bearnum wǣron
manig gehālgod for hālgum: Iurmin his sunu and ealla his dohtra; Seaxburh,
Æþelþryþ, Æthelburh and ēac Wihtburh.

Lytel witon wē of Annan līfe and of his cynedōme. In þǣm 631. gēare hycgeþ man
þe hē wæs æt Exaninge, nēah þǣm Dēofles Dīce. In þǣm 645. wæs Cēnwalh Westseaxna
Cyning adrifen of his rīce fram Pendan Cyninge and, under Annan handa wæs hē tō
Crīstendōme gebroht þanne wunede hē on wræcce in Annan hīrede. Þā cwōm hē eft on
his āgnum folce þā staðolede Cēnwalh eft Crīstendōm on Westseaxum and siþþan
ætfealh sēo þēod fæstlīce Crīstendōme.

Ymbe þæt 651. wæs þæt land ymbe Elige gecnytted tō Ēastengla rīce, þan Æþelþryþ
Annan dohtor beweddod wæs þæs landes hlāforde. Annan rīce gelendede þæt mynster
æt Cnobheresbyrig. In þǣm 651., æfter Pendan onrǣse on Cnobheresbyrig be nīede
flēah Anna on wræcce, and man hycgeþ þe hē fōr westweardes on Magonsǣte. Hē
agēnhwyrfde on Ēastenglas ymbe þæt 653. gēar, ac sōna æfter awann Penda þæt rīce
and æt sæcce be Bulcampe adilgode Mierce þā Ēastengla fyrde, þǣrof wæs Anna
heretoga and on þǣm wælfelda aswefnedon Anna and his Iurmin his sunu.

Annan æftergenga wæs his brōðor, se wæs Æþelhere. Botwulfes mynster æt Icenhō
meaht bēon gemyndgung for þǣm cyninge. Æfter Annan dēaþe wearþ Ēastengla rīce
læsse in Miercna rīces sceadwe.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglia

Englaland is an mægþ (þe man England on nīwan Englisc hæt) þe is se dæl þæs
Geanedan Cynerices (þe man the United Kingdom on Modernan Englisc hæt). Hit norþ
ligeþ ymb Scottwara land and ymb Walewara land west and þus hit hafaþ
land-gemære mid Scottwara lande (þe man Scotland on Modernan Englisc hæt) and
mid Walewara lande (þe man Wales on Modernan Englisc hæt). Hit ligeþ on
westan-norþan Europe. Sæs þe þæt Englaland utanymblian sind be-westannorþan se
Irisc Sæ (the Irish Sea) and be-westansuþan se Celtlic Sæ (the Celtic Sea).

Englalandes nama cymþ of þǣm Englum, anum þriora mægþa Germania þe hie ofcomon
to Englande, oþerum twæm mægþum þe hie ofcomon to Englalande to eardian sind
Eald-Seaxa mægþ and Iota mægþ, þe habbaþ Englaland gesetled þǣm 5an and 6an
gēarhundredum. Siþþan 1707, þe man Grēate Bryten scōp, nu Englaland is ungewilde
þeod.

Englaland wæs in gēardagum cynerīce. Æþelstan cyning wæs sē ǣrresta cyning eall
Englacynn to geānlǣcenne in ānum rīce. Englalandes endemestan undercyning
aflīemed Ēadred Engla Cyning and Englarīce wæs an.

Mid Scottarīce wæs Englarīce geānlǣhte be Anne Cwēne in 1707, Grēate Bryten
Cynerīce to scieppenne.



https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albion

Englaland is an mægþ (þe man England on nīwan Englisc hæt) þe is se dæl þæs
Geanedan Cynerices (þe man the United Kingdom on Modernan Englisc hæt). Hit norþ

https://ang.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aix-en-Provence/gw

Æx oðra naman Æx-in-Profentse is Franclandes burg, in þæs rīces sūþdǣle. Hiere
nama on Francum is Aix (man sægþ "eks"), oþþe Aix-en-Provence, forþǣm is Aix
nama be manigum wicum geboren þā stent ofer hātum wiellum. Hiere nama is of þǣm
Lǣden naman Aquae Sextiae.

Æx stent 189 mīla be norðen Marseille þǣre ceastre. He is in
Profentse-landscipe, and in þǣre Bouches-du-Rhône département, ðærof is hit
sous-préfecture (se is 'underþegndōm'). Þēos burg hæfþ ymbe 130,000 onwuniendas.

Se mētere Paul Cezanne wæs geboren in Æxe, and wunode and āmētede þǣr swā
geþogen.

Aix (Aquae Sextiae) wearþ geseted in 123 BC fram þǽm Rómániscan consule Sextius
Calvinus, þe his naman his springum geaf, swá "Aquae Sextiae Salluvorum." In 102
BC his neāhness wæs the scene of the Battle of Aquae Sextae when Romans under
Gaius Marius defeated the Cimbri and Teutones, with mass suicides among the
captured wifmannum, which passed into Roman legends of Germanic heroism (cf
Ierome, letter cxxiii.8, 409 A.D. [1]).

In the 4th century BC it became the metropolis of Narbonensis Secunda. It was
occupied by the Visigoths in 477. In the succeeding century was repeatedly
plundered by the Franks and Lombards, and was occupied by the Saracens in 731.
Aix, which during the middle ages was the capital of the county of Provence, did
not reach its zenith until after the 12th century, when, under the houses of
Aragon and Anjou, it became an artistic centre and seat of learning.

With the rest of Provence, it passed to the crown of Francland in 1487, and in
1501 Louis XII established there the parliament of Provence which existed until
1789. In the 17th and 18th centuries the town was the seat of the intendance of
Provence.

Aix-en-Provence is situated in a plain overlooking the Arc, about a mile from
the right bank of the river. The city slopes from North to South and the
Montagne Sainte Victoire can easily be seen to the Norþ East.

The Cours Mirabeau, a wide thoroughfare, planted with double rows of
plane-trees, bordered by fine houses and decorated by fountains, divides the
town into two portions. The new town extends to the south and west, the old town
with its wide but irregular streets and its old mansions dating from the 16th,
17th and 18th centuries lies to the north.

The cathedral of Saint-Sauveur, which dates from the 11th, 12th and 13th
centuries, is situated in this portion of Aix. It is preceded by a rich portal
in the Gothic style with elaborately carved doors, and is flanked on the north
by an uncompleted tower. The interior contains tapestry of the 16th century,
other works of art and a baptism pool from first century. The archbishop's
palace and a Romanesque cloister adjoin the cathedral on its south side. The
church of Saint-Jean-de-Malto, dating from the 13th century, contains some
valuable pictures.

The Hotel de Ville, a building in the classical style of the middle of the 17th
century, looks on to a picturesque square. It contains some fine woodwork and a
large library which includes many valuable manuscripts. At its side rises a
handsome clock-tower erected in 1505.

Se tún, which is the seat of an archbishop and court of appeal, and the centre
of an académie (educational circumscription), numbers among its public
institutions a Court of assizes, tribunals of first instance and of commerce,
and a chamber of arts and manufactures. It also has training-colleges, a lycée,
a school of art and technics, museums of antiquities, natural history and
painting, and several learned societies.

Aix is often referred to as séo burg þúsanda springa. Among them are the
Fontaine des Quatre Dauphins (Fountain of the Four Dolphins), built in 1667 by
Jean-Claude Rambot; King René's Fountain, built in the 19th century, of Roi René
holding a bunch of Muscat grapes, which he introduced into Provence; the
hot-water fountain dating back to 1734, which is covered in moss due to the
35 °C (93 °F) water; and the great fountain, from 1860, at La Rotonde, the large
roundabout at the center of town.
